[021,ii_021,iii]	atha rajata aṃśe dharmi aṃśe ca tat jñānam pramā eva vaiśiṣṭya aṃśe na pramā iti ced na vaiśiṣṭyasya pūrva jñāna aviṣaya tvena aprakāra tvāt vaiśiṣṭya vṛtti viṣaya tāyām rajata tva puras vartinoḥ prakāra tvena bhramasya vaiśiṣṭya aṃśe pramātvā apramātvā āpātāt na api sva vyadhikaraṇa prakāra an avacchinna viṣaya tā pratiyogi anubhavaḥ pramā prameyam idam iti jñāne prameya tva prakāraka viṣaya tān āśrayasya aprasiddhyā avyāpteḥ 
[021,iv]	na ca saṃyogi tva ādinā prameya tva prakāraka viṣaya tā vyatirekaḥ ghaṭa ādau prasiddhaḥ iti vācyam pratiyogita avacchedaka rūpavat tvena pratiyogi jñānasya abhāva dhī hetutvāt kim ca yat kiṃcid vyadhikaraṇa prakāra an avacchinna tvam bhrama sādhāraṇam prakṛta jñāna vyadhikaraṇa prakāra an avacchinna tvam nirvikalpaka avyāptam tasya niṣprakāraka tvāt iti 
[021,v_021,viii]	ucyate yatra yat asti tatra tasya anubhavaḥ pramā tadvati tad prakāraka anubhavaḥ vā yatra yat na asti tatra tasya jñānam tad abhāvavati tad prakāraka jñānam vā apramā tad anyatve sati anubhava tvam eva vā pramātvam tad prakāraka tvam ca tad vaiśiṣṭya viṣayaka tvam tad viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvam vā īśvarasya tad viśiṣṭa viṣayam jñānam na tu tad prakārakam nirvikalpakam ca pramā pramābahirbhūtam eva vyavahāra anaṅga tvāt avyapadeśya padena tad upagrahasya nāma jāti ādi yojanā rahitam api pratyakṣam asti iti atra tātparyam idam rajatam iti jñānam idantu avati tad anubhava tvāt pramā rajata tva abhāvavati tad prakāraka jñāna tvāt apramā aṃśe samūha ālambanam ca na apramā eka prakāra abhāvavatī api tad apratīteḥ 
[021,ix]	nanu evam avyāpya vṛtti bhāva abhāvayoḥ ekatra pramā pramā ca syāt tad abhāvavati tad prakāraka jñāna tvāt iti ced na bhinna bhinna avacchedena hi vṛkṣe saṃyoga tad abhāvau na vṛkṣa mātre virodhāt ananubhavāt ca tathā ca yatra vṛkṣe saṃyogaḥ na tatra tad abhāvaḥ yad avacchedena yatra yat asti iti vā vivakṣitam 
[021,x]	go tva ādeḥ api sāsnādi avacchedena vṛtteḥ pāka rakte śyāmaḥ ayam iti dhīḥ pramā eva kadācid tatra tad sattvāt idānīm śyāmaḥ iti tu apramā eva na ca yat tadbhyām lakṣaṇān anugamaḥ na hi pramā sarvatra pramā kim tu kvacid tathā ca kim jñānam kutra pramā iti tad tad viśeṣasya lakṣya tvena yat tadbhyām eva lakṣaṇam yuktam 
[021,xi_021,xii]	anye tu anubhava tvam eva prāmāṇyam bhrame api aṃśam ādāya pramāvī avahārāt rajata ādi pramā pramā ca viśiṣya lakṣaṇīyā rajatatvavati tad anubhavaḥ tad abhāvavati tad anubhavaḥ vā ityādinā nanu anubhava tu asya pramā pra māsādhāraṇyena tat jñānasya na niṣkampa pravṛtti aṅga tvam iti ced satyam viśeṣa viṣaya pramāyāḥ eva pravartaka tvāt 
[021,xiii_021,xv]	atirikta viṣaya tā pakṣe viṣaya tā āśraya āvṛttya prakāraka anubhavaḥ pramā kevala anvayini viṣaya tā āśraya āvṛttiḥ avṛttiḥ eva prasiddhaḥ yat vā yat prakārikā yā viṣaya tā tad prakāra samāna adhikaraṇa viṣaya tākaḥ sva prakāra samāna adhikaraṇa viṣaya tākaḥ vā anubhavaḥ pramā jhryat prakāra āṭayā viṣaya tā tad prakāra vyadhi karaṇa viṣaya tākam sva prakāra vyadhi karaṇa viṣaya tākam vā jñānam bhramaḥ 
[021,xvi_021,xvii]	prakāra bhedena ekatra viṣaya tā bhedaḥ iti lakṣaṇa dvaya samāveśāt pramā bhrama saṃkaraḥ yat vā viśeṣya niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva apratiyogi prakāraka viṣaya tā pratiyogī viśeṣya niṣṭa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi prakāra an avacchinna viṣaya tva pratiyogī vā viṣaya tā samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi prakāraka viṣaya tva apratiyogī vā viṣaya tā samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi prakāra an avacchinna viṣaya tā pratiyogī vā anubhavaḥ pramā 
[021,xviii]	sva samāna adhikaraṇa prakāra an avacchinna viṣaya tā pratiyogi jñānam sva vyadhikaraṇa prakāra avacchinna viṣaya tā pratīyogi jñānam vā bhramaḥ idam rajatam iti bhrame ca viṣaya tā dvaye vyadhikaraṇa prakāra avacchinna tva tadanavacchinna tvayoḥ viṣaya tva pratiyogi tva tadapratiyogi tvayoḥ avirodhāt samūha ālambane ca viṣaya tā bhedāt na pramā pram ālakṣaṇe avyāpti ati vyāptī 
[022,i_022,ii]	vastutas tu viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣaḥ na asti eva māna abhāvāt sāmānyatas jñāne jñāte tasya kvacid viśeṣaṇa tā iti sāmānyatas viśeṣaṇa tā jñāne api ghaṭa mayam jānāti na vā iti saṃdeha tādavasthyāt tasmāt ghaṭa tad jñānayoḥ svarūpa grahe api tadīya tvam tat viṣaya tvam na gṛhītam iti tad viṣaya tve saṃdehaḥ tadīya tvam ca saṃbandham vinā tad saṃbandha svabhāva tvam tat uktam prakāśasya sataḥ tadīyatā mātra nibandhanaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ tad viṣaya tvam iti 
[022,iii]	saṃbandham vinā katham tadīya tvam saṃbandhasya eva svabhāva tvāt yathā tava eva viśeṣaṇa tāyām anyathā anavasthānāt anyatra api svarūpa saṃbandhe eṣā eva gatiḥ anyathā sāmānyena abhāva samavāyayoḥ jñāne adhikaraṇe jñāte tayoḥ saṃśayaḥ na syāt adhikaraṇa tad u bhaya svarūpāṇām jñāta tvāt tatra api abhāva samavāyayoḥ viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣaḥ na gṛhītaḥ iti ced na sāmānyatas tat grahe api saṃśayāt 
[022,iv_022,vi]	yuttu samūha ālambana viśiṣṭa jñānayoḥ viśeṣa anubhavāt viśiṣṭa jñāne viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣaḥ viṣayaḥ iti tat na viśeṣaṇa tām ādāya api samūha ālambana saṃbhavāt tatra api viśeṣaṇa tā antara svīkāre anavasthā samūha ālambanāt tu viśiṣṭa jñānasya viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa kṛtaḥ kārya kṛtaḥ prakāra kṛtaḥ vā prakāraḥ api viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣaḥ sa ca dharmiṇī eva astu iti ced na tam ādāya api samūha ālambana saṃbhavāt 
[022,vii_022,viii]	nanu sarva jñānānām yathārtha tvāt pramāṇa lakṣaṇe vyāvartya aprasiddheḥ viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyam anyathā ākhyātau māna abhāvāt tathā hi rajata arthi pravṛtti viṣaya tvam rajata tva prakāraka anubhava viṣaya tva vyāpyam rajata arthi pravṛtti viṣaya mātra vṛtti dharma tvāt rajata mātra vṛti dharma vat iti anyathā ākhyāti vyāpyam sidhyati iti aprāpta kāla tvam rajata mātra vṛtti tvam ca upādhiḥ śukti vṛtti jñāna viṣaya tā rajata tva prakārikā rajata arthitā janya pravṛtti viṣaya vṛtti viṣaya tā tvāt rajata vṛtti viṣaya tāvat iti atra rajata vṛtti tvam upādhiḥ rajata tvam arajata vṛtti jñāna viṣaya tāvacchedakam arajata viṣaya pravṛtti hetu jñāna prakāra tvāt śukti tva vat iti atra rajata āvṛtti tvam upādhiḥ 
[022,ix]	rajata tva prakārikā jñāna viṣaya tā arajata vṛttiḥ arajata niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyoginī vā arajata viṣaya pravṛtti hetu jñāna viṣaya tā tvāt śukti vṛtti viṣaya tāvat iti atra rajata āvṛtti tvam upādhiḥ viṣaya tāyāḥ nirasta tvāt ca vivāda padam rajata jñānam śukti viṣayakam śuktau pravartaka jñāna tvāt śukti jñāna vat iti atra jñāyamāna iṣṭa bheda agrahe kāraṇa tāvacchedakam rajata jñānam na pravartakam iti asiddhiḥ 
[022,x]	śuktiḥ rajata jñāna viṣaya tā āśrayaḥ rajata arthi pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt rajata vat iti atra rajata tvam upādhiḥ śuktau rajata arthi pravṛttiḥ svadharmi dharmika rajata tva prakāraka jñāna sādhyāḥ rajata arthi pravṛtti tvāt rajata pravṛtti vat iti atra rajata viṣaya tvam upādhiḥ sva padārthān anugamaḥ ca tad parityāge tu rajata arthi pravṛtti dharmika rajata tva prakāraka jñānena ubhaya siddhena rajata smaraṇena artha antaram 
[022,xi]	ucyate rajata arthitā janyā śuktau pravṛttiḥ iṣṭa pravṛtti viṣaya viśiṣṭa jñāna sādhyā pravṛtti tvāt śuktau śukti arthi pravṛtti vat na ca iṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtti tvam upādhiḥ sādhana viśeṣita tvāt yat vā rajata icchā janya śukti viṣaya pravṛtti janaka rajatatva prakārakam jñānam śukti viśeṣyakam śukti pravṛtti prayojaka jñāna tvāt śuktau śukti arthi pravṛtti janaka jñāna vat avacchedaka tve api prayojaka tva at na asiddhiḥ hetu tvam api tasya sādhayiṣyāmaḥ tathāvidham idam jñānam vā rajata tva prakārakam rajata icchā janya pravṛtti hetu jñāna tvāt satya rajata jñāna vat 
[022,xii_023,i]	na ca grahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ viśiṣṭasya jñānasya vā pakṣa tve bādhaḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ vā ubhaya siddhena śukti niṣṭha pravṛtti hetu tvena pakṣa tvāt anyathā sādhya tad abhāvavataḥ pakṣa tvena anumāna ucchedaḥ samavāya ati indriya tva vādinam prati agṛhīta asaṃsargaka dharma dharmi viṣayakam ekam jñānam eva viśiṣṭa jñānam sidhyati na ca evam ubhaya ravyātiḥ na anyathā khyātiḥ iti vācyam vyadhikaraṇa prakāraka jñānasya tattvāt 
[023,ii_023,iv]	na ca visaṃvādi pravṛtti ajanaka tvam upādhiḥ tathāvidhe idaṃjñāne rajata jñāne ca tvad mate sādhya avyāpaka tvāt na api doṣa ajanya tvam parasya jñāna mātre tathā tvāt anyathā tayoḥ eva sādhya avyāpaka tvāt na ca aprayojaka tvam iṣṭa purovarti viśiṣṭa jñānasya pravṛtti hetu tvāt atra prābhākarāḥ aprayojakam idam svatantra upasthita iṣṭa bheda agrahāt eva pravṛtti upapatteḥ kim viśiṣṭa jñānena pareṇa api āropaniyama artham tad abhyupagamāt na ca rajate pravṛttim prati viśiṣṭa jñānasya hetu tvāt iha api tad siddhiḥ pravṛtti mātre bheda agrahe sati iṣṭa purovarti jñānasya lāghavena hetu tvāt na tu sat api viśiṣṭa jñānam tantram gauravāt 
[023,v]	na ca rajate iṣṭa purovarti bheda grahasya aprasiddhyā katham tad abhāvaḥ iti vācyam puras varti niṣṭhe bhede rajata pratiyogi tva jñāna viṣaya tva abhāvasya puras vartini iṣṭa bhinna tva prakāraka jñāna viṣaya tva abhāvasya vā hetu tvāt na ca abheda vyavahāraḥ vyavaharta vyadhī sādhyaḥ na tu tad abhāva āgrahāt anyathā bheda agrahāt bheda vyavahāra āpattiḥ iti vācyam icchā ādīnām jñāta puras varti mātra viṣaya tvāt abheda abhilāpaḥ api jñāta bhedasya asaṃsargā grahāt iti na ajñāte vyavahāraḥ 
[023,vi^1]	nanu pītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ na śvetaḥ iti bheda jñāne api śveta abheda anumityā śveta arthi pravṛtteḥ abheda dhīḥ tad hetuḥ iti ced na tava api pītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ iti abheda jñānāt pīta arthī na pravartate bheda anumiteḥ iti bheda āgrahaḥ eva tad hetuḥ syāt bhrama tvena jñātam abheda jñānam akiṃcitkaram iti yadi tadā bhrama tvena jñātam bheda jñānam api tathā yat vā iṣṭa bheda aviṣayakam jñānam pravartakam na ca abheda anumita āviṣṭa bhedaḥ viṣayaḥ atas eta pūrvam bheda pratyaye api sa pratyayaḥ na bheda grāhi iti diś moha pratibimba ādi pratyayāḥ nanu evam rajate api viśiṣṭa jñānam na sidhyet pravṛtteḥ bhedā grahādeva upapatteḥ idam rajata tayā jānāmi rajata tayā jñātam iti anubhavaḥ śuktau api tulyaḥ na ca śuktau rajata tva bādhāt saḥ api asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ 
[023,vi^2]	bādhasya api viśiṣṭa jñāna tve māna abhāvāt iti ced na tatra hi rajatasya na smṛtiḥ prāk ananubhavāt grahaṇam ca tasya dharmi viṣayakam yogi adharmi yogena rajata tva jāti grahāt iti artha siddham dharma dharmi viṣayakam ekam jñānam na ca rajata tvasya śukti anubhava viṣaya tve hetuḥ asti na ca pratyabhijñāna vat saṃskāra indriye hetū tayoḥ atra bhinna viṣayaka tvāt ekadā svatantra upasthita viruddha aneka bheda agrahe saṃśayaḥ 
[023,vii]	krameṇa upasthitān eka bheda āgrahaḥ yena sa kramika viparyaya dvaya rūpaḥ syāt anyathā tava api apratīkārāt na ca saṃśaya anantaram viparyaya daśāyām ubhaya bheda agrahe saṃśayaḥ eka bheda agrahe anyathā khyātiḥ doṣa mahimnā hi ekasya na svātantryeṇa upasthitiḥ kim tu abhāva viśeṣaṇa tayā iti tad bheda agrahaḥ api akiṃcitkaraḥ na ca saṃśaya anantaram dhūma bhramāt asti kvacid vahni arthi pravṛttiḥ na tu tena vinā na ca tasya svatantra upasthita vahni asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ dvāram saṃśaya anurodhena tasya prāk api sattvāt vahni anumitiḥ dvāram iti vācyam liṅga bhramasya hi nirvahni tvasya svātantryeṇa upasthiti pratibandhaka tvena niyamataḥ svatantra vahni smṛtiḥ dvāram iti na saṃśayānyatha āravyātī na ca parvatasya pratyakṣa tve vahneḥ ca smaraṇe pratyakṣa bhramāt na viśeṣaḥ iti sākṣāt karomi iti syāt na tu anuminomi iti vācyam liṅga jñāna anantara bhāvi tva pratisandhāna apratisandhānābhyām ubhaya saṃbhavāt 
[023,viii_023,ix]	evam svatantra upasthitā aniṣṭa bheda āgrahaḥ api nivartakaḥ tena idam rajatam na śukttiḥ iti abhāva pratiyogi tvena aniṣṭa upasthiteḥ tad bheda agrahaḥ na nivartakaḥ śuktyabhāva asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ ca nakārasya arthaḥ iti na anyathā ākhyātiḥ aniṣṭa abheda grahasya nivartaka tve ca rajate eva na idam rajatam iti kṛtvā na nivarteta anyathā anyathā ākhyāti āpatteḥ atas eva rajate eva na idam rajatam iti jñāne api na pravṛtti anyathā ākhyātī rajata bheda asaṃsarga āgrahāt 
[023,x]	nanu rajata raṅgayoḥ ime raṅga rajate iti atra pratyekam ubhaya bheda agrahe yugapad pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām iti ced na evaṃvidha bhrame māna abhāvāt kāryaḥ nneya dharmāṇām yathākāryam unnayanāt krama utpanna jñānayoḥ bheda agrahāt eka tva abhimānaḥ anyathā tava api svatantra ubhaya bheda agrahāt pratyekam rajatam raṅgam vā iti saṃśayaḥ syāt yat eva vā tatra viparyaya niyāmakam tatas eva pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām tad hetoḥ eva iti nyāyāt 
[023,xi_023,xii]	yat tu prasakta pratiṣedha ātmā bādhaḥ akhyātau na yujyate sādhayati anyathā ākhyātim bādhaḥ eva hi naḥ sphuṭam iti tad viparītam paraspara viruddha tva aviśeṣeṇa bādhya tva avyavasthiteḥ viruddha arthakatayā utpanna tvam ca tulyam pūrveṇa api kvacid parasya bādhāt tasmāt abheda agrahāt prasañjitaḥ vyavahāraḥ bheda grahāt bādhyate iti yuktam 
[023,xiii_024,i]	upekṣā bhrame ca śabda prayogaḥ bādhyaḥ tad īyatā mātra svabhāva tvāt tad viṣaya tvasya katham rajatīya mātra jñānam arajati iyam svabhāva vyāghātāt na ca ubhayīyam samūha ālambana āpatteḥ tat uktam anyasya hi anyathā ābhānam pratītya eva parāhatam parasmin bhāsamāne tu na param bhāsate yatas iti 
[024,ii^1]	viṣayam vinā eva tat ākāram jñānam iti sa ākāra vādaḥ jñāna ayatha artha tve ca jñāna mātrasya tad śaṅkayā na niṣkampa pravṛttiḥ na ca doṣa ajanya tva ādinā viśvāsaḥ bhramāt aviśvāse pravṛtti abhāva āpatteḥ na api tat jñānāt jñāna tvena tatra api aviśvāsāt tat ucyate aho bata mahān eṣa pramādaḥ dhīmatām api jñānasya vyabhicāri tve viśvāsaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ iti bhramasya ca sat mātra viṣayaka tvena ayathārtha tā asat viṣayaka tve asat khyātiḥ na ca tatra hetuḥ asti śabdasya āpta uktasya nirdoṣasya liṅgasya ca ahetu tvāt na ca śabda anumāna ābhāsāt sā yogyatā ādimattayā śabdasya liṅga vat tayā pakṣasya jñānācśābda anumitī na ca ābhāse tat jñānam asti hetu abhāvāt eva kim tu agṛhīta asaṃsarga jñāna dvayam tatra indriyasya saṃbaddha grāhaka tvāt na ca pratyabhijñāna vat 
[024,ii^2]	ukta uttara tvāt na ca doṣa vaśāt asaṃbaddhe api vijātīyam kāryam doṣasya ajanaka tvāt na hi duṣṭāt kuṭaja bījāt yavāṅkuraḥ bhasmakam ca na doṣaḥ kim tu vahneḥ udbhavaḥ tasya ca dāha sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam eva rasa arjanam tu na bhavati bhakṣya dāhāt dava dahana dagdha vetravījam ca naṣṭam eva tad bhasmanaḥ kadalī janaka tvam tat uktam sa ākāra vādāt asataḥ na bhānāt saṃvid virodhāt atha hetu abhāvāt dhiyām anāśvāsa bhayāt ca na iṣṭā yatas anyathā khyāti ḥ atas yathārthā tasmāt vivāda padam jñānam na vyadhikaraṇa prakārakam jñāna tvāt satya jñāna vat bheda agraha janya rajata tva prakāraka śukti icchāyām pratiyogi prasiddhiḥ jñāna tvam sva vyadhikaraṇa prakāra avacchinna viṣaya tā pratiyogi vṛtti na bhavati jñāna mātra vṛtti dharma tvāt pramātva vat na ca cakṣuḥ cākṣuṣa satya jñāna atirikta jñāna janakam indriya tvāt rasana vat iti pratirodhaḥ aprayojaka tvāt cākṣuṣa jñāna atirikta jñāna janaka tva upādheḥ anyathā ākhyāteḥ api dharmi aṃśe satya tvāt tulya nyāyatayā vyāpake api vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca 
[024,iii]	evam svarūpataḥ viṣayataḥ ca agṛhīta bhedam jñāna dvayam eva visaṃvādi pravatti hetuḥ tat uktam saṃnihita rajata śakale rajata matiḥ bhavati yādṛśī satyā bheda anadhyavasāyāt iyam api tādṛś parisphurati iti vyavahāra mātrasya bheda agrahajanya tve api tasya saṃvāda tadabhāvābhyām jñāne yathārtha tva ayatha artha tva vyapadeśaḥ atas eva loke uṣṇam jalam iti jñāne na ayathārtha tva vyapadeśaḥ upekṣā jñāne tu tad vyapadeśaḥ tad yogya tvāt 
[024,iv_024,v]	sidvāntaḥ tu satya sthale pravṛtti mātram pratīṣṭa purovarti jñāne hetu tayā vyavasthite ati prasaṅga vāraṇa artham viṣaya tayā vaiśiṣṭyam eva kāraṇa tāvacchedakam kalpyate lāghavāt kāraṇa tā graha samaye jñāna vitti vedya tayā śīghra upasthitika tvāt bādhaka abhāvāt ca svatantra upasthita iṣṭa bheda āgrahaḥ kāraṇam tādṛśa bheda agraha tvam ca kāraṇa tāvacchedakam gauravāt kalpanīya upasthitika tvāt ca viśiṣṭa jñāne api hetu tvena āvaśyaka tvāt bheda āgrahaḥ eva hetuḥ iti ced na 
[024,vi_024,vii]	viśiṣṭa jñāne tad hetu tvasya tad kalpana uttara kalpya tvena pravṛtti kāraṇa tā graha samaye tad anupasthiteḥ na ca evam mithyājñāna kalpane gauravam pramāṇa pravṛtti samaye siddhi asiddhi parāhata tvena phala mukha gauravasya adoṣa tvāt pramāṇavataḥ tasya nyāyya tvāt evam ca visaṃvādi pravṛttiḥ api viśiṣṭa jñāna sādhyā pravṛtti tvāt satya pravṛtti vat kḷpta kāraṇam vinā anupapatteḥ ananyathā siddha tayā pravṛttyā samānīta viśiṣṭa jñāna balāt tad kāraṇam sa doṣam indriya ādi eva sarvatas balavatī hi anyathā anupapattiḥ na ca bheda agrahāt pravṛtti upapattiḥ api viparīta catuṣke yugapad pravṛtti nivṛtti āpatteḥ 
[024,viii_024,ix]	na ca tatra māna abhāvaḥ ime raṅga rajate iti satya jñāna vat rajataraṅgayoḥ pratyeka bhrama sāmagryoḥ ekadā sattvena tādṛśa bhrama utpatteḥ ānubhavika tvāt anyathā samūha ālambana ucchede dvi tva ādi a pratyakṣata āpatteḥ ime raṅga rajate iti śabda ābhāsā t evaṃvidha bhrama saṃbhavāt ca mama doṣa mahimnā rajata raṅgayaḥ rajataraṅga bheda grahān na saṃśayaḥ tava ca ekatra svatantra ubhaya bheda agrahāt pratyekam raṅgam rajatam vā iti saṃśayaḥ syāt 
[024,x]	atha yat dharma jñānāt yat upasthitiḥ tatra tad bheda agrahāt pravṛtti nivṛttī raṅga rajata dharmeṇa rajataraṅge smārite na tu raṅgarajate māṣa rāśi stham asī viṣaye māṣa arthi pravṛttiḥ masī nīlim asmārita māṣa bheda āgrahāt anubhūyamāna āropaḥ asiddhaḥ eva anyathā tava api pratyekam ubhaya jñānam syāt iti ced mā evam śabda ābhāsāt pratyakṣāt vā iṣṭa aniṣṭa upa sthitau tad abhāvāt mamatu eka dharmāt ubhaya upasthitau api rajataraṅgayoḥ tad tayā na jñānam doṣāt iti ubhaya siddham viparīta jñānam ca doṣāt na ca evam āvaśyaka doṣāt eva pravṛtti nivṛttī satya sthale tad abhāvāt na ca visaṃvādinī doṣāt indriya liṅga śabda ādi doṣāṇām ananugata tvāt tad janya jñāne ca jāti bhedāt 
[024,xi_024,xiii]	navyāḥ tu raṅga vṛtti tayā jñāta dharmasya rajate utkaṭākāṅkṣā tena saha bhūyas sahacāra darśanāt na raṅge alpa tathā tvāt iti tatra anutkaṭā sā evam rajata vṛtti tayā jñāta dharmasya api atas utkaṭākāṅkṣayā anutkaṭa ākāṅkṣā pratibandhāt na raṅge nivṛttiḥ evam rajate na pravṛttiḥ iti tat na ime raṅga rajate iti śabda ābhāsāt yugapad pravṛtti nivṛtti prasaṅgāt śabdāt upasthitau ākāṅkṣāyāḥ tulya tvāt kim ca evam dharmayoḥ bhūyaḥ alpa sahacāra avagamāt utkaṭān utkaṭa koṭikaḥ raṅgam rajatam vā iti saṃśayaḥ syāt utkaṭān utkaṭākāṅkṣā kalpane māna abhāvāt utkaṭa tva anirukteḥ ca 
[025,i]	syāt etat saṃvādi visaṃvādi pravṛttyoḥ vaicitrye viśiṣṭa jñāna bheda āgrahau hetū kḷpta tvāt na tu viśiṣṭa jñāna satya tva asatya tve gauravāt asiddheḥ ca pravṛtti nivṛtti mātre ceṣṭā aniṣṭa purovarti jñānam hetuḥ iti na ananugamaḥ na tu viśiṣṭa jñānam gauravāt na ca bheda grahe ati prasaṅgaḥ viśiṣṭa jñānam bheda agraham ca viśeṣa dvaya hetum vinā sāmānya hetoḥ kārya anutpādāt na hi nirviśeṣam sāmānyam nāma anyathā andhasya tvac saṃbandhe mahati udbhūta rūpavati candra mahasi pratyakṣatā āpattiḥ dravya sākṣātkāra hetoḥ sattvāt 
[025,ii_025,iii]	evam raṅge rajate ca visaṃvādinyau bhavataḥ bheda agrahāt na ca saṃvādinyau viśiṣṭa jñāna abhāvāt atha rajataraṅgayoḥ rajataraṅga bheda agrahāt visaṃvādinyau balāt syātām tad sāmagrī sattvāt visaṃvādinī tatra satya rajate na saṃbhavati iti ced atas eva bheda āgrahaḥ na tad hetuḥ tad sattve api tad abhāvāt na ca pravṛtti nivṛtti gatam visaṃvādi tvam saṃvādi tvam apekṣya tad hetunā te janyete kāraṇasya kārya anapekṣaṇāt iti 
[025,iv_025,v]	mā evam pravṛtteḥ aniṣṭa viṣaya tvam nivṛtteḥ iṣṭa viṣaya tvam visaṃvādaḥ tathā ca aniṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtta āviṣṭa viṣaya nivṛttau ca bheda āgrahaḥ hetuḥ iti katham tatas iṣṭa aniṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām tatra tasya asāmarthyāt iti atra brūmaḥ jñānam sva viṣaye pravartakam iti ādya pravṛttau saṃvādi pravṛttau ca sarvaiḥ avadhāritam lāghavāt bādhaka abhāvāt ca tatas iṣṭa jñānam śuktau pravartakam tat viṣayakam tad vyavahāra hetu tvāt sva aviṣaye tasya asāmarthyāt 
[025,vi]	atha bheda agrahāt grahaṇa smaraṇāt ca āvaśyakāt visaṃvādi pravṛtti upapatteḥ viśiṣṭa jñāna kalpane gauravāt ca sva aviṣaye api jñānam pravartakam iti kalpanāt sarvaiḥ prathamam avadhāritam api tyajyatām iti ced na prathama pravṛtta pramāṇa balena tatra api viśiṣṭa jñāna kalpanāt tatra bādhakam vinā tad virodhena kalpa antara anudayāt ca phala mukha gauravasya adoṣa tvāt anyathā prathamam sarvaiḥ gṛhītā api kārya anvite śaktiḥ siddhārtha darśanāt gauravāt ca parityajyeta iti sādhu samarthitam guru matam 
[025,vii]	nanu sva viṣaye jñānam pravartakam iti satyam kim tu visaṃvādi pravṛttau idam jñānam eva pravartakam na tu iṣṭa jñānam api tat hi jñāyamāna iṣṭa bheda agrahe kāraṇa tāvacchedakam lāghavāt iti daṇḍa tva vat anyathā siddham evam hi tad pratibaddha vyavahāra anukūla tvam tat viṣaya tvam rajata jñānasya śuktau na asti anyathā rajata jñānasya śukti viṣaya tva āpatteḥ saṃvādi pravṛttau ca iṣṭa jñānam pravartakam tasya viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt abhedena avacchedaka tva abhāvāt iti mama siddhāntasāraḥ iti ced 
[025,viii_025,ix]	ucyate svatantra anvaya vyatireka ādiṣṭa jñānam hetuḥ eva na tu itara hetu ta avacchedakam anyathā siddham vā na hi iṣṭa jñānam ādāya eva iṣṭa bheda āgrahasya anvaya vyatirekau yena daṇḍa tva vat tad avacchedakam na api iṣṭa jñānasya bheda agrahagarbha tvena anvaya vyatirekau yena daṇḍa rūpavat tat anyathā siddham anyathā agṛhīta bheda iṣṭa jñānam hetuḥ avacchedakaḥ bheda agrahaḥ iti eva kim na syāt tasmāt svatantra anvaya vyatirekāt ubhayoḥ api hetu tvam 
[025,x_025,xi]	kim ca iṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtti sthale pravṛtti mātram pratīṣṭa jñānasya hetu tvāt iyam api pravṛttiḥ tad janyā kḷpta hetum vinā kārya anutpatteḥ na ca iṣṭa jñāna janya tve iṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtti tvam avacchedakam gauravāt bādhakam vinā sāmānyayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamāt atas eva tat na upādhiḥ api atha tatra api idam jñānam pravartakam daiva adhīnam tasya iṣṭa viṣaya tvam api iti ced tarhi iṣṭe idam iti jñānāt eva pravṛttiḥ syāt na hi atra iva tatra api jñāyamāna iṣṭa bheda āgrahaḥ pravartakaḥ etena na rajata jñānam śukti viṣayakam tad pratibaddha vyavahāra ahetu tvāt iti nirastam asiddheḥ 
[025,xii]	nanu jñānam yathārtham eva iti vyāptiḥ eva tad bādhikā atas eva pravṛtti mātre viśiṣṭa jñānam iṣṭa jñānam ca hetuḥ lāghavāt sva viṣaye jñānam pravartakam sarvaiḥ eva adya pravṛttau tathā avagamāt asatya sthale iṣṭa jñānam api pravartakam na tu bheda agrahe hetu tāvacchedakam iti anyathā ākhyāti sādhanam na bhavati iti ced na teṣām anyathā siddhau anvaya vyatireka avadhārita kāraṇa tā mūlaka tvena taiḥ eva vyāpti bādhāt kḷpta hetum vinā kārya anutpatteḥ vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt ca jñāna ayatha artha tve api niṣkampa pravṛtti ādi upāyasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt 
[025,xiii_025,xiv]	etena saṃskāra indriyābhyām pratyabhijñāna vat śabda ābhāsa āditas vā parasparam saṃbandha virahiṇi ekam jñānam na bhavati iti jñānam yathārtham eva iti vyāptiḥ iti nirastam vyāpti ādi asiddheḥ sāmagrī sattve kārya āvaśyaka tvāt ca eka deśinaḥ tu rajata raṅgayaḥ rajataraṅga bheda agrahāt na yugapad pravṛtti nivṛttī na ca anyathā khyātiḥ doṣa vaśāt puras vartinam vihāya smṛta raja taraṅgābhyām purovartini bheda grahāt na ca rajata tvena smṛtiḥ saṃskāra gocara sarva rajata viṣayā syāt sāmānya pratyāsatteḥ tulya tvāt iti vācyam tat ta aṃśe rajata tve ca pratyāsattau api doṣāt smṛti anubhava pratibandha vat upapatteḥ 
[025,xv_026,i]	kim ca pratyakṣe sāmānyam pratyāsattiḥ smaraṇe tu manaḥ karaṇam saṃskāraḥ pratyāsattiḥ na tu tasya sāmānyam pratyāsattiḥ akaraṇa tvāt tat na ekaraṅga rajata mātra jñāna anantaram tayoḥ eva yama jayoḥ vā viparīta catuṣke ati prasaṅgāt anyathā ākhyāteḥ vā anye tu rajate na idam rajatam iti jñānam rajata tva asaṃsarga agraha rūpam rajata bheda asaṃsarga agraha rūpam pravṛtti pratibandhakam iti 
[026,ii_026,iii]	tat na anya vṛtti tayā upasthitasya rajata tva asaṃsargasya rajata bhedasya ca raṅge asaṃsarga āgrahāt nivṛtti prasaṅgāt raṅge ca tayoḥ asaṃsarga grahe anyathā khyātiḥ rajate rajata bheda asaṃsargā saṃsargasya asaṃsarga āgrahāt nivṛttiḥ iti ced na bheda asaṃsarga asaṃsargasya bheda saṃsarga rūpa tvena rajata bheda saṃsarga asaṃsarga grahāt raṅge nivṛtti prasaṅgāt rajata bheda saṃsarga asaṃsarga grahe ca anyathā khyātiḥ rajata vṛtti tayā upasthite bhede rajata bhedena saha bheda āgrahaḥ pravṛtti pratibandhakaḥ evam raṅge nivṛttau api iti ced na evam api śabda ābhāsāt yugapad pravṛtti nivṛtti āpatteḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣaya niṣṭha bhedayoḥ raṅga rajata bhedayoḥ ca śabdāt anupasthityā pratibandhaka tva abhāvāt 
[026,iv]	apare tu puras varti niṣṭhatayā jñāte bhede iṣṭa aniṣṭa pratiyogi tva abhāva grahāt pravṛtti nivṛttī tathā hi raṅge rajata bhedaḥ san api doṣān na bhāsate anyasmāt bhāsate eva tathā ca raṅga vṛtti tayā jñāte bhede rajata pratiyogi tva abhāva grahāt yathārthāt eva raṅge pravṛttiḥ raṅga pratiyogi tva abhāvaḥ san api doṣān na bhāsate iti tatra na nivartate evam rajata niṣṭhatayā upasthite bhede raṅga pratiyogi tva abhāva grahāt rajate nivartate rajata pratiyogi tva abhāvaḥ san api doṣān na gṛhyate iti na yugapad pravṛtti nivṛttī na ca raṅga vṛtti bheda tvam rajata bhede api asti iti tena rūpeṇa saḥ api bhāsate sāmānya buddheḥ sarva viśeṣa viṣaya tvāt tathā ca rajata bhede api tad pratiyogi tva abhāva grahe anyathā khyātiḥ iti vācyam pratyāsattau api raṅga vṛtti bheda tvena rajata bhedasya doṣeṇa agrahāt iti 
[026,v_026,vi]	mā evam idam rajatam iti jñānam anvaya vyatirekābhyām pravartakam iti anubhava siddham tat ca satya sthale viśiṣṭa jñānam anyatra jñāna dvayam ekam vā jñānam iti vivādaḥ tatra tat jñānam na pravartakam iti anubhava bādhitam tat api hetuḥ iti api na tasya satya sthale asiddha tvāt viśiṣṭa jñāna apekṣayā guru tvāt śabda ābhāsāt pravṛttau bheda ādi jñāna abhāvāt ca evam nivṛttau api anye tu iṣṭa vṛtti tayā gṛhyamāṇaḥ aniṣṭa vṛtti tayā ca agṛhyamāṇaḥ dharma sva āśraye pravartakaḥ iti sa ca dharmaḥ rajate rajata tvam raṅge rajata sādṛśyam evam nivṛttau api iti na yugapad pravṛtti nivṛttī iti 
[026,vii]	tat na evam hi ime raṅga rajate iti śabda ābhāsāt raṅga rajatayoḥ pravṛtti nivṛttī na syātām rajata vṛtti dharmasya ca raṅge raṅga vṛtti dharmasya rajate śabdāt anupasthiteḥ na ca śabda anantaram pratyakṣeṇa tayoḥ upasthitiḥ tatra hetuḥ na śabdaḥ iti vācyam ananyathā siddha śabda anuvidhānāt ime rajataraṅge iti svakīyam yathārtha jñānam anādṛtya tatra eva ime raṅga rajate iti pratāraka vākye viśvāsena pravṛtti nivṛtti darśanāt ca 
[026,viii]	itare tu rajate rajata tvam na gṛhyate doṣāt tathā ca rajata vṛtti tayā yāvat upasthita dharmasya rajata tvena bheda agrahān na pravartate raṅga vṛtti tayā upasthitasya ca kasyacid dharmasya rajata tvena bheda agrahādraṅge pravartate evam nivṛttau api yathā tava abheda grahe api māna antarāt bheda grahaḥ pravṛtti pratibandhakaḥ tathā rajate rajata bheda grahe api rajata vṛtti tayā yāvat upasthitasya rajata tvena mama bheda grahaḥ pravṛtti pratibandhakaḥ iti tat na etad apekṣayā viśiṣṭa jñānasya laghu tvena anvaya vyatirekābhyām ca hetu tvāt na ca hetu abhāvaḥ pratyabhijñāna vat saṃskāra indriyābhyām viśiṣṭa dhī saṃbhavāt tasya jñāna dvaya tve abheda ucchedaḥ tasya tad eka māna tvāt na ca eka viṣaya tvena tayoḥ paraspara sahakāritā nāma viśiṣṭa nāmi pratyakṣe tat ta aṃśe ca tad abhāvāt gauravāt ca na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ bheda agrahasya api tad hetu tvāt 
[026,ix]	atha pratyabhijñāyai ekatve api tat ta aṃśe na sākṣātkāri tvam tatra indriya asaṃnikarṣāt tat jñāna janya tvāt ca kim tu smṛti tvam purovarti abheda aṃśe ca sākṣāt tvam smṛti tvam anubhūti tvam ca na jātiḥ avyāpya vṛttiḥ vā iti ced tarhi saṃskārāt asaṃnikṛṣṭam api bhāsate iti tava api anumatam tathā ca tava eva rītyā pratyabhijñāna vat idam rajatam iti ekam jñānam astu tad sāmagrī sattvāt mama tu indriya janya tvāt jātya saṃkarāt ca sākṣātkāri tvam eva ubhaya tra 
[026,x]	nanu yaḥ yat sākṣātkāraḥ sa tad indriya saṃnikarṣa janyaḥ na ca rajate saḥ iha asti iti ced na pratyabhijñāyai indriya janya tayā sākṣātkāri tvena tat tāyām nāmni ca vyabhicārāt saṃskārasya smṛteḥ vā saṃnikarṣa tvāt ca na ca rajata tva pratyakṣe saṃyukta samavāyasya pratyāsatti tvena hetu tvāt tam vinā na tat iti vācyam tad viśiṣṭa jñāne viśeṣaṇa jñāna upakṣīṇa tvena tasya ahetu tvāt na hi viśiṣṭa dhī sāmagrī sattve tena vinā tad vilambaḥ 
[026,xi_026,xii]	kim ca viśeṣaṇa jñānam viśeṣya saṃbandhaḥ tayoḥ asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ iti pratyabhijñāsatya pratyakṣa sādhāraṇasya viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa hetoḥ bhrame api saṃbhavāt rajata sākṣātkāre rajata saṃyogasya hetu tve api viśeṣya saṃnikarṣa tvena hetu tā na tu rajata saṃyoga tvena yat sāmānye yat sāmānyam hetuḥ tad viśeṣe tad viśeṣasya hetu tva niyamāt saṃyogasya viśeṣya bhāna sām agryantarita tvena anyathā siddha tayā viśeṣa sāmagrī antarākalpanāt gauravāt ca pratyakṣa hetu tvena kḷpta viśeṣya saṃbandhāt eva tad upapatteḥ api ca pravṛttau svatantra upasthita iṣṭa bheda āgraha kāraṇa tva apekṣayā rajata sākṣātkāre viśeṣya saṃnikarṣa tvena hetu tvasya laghu tvāt 
[027,i]	vastutas tu doṣāt bhramaḥ iti ubhaya siddham tatra bhramaḥ na asaṃsarga graha abhāvaḥ tasya adhikaraṇa rūpa tve asādhya tvāt tad jñāna rūpa tve ca tasya pramātvena doṣa ajanya tvāt bhrama sthāna abhiṣikta pramā doṣa janyā eva iti ced na tasyāḥ kḷpta sāmagryantara janya tvāt iti bhramaḥ asatyajñānam iti asaṃnikṛṣṭam api doṣāt bhāsate iti abhyupeyam api ca doṣasya viśiṣṭam eva jñānam vyāpāraḥ pravṛtau tad hetu tvasya kḷpta tvāt na ca bheda āgrahaḥ kalpanīya kāraṇa bhāva tvāt yat tu duṣṭāt kāryam na iti tatra bīja indriya sādhāraṇam na duṣṭa tvam ekam asti 
[027,ii]	evam pratyakṣam api anyathā ākhyātau mānam kāraṇa bādhā bhāvāt tathā hi idam rajata tayā jānāmi iti anuvyavasāya sākṣikam eva anyasya anyathā bhānam na hi viṣaya tve anuvyavasāyāt anyat pramāṇam na hi atad viṣayaḥ tad jñāna viṣaya tvena na vā tad aviṣayakam tad viṣayaka tvena anuvyavasīyate anuvyavasāyasya pramātu a niyamāt anyathā ghaṭa jñāne api kadācid paṭam jānām iti syāt na ca bheda agrahadaśāyām rajata jñāna viṣaya tva asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ śuktau bheda grahe api śuktiḥ rajata tvena mayā jñātā śuktau rajata ajñānam me vṛttam iti anuvyavasāyāt 
[027,iii_027,v]	atha vicāra sādhya asaṃsarga graha bādhyaḥ ayam asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ tena vicāram vinā bheda grahe api avatiṣṭhate iti ced na idam rajata tayā jānāmi iti atra śukti karmakarajata tu aprakāraka jñāna asaṃsarga āgrahasya ātmani asaṃbhavāt tādṛśa jñāna aprasiddheḥ na ca idam jānāmi iti rajatam jānāmi iti tad ākāraḥ tṛtīya arthasya prakāra tvena prakāriṇaḥ abhāne abhāna prasaṅgāt viśiṣṭa jñānam ca sarvatra viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyīyam iti anyathābhānam api tathā jñāne rajata tva anabhyupagamāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya viṣayaka tvāt ca na sa ākāra vādaḥ 
[027,vi]	yat tu jñāna mithyā tve bādhya bādhaka vyavasthā na syāt aviśeṣāt iti tat na ananyathā asiddhāyāḥ dhiyaḥ bādhaka tvāt tathā hi yatra duṣṭa aduṣṭa indriya janyam paraspara nirapekṣam ekatra viruddham jñāna dvayam utpadyate tatra prathamam anupajāta virodhi tvāt na anāgatam bādhate tasya aprāpta tvāt uttaram tu sva kāraṇāt utpadyamānam upajāta virodhitayā na anupamṛdya pūrvam utpattum arhati iti pūrvam bādha ātmakam utpadyate anyathā na utpadyeta eva na ca evam eva iti vācyam anubhava virodhāt yat āhuḥ 
[027,vii_027,ix]	pūrvāt para balīyaḥ tvam tatra nāma pratīyate anyonya nirapekṣāṇām yatra janma dhiyām bhavet iti yatra pūrva apekṣam uttaram jñānam utpattum unmukham tatra upajīvya pūrva virodhena uttaram na utpadyate atas ajātam sat pūrvam katham bādhatām yathā pratyakṣa ādi viruddha anumitiḥ nanu bhramasya kim bādhyate na svarūpam tasya sattvāt na api rajata tva prakāraka tvam śukti viṣayaka tvam vā tayoḥ apanetum aśakyatvāt jātam hi tat rajata tvena śuktim viṣayīkṛtya na api vyavahāraḥ pravṛtti ādeḥ vṛtta tvāt na api anāgata vyavahāra janaka tvam tasya kāraṇa abhāvāt eva asaṃbhavāt 
[027,x_027,xi]	ucyate bādhakena bhramasya bhramatu a buddhiḥ eva bādhaḥ yat tu dhiyām ayathārtha tve katham āśvāsaḥ iti tat na prāmāṇya graha upāyasya darśita tvāt satya tva niyame api sat asaṃsarga āgrahasya agṛhīta asaṃsargasya jñāna dvayasya ca bahuṣu darśanāt katham āśvāsaḥ atha sat asaṃsarga āgrahasya pratisandhānam vilambitam sat viṣaya tvam ca śīghra upasthitam iti autsargika sat viṣaya tva jñānāt viśvāsaḥ yatra tu kadācid saṃśayaḥ tatra jñāna antarāt eva saṃśaya nivṛttiḥ iti ced mama api autsargikam dhiyām satya tvam bādhakena apanodyate iti tad anavatārāt satya tva viśvāsaḥ 
[027,xii_027,xiii]	kim ca tava jñāna antare api aviśvāsaḥ viśeṣa darśanāt viśvāsaḥ tulyaḥ eva yathā ca tatra api na saṃdehaḥ tathā uktam paratas prāmāṇye anye tu smṛta yogya vaidharmya abhāvaḥ adhikaraṇam tat jñānam vā tat ca pratyakṣatas eva gṛhītam iti yuktaḥ viśvāsaḥ ayogye bhedake adhikaraṇe ca bheda saṃśaye jñāna antarāt viśvāsaḥ iti 
[027,xiv_027,xvii]	tat na ubhayatra api jñāna antarāt viśvāsa tulya tvena śiṣya dandhana mātra tvāt vastutas tu bheda āgrahādeva abheda vyavahāra upapattauvabheda viṣaya tvam kvāpi na siddham asti iti katham sat viṣaya tva siddhiḥ yat tu doṣaḥ na hetuḥ iti tat na phala balena tathātvāt atha idam rajatam iti jñānam katham ayathārtham idaṃrajatayoḥ sattvāt na ca tad ubhaya tādātmyam asat ubhayam tādātmyam ca iti atas adhikasya abhāvāt tayoḥ ca sattvāt asattve vā asat khyātiḥ evam saṃsarga āropaḥ api iti 
[027,xviii_028,i]	ucyate sat mātra viṣaya tve api tad abhāvavati tad prakāraka tvam prakāra vyadhi karaṇa viṣaya tāka tvam vā ayathārtha tvam prāñcaḥ tu tādātmya saṃsargayoḥ asatorā iva manyante viṣaya tvam na ca evam asat khyātiḥ sat uparaktasya atyanta asataḥ khyāti abhyupagamāt sat anuparaktasya akhaṇḍasya atyanta asataḥ khyātiḥ asat khyātiḥ na abhyupeyate kāraṇa abhāvāt tad anupapattiḥ tulyā eva iti ced na atra viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagryāḥ darśita tvāt tat uktam vācaspati miśraiḥ tasmāt yat anyathā santam anyathā pratipadyate tad nirālambanam jñānam asat ālambanam matam iti 
[028,ii_028,iii]	sā ca pramā caturvidhā pratyakṣa anumiti upamiti śābdī bhedāt evam catasṛṇām tāsām karaṇam pramāṇam api caturvidham pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabda bhedāt anyeṣām yathāyatham eṣu eva antar bhāvāt tathā ca vakṣyāmaḥ nanu na pratyakṣam tāvat indriya artha saṃnikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyabhicāri ātma anumiti smṛtyoḥ jñāna mātre ca ati vyāpteḥ ātmanaḥ arthasya manasā indriyeṇa saṃyogāt utpatteḥ īśvara pratyakṣa avyāpteḥ ca saṃnikarṣasya ca saṃyoga ādi rūpa tvena ananugamāt ca saṃyoga ādi anyatamasya ca anirdhārita eka paratve bhāga asiddhiḥ itara bheda sādhane vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam ca indriya arthayoḥ eka janya tvasya lakṣaṇa tve vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam na ca tayoḥ eka eka janya tvam eva lakṣaṇam ātma manaḥ janya tvena jñāna mātre gata tvāt indriyasya pratyakṣa nirūpya tvāt ca na api jñāta karaṇa ājanya tve sati satyaḥ anubhavaḥ pratyakṣam liṅga ādeḥ ajanakatayā jñānasya ajñātasya karaṇa tve anumiti ādau gata tvāt jñāna ajanyaḥ anubhavaḥ satyaḥ iti api na viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa avyāpteḥ tasya viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvāt na api satya tve sati sākṣātkāri tvam niyata vyañjaka abhāvena grahītum aśakyatayā tasya jāti tva asiddheḥ sattve vā tat eva lakṣaṇam vyavahāra nimittam ca astu kim jātyā 
[028,iv]	ucyate pratyakṣasya sākṣātkāri tvam lakṣaṇam cākṣuṣa ādi jñāne sākṣāt karomi iti anugata buddheḥ bādhakam vinā jāti viṣaya tvāt na ca indriya janya tvam tathā anyonya āśrayāt indriyasya atīndriya tvāt ca na ca niyata vyañjaka abhāvāt na jātiḥ go tva ādau sāsnādeḥ iva ananugatasya api cakṣuḥ karaṇaka anubhava tva ādeḥ vyañjaka tvāt 
[028,v_028,vi]	na ca jātau anugata vyañjaka niyamaḥ jñāna icchā sukha duḥkha ādeḥ tad abhāvāt pratyuta niyata vyañjaka sattve jātya siddhiḥ eva tatas eva anugata buddhi upapatteḥ nirvikalpakeśvara yogi pratyakṣe ca pratyakṣa tvam dharmi grāhaka māna siddham yoga ja dharma ajanya janya sva viṣaya ka sa vikalpakājanya sāmānya lakṣaṇa pratyāsattya janya janya pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇam anāgata gocara sākṣātkāra hetu pratyāsatti ajanya janya sākṣātkāra tvam 
[028,vii_028,ix]	anye tu sāmānya jñāna pratyāsattyoḥ indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇatā antarbhāvāt tat janyam pratyakṣam saṃgrāhyam eva iti sva viśeṣya janyam jñānam janya pratyakṣam ātma viśeṣyaka anumiti śābda smṛtiṣu viśeṣya tvena tasya na hetu tvam viśeṣyam vinā api tāsām utpatteḥ kim tu samavāyi tvena yat vā indriya janyam jñānam janya pratyakṣam indriya tvena janaka tvam vivakṣitam janya pratyakṣa mātre indriya tvena cakṣuḥ ādīnām kāraṇa tā anugata hetum vinā anugata kāryasya ākasmika tva āpatteḥ smṛti anum iti ādau ca manasaḥ na indriya tvena hetu tvam kim tu manaḥ tvena anyathā smṛti ādeḥ sākṣātkāra tva āpatteḥ 
[028,x_028,xiii]	indriya tvam ca smṛtya janaka manassaṃyoga āśraya tvam prāṇa śarīra ātmānaḥ ca smṛti janaka manassaṃyogavantaḥ śabda itara udbhūta viśeṣa guṇān āśraya tve sati jñāna hetu manassaṃyoga āśraya tvam vā jñāna akaraṇakam jñānam iti tu vayam viśiṣṭa pratyakṣe ca viśeṣaṇa jñānam na karaṇam vyāpāra abhāvāt viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya pratyakṣe ca viśeṣaṇa jñānam hetuḥ na tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa dhīḥ api viśeṣaṇa dhī dvārā karaṇam māna abhāvāt pratyabhijñāyām tu tat ta asmṛtiḥ kāraṇam na tu saṃskāra dvārāḥ anubhavaḥ karaṇam tasyāḥ saṃskāra janya tve smṛtitva āpatteḥ smṛti tve lāghavena saṃskāra janya tvasya tantra tvāt tad hetutvena eva tad siddheḥ ca 
[028,xiv]	prābhākarāḥ tu sākṣāt dhīḥ pratyakṣam sākṣāt tvam ca na jātiḥ niyata vyañjaka abhāvāt na api sa vikalpaka anapekṣa jñāna tvam pratyabhijñā sā dṛśya dvi tva ādi pratyakṣā vyāpanāt kim tu yat jñānam yat viṣaya tve sa vikalpakā janyam tat tatra sākṣāt hīḥ miti mātṛ prakāśe ca sarvam eva jñānam pratyakṣam jñāna ajanya tvāt jātau anugata dhīḥ api pratyakṣāḥ jāti vyakti nirvikalpaka janya tvāt sādṛśya ādi viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya pratyakṣe ca na viśeṣaṇa jñānam hetuḥ tena vinā api yugapad indriya saṃnikṛṣṭe viśiṣṭa pratyaya udayāt 
[029,i_029,ii]	dīrgha ādi pratyakṣe ca na hasvādi jñāna apekṣā kim tu tad vyavahāre anumiti ādeḥ meyā aṃśe pratyabhijñāyāḥ ca tat ta aṃśe jñāna janya tvāt na pratyakṣa tvam kim tu parokṣa tvam eva miti mātraṃśe idanta aṃśe ca dvayoḥ eva pratyakṣa tvam yat tu tat tā prakāśe na tat tāsa vikalpaka tvena kāraṇa tā kim tu tat ta ajñāna tvena tat na anumiti ādau api liṅga ādi jñāna tvena anumeya ādi tulya tvāt iti 
[029,iii]	atra ucyate yadi tat tāyām pratyabhijñā parokṣa anubhava rūpā tadā na utpadyeta tad hetu liṅga ādeḥ abhāvāt tat ta ajñāna sahitam indriyam janakam iti ced tarhi indriya janya tvāt tatra sākṣāt dhīrā iva syāt na ca jñāna anapekṣa indriya janya tvam tatra tantram gauravāt jñāna sahita indriya janya tvena īdanta aṃśe api apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt ca na hi ekasmin jñāne janayitavye tad apekṣā tad anapekṣā ca saṃbhavati 
[029,iv_029,v]	aṃśe tat ubhayam api iti ced na jñāne aṃśasya viṣaya tvena tad ajanya tvāt evam miti mātraṃśe ca sarvam jñānam na pratyakṣam indriya ajanya tvāt sākṣātkāre tasya kāraṇa tvāt manaḥ janya tve anumeya aṃśe api tattva prasaṅgaḥ na ca jñāna mātra sāmagrī janya tvam pratyakṣa tve tantram gauravāt jñāna mātram ca na jñāna tvam tasya ajanya tvāt na api sarvam jñānam pratyakṣa jñāne pratyekam sarva jñāna sāmagrya janya tvāt sarva jñāna sāmagrya prasiddheḥ ca api ca jñāne avayava abhāvena aṃśaḥ viṣayaḥ eva viṣaye ca jñānam na kāraṇam atas anumiti pratyabhijñayoḥ sva viṣaye anumeye tat tāyām ca pratyakṣa tvam syāt viṣayasya sa vikalpakā janya tvāt 
[029,vi]	atha pratyabhijñāyām tad tāviṣaya tvena tat jñānam kāraṇam evam anum iti ādau meya viṣaya tve api mitimātri dantā dharmi viṣaya tve ca na jñānam kāraṇam kim tu jñāna sāmagri iti ced na tad viṣaya tvam hi jñāne sva kāraṇa adhīnam tadīya svabhāva tvam sva rūpa viśeṣaḥ sa ca eva daṇḍi jñāna ādau ca avyāptiḥ tasya anum iti ādi vat viśiṣṭa jñāna tvena viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvāt na ca parokṣa tvam upādhiḥ pratyabhijñāyām prathama utpanna jāti vyakti jñāne janye jāteḥ anugata pratyakṣe ca sādhya avyāpaka tvāt 
[029,vii_029,viii]	pūrva vyakti vṛtti tve sati etat vyakti vṛtti tvam anugata tvam iti tatra pūrva anubhūta vyakteḥ viśeṣaṇa tvena tatra jñānasya anugata tva pratyakṣe kāraṇa tvāt anyathā prathamam api anugata dhī prasaṅgaḥ atas eva jñāna sākṣāt ajanyam jñānam pratyakṣam pratyabhijñāyām saṃskāraḥ eva sākṣāt janakaḥ jātau anugata dhīḥ api saṃskāra janyā evam sādṛśya ādi pratyakṣe api pratiyogi saṃskāraḥ eva kāraṇam iti nirastam daṇḍa anubhava janya daṇḍi pratyakṣe dhārāvāhika pratyakṣe ca avyāpanāt uttara viśiṣṭa jñāne pūrva viśiṣṭa anubhavasya eva viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena hetu tvāt saṃskārasya smaraṇa itarājanaka tvāt ca anyathā pratyabhijñā ādeḥ saṃskāra janya tvena smṛti tvam syāt iti ukta tvāt 
[029,ix]	pratyakṣa viśeṣe saṃnikarṣa viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ ananugataḥ eva saṃyogena dravya grahaḥ saṃyukta samavāyena rūpa karmaṇoḥ grahaṇam saṃyukta samaveta samavāyena rūpa tva ādeḥ samavāyena śabdasya samaveta samavāyena śabda tva ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tayā śabda abhāvasya indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tayā samavāya ghaṭa abhāva ādeḥ yogya saṃnikarṣāt eva grahaḥ na saṃnikarṣa mātrāt 
[029,x_029,xi]	atha sūkṣma avayava avacchedena avayavi saṃyoge api na tat grahaḥ iti mahā avayava avacchedena saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ tathā ca avayava indriya saṃyogaḥ eva hetuḥ na ca grāhya saṃyoga avacchedaka avayava saṃyoga apekṣayā grāhya saṃyogasya laghu tvāt saḥ eva hetuḥ tasya atiprasakta tvāt etena sva avayava saṃyoga apekṣayā sva saṃyogasya laghu tvāt saḥ eva hetuḥ iti nirastam na api avacchedaka saṃyogena anyathā siddhau tatra api avacchedaka antara saṃyogena anyathā siddhiḥ iti saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ eva na syāt iti vācyam alpataratama bhāga avacchedena saṃyogasya hetu tve ati prasaṅgāt iti 
[029,xii]	mā evam dravya grahe avayavi mātra grahe vā sthūla avayava avacchedena saṃyogaḥ na na hetuḥ ātma trasa reṇu sūkṣma bhāga grahe vyabhicārāt kim tu ghaṭa ādi grahe sa hetuḥ evam ca ātma ādi dravya grahaḥ grāhya saṃyoga janyaḥ iti ghaṭa ādi grahaḥ api tadvat eva sva grāhya saṃyoga janyaḥ iti tasmin sati api ghaṭa ādi grahaḥ na asti iti yadi tadā sthūla avayava saṃyogaḥ avacchedakaḥ astu tad saṃyogaḥ api vā hetuḥ na tu kḷpta hetu parityāgaḥ 
[029,xiii_029,xv]	ced nanu saṃyukta samavāyena avayavi grahaḥ astu na tu saṃyoga ādiḥ tatra hetuḥ tasya rūpa ādi grahe kḷpta tvāt na ca lāghavāt saṃyogaḥ eva tathā tasya kalpanīya kāraṇa tvāt iti na ātma grahe indriya saṃyogasya kāraṇa tvāt anyatra api dravya sākṣātkāra tvena tathā kalpanāt na ca bahis indriya dravya grahe avayavi grahe vā saṃyukta samavāyaḥ kāraṇam lāghavena saṃyogasya eva kāraṇa tvena kalpanāt 
[030,i]	nanu saṃyukta samavāyaḥ na gandha grāhakaḥ kiṃtu āśraya saṃyogaḥ evam gandha tva grahaḥ api āśraya āśraya saṃyogāt iti saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ api na hetuḥ na ca gandhe sati gandha samavāyam vinā gandhāgrahaḥ asti na ca evam saṃyukta ghaṭe bhāvi gandha grahaḥ syāt gandhasya api sva grahe hetu tvāt na ca gandhasya pratyakṣa tvena indriya saṃnikarṣa āśraya tvam anumeyam śabda pratyakṣa hetoḥ samavāyasya gandhe api sattvāt gandha indriya saṃnikarṣa sādhane sādhya aprasiddheḥ 
[030,ii_030,iii]	mā evam gandha samavāyi saṃyogasya hetu tve hi yadi gandha samavāyasya viśeṣaṇa tā tadā sa hetuḥ eva upalakṣaṇa tve ca saṃyukta dravya mātram upalakṣyam tathā ca ghaṭa saṃyogāt paṭa gandha graha prasaṅgaḥ atha sva samavāyi saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ tatra samavāyaḥ avacchedakaḥ iti ced tarhi saṃyogi samavāyasya hetu tve saṃyogaḥ avacchedakaḥ samavāyaḥ hetuḥ iti tulyam tat etat parivartya kṣauma paridhānam iti ucyate 
[030,iv]	nanu saṃyukta samavāyaḥ na saṃyogaḥ na vā samavāyaḥ na ubhau vā gandhe indriye ca āvṛtteḥ na ca indriyeṇa gandhasya paramparā sambandhaḥ paramparā hi saṃyoga samavāya aveba tatra virodhaḥ eva na adhikaḥ apasiddhāntāt iti ced na indriya tad saṃyoga tad āśraya samavāyānām eva paramparā sambandha tvāt anyathā nīlatva jāteḥ paramparā sambandhena vastra carma kambaleṣu anugata vyavahāra ucchedaḥ 
[030,v]	nanu saṃyukta samaveta samavāyāt na rūpa tva ādi grahaḥ tad abhāvāt iti ced na tad anabhyupagame api rūpa ādi sādṛśyasya tatas grahāt na ca dravya sādṛśyāt eva tad vyavahāraḥ bādhakam vinā pratītyaviśeṣāt vaiparītya āpatteḥ āśraya vaisādṛśye api rūpa rasa ādeḥ sādṛśya anubhavāt ca rasa tva madhura tvac andha tva surabhi tva ādiḥ ca jātiḥ anugata pratyayāt rūpe ca yadi api idam nīlam iti anubhavaḥ na tu idam rūpam idam rūpam iti tathā api pītaḥ varṇaḥ nīlaḥ varṇaḥ iti varṇa ākāra anugata buddhiḥ asti rūpa tve mānam na ca cakṣuḥ ādi ekaika indriya grāhya tvam rūpa tva ādikam bādhakam vinā anugata buddheḥ jāti viṣaya tvāt indriya atīndriya tvena cakṣuḥ ādi agrahe api rūpa tva ādi pratīteḥ na hi ananu saṃhita upādheḥ upahita pratyayaḥ atīndriya rūpa rasa gandhān anumāna āpatteḥ ca yogyatāyāḥ rūpa tva ādi jāti nirūpya tvāt 
[030,vi]	yadi api tad mate nīla pīta ādi ekaikam eva nityam na atīndriyam tathā api cakṣuḥ ghrāṇa ādi rūpasya āloka pṛthivī ādi rūpa abhinna tvena pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca ekam eva rūpam udbhūtam anudbhūtam ca iti virodhāt rūpa tva ādinā paraspara vyāvṛtta tayā jñātasya rūpa ādeḥ upalabdhyā tad kāraṇa tvena paraspara vyāvṛtta cakṣuḥ ādi anumitiḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta cakṣuḥ ādi anumitau ca cakṣuḥ grāhya tva ādinā rūpa ādi paraspara vyāvṛtta dhīḥ iti anyonya āśrayāt ca nīla pīta ādi pratītau bhinna bhinna karaṇa tva siddhau api tad tad karaṇa grāhya tvasya sarva rūpeṣu asiddhiḥ 
[030,vii]	nanu nīla pīta ādi upalabdhi karaṇeṣu gandha rasa sparśa avyañjaka tve sati nīla ādi vyañjaka tvāt āloka vat iti taijasa tvam prasādhya taijasa indriya grāhya tvena nīla ādau rūpa ākāra anugata dhīḥ evam gandha ādau api iti ced na evaṃpraṇālī jñāna abhāve api rūpa rasa ādau anugata pratyayāt nīla ākāra anugata buddheḥ ca nīla tvam jātiḥ na ca cakṣuḥ grāhya tvam tat pīta ādau gata tvāt 
[030,viii_030,ix]	nanu ekaikāḥ eva nīla aruṇa ādi vyaktayaḥ nānāmasī nīlimni bheda grahe api tattvena pratyabhijñānāt na ca aneka vyakti vṛtti tve nitya tve jāti tva āpattiḥ jāteḥ saṃsthāna mātra vyaṅgya tvāt avayava avayavi vṛtti tvāt go tva ādinā para apara bhāva anupapatteḥ ca nīla itara ādi pratītiḥ ca tad anya rūpa asaṃbhedāt iti ced na pākena śyāmam naṣṭam raktam utpannam iti pratyayāt na ca asau bhramaḥ bādhaka abhāvāt na ca utpāda vināśa pratyayasya samavāyaḥ viṣayaḥ tad anullekhāt evam ca madhura ādi rasānām saurabhā saurabhāṇām ca gandhānām ekaika tvam syāt nīla ādi tulya tvāt evam astu iti ced na teṣām utpāda vināśa anubhavāt ekaika tve madhuratara tva ādi anupapatteḥ ca 
[030,x]	nanu śrotreṇa samavāyena śabda grahe sarva śabda upalabdhiḥ syāt na ca karṇa śaṣkulī avacchedena utpannaḥ gṛhyate avacchedyasya ākāśa tvena aviśeṣāt tad anya tve śabdasya tatra asamavāyāt tasmāt yaḥ śabdaḥ yam prati yogyaḥ sa tena gṛhyate na anyaḥ na ca puruṣa viśeṣam prati yogya tvam na svarūpam ananugamāt na ca jātiḥ tasyāḥ niṣpratiyogika tvāt na hi gauḥ kaṃcid pratyagauḥ iti vācyam sa pratiyogika tvam hi na sa avadhi tvam dīrgha tva ādi vat na api itara dhīni rūpya tvam abhāva vat kim tu śabda grahe sā jātiḥ kāraṇam tad avacchedikā vā atas eva na kurvat rūpa tva praveśaḥ sahakāritāsu īkārāt sarva sādhāraṇa tvam iṣṭam eva sarvaiḥ tathā vyavahriyamāṇa tvāt go tve api tat eva tat śabda mātrasya yogya tvam ananugatam eva guṇa yogya tva vat iti 
[030,xi]	mā evam śabdasya pratyakṣa tvena pratyāsatti sādhanāt na ca samavāyaḥ ati prasaktaḥ anyaḥ anabhyupagataḥ iti vācyam karṇa saṃyoga avacchinna samavāyasya pratyāsatti tvāt karṇa saṃyogaḥ hi samavāya vṛttyā śabda ādhāra tāyām paricāyakaḥ evam ca iha śabdaḥ na iha śabdaḥ iti anubhavāt śabdasya avyāpya vṛtti tve siddhe yasya śabdasya samavāya vṛttyai ādhāratā karṇa saṃyogena avacchidyate sa gṛhyate yasya tu tad atyanta abhāvena avacchidyate sa na gṛhyate tathā saṃyogasya samavāyena ādhāratā hasta saṃyogena avacchidyate na tad abhāvena iti hasta saṃyoga avacchedena gṛhyate na anyatra anyathā hasta saṃyogasya anavacchedaka tve sarvam idam samānam iti saṃyogasya api sarvatra upalabdhiḥ syāt na ca evam samavāyaḥ api avyāpya vṛttiḥ samavāyena vṛttyā tasya ādhāra āvṛtti tvāt abhāvaḥ tu viśeṣaṇa tayā vyāpya vṛttiḥ eva 
[030,xii_030,xiii]	na ca evam sarvatra sarva śabda upalabdhiḥ syāt śabda samavāyasya sattve api anyatra śabda atyanta abhāva sattvāt atha vīṇā ādau śabdaḥ iti abādhita anubhava balāt tad avacchinnam nabhaḥ śrotram na tu karṇa avacchinnam eva karṇe na śabdaḥ kim tu vīṇāyām iti anubhavāt anyathā karṇe śabdaḥ iti dhīḥ syāt na ca ananta vīṇā ādi avacchedaka tvena ananta śrotra svīkāre gauravam śabda deśa tvena ekatve ca atiprasaṅgaḥ sarva deśānām śabda avacchedaka tvāt iti vācyam vīṇā ādi deśa tā grahasya bādhakam vinā pramāṇa tve gauravasya nyāyya tvāt pratyuta sarvatas dikṣu ananta śabda santāna utpāda krameṇa karṇa utpāde kalpanā gauravam māna abhāvāt na ca dūra saṃnidhānayoḥ śabdānām abādhita tāra manda tva ādi vaidharmya pratītyā bheda siddheḥ saṃtāna siddhiḥ dūra tva ādi doṣāt tāra tva agrahe manda tva āropāt tad upapatteḥ vyavahita karṇe śabda anutpāda vat vyavahita śabda anupalabdhiḥ nimitta vāyu saṃyoga abhāvāt 
[031,i_031,ii]	vyavadhāna abhāvasya hetu tvāt tasya saṃnidhi upakṣīṇa tvāt karṇa anupaghātaḥ api hetuḥ iti na tad upaghāte śabda grahaḥ iti mā evam karṇa avacchedena api śabda grahāt karṇa śaṣkulī api avacchedikā iti karṇa avacchinnam eva nabhaḥ śrotram āvaśyaka tvāt lāghavāt ca śabda mātra grahe tad anuvidhānāt śarīra saṃyuktasya sataḥ sākṣāt pratīti sādhanasya indriya tvāt karṇena vīṇā śabdam śṛṇomi iti tad kāraṇa tvena ābādhita anubhavāt ca na tu vīṇadikam ananta tvāt śabda mātra grahe tad ananuvidhānāt vīṇā ādi avacchinnasya nabhasaḥ śarīra asaṃyukta tvena anindriya tvāt vīṇayā śabdam śrṛṇomi iti ananubhavāt ca 
[031,iii]	katham tarhi vīṇāyām śabdaḥ iti jñānam śrūyamāṇasya śabdasya tad anadhikaraṇa tvāt iti ced na na hi sarvatra śabde mṛdaṅga ādi adhikaraṇa graha niyamaḥ anyathā kvacid api deśe saṃdeha viparyaya tad anud lekhānām anupapatteḥ yatra api asti tatra śarīre sukham itivat utpattaye paraṃparayā vīṇā ādi apekṣaṇāt tad adhikaraṇa tvam tava api vīṇāyāḥ śabdān āśraya tvena tathā eva adhikaraṇa tvāt 
[031,iv]	nanu evam karṇe aneka gakāra utpāde aneka grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ na ca eka grahe anyagraha sāmagrī pratibandhikā kolāhale tathā adarśanāt iti ced na tāreṇa manda abhibhavāt tulya tve vā aneka grahasya iṣṭa tvāt bheda āgrahaḥ tu atyanta sārūpyāt evam ca vīṇā ādeḥ aśrotra tve maitreṇa aham anuvākam adhyāpitaḥ yad gītam tvayā śrutam tat mayā api iti ādi pratītīnām tad uccāraṇa ādi prayojya jātīya tvam viṣayaḥ śabde hi kāraṇa viśeṣa prayojyā jātiḥ avaśyam vācyā anyathā śabda viśeṣeṇa putra ādi anumānam na syāt jātim vinā viśeṣa antara abhāvāt evam ca karṇa avacchinnasya nabhasaḥ śrotra tve tena vīṇā ādi prabhava śabda grahaḥ na tatra santāna krameṇa utpādam vinā iti ananya gatika tayā tad kalpanā api prāmāṇikī 
[031,v]	śabdena ca avyavahita paramāṇu deśa utpāda krameṇa na śabda ārambhaḥ yena meghaja ādi śabdānām bhū loka prāptiḥ yuga antare api na syāt kim tu megha ādi abhihata sarvatas gāmi mahā vāyoḥ mahati deśe saṃyoga nimittam āsādya ādya śabdena sarva digvartī śabdaḥ ekaḥ eva janyate nimitta saṃyoga anurodhi tvāt vibhu kāryāṇām uttarottareṇa api adhika adhika deśataḥ sarvatra ekaikaḥ eva śabdaḥ vīcī utpādyate atas eva sarvaiḥ eka śabda grahaḥ 
[031,vi_031,viii]	vāyoḥ ca nayana vat mahā vegatayā śīghra gāmi tvena agrima śabda ārambhāt ādya śabda anantaram acireṇa eva śabda upalambhaḥ vāyoḥ eva ca mandataratamādi krameṇa manda ādi śabda utpattiḥ yat vā ādya śabdena kadamba golaka vat daśa diśi daśa śabdāḥ ārabhyante taiḥ ca daśa śabda santānāḥ iti nanu eka śabdena katham aneka śabda ārambhaḥ sāmagrī bhedāt iti ced na sarvatas aneka vāyu ādi sahakārāt prāc abhāva bhedāt vā 
[031,ix]	na ca tad itara hetu sākalye tad bhedāt na kārya bhedaḥ tathā adarśanāt iti vācyam kārya bhedaḥ hi sāmagrī bhedāt sa ca hetu antara bhedāt iva prāc abhāva bhedāt api anyathā samavāyi ādi bhede api kārya vaijātyam na syāt ghaṭa vyaktiṣu tathā adarśanāt pāka je rūpa ādau hetu antarā abhede api prāgabhāva pūrvarūpa ādi dhvaṃsa bhedena bhedāt ca 
[031,x]	atha rūpa ādi eka eka prāgabhāva dhvaṃsayoḥ sarvatra tulya tve kim vinigamakam gandha ādi prāc abhāvānām rasa ādau vyabhicāre api gandha ādau rasa ādi prāc abhāvānām avyabhicārāt iti ced na vāyu sparśe gandha rasa rūpa prāc abhāva pradhvaṃsānām tejaḥ rūpe gandha rasa abhāvayoḥ jala rase gandha prāgabhāvasya vyabhicāreṇa ahetu tve sva prāga bhāva hetu tāyāḥ āvaśyaka tvāt pāka jeṣu rūpa rasa sparśeṣu gandha ādi prāgabhāvānām anyathā siddha tvāt ca rūpa ādiṣu tathā adarśanāt gandhe api sva prāgabhāvasya avaśya hetutvāt abhāva antarāṇām anyathā siddha tvam yat vā rūpa rasa sparśa tulya tve api agni saṃyoga viśeṣāt kvacid saurabham asaurabham ca utpadyate na ca agni saṃyogaḥ rūpa ādi mātre kāraṇam vyabhicārāt evam rasa ādau api nanu kārya mātre prāc abhāva mātram na hetuḥ tayoḥ vyatireka kālān avagamāt sarva muktau itara hetu abhāvāt eva kārya anutpādāt iti ced na hetu antara sattve api utpannasya punar anutpādena prāgabhāvasya hetu tvāt ekā sāmagrī janayati svabhāvāt iti ced na kārya anutpādasya sāmagrī viraha prayojya tva niyamāt 
[031,xi_031,xii]	na ca kārya sahabhāvena kāraṇa tvam gauravāt na ca vinaśyat avasthe samavāyini kārya anutpatteḥ tathātvam iti vācyam tāvatā samavāyi kāraṇasya eva tathātvāt kāraṇa mātre māna abhāvena tasya aprayojaka tvāt nanu samaveta samavāyaḥ na grāhakaḥ śabda tva ādi jāteḥ abhāvāt iti ced na rūpa tva ādi nyāyena tad sādhanāt 
[032,i_032,ii]	nanu samavāya asiddheḥ na sā pratyāsattiḥ vipratipattiḥ ca śuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti pratītiḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha viṣayā na vā iti atha jāti guṇa kriyā tadvantau mithas sambaddhau anubhūyete na hi asaṃbaddha svarūpa dvaye viśiṣṭa dhīvī a padeśau iti ced na saṃbaddha anubhavena hi saṃbandhaḥ na viśeṣaṇam bhāsate tasya prathamam ajñānāt saṃyoginau imau iti vat samavāyinau iti ananubhavāt ca na api viśeṣyaḥ anayoḥ samavāyaḥ iti ananubhavāt na api svarūpeṇa bhāsate samavāyam jānāmi iti viṣayatān anubhavāt 
[032,iii]	nanu nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ ityādi anubhavaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha viṣayaḥ viśiṣṭa pratīti tvāt daṇḍi jñāna vat iti ced na aghaṭam bhū talam jñātam iṣṭam kṛtam ca iti atra vyabhicārāt saṃbandha viṣaya tve bādhakam vinā iti viśeṣaṇam iti ced na bādhaka abhāvasya eva samartha tve śeṣa vaiyarthyāt sādhaka abhāvena sat pratipakṣāt ca bādhaka abhāvasya sādhaka tva vat sādhaka abhāvasya bādhaka tvāt tasmāt ubhaya abhāve saṃśayaḥ syāt 
[032,iv_032,v]	na ca pratītiḥ eva samavāya sa adhikā tasyāḥ tad viṣaya tva asiddheḥ anyathā anyonya āśrayāt atha aghaṭam bhū talam jñātam ityādi api viśiṣṭa dhīḥ saṃbandha viṣayā kim tu bhrāntā bādhaka sattvāt iti ced tarhi bhū tale aghaṭa tvasya jñāta tva ādeḥ ca abhāvaḥ syāt tathā ca vyavahāra vilopaḥ saṃbandhaḥ ca na saṃyogaḥ samavāyaḥ vā anyataraḥ vā bādhāt asiddheḥ vā na api saṃbandha mātram jñāpaka tva ādinā siddha sādhanāt 
[032,vi]	na api aviśiṣṭa vyāvṛtta viśiṣṭa jñāna niyāmakaḥ abhāva jñāna ādau iva svarūpa saṃbandhena artha antara tvāt na ca saṃbandhi bhinna tvam sādhye viśeṣaṇam abhāva jñāna ādinā vyabhicārāt bādhaka abhāvasya ca viśeṣaṇa tvam hetau nirastam eva vinā api bhinna saṃbandham abhāva jñāna ādau iva viśiṣṭa dhī saṃbhavena aprayojaka tvāt ca viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣa rūpaḥ prakāra ādi kṛtaḥ vā viśeṣaḥ saṃbandha āviṣaya tve api tulyaḥ 
[032,vii]	syāt etat avayava guṇa kriyā jāti tadvatām iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iha paṭe śauklyam iha calanam paṭa tvam ca iti ihapratyayaḥ ādhāra ādheya saṃbandha nimittakaḥ yathārtheha pratyaya tvāt iha kuṇḍe badaram iti pratyaya vat iti ced na iha bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvaḥ jñānam ca ityādau vyabhicārāt bādhakam vinā iti asya nirasta tvāt tathā eva ādhāra ādheya bhāvāt eva upapatteḥ ca utpattaye sthitaye jñaptaye ca apekṣaṇīyasya ādhāra tvāt 
[032,viii]	anye tu śabda jāti rūpa ādiḥ indriya saṃbaddhaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt ghaṭa vat iti anumānāt saṃyoga bādhe indriya saṃbandha ghaṭaka tayā samavāya siddhiḥ indriyasya saṃbaddha grāhaka tvāt atas eva samāvāyaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ indriyeṇa asaṃbandhāt na ca saṃbandha tvena tad siddhiḥ anavasthānāt svabhāvāt eva jñāna vat sva saṃbaddha vyavahāra kāri tvāt ca samavāyaḥ hi saṃbandham vinā eva svabhāvāt eva kasyacid na ca jāti ādeḥ api svabhāvāt eva sva saṃbaddha vyavahāra kari tve samavāya vilopaḥ jāti ādeḥ indriya asaṃbandhe samavāyavat a pratyakṣa tva āpātāt iti 
[032,ix]	tat na samavāya svīkāre api svarūpa saṃbandhasya āvaśyaka tvāt ghaṭa jñānayoḥ bhū tala abhāvayoḥ iva vā dravyeṇa guṇa jāti ādibhiḥ svarūpam eva saṃbandhaḥ astu tathā ca śabdasya indriya viśeṣaṇa tayā śabda tvasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa tayā rūpa ādi jāti ādeḥ indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tayā rūpa tva ādeḥ indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa tayā svabhāva saṃbandha rūpayā grahaṇa saṃbhave kim samavāyena dravye svabhāva saṃbandhāt na indriyeṇa grahaṇam iti katham guṇa ādeḥ tena grahaḥ iti ced samavāyena api na dravya grahaṇam iti tulyam 
[032,x_032,xi]	apare tu ekatra ghaṭe āma pākadaśāyām krameṇa śyāma rakta rūpa upalambhaḥ asti sa ca na tad ubhaya nibandhanaḥ rūpasya nitya tvena ekadā upalambha āpatteḥ nitya tvāt eva ca na tayoḥ utpāda vināśau tasmāt tayoḥ saṃbandhasya tau syātām saḥ eva samavāyaḥ iti tat na śyāmam naṣṭam raktam utpannam iti ādya bādhitām ubhavāt samavāyasya utpāda vināśa anullekhāt ca tvad mate tasya atīndriya tvāt anyathā avayavi jñāna gandha rasa ādeḥ api nitya tvam samavāyasya utpāda vināśau iti kim na rocayet na hi utpāda vināśa pratītiḥ aprāmāṇikī bādhakam vinā iti 
[032,xii]	ucyate guṇa kriyā jāti viśiṣṭa buddhayaḥ viśeṣaṇa saṃbandha viṣayāḥ viśiṣṭa buddhi tvāt daṇḍī iti buddhi vat na ca vyabhicāraḥ abhāva ādi viśiṣṭa buddheḥ api svarūpa saṃbandha viṣaya tvāt na ca evam atra api tena eva artha antaram yatas guṇa kriyā jāti viśiṣṭa buddhīnām pakṣa dharma tā balena viṣayaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sidhyan lāghavāt ekaḥ eva sidhyati saḥ eva samavāyaḥ na tu svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ tad tad svarūpāṇām ananta tvāt saṃbandha tvena akḷpta tvāt ca 
[032,xiii]	athavā viśeṣaṇa saṃbandha nimittikāḥ iti sādhyam hetau tu satya tvam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇa saṃbandhaḥ ca kāraṇa tvena ekaḥ eva sidhyati lāghavāt anugata kāryasya anugata kāraṇa niyamya tvāt ca na tu svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ teṣām ananugata tvāt ananta tvāt ca na ca ubhayam api aprayojakam viśiṣṭa sākṣātkārasya saṃbandha aviṣaya tve tad ajanya tve vā gavāśvādau api viśiṣṭa buddhi prasaṅgāt 
[032,xiv]	navyāḥ tu guṇa kriyā jāti viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ saṃbandhi bhinna viśeṣaṇa saṃbandha viṣayāḥ nirviṣayaka bhāva viśeṣaṇaka viśiṣṭa buddhi tvāt itara nirūpaṇa anirūpya viśeṣaṇaka viśiṣṭa buddhi tvāt vā atas abhāva ādi viśiṣṭa budvau na vyabhicāraḥ na ca aprayojakam nirupādhi saṃbandha śāli tvāt saṃbandhaḥ ca aviśiṣṭa vyāvṛtta viśiṣṭa dhī niyāmakaḥ 
[033,i]	yat vā indriya pratyāsatti tvena samavāya siddhiḥ tathā hi guṇa kriyā jāti sākṣātkāraḥ indriya saṃbandha sādhyaḥ janya pratyakṣa tvāt daṇḍi jñāna vat iti atas sākṣāt saṃbandha bādha kāraṇa tvena indriya saṃyukte saṃbandhaḥ sidhyan pakṣa dharma tā balāt lāghavena anugataḥ samavāyaḥ ekaḥ eva sidhyati anugata kāryasya anugata kāraṇa janya tvāt na tu saṃyukta viśeṣaṇa tā rūpa svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ tasya ca tad tad rūpa ādi rūpa tvena ananugata tvāt 
[033,ii_033,iv]	evam rūpa tva rasa tva sākṣātkāre api kāraṇa tvena indriya saṃbandhaḥ samavāyaḥ eva anugataḥ sidhyati lāghavāt na tu indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā tasyāḥ rūpa tva ādi svarūpa tvena ananugata tvāt atas eva saṃyogaḥ viśeṣaṇa tā ca pratyāsattiḥ astu na tu samavāya ādi catuṣṭayam iti nirastam tasyāḥ tad tad svarūpa tvena ananugata tvāt pratyāsatti tvena abhyupagate ca samavāye pratyakṣatā saṃbandhi dvaya pratyakṣa tvāt nanu evam abhāva viśiṣṭa pratyakṣe api viśiṣṭa buddhi tvāt saṃyoga samavāya bādhe anugatam vaiśiṣṭyam saṃbandhaḥ viṣayaḥ nimittam ca bhavet iti ced 
[033,v]	na tasya hi samavāyavat eka tve ghaṭa abhāvavati paṭavati paṭa abhāva dhī prasaṅgaḥ ghaṭa abhāva vaiśiṣṭyam eva hi paṭa abhāva vaiśiṣṭyam paṭa ābhā vaiśiṣṭi a sattve api paṭa abhāvaḥ na asti tatas tasya bhinna tvāt iti ced na paṭa abhāva abhāvasya abhāva tve saḥ api vaiśiṣṭyena sambandhena tatra asti vaiśiṣṭyasya eka tvāt vaiśiṣṭa casya eka tvāt paṭa abhāva abhāvasya bhāva tve ca paṭaḥ eva pratibandhakaḥ vācyaḥ evam paṭa abhāvaḥ paṭa abhāva dhī hetuḥ syāt vaiśiṣṭyena saṃbandhena tatra asti eva 
[033,vi]	vaiśiṣṭyasya pratyabhāva vyakti nānātve ca abhāva viśiṣṭa buddhau na ekaḥ saṃbandhaḥ kāraṇam viṣayaḥ vā iti tad abhāva pratyakṣe ananugatam eva vaiśiṣṭyam viṣayaḥ kāraṇam ca vācyam tathā ca ananugata tad tad svarūpa rūpāḥ viśeṣaṇa tā eva astu kḷpta tvāt kim ananta vaiśiṣṭyena samavāyasya vaiśiṣṭyasya ca pratyakṣa tve tvayā api indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇatā svīkārāt 
[033,vii_033,viii]	nanu samavāyasya ekatve katham rūpinī rūpa vyavasthā ghaṭena saha rūpa saṃbandha rūpa tvam samavāyasya na vāyunā iti ced na rūpa saṃbandha rūpa tvam samavāyasya svarūpam eva yadi tadā rasa saṃbandha rūpa tvam na syāt tayoḥ virodhāt anyat ca durvacam iti ced ucyate vāyau rūpa samavāya sattve api rūpa atyanta abhāvaḥ asti na ghaṭe katham evam adhikaraṇa svabhāvāt abādhita rūpinī rūpa pratīteḥ ca 
[033,ix]	nanu evam jñātaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti pratīteḥ jñāta tā api syāt vartamāne bādhaka abhāvāt atīta anāgatayoḥ ca tat dhīḥ bhrāntā iti ced na atīta anāgatayoḥ jñāta tāyāḥ abhāve vyavahāra abhāva āpatteḥ tasya jñāta tā asādhya tvāt na ca jñāta tā jñānam eva vyavahāra hetuḥ gauravāt atīta ādau jñāna tad viṣayau eva jñāta tā adhī gocarau iti ced tarhi vartamāne tau eva tad viṣayau na hi atīta vartamānayoḥ jñāta tā pratītyoḥ viṣaya vailakṣaṇyam īkṣāmahe 
[033,x]	nanu rūpa ghaṭayoḥ na samavāyaḥ kim tu abhedaḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti atra daṇḍi puruṣayoḥ iva nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti atra api nīla ghaṭayoḥ abadhita abheda anubhavāt nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti buddhyoḥ viśeṣaṇa sambandha mātra gocara tve nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti vat daṇḍaḥ puruṣaḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti vat nīlī ghaṭaḥ iti api syāt tasmāt ekatra abhedaḥ viṣayaḥ aparatra viśeṣaṇa saṃbandhaḥ viṣayeṇa eva dhiyām viśeṣāt 
[033,xi]	athavā viśeṣaṇa tā viśeṣya tāvacchedakayoḥ nīla tva ghaṭa tvayoḥ eka vṛtti tvam jñāyate daṇḍitva puruṣa tvayoḥ iva puruṣe evam nīla ghaṭa padayoḥ śābdam api sāmānādhikaraṇyam yujyate nīlatva ghaṭa tvābhyām bhinna pravṛtti nimittābhyām tayoḥ eka pravṛtteḥ na ca matupaḥ lopāt abheda upacārāt vā nīla padam nīla vat param iti vācyam na hi prayogam sādhakam brūmaḥ kiṃtu nīla ghaṭayoḥ abheda pratītim pade api na upacāra ādi kalpanā gauravāt mukhye bādhaka abhāvāt ca iti 
[033,xii]	ucyate śukla paṭa śabdayoḥ eka artha tve ghaṭaḥ kumbhaḥ iti vat śuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti saha prayogaḥ na syāt andhasya paṭa graha vat rūpa grahaḥ rūpa agraha vat paṭa agrahaḥ api vā syāt mahārajata rakte paṭa graha vat śukla grahaḥ śukla agraha vat paṭa agrahaḥ api bhavet paṭamānayā iti ukte yam kaṃcid śuklam ānayet apaṭaḥ paṭaḥ iti vat aśuklaḥ paṭaḥ iti virudhyeta paṭa śuklayoḥ abhedāt agri saṃyogāt ekatra śyāma raktayoḥ vināśa utpāde ghaṭasya tau syātām ghaṭa sattve vā tayoḥ api na syātām 
[033,xiii]	atha śukla tva ādīnām dravya bhedāt tad bodha artham saha prayogaḥ andha ādinā śukla ādi grahe śukla tva ādīnām agrahaḥ upapadyate śukla tva ādi jāteḥ ca dravyeṇa abhedaḥ na samavāyaḥ kiṃtu svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ iti ced na śukla tva madhura tva surabhi tva uṣṇa tva ādīnām dravya vṛtti tve dravya grāhaka tvac ādibhiḥ grahaṇa prasaṅgāt rūpa tva ādīnām dravya vṛtti tve pratiniyata indriya grāhya tā eva na syāt yogya vṛtti tvena jāteḥ grahaṇa yogya tvāt tad tad jāti tvena yogyatve ananugamāt tasmāt rūpa tva ādīnām pratiniyata indriya grāhya tā api guṇa guṇi bhede mānam abhede ca katham paṭasya śuklam rūpam iti bheda buddhiḥ paṭaḥ nīlim eti buddhi prasaṅgaḥ ca 
[033,xiv]	nanu ekānta abhede sarvam idam dūṣaṇam vayam tu bheda abheda vādinaḥ tathā ca bhedam ādāya apaunaruktyādi bheda abhede ca uktam eva pramāṇam pratyakṣam atha vā ubhaya siddha bhede sāmānādhikaraṇya dhīra bhede pramāṇam yat vā atyantam abhede bhede ca na sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti tatas eva bheda abheda siddhiḥ na ca bheda abhedayoḥ paraspara viraha rūpa tayā viruddhayoḥ katham ekatra samāveśaḥ iti vācyam saṃyoga tad abhāvayoḥ iva avirodhāt pāka anantaram raktaḥ ayam na śyāmaḥ iti abādhita anubhava balāt tatra eva tad anyonya abhāva siddheḥ tvayā api bheda abheda svīkārāt anyonya abhāva tvam avyāpya vṛtti nitya abhāvavat vṛtti abhāva tva sākṣāt vyāpya dharma tvāt atyanta abhāva tva vat nitya iti vā na viśeṣaṇam avyāpya vṛtti pratiyogika prāc abhāva pradhvaṃsayoḥ avyāpya vṛtti tvāt iti atas api bheda abheda siddhiḥ 
[034,i]	ucyate tasya eva tatra abhāvaḥ avaccheda bhedena vartate jñāyate ca yathā saṃyoga ādi a bhāvaḥ śyāmā avacchinnasya tasya eva anyonya abhāvaḥ tatra eva rakta avacchinne tad anyonya abhāva abhāvaḥ ca śyāmā avacchedena tat iha api nīlasya anyonya abhāvaḥ ghaṭa tva avacchedena iti nīlāt ghaṭasya bhedaḥ astu abhedaḥ tu nīla anyonya abhāva abhāva rūpaḥ na ghaṭe ghaṭa tva avacchedena eva virodhāt eka avacchedena bhāva abhāvayoḥ ekatra āvṛtteḥ ajñānāt ca na api avacchedaka antareṇa ghaṭa tva avacchinne ghaṭe tad abhāvāt tad ajñāne api nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti anubhavāt ca na ca anyonya abhāva rūpaḥ bhedaḥ astu abhedaḥ tu na bheda abhāvaḥ kim tu anyaḥ eva iti vācyam abheda vyavahāre tasya ahetu tvāt tasmāt nīlaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti atra nīla saṃbandhaḥ eva bhāsate tathā sati nīlī ghaṭaḥ iti dhīḥ syāt iti uktam iti ced nīlī ghaṭaḥ iti atra buddhau yadi saṃbandha viṣaya tvam āpādyate tat iṣyate eva matupaḥ lopāt abheda upacārāt vā nīla padam eva nīla vat param iti 
[034,ii]	nanu śabda rūpa ādiṣu viśeṣaṇa tā indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā vā grāhikāḥ tu kim samavāya ādinā atha viśeṣaṇa tāyām samavāyaḥ indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tāyām ca saṃyukta samavāya ādiḥ upajīvyaḥ taiḥ vinā tayoḥ abhāvāt iti ced viśeṣaṇa tā svarūpe teṣām upajīvya tvam na tu tasyāḥ pratyāsatti tve api taiḥ vinā api samavāya abhāvayoḥ viśeṣaṇa tā sattvāt 
[034,iii_034,iv]	saṃyukta samavāya ādiḥ api tatra asti iti ced āstām na tu pratyāsattiḥ kim tu viśeṣaṇa tā eva kḷpta tvāt saṃyukta samavāya ādikam vinā viśeṣaṇa tā rūpa ādau na jñāyate ced mā jñāyi na hi sā pratyāsattiḥ jñātā api tu svarūpa satī mā evam śabda ādīnām sākṣātkāra viṣaya tvena indriya saṃbandha anumitau śabda ādau samavāya ādikam jñātvā eva viśeṣaṇa tā grahaḥ iti avaśyam prathama upasthita tvāt samavāya ādiḥ eva viṣayaḥ na viśeṣaṇa tā carama upasthita tvāt 
[034,v]	nanu abhāva grahe na indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā pratyāsattiḥ cakṣuṣā saṃyukte paramāṇu ādau yogyasya jala tva ādeḥ abhāva graha prasaṅgāt kim tu sva grāhya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā mahati vāyau udbhūta rūpa abhāvasya kusume saurabha abhāvasya guḍe tikta tva abhāvasya vā na cakṣuḥ ādinā grahaḥ api tu yogyā anupalabdhyā saḥ anumīyate indriya viśeṣaṇa tā api na pratyāsattiḥ cakṣuḥ ādinā sva viśeṣaṇa jala tva ādi abhāva graha prasaṅgāt yadi śabda abhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ tadā pratyāsatti antaram kalpyam tad abhāve pratyakṣaḥ eva na bhavati iti ced 
[034,vi]	mā evam lāghavāt indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā eva pratyāsattiḥ na ca evam paramāṇau jala tva ādi abhāva graha prasaṅgaḥ yatra hi yat sattvam anupalabdhi virodhi tatra tasya abhāvaḥ indriya saṃnikarṣeṇa gṛhyate na ca paramāṇu ādau jala tva ādi sattvam anupalabdhi virodhi yogya saṃyukta samavāya abhāvena pṛthivī tva vat anupabdhi saṃbhavāt mahati vāyu ādau udbhūta rūpa ādi abhāvaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi grāhyaḥ eva tatra udbhūta rūpa ādi sattve anupalabdhi anupapatteḥ atas eva stambhe piśāca tādātmya abhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ stambha tādātmye ca tasya stambhasya iva anupalambha asaṃbhavāt evam śabdasya api abhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ tadā tatra śabda sattvasya anupalabdhi virodhi tvāt iti tatra indriya viśeṣaṇa tā eva pratyāsattiḥ cakṣuṣi jala tva ādi sattvam ca na anupalabdhi virodhī iti cakṣuṣā na tad grahaḥ 
[034,vii]	nanu abhāve na viśeṣaṇa tā pratyāsattiḥ kim tu samavāyaḥ eva samavāya sādhaka viśiṣṭa pratīteḥ aviśeṣāt na ca samaveta tve tasya bhāva tva āpattiḥ bhāvasya tattve abhāva tva āpattiḥ iti vaiparītyasaṃbhavāt rūpa ādau pratyāsatti tvena samavāya kalpanam abhāve api tulyam viśeṣaṇa tā api tulyā prāc abhāva pradhvaṃsau pratiyogi āśraye samavetau pratiyogi āśraya nāśa janya dhvaṃsaḥ deśe samaye vā samavaiti tatra eva nirūpaṇāt na ca samavāyi nāśe dhvaṃsa nāśaḥ ghaṭa unmajjana prasaṅgāt bhāva tvasya upādhi tvāt ca anyathā tava api tasya janya tvena nāśāpattiḥ 
[034,viii]	atha evam anyonya atyanta abhāvayoḥ nitya tve aneka samaveta tve ca jāti tva prasaṅgaḥ na ca tatra bhāva tvam tantram gauravāt na ca abhāvānām viśiṣṭa pratītau viśeṣaḥ yena atra samavāya parityāgaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa tva abhāva ādeḥ jāti tve sattva dravya tva pṛthivī tva ādinā para apara bhāva anupapatteḥ teṣām vyāpya tve ghaṭe tad abhāva prasaṅgaḥ vyāpaka tve sāmānya ādau ghaṭa tva abhāvaḥ na syāt iti 
[034,ix]	ucyate samaveta tve dhvaṃsasya samavāyi kāraṇa nāśāt nāśaḥ syāt na ca nāśya tve bhāva tvam tantram gauravāt prāgabhāve abhāvāt ca asamaveta tve tad dhvaṃsasya janya tve api na nāśaḥ āśraya nāśa ādeḥ abhāvāt ghaṭa unmajjana āpatteḥ na naśyati iti ced na na hi prayojana kṣati bhayena sāmagrī na kāryam arjayati tasmāt unmajjana abhāva nirvāhaka dhvaṃsasya asamaveta tvam kalpyatām samavāyi nāśāt dhvaṃsa paraṃparākalpane ca ghaṭakapāla ādeḥ āparamāṇu nāśe ghaṭa ādi tad dhvaṃsa virādhī caramaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ paramāṇu vṛttiḥ syāt tathā ca na pratyakṣaḥ ghaṭa dhvaṃsasya kapāla samaveta tve ca na bhū tale nirūpaṇam syāt ubhaya vṛtti tve ca vyāsa jya vṛtti tvena kapālam vinā na nirūpyeta 
[034,x]	nanu abhāva grahaḥ na indriyāt kim tu yogyā anupalabdheḥ tad upalambhe tad abhāva āgrahāt na ca evam bhāva buddhiḥ api abhāvānupalabdheḥ eva na indriyāt iti vācyam bhāva grahe indriya anuvidhānāt anyathā nimīlita akṣasya api ghaṭa abhāva anupalabdhyā ghaṭa graha prasaṅgaḥ atas eva bhāva grahe abhāva anupalabdhiḥ pṛṣṭha lagnā api na hetuḥ indriyeṇa anyathā siddha tvāt na hi indriya artha saṃnikarṣe sati tām vinā bhāva dhī vilambaḥ abhāva grahe api indriyam hetuḥ tad anuvidhānāt iti ced na abhāvena cakṣuḥ ādeḥ prāpti abhāvena āśraya grahe tad upakṣayāt 
[034,xi_035,ii]	atha adhikaraṇa dhīḥ indriya vyāpāraḥ na ca tayā tad anyathā asidvam anyathā saṃnikarṣa upakṣīṇa tayā indriyam na hetuḥ syāt iti ced na hetu tve siddhe tad vyāpāra tvam tat eva na asti prāpti abhāvāt etena adhikaraṇa graha indriyayoḥ pṛthak anvaya vyatireka grahāt daṇḍa cakrayoḥ iva hetu tvam dvayoḥ iti nirastam prāpti abhāvena abhāva āgrāhaka tvāt na ca indriyam prāpta viśeṣaṇam aprāptam api gṛhṇāti saṃyukta samavāya ādi uccheda prasaṅgāt prāpta caitra gata aprāpta daṇḍasya api graha prasaṅgāt indriyasya prāpta grāhaka tvāt ca na ca viśeṣaṇa tā prāptiḥ anyatra tad akalpanāt na ca samavāye tad kalpanam tasya anabhyupagamāt tatas eva atīndriya tvāt vā atha abhāvasya indriya grāhya tvena saṃyoga ādi bādhe iha eva sā kalpyate rūpa ādau tad bādhe saṃyukta samavāya ādiḥ iva iti ced 
[035,iii]	tatra anupakṣīṇa indriya anuvidhānāt tathā eva iha sva āśraya grahaḥ eva tad upakṣīṇam lāghavāt na tu prāpti antara kalpanā gauravāt anyathā tvac anu vidhānāt rūpam vinā api vā ayudhīḥ pratyakṣā iti na sā sparśa liṅga grahe upakṣīyeta kim ca viśeṣaṇa tāyām indriya grāhya tvam tena sā iti anyonya āśraya tvam api ca viśeṣaṇa tā grāhya svarūpam eva na ca tvac ādau svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ hetuḥ kim tu yathāyatham saṃyoga samāvāyau na ca tayoḥ anyonya vyabhicārāt indriyam saṃbaddham gṛhṇāti iti eva vyāptiḥ iti vācyam dṛṣṭānte hi saṃbandhi gataḥ saṃbandhaḥ hetuḥ gṛhītaḥ cakṣuṣi anyatra api tathā na tu grāhya svarūpam saṃbandhasya saṃbandhi bhinna tva niyamāt na hi saḥ eva tat vān tena eva bhavati svarūpa saṃbandhasya hetu tve ca rūpa ādi grahaḥ api tatas eva astu kim samavāya ādinā atas saṃyoga viśeṣaṇate eva pratyāsattī iti ṣoḍhā kīrtanam api viphalam 
[035,iv]	etena āloka apekṣaṇe cakṣuḥ apekṣā tasya tad eka sahakāri tvāt iti nirastam prāptim vinā cakṣuṣaḥ ahetutvāt ālokasya ca pratiyogi grāhaka tvena yogyatā ghaṭaka tayā abhāva grāhaka tvāt na ca evam pratiyogi upalambhaka tvena cakṣuḥ api hetuḥ evam hi tat tat vyāpya itara tad ulambhaka sākalye anupalabdhiḥ grāhikā bhavati iti vācyam prāptim vinā tasya ahetutvena āśraya graha upakṣayāt 
[035,v]	nanu evam andhasya tvac indriya upanīte nīle smṛta pītasya anupalabdhyā abhāva graha prasaṅgaḥ pratiyogi grāhaka indriya grāhya tve tu abhāvasya na ayam doṣaḥ andhasya cakṣuḥ abhāvāt iti ced na abhāva grāhaka tvena abhimatam indriyam āśraya graha upakṣīṇam tathā ca pratiyogi grāhaka indriyeṇa āśraya grahe anupalabdhyā abhāva grahāt anyathā cakṣussaṃyukte paramāṇau jala tva abhāva graha prasaṅgaḥ 
[035,vi]	atha evam vāyau rūpa abhāvaḥ jale tikta abhāvaḥ pāṣāṇe saurabha abhāvaḥ ca na gṛhyeta vāyu ādīnām pratiyogi grāhakaiḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ agrahāt na ca tava api te abhāvāḥ katham pratyakṣāḥ vāyu ādīnām tad indriya ayogya tvāt iti vācyam liṅgena tvac ādinā vā upanīte vāyu ādau yogya rūpa ādi abhāva viśeṣyakam pratyakṣam cakṣuḥ ādinā eva na vāyu ādi viśeṣyakam pratyakṣe yogya viśeṣyasya hetu tvāt iti ced na vāyu ādau rūpa ādi abhāva pratītanām anupalabdhi liṅgaka tvāt tava nīrūpaḥ vāyuḥ iti vāyu viśeṣya abhāva pratīti vat 
[035,vii]	atha bhū tale abhāva dhīḥ indriya janyā sākṣātkāri tvāt tatas eva viśeṣaṇa tā kalpanam api na ca sākṣātkāri tvam asiddham parokṣa tve ajñāta karaṇaka tva anupapatteḥ tathā hi mandira udare caitraḥ nipuṇam anusṛtaḥ api na ca upalabdhaḥ iti āpta vākya avagata anupalabdhyā śrotā anum inoti na āsīt tatra caitraḥ iti evam abhāvadhīḥ parokṣā ced tadā na ajñāta karaṇikā parokṣatva ajāteḥ jñāta karaṇa prayojya tvāt jñāta karaṇa tvam ca jñāna karaṇa tvam liṅga ādeḥ ajanaka tvāt tasmāt sākṣātkāri tvam ajñāta karaṇa tvāt na ca indriya janya tvam upādhiḥ tatas eva tad sādhanāt iti ced 
[035,viii]	mā evam parokṣa tvam hi na jātiḥ anubhava tvena saṃkara prasaṅgāt kim tu sākṣātkāri bhinna jñāna tvam evam ca abhāva jñānam parokṣam eva smṛti vat yathā ca jñāta karaṇa tve api śābda ādiḥ na anumitiḥ evam ajñāta karaṇa tve api indriya janyam sākṣātkārī anupalabdhi janyam tat vijātīyam anupalabdham yadi ca ajñāta karaṇa tvena sākṣātkāri tvam tadā jñāta karaṇa tvena śābda ādeḥ anumiti tva āpattiḥ jñāta karaṇa tve api liṅga ādi karaṇa bhedāt anumiti ādi phala bhedaḥ iti ced ajñāta anupalabdhi indriya karaṇa bhedāt phala bhedaḥ iha api evam ca sākṣātkāri tve indriya janya tvam parokṣa tve ca tad ajanya tvam prayojakam na tu jñāta ajñāta karaṇa janya tvam gauravāt smṛtau abhāvāt ca 
[035,ix]	nanu anupalabdhiḥ na mānam bhāva bhūta māna saha kṛtasya eva manasaḥ bāhya anubhava janaka tvāt iti ced na bhāva tvasya guru tvena aprayojaka tvāt anyathā indriya saha kṛtasya eva manasaḥ bāhya anubhava janaka tvām iti anumāna ādi na mānam syāt na ca idam abhāva jñānam bhāva māna saha kṛta mana ssādhyam bāhya abhāva jñāna tvāt liṅga ādi janya abhāva jñāna vat iti vācyam ayam abhāvaḥ na indriya grāhyaḥ abhāva tvāt ayogya abhāva vat iyam abhāva buddhiḥ na indriya janyāḥ abhāva buddhi tvāt liṅga ādi janya abhāva buddhi vat iti sat pratipakṣāt 
[035,x]	atha pratiyogi grāhakam mānam tad abhāvam api gṛhṇāti yathā anumāna ādi pratiyogi grāhakam ca indriyam atas abhāva grāhakam iti ced na bhāva grāhakayoḥ eva liṅga śabdayoḥ tad abhāva āgrāhaka tvāt pratiyogi grāhaka jātīyam mānam tathā iti ced na upamāne vyabhicārāt na ca cakṣuṣṭvā ādi kama bhāva grāhaka vṛtti jāti tvāt upamāna tvam ca na jātiḥ iti vācyam prāptim vinā cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāva grāhaka tva sādhanāt 
[035,xi]	atha bhāva vṛtti abhāva bhramaḥ sa ca karaṇa doṣāt na ca pratiyogi smṛti āśraya grahānupalabdhayaḥ svarūpataḥ duṣṭāḥ kim tu indriyam pitta ādinā duṣṭam iti tat eva ca bhrama hetuḥ iti abhāva pramāyām api tat eva mānam iti ced na indriyasya api duṣṭa tvam doṣa sāhitya mātram na tu anyat tat ca anupalabdhau api tulyam na ca jñāta karaṇa ajanya bhrama tvena indriya janya tvam evam hi abhāva pramākaraṇa tvam api indriyasya tatas eva astu kim anayā kusṛṣṭyā evam astu iti ced na prāpti abhāvena ukta uttara tvāt kim ca asaṃnikṛṣṭe api doṣāt upanīte abhāve bhramaḥ indriyeṇa saṃbhavati cakṣuṣā pāṣāṇaḥ surabhiḥ iti bhrama vat abhāva pramā na saṃbhavati prāpti abhāvāt iti uktam 
[035,xii]	nanu adhikaraṇa abhāvayoḥ viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ asti sā na indriya janyāḥ abhāva buddhi tvāt na anupalabdhi janyāḥ bhāva buddhi tvāt na ubhaya janyāḥ jāti saṃkara prasaṅgāt atas ubhaya grāhakam indriyam abhyupeyam iti ced abhāvavat bhū talam iti anupalabdhi upanīta abhāva viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ indriyeṇa eva cakṣuṣā candanam surabhīti vat bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti ca cakṣuḥ upanīta bhūtale abhāva buddhiḥ anupalabdhyā eva ghrāṇena candane saurabham iti vat 
[036,i_036,ii]	yat tu vyāpāra abhāva at na anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam vyāpāravataḥ eva karaṇa tvāt iti tat na kriyayā ayoga vyavacchedena saṃbandhi karaṇam na tu vyāpāra vat iti api viśeṣaṇam gaura vat iti atra ucyate pratiyogi grāhaka indriyeṇa āśraya grahaḥ na hetuḥ prāk na astita agrahe tu vyabhicārāt vāyu ādau ca rūpa ādi abhāva dhīḥ indriya janyā eva na anupalabdhi liṅga janyā anupalabdheḥ ajñānāt āpta vākyasya iva tad jñāpakasya abhāvāt 
[036,iii]	atha ajñātā eva rūpa ādi upalambhasya anupalabdhiḥ rūpa ādi anupalabdhim gṛhṇāti bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvam iva iti ced tvad mate upalambhasya atīndriya tvena yogyā anupalabdhyā upalambha abhāvasya grahītum aśakyatvāt anupalabdhi mātrasya abhāva āgrāhaka tvāt astu tarhi jñānam yogyam iti ced na apasiddhāntāt yogya tve api bhū talīya ghaṭa abhāve api jñātā eva yogyā anupalabdhiḥ liṅgam astu yogya ghaṭa upalambhasya anupalabdhyā graha saṃbhavāt kṛtam anupalabdhyā māna antareṇa 
[036,iv]	ghaṭa abhāva dhīra jñāta karaṇikā liṅga ādi anusaṃndhānam vinā jāyamāna tvāt iti ced na vāyu ādau rūpa ādi abhāva pratītiḥ api tathā atha rūpa ādi mattayā jñāta tva abhāvaḥ tad anumita rūpa vattā anupalabdhiḥ vā liṅgam iti ced na vāyu ādau jñāta tva abhāvasya api rūpa ādi abhāva tulya tayā grahītum aśakyatvāt vāyu ādau tasya pratyakṣa tve rūpa ādi abhāvaḥ api tathā astu na api kāya vāc vyavahāra abhāvena anupalabdhiḥ anamīyate upekṣā jñāna mūka svapnayoḥ darśanena vyabhicārāt na ca vyavahāra abhāva mātram liṅgam kasyacid vyavahāra abhāvasya vyabhicārāt sarva vyavahāra abhāvasya grahītum aśakyatvāt 
[036,v]	kim ca ghaṭavat tayā jñāta tva abhāvena tad anumita anupalabdhyā vā liṅgena bhū tala ādau abhāva anumitiḥ astu kim māna antareṇa anupalabdhyā api ca pratiyogi grāhaka indriya janyam adhikaraṇa jñānam anupalabdhi sahakāri tadā syāt yadi tena vinā sā na abhāvam bodhayet na ca etat dṛṣṭam vāyu ādau rūpa ādi abhāve tathā dṛṣṭam iti ced na asiddheḥ na ca vyāpti balāt sahakāri tvam evam hi vāyu ādau rūpa ādi abhāva pratyayaḥ anupalabdheḥ bhavan tādṛśa āśrayam ākṣipet anākṣepe vai anupalabdheḥ nabhavet tatas na bhavati kim tu liṅgāt iti ced liṅgam api sā eva tat ca dūṣitam eva 
[036,vi_036,vii]	kim ca na anupalabdhiḥ liṅgam tatas hi nīrūpaḥ vāyuḥ iti anumitiḥ syāt na tu vāyau rūpa abhāvaḥ iti api ca ghaṭavatī upalambha prāk kāle anupalabdhyā ghaṭa smṛtimataḥ kutas nābhauva dhīḥ ghaṭa abhāva abhāvāt iti ced tarhi abhāva rūpa artha janyā bhāva buddhiḥ artha janya tvena sākṣātkāriṇī indriya janyā ca syāt tadā ghaṭaḥ eva pratibandhakaḥ iti ced tathā api tad abhāvaḥ abhāva buddhau janakaḥ eva syāt 
[036,viii_036,ix]	syāt etat gṛham upalabhya nirgataḥ caitraḥ yatra kenacid pṛṣṭaḥ tatra maitraḥ āsīt iti sa ca kṣaṇam dhyātvā anupalabdhyā tatra maitra abhāvam avagamya āha na āsīt tatra maitraḥ iti sā iyam prāṅna āstitādhīḥ na smṛtiḥ purā gehe anubhūyamāne maitra asmaraṇena tad abhāvān anubhavāt evam ca tatra eva indriya vyāpāram vinā eva anupalabdhyā abhāva anubhavāt anyatra api sā eva hetuḥ kḷpta tvāt tat āhuḥ sva rūpa mātram dṛṣṭam hi veśma ādi artham smaran atha tatra anyena astitām pṛṣṭaḥ tadā eva pratipadyate iti 
[036,x_036,xi]	mā evam prāṅānāstitāyām hi na tāvat ajñāta anupalabdhiḥ bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvasya iva abhāva grāhikā tadānīm gehasya viprakṛṣṭa tvena yogyā anupalabdheḥ abhāvāt na api jñātā anavasthā prasaṅgāt anupalabdheḥ api abhāva rūpa tayā anupalabdhi antareṇa grāhya tvāt upalambhasya anupalabdhiḥ ajñātā eva svarūpa satī maitra anupalabdhim gṛhṇāti ced tu ad naye upalambhasya atīndriya tvena tad abhāvasya yogyā anupalabdhi agrāhya tvāt atha gehasya yogya maitravat tayā smaraṇa arhasya smaraṇa abhāvaḥ tatra ajñātaḥ eva gehe maitra abhāva grāhakaḥ iti ced na svarūpa satas smaraṇa abhāvasya grāhaka tve tasmin satyabhāva saṃśaya viparyaya abhāva prasaṅgāt bhavati ca kadācid tatra āsīt iti viparyayaḥ tatra āsīt na vā iti saṃśayaḥ ca 
[036,xii]	atha doṣāt saṃśaya viparyayau na ca asādhāraṇam pramākaraṇam dūṣayantaḥ eva doṣāḥ saṃśaya ādi hetavaḥ bhavanti na ca atra svarasa siddhasya yogyā smaraṇasya kiṃcid dūṣitam iti vācyam doṣa sāhityam eva hi karaṇānām duṣṭa tā na hi dūra tva ādinā cakṣuṣaḥ kiṃcid apakriyate kim tu maṇyādeḥ dāhaḥ iva svarūpa satām eva pratibandhaka tvam iti ced na ajñātāt yogyā smaraṇāt tatra abhāva dhīritya siddheḥ kim tu manasā jñātāt yogya asmaraṇāt liṅgāt pramāṇa tvena kḷptāt tatra abhāva prati iti upapattau na anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇa antaram kalpyate 
[036,xiii]	yogya smaraṇa abhāvaḥ na manaḥ grāhyaḥ pratyāsatti abhāvāt jñānasya ayogya tvāt vā iti ced na vāyu ādau rūpa ādi abhāva pratīteḥ alaiṅgika tvena indriya anuvidhānena tad janya tve siddhe indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tāyāḥ pratyāsatti tva kalpanāt tat jñānam pratyakṣam jānāmi iti anubhavasya liṅga ādi ajanya tvāt na ca jñāta tā liṅgam nirākṛta tvāt tava api katham abhāve saṃśaya viparyayau iti ced na liṅga saṃśaya viparyayābhyām laiṅgika saṃśaya viparyaya darśanāt
