[037,i_037,ii]	yadā tu su nipuṇena eka jñāna viṣaya tā yogyasya maitrasya anubhave sati smaraṇa arhasya asmaraṇam avadhāryate tadā anumitiḥ pramā atas eva asmaraṇa mātrasya vyabhicāram upalabhya tat upekṣya viśiṣṭa asmaraṇam jñātu kāmasya praṇidhānam upayujyate anyathā dhyānam anupapannam svarūpa satas eva asmaraṇasya abhāva grāhaka tvāt tasmāt yogyā smaraṇam liṅga tvena eva upayujyate prayogaḥ tu tad geham tadā maitra abhāva vat tad tulya parimāṇa ādi yogi tayā smaraṇe api tadvat tayā asmaryamāṇa tvāt yat evam tat evam yathā ghaṭa abhāvavat bhū talam iti 
[037,iii_037,iv]	atha abhāvaḥ bhāva ātmā eva tatas tatra saṃyoga ādiḥ eva grāhakaḥ iti na tatra viśeṣaṇa tā pratyāsattiḥ tatra prāñcaḥ asti tāvat iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti abādhitā buddhiḥ sā ca iyam na bhū tala ālambanā ghaṭavatī api prasaṅgāt na api kevala tad ālambanā atirikta kaivalya anabhyupagamāt bhū talam eva kaivalyam iti ced tarhi paunaruktyam adhikam abhede ādhāra ādheya bhāva anupapattiḥ ca 
[037,v]	atha adhika abhāva vādinā api abhāvaḥ sa āśrayaḥ vācyaḥ deśa ādi niyamena vyavahārāt tathā ca asti bhū tale viśeṣaḥ yaḥ abhāva āśrayaḥ sa na bhū tala mātram ghaṭavatī api prasaṅgāt na abhauva yuktam anyonya āśrayāt na ca ghaṭa vat virodhāt iti ced na viśeṣasya eva abhāva āśraya tvāt sa ca ananugataḥ eva eka āśrayatā tu ananugatasya api ghaṭa āśrayatā iva bhavati 
[037,vi]	kim ca kutra abhāvaḥ iti yatra pratīyeta iti eva uttaram kva pratīyeta iti atra yatra asti iti eva anyathā go tva ādikam api na svīkriyeta tad āśraya viśeṣāt eva vyavahāra saṃbhavāt tathā api kīdṛśi bhū tale abhāvaḥ iti ced abhāva pūrva samaye kīdṛśam bhū talam iti praśne ghaṭa vat iti uttaram abhāva samaye abhāva vat iti madhya samayaḥ tu na asti eva iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti ādhāra ādheya bhāva pratīteḥ ca abhāva ādhāra tvam bhū talasya na pratīyate kiṃtu tanmātra buddhi viṣaya tvam iti ced aho vyākhyā kauśalam anubhavaḥ api vyākhyāya kathyate tanmātra padārtha anirvacanam ca na hi bhū tala baddhiḥ tanmātra buddhiḥ ghaṭa vat bhū tala buddheḥ api bhū tala buddhi tvāt sā buddhiḥ na bhū talasya kiṃtu ghaṭa bhū talayoḥ agnīṣomayoḥ iva devatā tvam iti ced na tatas bhū tala avi avahāra prasaṅgāt bhū talasya aviṣaya tvāt āśubhā vibhū tala viṣaya ka jñāna antarāt iti ced tarhi sā eva bhū tala buddhiḥ tanmātra budviḥ iti tad deśe ghaṭa abhāvasya vyavahāra prasaṅgaḥ 
[037,vii]	etena bhū tala indriya saṃnikarṣa jaghaṭa vat bhū tala indriya saṃnikarṣa ja jñānayoḥ viśeṣaḥ aṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ sāmagrī bhedasya kārya bheda niyata tvāt tathā ca saḥ eva tanmātra padārthaḥ iti nirastam tatas api bhū tala vyavahārāt pratiyogi tad vyāpya itara janitā bhū tala buddhiḥ abhāvaḥ iti ced na ghaṭavati tad janitāyāḥ api itara janita tvāt tanmātra janitā sā iti ced na mātrā arthasya abhāva tvāt tasya ca aparijñānāt ghaṭāviṣayā satī bhū tala viṣaya iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt 
[037,viii_037,ix]	kiṃca pratiyogi nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇaḥ abhāvaḥ buddhiḥ tu na tathā pratiyogi prakāśam vinā api buddhi nirūpaṇāt vyavahāra artham dṛśya pratiyogi jñāna apekṣāḥ abhāvaḥ jñātaḥ eva iti ced na vyavahārasya vyavahartavya upalambha nibandhana tvena tathā adṛṣṭa cara tvāt yadi ca pratiyogi smaraṇa sāpekṣā tanmātra dhīra bhāva padārthaḥ tadā andhakāra ādau yā tanmātra dhīḥ sā abhāvaḥ na syāt tathā ca tatra vicaran kaṇṭakaiḥ vidhyeta kaṇṭaka smaraṇam vinā kaṇṭaka abhāva abhāvāt nirjane bandha vicchede api jala nissaraṇam na syāt tadānīm tanmātra buddheḥ sarvathā abhāvāt 
[037,x_037,xii]	kim ca tanmātra dhī nāśe ghaṭa unmajjana prasaṅgaḥ ghaṭa abhāva abhāvasya ghaṭa tvāt yadi ca abhāvaḥ na atiriktaḥ tadā yatra ghaṭa saṃsṛṣṭa tva buddhiḥ āsīt kutas tatra tanmātra dhīḥ mudgara pāta janyā atirikta viṣaya anaṅgīkārāt atirikta abhāve kim mānam iti ced na asti iti buddhiḥ eva nanu abhāva vyavahāra anupapattiḥ anyonya āśrayāt iti atra prābhākarāḥ ghaṭa vat bhū tala buddhi bhinnā bhū tala buddhiḥ abhāva vyavahāra kāraṇam na ca doṣāt ghaṭavati ghaṭavat tva ajñāne bhū tala jñānam abhāvaḥ syāt iti vācyam ghaṭavataḥ bhū talasya jñānāt bhinnasya bhū tala jñānasya abhāva tvāt tad bhramāt ca abhāva bhramaḥ 
[037,xiii]	vastutas atyanta abhāve pratiyogim ad adhikaraṇa jñānasya aprasiddheḥ pratiyogi mat jñāna bhinnam adhikaraṇa jñānam vyadhikaraṇa abhāva vyavahāre kāraṇam samāna adhikaraṇa niṣedha pratītiḥ ca pratiyogi adhikaraṇayoḥ svarūpa bhedam ālambate tena ghaṭavat tvena jñāyamāne api bhū tale bhū talam ghaṭaḥ na iti pratītiḥ tathā ca yasya abhāva jñāna kāraṇa tvam pareṣām tat eva abhāva vyavahṛti kāraṇam astu na hi adhikaraṇa buddhim vinā tad buddhiḥ na ca bhū tala buddhiḥ tathā ghaṭavatī api prasaṅgāt na ca abhāva adhikaraṇa bhū tala viṣaya tvāt buddheḥ viśeṣaḥ pratiyogi sattve api prāk nā āsīt idam atra iti pratīteḥ 
[037,xiv_038,i]	kim ca jñāna viṣaya bhū talasya abhāvaḥ yadi viśeṣaṇam tadā abhāva jñānam eva tat jñāna kāraṇam upalakṣaṇam ced na kaścid viśeṣaḥ pratiyegi mattayā anupalabdhiḥ api kāraṇam iti ced na pratiyogi mattayā upalambhe api prāk nā āsīt idam atra iti pratīteḥ buddhyoḥ ca viśeṣaḥ sva rūpa viśeṣau eva na anyonya abhāvaḥ anavasthānāt ātma āśrayāt vā bhū tala jñāna apekṣayā ghaṭa vat bhū tala jñāna tvam eva vā vaidharmya bhedaḥ na ca atirikta abhāva pakṣe api anyonya abhāve atyanta abhāve ca nitye mānam asti pratiyogini buddhi sthe adhikaraṇa svarūpasya eva anati prasañjaka tvāt na hi tatra adhikaraṇasya pratiyogi tādātmyam pratiyogimat tvam vā saṃbhavati atas eva abhāve abhāva antaram tvayā na svīkriyate adhikaraṇasya tad vairūpya abhāvāt 
[038,ii_038,iv]	nanu arthena eva viśeṣaḥ buddheḥ na ca artha bhedaḥ asti mā evam na hi tāvat arthaḥ jñāna kāraṇam avaśyam kim tu sāmagrī viśeṣāt buddhi viśeṣaḥ jāyate dhārāvāhika buddhi vat yat vā ghaṭa vat bhū tala bhinnam bhū talam abhāvaḥ yatra pareṣām abhāvaḥ bhedaḥ ca svarūpam eva tādātmyena apratītau pratītiḥ iti tava api svarūpa bheda lakṣaṇam idānīm idam bhū talam ghaṭa vat bhū talam na bhavati iti pratīteḥ etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ yat tava samāna adhikaraṇa niṣedha pratītiḥ iyam anyonya abhāva bhedam avagāhate mama tu svarūpam 
[038,v]	nanu yat eva bhū talam ghaṭa vat bhū talā bhinnam āsīt tat eva katham tat bhinnam iti ced na tava api abādhita samāna adhikaraṇa niṣedha pratīti balena anyonya abhāva siddhau tathā tvasya durvāra tvāt samaya bhedena eva bheda abhedau na virudhyete iti tu samam yadi ca ghaṭa vat bhū talā bhinnam tat idānīm syāt tadā ghaṭa vat bhū tala vyavahāraḥ tatra syāt ghaṭa tad abhāva avacchedaka bhedena anyonya abhāva tad abhāvau bhū tale vartete iti ced mama api bhū tala ghaṭa vat bhū tala buddhi avacchedena svarūpa bheda tad abhāvau vartete iti gṛhāṇa 
[038,vi]	nanu bhū tale ghaṭaḥ asti na vā iti saṃśayaḥ ghaṭaḥ na asti iti viparyayaḥ vā katham bhavet pratiyogini buddhi sthe adhikaraṇasya tat jñānasya ca abhāvasya upalambhāt iti ced na bhū tale tad jñāne vā ghaṭa vat bhinna tvasya ghaṭa vat bhū tala jñāna bhinna tvasya ca doṣa vaśena aniścayāt bhū tala tajjñāna svarūpāṇām ananugamāt katham anugata vyavahāraḥ iti ced na abhāve api tulya tvāt na hi abhāva tvam sāmānyam abhāva tva gata anyonya abhāva avyāpaka tvāt 
[038,vii]	na ca bhāva virodhi tvam virodhasya abhāva nirūpya tvāt bhāva abhāvayoḥ saha avasthāna abhāvasya svarūpa anatiḥ ekāt ca na api bhāva pratiyogi tvam pratiyogi tvasya abhāva viraha rūpa tvāt abhāva abhāva asya bhāvasya bhāva apratiyogika tvāt ca na api sa pratiyogika tvam samavāya sādṛśi a ādīnām api tathātvāt na api parakīya svabhāva tvam jñāna ādi gata tvāt svabhāva śabdasya svarūpa arthe ananugamāt ca na api sattā śūnya tvam sattāyām eva gata tvāt śūnya tvasya abhāva rūpa tvāt ca sattā atyanta abhāvavat tvam abhāva tvam atyanta abhāvaḥ ca abhāva tvānavagatau api avagataḥ iti ced na abhāve abhāva anabhyupagamāt tathā ātve api tatra eva tad abhyupagamāt 
[038,viii_038,x]	sattā bodha vidhura tvam abhāva tvam sāmānya ādau satta avagame api bādhāt sā tyajyate abhāvasya tad viruddha tayā eva pratiteḥ iti ced na virodhi tvasya sva rūpa anatiḥ ekāt saha anavasthāna niyamaḥ virodhaḥ iti ced na anavasthānasya avasthāna abhāva tvena ātma āśrayāt bhāva bhinna tvam iti ced na bhedasya svarūpa anyonya abhāva rūpa tve ukta doṣāt vaidharmyasya cintyamāna tvāt prāgabhāva tva ādeḥ abhāva nirūpya tvāt evam ced abhāve api na anugamaḥ tadā kim adhikena sva rūpa viśeṣāt eva ghaṭa vyavahāraḥ api astu iti ced na bhū tala vilakṣaṇa ghaṭa anubhavāt ekaḥ eva abhāvaḥ anugataḥ iti ced na tasya nitya tvena pratiyogi kāle api abhāva vyavahāra prasaṅgāt prāc abhāva ādi vyutpādana virodhāt ca yat vā abhāva vādinā api abhāva jñāna kāraṇam anugataḥ bhū tala buddhi viśeṣaḥ svīkāryaḥ tad varam saḥ eva astu prameyam pramāṇam ca sva prakāśa tvāt buddhīnām 
[038,xi]	nanu tanmātra buddheḥ abhāva tve tasyāḥ sva prakāśa tvena pratiyogi jñāna apekṣā na syāt iti ced na na grahaṇāya tad apekṣā kim tu vyavahārāya jñānasya satyām icchāyām vyavahāra artham adhika apekṣā iti ced na dṛṣṭā hi vyavahāra artham adhika apekṣāḥ yathā parimāṇasya dīrgha tva vyavahāre tathā hi adhika saṃkhyā avacchinna hasta vitasti ādi avacchedaḥ parimāṇasya dīrgha tvam tad viparītam tu hrasva tvam tādṛśa parimāṇam ca avayavi graha sama kālam eva anubhūtam dīrgha tva vyapadeśaḥ tu alpa saṃkhyā ādi avacchinna hasta ādi avacchedya parimāṇa jñānam apekṣate tanmātra buddheḥ abhāva tve dṛśya pratiyogi jñāna apekṣa tayā dṛśyatā saṃpatti artham keśa kīṭa ādi sūkṣma jijñāsā api arthavatī na ca tanmātra buddheḥ abhāva tve tad vināśe abhāva abhāve bhāva unmajjana prasaṅgaḥ iti mokṣe puruṣa antarasya niyame pramāṇam na asti iti ced na kāryāt kāraṇa kalpanāt na ca evam buddhi nāśe punar saṃsāritā buddhi dhārā sattvāt na ca sarva muktiḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt pratiyogimad adhikaraṇa bhinna adhikaraṇa svarūpasya abhāva tve sarvam samañjasam eva iti pūrva pakṣaḥ 
[038,xii]	siddhāntaḥ tu sa pratiyogikaḥ abhāvaḥ anubhūyate ghaṭaḥ na paṭaḥ na iti anubhavāt na tu tanmātram atas abhāva vitti vedya tvam pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogi jñāna adhīna jñāna tvam ca abhāvasya anubhava sākṣikam gosādṛśya vat na ca kevalam adhikaraṇam tat jñānam vā abhāvaḥ pratiyogi jñānam vinā api tad vitteḥ tad vittau pratiyoginaḥ aviṣaya tvāt ca sa pratiyogika tva abhāve ca kasya pratiyogī ghaṭaḥ 
[038,xiii]	atha kevalam adhikaraṇam tat jñānam vā abhāvaḥ sa ca apratiyogikaḥ eva abhāva vyavahāraḥ tu pratiyogi jñānam apekṣate iti tasya pratiyāgī ghaṭaḥ ghaṭa tadabhāva vyavahārayoḥ virodhāt iti ced na iha ghaṭaḥ na iti nañarthasya pratiyogī ghaṭaḥ anubhūyate na tu abhāva jñāna anantara bhāvinaḥ abhāva vyavahārasya tasya abhāva anubhava samaye apratīteḥ vyavahriyate asau na tu anubhūyate iti ced na tādṛśa anubhavam vinā tathā vyavahāra abhāvāt vyavahāre pratiyogi jñāna apekṣā iti api na yuktam vyavahartavyajñānasya satyām icchāyām vyavahāre adhika apekṣāyāḥ adṛṣṭa cara tvāt lāghavāt iha tathā kalpyate na tu abhāvaḥ iti ced na vyavahāra mātre tathā kāraṇa tva anavadhāraṇāt vyavahāra viśeṣasya ananugata tvāt 
[038,xiv]	hrasva tva dīrgha tve ca parimāṇa antare eva tava api adhika saṃkhyā avacchinna hasta ādi avacchedya tvam parimāṇasya hrasva tvam dīrgha tvam ca alpa adhikau adhi jñāna adhīna jñānam atas dravya sama kālam parimāṇa anubhave api na anubhūtam iti na tadā tad vyavahāraḥ go sādṛśyam yadi api gavaya gatāni sāmānyāni tad jñāna sama kālam eva anubhūtāni tathā api go vṛtti tve sati gavaya vṛtti tvam go sādṛśyam go jñāna adhīna jñānam iti na tadā sādṛśya vyavahāraḥ 
[039,i]	syāt etat asti tāvat kasyacid jñānāt kvacid abhāva pada prayogaḥ sarva siddhaḥ tatra prayoga ālambanam bhū tala ādi eva ghaṭa vat atiriktā prakāśāt tatas ca yat apekṣam yasya abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvam tat tasya abhāvaḥ iti upeyate tad buddhi janita abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvam eva ghaṭa bhū talayoḥ pratiyogi anuyogi rūpaḥ sa bandhaḥ atas eva bhū talasya sa pratiyogika tvam tad buddhi janita abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvena tad buddhim vinā abhāva pada prayoga aviṣaya tvāt anena eva upādhinā ghaṭa abhāva ādi pada vyutpatti grahaḥ iti ced tat na abhāva pada prayoga ālambanam na bhū talam na hi bhū talam ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti pratīti prayogau api tu bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti bhū tale ghaṭaḥ iti vat bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti bhū tala adhikaraṇa atirikta nañartha prakāśāt 
[039,ii]	api ca ghaṭa buddhi janita abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvam bhū talasya ghaṭa abhāva tvam tathā ca ghaṭa abhāva tve tasya avagate ghaṭa abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvam ghaṭa abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tve ca jñāte tasya ghaṭa abhāva tvam iti anyonya āśrayaḥ pada pravṛtti nimitte avagate pada prayoga niyamāt ghaṭa abhāva tvam ca ghaṭa abhāva pade pravṛtti nimittam yadi ca bhū talam sa pratiyogikam tadā pratiyoginam vinā kevalam na bhāseta sādṛśya ādi vat ghaṭa abhāva pada prayoga daśāyām tat sa pratiyogikam na anyadā iti ced tarhi ghaṭa pratiyogika tve tasya ghaṭa buddhi janita abhāva pada prayoga viṣaya tvam sati ca tasmin ghaṭa pratiyogika tvam iti anyonya āśrayaḥ kevalasya apratiyogika tvāt evam ca go buddhi janita sadṛśa pada prayoga viṣaya tvam gavayasya go sādṛśyam astu kṛtam atirikta sādṛśyena iti sa pratiyogika padārtha apalāpaḥ 
[039,iii_039,iv]	api ca na kevalam bhū talam abhāvaḥ bhū tala abhāvayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāva anubhavāt abhede tad anupapatteḥ duḥkha vat ātma bhinnasya ca ātmanaḥ duḥkha abhāva tve mokṣasya apuruṣa artha tva prasaṅgaḥ ātmanaḥ asādhya tvāt atha ghaṭa vat bhū tala jñāna bhinnam bhū tala jñānam abhāvaḥ tasya ca bhū tala ādhāra tā svarūpa saṃbandhena anubhūyate iti ced na tasya niṣpratiyogika tvena abhāva tva anupapatteḥ iti ukta tvāt 
[039,v_039,vi]	api ca tat jñānam kim sva rūpa sadeva abhāva vyavahāra kāraṇam bhū talādhikaraṇaka niṣedha rūpa tayā anubhūyānam vā na ādyaḥ svarūpa sataḥ bhū tala ādheya tayā prati iti anupapatteḥ na dvitīyaḥ ghaṭa vat bhū tala jñānasya tadānīm anupasthiteḥ tad bhinna jñānasya pratyetum aśakyatvāt kim ca yadi ghaṭa vat bhū tala jñānāt bhinna bhū tala jñānam abhāvaḥ tadā ghaṭavati doṣāt ghaṭavat tva ajñāne bhū tala jñānam abhāvaḥ bhavet tathā ca tat eva tadā eva ghaṭa vat ghaṭa abhāva vat ca syāt na syātām ca ghaṭa abhāva jñāna tad vyavahārau visaṃvādinau viṣaya ābādhāt 
[039,vii]	atha vastutas ghaṭavataḥ bhū talasya jñānāt bhinnam bhū tala jñānam abhāvaḥ na ca ghaṭavati bhū tala jñānam tathā vyavahāraḥ tu visaṃvādī tathāvidha bhrama adarśanāt iti ced tarhi ghaṭavataḥ bhū talasya jñānāt bhinna tvena jñānam bhū tala jñānam abhāva vyavahṛti hetuḥ na ca tad saṃbhavati sva prakāśena anuvyavasāyena vā adhikaraṇa jñāne tad aprakāśāt bheda pratiyoginaḥ anupasthiteḥ na ca jñāna antareṇa tathā anubhavaḥ yogyā anupalabdhyā tatra ghaṭa abhāva niścayam vinā tathā niścetum aśakyatvāt 
[039,viii]	api ca adhikaraṇa tad jñānānām ananugata tvena anugata abhāva vyavahāra anupapattiḥ na ca atirikta abhāva pakṣe api tathā abhāva tvasya anugatasya abhāvāt iti vācyam anugata abhāva tvam vinā api ghaṭa ādiḥ na paṭaḥ iti samāna adhikaraṇa niṣedhāt anugata vyavahāraḥ paṭānyonya abhāvena ekena evam ghaṭa ādau na go tvam iti anugata vyavahāraḥ ekena atyanta abhāvena kapāleṣu bhū taleṣu idānīm ghaṭaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ iti anugata vyavahāraḥ dhvaṃsena ekena ghaṭa anutpāda daśāyām eteṣu ghaṭaḥ na asti iti anugata vyavahāraḥ ekena prāc abhāvena evam catvāraḥ anugata niṣedha vyavahārāḥ catasṛbhiḥ eva vyaktibhiḥ kriyante tava tu abhāva catuṣṭayam tad tad adhikaraṇa tad tad buddhīnām ananugata tvāt na saṃbhavati anugata abhāva catuṣṭaya vyavahārasya pratyeka abhāvena upapādayitum aśakya tvāt iti atiriktā bhāva vyakti catuṣṭaya siddhiḥ tasya ca yathā abhāva tvena ekena eka padārtha tvam tathā anupadam eva vakṣyāmaḥ 
[039,ix_039,x]	syāt etat yasmin samaya viśeṣe yatra bhū tale abhāvaḥ paraiḥ svīkriyate tad samaya viśeṣa yogaḥ eva bhū talasya ghaṭa abhāvaḥ evam ca iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti ādhāra ādheya bhāva pratītiḥ api upapadyate samaya viśeṣa yogasya bhū tala vṛtti tvāt na ca samaya viśeṣa yogasya abhāva tve ananugamaḥ doṣaḥ atirikta abhāva pakṣe api tulya tvāt abhāva tvasya jāteḥ upādheḥ vā asattvāt yadi ca abhāva pratīti prayoga anugama artham tatra dharma antaram svīkriyate tadā samaya viśeṣa yoga vṛttyā iva tat astu lāghavāt iti tat na samaya viśeṣa yogasya niṣpratiyogika tvena abhāva vyavahāra asāmarthyāt kim ca bhū tala vat samaya viśeṣaḥ api abhauva ādhāratayā anubhūyate idānīm bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti pratīteḥ na ca tad samaya viśeṣe tad samaya viśeṣa yogaḥ abhede saṃbandha anupapattau ādhāra ādheya bhāva abhāvāt 
[039,xi]	api ca samaye kim abhāva āśraya tā eva viśeṣaḥ tad tad samaya svarūpam vā ādye abhāva svīkāraḥ dvitīye ananugamaḥ mama tu eka abhāva vyakteḥ eva tathā nānā samaya vṛtti tvāt kim ca samaya viśeṣa yogāt idānīm bhū talam iti pratīti prayogau syātām viśeṣaṇasya sva prakāraka viśiṣṭa pratyaya janaka tvāt na tu bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti yadi ca tad tad samaya viśeṣa yogāt bhū tale ghaṭa abhāva vyavahāraḥ tadā yādṛśa saṃsthāna viśeṣa viśiṣṭe kapāle ghaṭaḥ vartate tādṛśa kapāla ādikam eva tad tad samaya viśeṣa yogāt ghaṭa ādi vyavahāra janakam aḥ tu kim ghaṭa ādinā pratītiḥ ca tulyā 
[039,xii_040,ii]	etena dṛṣṭaḥ tāvat ayam ghaṭaḥ atra ca patan dṛṣṭaḥ tathā mudgaraḥ dṛṣṭā karpara saṃhatiḥ param itaḥ abhāvaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ aparaḥ tena abhāvaḥ iti śrutiḥ kva nihitā kim ca atra tad kāraṇam svādhīnā kalaśasya kevalam iyam dṛṣṭā kapāla āvalī iti nirastam mudgara pātāt vinaṣṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti prati iti atirikta vināśa anubhavāt na ca kevala bhū talam tat buddhiḥ vā tad janyā tena vinā api tayoḥ sattvāt tvad mate ca tayoḥ abhāva mātra tvena vināśa tva ayogāt yoge vā abhāva mātrasya vināśi tvā āpattiḥ 
[040,iii_040,iv]	atha tvad mate yat vināśakam tat eva tad sahitam bhū talam jñānam vā vināśaḥ iti ced na mudgara pāta janyaḥ hi vināśaḥ anubhūyate na ca tasya eva tad janaka tvam sa pratiyogikaḥ ca vināśaḥ anubhūyate na ca mudgara pātaḥ tathā nanu abhāvena samam bhū talasya saṃbandha abhāvāt katham bhū tale ghaṭa abhāva pratyayaḥ svarūpa saṃbandhāt iti ced tarhi ghaṭa vat bhū talasya api catvarīya abhāvena svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ asti bhū talam abhāvaḥ ca iti adhikasya svarūpa saṃbandhasya abhāvāt 
[040,v]	pratiyogi āropaḥ eva svarūpa saṃbandhaḥ atas eva āropya niṣidhyate iti ucyate iti ced na tatra abhāva saṃbandhe satya āropaḥ saḥ eva ca abhāva saṃbandhaḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ iti ced na saṃbandha antaram antareṇa viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana yogya tvasya svarūpa saṃbandha tvāt na ca ghaṭa vat bhū tala catvarīya abhāvayoḥ parasparam viśiṣṭa pratyayaḥ jñāna viṣayayoḥ samavāya sama vāyinoḥ iva saṃbandha antara abhyupagamane ca anavasthā abhiyā tad saṃbandha saṃbandhinoḥ api tādṛśa saṃbandha svīkārāt iti siddhaḥ atiriktaḥ abhāvaḥ iti tad grāhikā viśeṣaṇa tā iti siddham etat 
[040,vi_040,viii]	grahaṇāt ṣoḍhā saṃnikarṣaḥ pratyakṣa viśeṣe kāraṇam viṣayeṇa āloka saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ ca tatra kāraṇam na tu cakṣuṣā prakāśa sthena cakṣuṣā andhakāra sthasya agrahaṇāt vaiparītye ca nanu evam para bhāga avacchedena āloka saṃyuktaḥ api ghaṭaḥ gṛhyeta na ca avayavi graha sāmagryāḥ sva avayava graha sāmagrī niyamāt para bhāga avacchinnaḥ na gṛhyate iti vācyam tri aṇuke vyabhicārāt pratyakṣa avayave ca sāmagrī bheda kalpane māna abhāvāt 
[040,ix_040,x]	atha abhimukha avayava avacchedena ghaṭa āloka saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam tarhi abhimukha avayava avacchedena cakṣuḥ āloka saṃyogaḥ api hetuḥ astu yadi ca āloka saṃyoga avacchinne cakṣuḥ saṃyogaḥ tathā samāna deśatā virodhaḥ ca nibiḍayoḥ eva anyathā paṭa mahārajatayoḥ paṭa udakayoḥ ca agraha prasaṅgaḥ tarhi ghaṭa saṃyoga avacchinne cakṣuḥ āloka saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam astu atha cālinī nyāyena āloka saṃyoga saṃnihite cakṣuḥ ghaṭa saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam tadā ghaṭa cakṣussaṃyoga saṃnihite cakṣuḥ āloka saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ aḥ tu iti ced na evam anvaya vyatirekābhyām viṣaya āloka saṃyogasya kāraṇa tve niścite tena eva upapattau na cakṣuḥ āloka saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam kalpyate 
[040,xi^1]	anye tu dvayoḥ api āloka saṃyogayoḥ kāraṇa tve viṣaya āloka saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam eva iti nanu abhimukha avayava avacchedena viṣaya āloka saṃyogayoḥ kāraṇa tve āvaśyaka saṃyogaḥ eva hetuḥ astu iti ced na avayava saṃyoga mātrasya ati prasakteḥ sva avayava saṃyogaḥ vaktavyaḥ tathā ca sva saṃyogaḥ eva lāghavāt avayava saṃyogena ca anyathā siddhau kāraṇa tā eva na syāt saṃyogasya iti uktam ālokasya udbhūta rūpam api vyañjakam anvaya vyatireki tvāt na tu tejaḥ kāraṇa tā avacchedekam tat ūṣma ādīnām cākṣuṣa tva abhāvāt na ca svātantryeṇa anvaya vyatireki tvāt dvayoḥ api hetu tvam anyathā daṇḍa ādeḥ api cakra avacchedaka tvam syāt iti vācyam udbhūta rūpa tejaḥ mātrayoḥ samavadhāne kārya anudayāt iti ced 
[040,xi^2]	mā evam udbhūta rūpasya tejaḥ tvam tejasaḥ ca udbhūta rūpa tvam vā avacchedakam iti vinigamaka abhāvāt ubhayoḥ api hetu tvāt daṇḍa cakrayoḥ iva ekaikam vihāya aparasya anvaya vyatireka abhāvāt evam cakṣuṣaḥ rūpam api vyañjakam vyañjaka tejaḥ rūpa tvāt āloka rūpa vat rūpasya vyañjaka tve udbhūta rūpa tvam tejaḥ gata udbhūta rūpa tvam vā na upādhiḥ vyabhicāreṇa gauraveṇa ca aprayojaka tvāt kim tu vyañjaka rūpam eva tathā lāghavāt viṣaya stham api rūpam udbhūtam sahakāri tad udbhave ca mānam indriya āloka ādi pratyāsannam mahat avayavi vāyu upanīta surabhi śīta ūṣma cakṣuḥ ādikam sākṣātkāra kiṃcid samavadhāna śūnyam apratyakṣa tvāt andhakāra stha ghaṭa vat iti 
[040,xii]	tat ca kāraṇam lāghavāt anugatam sāmanyam rūpa ādi vṛtti na dravya gatam ūṣmā ādau sparśa grahe rūpasya prabhā ādau rūpa grahe sparśasya graha prasaṅgāt udbhavatvā eka artha samavāya aviśeṣāt anyathā sparśa rūpayoḥ agraha prasaṅgāt na api ubhaya vṛtti rūpa ādi vṛtti tvena eva upapatteḥ rūpa sparśayoḥ tu tat nānā eka grahe api aparasya āgrahāt na ca rūpa tva ādinā para apara bhāva anupapattiḥ tāra tva ādi vat nānā tvāt rūpa ādi pratyakṣe ekaika udbhavasya eva prayojaka tvāt 
[040,xiii_041,i]	nanu mahat tvaḥ eva udbhava tvam astu tat eva pratyakṣa tve tantram lāghavāt na rūpe api gauravāt iti ced na āśraya mahat tva udbhava abhāve api gandha sparśayoḥ pratyakṣa tvena udbhava tvam iti pratyakṣa mūrta viśeṣa guṇa tvena rūpe api udbhava tvāt na mahat tve sāmānya guṇa tvāt atha anudbhava tvam eva jātiḥ apratyakṣa tva prayojaka tvena sākṣāt eva tad kalpanāt tad abhāvāt pratyakṣa tvam iti ced na apratyakṣatāyāḥ pratyakṣa kāraṇa viraha prayojya tvena pratyakṣa kāraṇasya lāghavena jāteḥ kalpanāt na tu pratibandhaka tvena anudbhava tvam kalpayitvā tad abhāvaḥ kāraṇam gauravāt iti saṃpradāya vidaḥ 
[041,ii]	vayam tu brumaḥ śukla tva ādinā kāraṇa rūpa agni saṃyoga prayojyābhyām jātibhyām para apara bhāva anupapattyā rūpa vṛtti udbhava tvam anekam vācyam tathā ca udbhūta tvena kāraṇa tve ananugamaḥ tasmāt anudbhava tvam śukla tva ādi vyāpyam nānā jātiḥ tad abhāvakūṭaḥ tu pratyakṣa tve prayojakaḥ anyathā anugata pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ evam sparśa ādau api 
[041,iii]	atha vā udbhūta tvam anudbhūta tvam vā na jātiḥ kim tu rūpa tva vyāpya jātimat tvam eva udbhūta tvam tad abhāvaḥ anudbhava tvam pratyakṣe rūpe śuklataratama tva ādi jātimat tvāt ūṣma cakṣuḥ ādi rūpe tu śukla tva mātram eva tad vyāpya jātau māna abhāvāt utkarṣa abhāvāt na ca rūpa tvam eva mānam lāghavena tasya prayojaka tve pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt evam sparśa ādau api iti itas api mahat tve na udbhava tvam prayojakam vāyu ādau mahattva utkarṣe api apratyakṣa tvāt 
[041,iv]	nanu bharjana kapāla gataḥ vahniḥ vāri stha ghaṭa vyañjaka tejaḥ ca gṛhyeta vāri kapālayoḥ pratyakṣa tvena udbhūta rūpavat tvāt tayoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ eva pratibandhakaḥ iti ced na jalakapāla ādīnām āloka vyaṅgya tayā tad grahe pratibandhaka tva abhāvāt pratibandhaka tve vā bharjana kapāla vāri saṃyogi vahni saurālokayoḥ agraha prasaṅgaḥ saṃyoge ca na viśeṣaḥ jāti kṛtaḥ anyatara karma ja tu ā ādinā saṃkara prasaṅgāt tāra tva vat nānātve gauravāt na api tad saṃyoga bhedaḥ ananugamāt iti 
[041,v]	mā evam jala stham tu tejaḥ gṛhyate eva ubhayoḥ svaccha tayā vivicya grahaḥ na bhavati bharjana kapāle ca anudbhūta rūpam udbhūta sparśam anyat eva tejaḥ tādṛśaiḥ avaya vaivahni sahacaritaiḥ ārabhyate ati tapta taila ādau kadācid udbhūta rūpa avayava praveśāt vahni ārambhaḥ api na ca evam dugdha sahacarita dadhi paramāṇubhiḥ eva dadhi ārambhaḥ dugdha dhvaṃsa janya dravya tvena khaṇḍa dugdha vat dadhnaḥ dugdha upādāna upādeya tvāt 
[041,vi^1]	nanu evam udbhūta rūpa vahni ādau udbhūta sparśaḥ na asti tad sahacarita tejaḥ antara niyamena tatra ūṣmabuddheḥ upapatteḥ udbhūta rūpa udbhūta sparśa sāmagrya ūrūṣmaṇi prabhā ādau virodha avadhāraṇāt iti ced na yam vahnim adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi iti abādhita pratyabhijñāna vaśāt darśana sparśanābhyām vahnau rūpa sparśayoḥ upalambhāt na ca tejaḥ tvam bādhakam udbhavān udbhavayoḥ nimitta bheda saṃsarga prayojya tvāt tejaḥ tu asya rūpavat vṛtti dravya tva sākṣāt vyāpya jāti tvena udbhūta rūpa sparśa vat vṛtti tvāt na ca udbhūta rūpa sparśayoḥ virodhaḥ 
[041,vi^2]	jala pṛthivyoru bhaya sattvāt tejasi virodhasya nimitta bheda upādhika tvāt iti udbhūta rūpa sahacaritayoḥ mahattva aneka dravyavat tvayoḥ yuganaddhavāhi tayā anvaya vyatireka tulya tve api dravya cākṣuṣa tve na aneka dravyavat tvam ubhayam vā tantram kim tu mahat tvam eva lāghavāt aneka dravya utkarṣam vinā api tūlaka ādau pracaya janyā utkṛṣṭa parimāṇāt pratyakṣa utkarṣa darśanāt ca dūra stha keśa rāśau dravya anutpādena mahat tva abhāve api ekakeśasya sajātīya saṃyogena aneka dravyavat tvāt dravya pratyakṣata iti aneka dravyavat tvam tatra tantram iti ced na aneka dravya saṃbandhi tvasya samavāyena prayojaka tvāt na tu saṃyogena atiprasaṅgāt tathā ca dūra grahaṇe sajātīya saṃyogasya aneka dravyavat tve sahakāritā vācyā sā mahat tve eva astu 
[041,vii]	nanu yadi udbhūta rūpavat tvam mahat tvam ca dravya pratyakṣatāyām sva rūpa yogya tā tadā daṇḍa tva vat tayoḥ kāraṇa tā na syāt iti ced na tat utkarṣāt pratyakṣa utkarṣeṇa tayoḥ kāraṇa tvāt na hi akāraṇa utkarṣam akāryam anuvidhatte daṇḍa tva ādau na evam prakāra bhedena ubhaya rūpa tvāt ca cākṣuṣa dravya jñāne viṣaya tvena tayoḥ kāraṇa tvam dravye anugata tvena kāraṇa tā avacchedaka tvam iti 
[041,viii]	nanu na udbhūta rūpavat tvam tatra tantram vāyoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt tathā hi vāyuḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣa sparśa āśraya tvāt mahat tve sati udbhūta sparśavat tvāt vā ghaṭa vat ūṣmā ādau pratyakṣa tvāt na vyabhicāraḥ na ca aprayojakam spārśana pratyakṣa tve mahat tve sati udbhūta sparśavat tvam prayojakam na udbhūta rūpavat tvam api gauravāt na ca pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpakaḥ sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpakaḥ ca udbhūta rūpavat tvam upādhiḥ spārśana pratyakṣa tve tasya aprayojaka tvāt tvac indriya vyāpāra anantaram vāyuḥ vātī iti pratīteḥ ca na ca sparśa liṅga agrahe tad upakṣayaḥ ghaṭe api tathā tva āpatteḥ laiṅgika tve ca sparśe vāyu vṛttiḥ iti dhīḥ syāt na tu anuṣṇa aśīta sparśaḥ vāyuḥ iti sparśa agrahe api śītaḥ vāyuḥ iti pratīteḥ ca na ca śīta dravya upanāyaka tvena anumite vāyau tathā dhīḥ bādhaka abhāvāt viśeṣa darśane satya āropa abhāvāt ca 
[041,ix_041,x]	atha ācākṣuṣa tvam spārśana tve bādhakam cakṣuṣā anupalabhyamānasya tvacā anupalambhāt iti ced tarhi cakṣuḥ eva dravya grāhakam tvacā sparśa mātram pratīyeta vāyau iva pratyabhijñā api tadvat eva atha anubhavasya durapahnava tvāt tvacā āśraya rahitaḥ eva sparśaḥ upalabhyate tadā vāyau api tulyam atha doṣa abhāve sati dravya grahe tad gata saṃkhyā ādi graha niyamāt vāyau sarvathā tad agrahāt na sa pratyakṣaḥ iti ced na na ca tāvat ayam vyaktau niyamaḥ pṛṣṭha lagna vastra ādeḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa agrahe tvacā grahaṇāt tad jātīye tu phūtkāra ādau saṃkhyā parimāṇa ādīnām vāyu abhighātasya ca śarīre pratyakṣa tvāt 
[041,xi]	syāt etat bahis indriya ja dravya sākṣātkāre mahat tve sati udbhūta rūpavat tvam prayojakam sati saṃbhave tyāga ayogāt na tu janya indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvam kārya mahat tva samāna adhikaraṇa viśeṣa guṇavat tvam vā rasana gata pitta dravyasya udbhūta tikta rasasya vāyu upanīta surabhi dravyasya ca pratyakṣatā āpatteḥ 
[042,i]	mā evam na udbhūta rūpavat tvam tathā nayana gata pitta dravyasya ca pratyakṣatā āpatteḥ astu vā udbhūta sparśavat tvam tatra tantram na ca evam prabhāyām apratyakṣa tvam prabhā hi tejasaḥ rūpam na dravyam tad āśraya tejaḥ pratītiḥ pratyakṣa rūpa liṅga adhīnā eva yathā tava ūṣma ādi pratītiḥ tatra saṃyoga karma ādi katham pratyakṣam iti ced cāndra sauradīpa prabhā ādau tu na kathaṃcid indranīla ādi prabhāyāḥ rūpasya pūrva deśa anupalambhena uttara deśa upalambhena liṅgena tad āśraya tejaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga ādi anumānam iti tu ad naye yathā tvacā sparśa mātra graha anantaram phūtkāre saṃgoga ādīnām 
[042,ii_042,iii]	etena dhūma bāṣpayoḥ aspārśana tvena udbhūta sparśa abhāve api cākṣuṣa tvam anyathā tad gata saṃyoga vibhāga karmaṇām pratyakṣatā na syāt liṅga abhāvāt iti nirastam na ca bahis indriya yogya aneka viśeṣa guṇavat tvam tantram tava trasareṇu prabhayoḥ apratyakṣata āpatteḥ gauravāt ca nanu evam vinigamaka abhāvāt ubhayoḥ api tathātvam astu tathā api vāyuḥ apratyakṣaḥ iti ced evam bahis indriya ja dravya sākṣātkāre cākṣuṣa tve spārśana pratyakṣa tve ca pratyekam udbhūta rūpavat tve sati udbhūta sparśavat tvam prayojakam paryavasyati iti gauravam mama tu cākṣuṣa tve udbhūta rūpavat tvam spārśana tve udbhūta sparśavat tvam yasya viśeṣe prayojaka tvam tasya anugatena rūpeṇa sāmānya prayojaka tvam iti dravya grāhaka bahis indriya vyavasthāpaka udbhūta viśeṣa guṇavat tvam sāmānya prayojakam iti lāghavam viśeṣasya sāmānyasya ca bhinna prayojya tva niyama anna ekam prayojakam 
[042,iv]	atha vāyuḥ yadi bahis indriya janya sākṣātkāra viṣaya dravyam spārśana sākṣātkāra viṣaya dravyam vā syāt udbhūta rūpaḥ syāt na ca evam tasmāt tathā tādṛśa sākṣātkāra viṣaya dravyasya rūpa janaka tva niyamāt iti ced na rūpa vat samaveta tvena hi dravyasya rūpa janaka tvam na tu tādṛśa sākṣātkāra viṣaya dravya tvena tasya rūpa janana uttara kālīna tvāt ghaṭaḥ yadi cakṣuḥ itara indriya grāhya dravyam syāt arūpam asparśam acākṣuṣa ādi syāt tvac indriyam yadi dravya grāhaka bahis indriyam syāt rūpa vat syāt sparśa grāhakam vā na syāt rūpa grāhi vā syāt cakṣuḥ vat na ca evam tasmāt na tathā iti ghaṭaḥ api na tvac indriya grāhyaḥ syāt tad gata saṃkhyā ādi jñānam phūtkāra ādau iva iti syāt spṛśāmi iti anuvyavasāyaḥ ca ghaṭa vat vāyau api 
[042,v_042,vi]	atha spārśana tve udbhūta sparśa vat udbhūtam rūpam api tantram udbhūta rūpavat tve cākṣuṣa tva vat spārśana tva darśanāt iti ced na udbhūta rūpavat tve sati api prabhāyām na spārśana tvam iti udbhūta sparśasya āvaśyaka tvena udbhūta rūpasya anyathā siddha tvāt na hi udbhūta sparśe sati udbhūta rūpa abhāvāt spārśana tva abhāvaḥ nanu evam sparśa gataḥ udbhavaḥ kāraṇam astu na tu rūpam akāraṇam iti ced tathā api sparśaḥ tad udbhavaḥ ca kāraṇam na tu rūpam api tasmin dvaye sati tad abhāvena tad abhāva adarśanāt vastutas rūpa sparśa gate udbhava tu ajātī kāraṇa tāva chedike na tu kāraṇe iti 
[042,vii]	ucyate dravyasya spārśana tve udbhūta sparśa mātram na tantram nidāgha ūṣmaṇi vāyu upanīta śīta uṣṇa dravye ca pratyakṣa tvena tad gata saṃkhyā parimāṇa saṃyoga vibhāga karmaṇām pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt yogi avyakti vṛtti tvena teṣām yogyatayā dravya grāhaka sāmagrī grāhya tva avadhāraṇāt na ca ūṣma ādi jātīye doṣa abhāve api ghaṭa ādau iva kara parāmarśe kadācid kena api saṃkhyā gṛhyate tathā udbhūta rūpavat tva mātrasya tathā tve cāndra ādi udyotasya nayana gata pitta dravyasya ca pratyakṣa tve tad gata saṃkhyā grahaḥ api syāt na ca ghaṭa ādau iva nipuṇam nibhālayantaḥ api tad gata saṃkhyā dvi tva ādi hasta vitasti ādi parimāṇam karma vā vīkṣāmahe iti eka eka vyabhicārāt vinigamaka abhāvāt ubhayam api bahis indriya dravya pratyakṣa tve prayojakam iti vāyuḥ apratyakṣaḥ na ca evam apasiddhāntaḥ pītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ ityādau nayana pitta pītim ā eva gṛhyate na tu pitta dravyam vayava tvāt prabhāyām iva tejasaḥ iti ṭīkā kṛtām abhidhānāt iti navīnāḥ 
[042,viii]	saṃpradāya vidaḥ tu calati pakṣi kāṇḍa ādau pūrva deśa vibhāga uttara deśa saṃyogayoḥ pratyakṣatā na syāt pūrva uttara deśasya prabhā maṇḍalasya anudbhūta sparśa tvena apratyakṣa tvāt tathā ca pareṣām calati iti pratītiḥ api tad liṅgikā na syāt asmākam api candra tārā ādau saṃyoga vibhāga liṅgaka gati anumānam na syāt na ca pūrva uttara deśe upalambha anupalambhābhyām saṃyoga vibhāgau anumāya tābhyām eva gati anumānam pūrva uttara deśayoḥ apratyakṣa tvena liṅga asiddheḥ tasmāt udbhūta rūpavat tvam tatra prayojakam iti vāyuḥ apratyakṣaḥ 
[042,ix]	nanu śītaḥ vāyuḥ iti āropaḥ na spārśanaḥ viśeṣyasya ayogya tvāt na ca prabhāyām tathā sāmānye bādhaka abhāvāt na api anumāna upanīte vāyau tvac indriya upanītaḥ śīta āropaḥ śīta dravya abheda āropaḥ vā manasā tad liṅga sparśa ādi catuṣkasya agrahaṇāt śīta sparśasya ātad liṅga tvāt na ca śīta dravya upanāyaka tvena anumite vāyau manasā śīta āropaḥ śītān āśraya tvena anumite vāyau tad anāropāt na api pītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ iti vat bahis indriya janyaḥ ayam bhramaḥ yena anumānika viśeṣa grahe api doṣa māhātmyāt bhavet śīta dravya upanayana janaka praṇālīm aviduṣaḥ api śītaḥ vāyuḥ iti pratyayāt ca na api liṅga ābhāsa janyā anumiti rūpaḥ bhramaḥ tat apratīteḥ śīta sparśasya vāyu liṅga tvena bhrama aviṣaya tvāt na ca śīta sparśa anumite dravye smṛta vāyu abheda āropaḥ vāyu viśeṣyaka śīta pratyayāt atas eva śīta sparśaḥ ayam vāyoḥ iti bhrama śarīram apāstam na ca svapna vibhrama vat sva utprekṣita padārtha saṃsarga āropavat ca mānasaḥ ayam tvac indriya vyāpāra anuvidhānāt iti 
[042,x]	ucyate yathā vāyu vaidharmyeṇa jala vṛtti tayā gṛhītasya śīta sparśasya vāyau āropaḥ diś moha vat doṣa māhātmyāt tathā śīta sparśe vāyu liṅga tva āra upād vāyavīyatva anumānam na ca evam śītaḥ vāyuḥ iti pratītiḥ na syāt iti vācyam śītaḥ ayam vāyavīyaḥ iti jñāna anantaram śītaḥ ayam vāyuḥ iti ca manasā āropāt anuṣṇaḥ vāyuḥ iti vat 
[042,xi]	atha tvac vyāpāra anantaram katham vā āyuḥ vātī iti pratītiḥ tad liṅga saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ apratyakṣa tvāt na ca śarīre vāyu abhighātaḥ eva tat liṅgam abhighātasya saṃyoga tvena apratyakṣa tvāt iti ced na abhighāta janya sukha duḥkha viśeṣeṇa abhighātam unnīya tasya sparśavat vegavat janya tvam anumāya vegena karma anumānāt evam praṇālīm aviduṣaḥ tad pratyaya asiddheḥ 
[042,xii]	atha vāyuḥ śītaḥ vātī iti katham viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya pratītiḥ ekā śīta viśiṣṭa pratīteḥ mānasa tvena karma pratīteḥ ānumānika tvena jāti saṃkara prasaṅgāt iti ced na śīta viśiṣṭa tvena smṛte vāyau karma anumānāt viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭyam na tu ubhayam viśeṣaṇam ekadā bhāsate na ca evam kalpanā gauravam doṣāya pratyakṣa tve balavat bādhaka sattvāt 
[043,i]	evam bahis indriya ja dravya pratyakṣa tve udbhūta rūpavat tvasya prayojaka tve vyavasthite pratyakṣa tu asādhyaka anumāne pakṣa dharma avacchinnasya sādhyasya sādhana avacchinnasya vā vyāpakam udbhūta rūpavat tvam upādhiḥ na ca viśiṣṭasya vyabhicāra vyatirekayoḥ sādhane artha antaram viśeṣya vyabhicāra vyatireka siddhi paryavasānāt iti upādhau vakṣyāmaḥ 
[043,ii]	atha vāyu vat ātmā api na pratyakṣaḥ dravya pratyakṣa tve udbhūta rūpavat tvasya tantra tvāt na ca liṅga jñānam vinā eva aham jānāmi iti pratyayāt na laiṅgika tvam jñānam aviduṣaḥ jānāmi iti viśiṣṭa pratyaya abhāvena jñānasya liṅga tvāt na ca ghaṭam aham jānāmi iti vartamāna pratyayaḥ na syāt ghaṭa jñānasya anumiti pūrva tṛtī yakṣaṇe vināśāt iti vācyam sthūla samaya upādhim ādāya vartamāna pratyayāt yathā kulāle ceṣṭā darśanena karoti iti anumitiḥ iti 
[043,iii_043,iv]	ucyate yaḥ aham ghaṭam adrākṣam saḥ aham ghaṭam spṛśāmi iti abheda pratyabhijñānāt ātmā pratyakṣaḥ na ca etat sparśana indriya janya jñāna āśrayaḥ aham tad darśana jñāna āśraya abhinnaḥ madīya ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tvāt tad darśana jñāna aśraya tva vat iti ātmā abheda pratyayaḥ iti vācyam mad aṃśasya apratyakṣa tvena anumāna liṅga asiddheḥ na ca jñānena ātma anumānam tatas tatra jñāne ātmīyatva anumānam tatas madīya ahaṃpratyaya viṣaya tva jñānam ātmani iti vācyam evam praṇālīm aviduṣaḥ api yaḥ aham saḥ aham iti pratyayāt na ca vāyau pratyabhijñānam asti sadāgatimat tvena gatasya punar ajñānāt saḥ eva punar purovātaḥ iti pratīteḥ tad jātīya anumiti rūpa tvāt tasmāt vāyuḥ bahis indriya apratyakṣaḥ nīrūpa dravya tvāt ākāśa vat na ca sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpakam udbhūta sparśān āśraya tvam upādhiḥ udbhūta sparśasya tatra ahetutvena upādheḥ sādhya avyāpaka tvāt 
[043,v]	kim ca udbhūta sparśavat tvasya bahis indriya janya dravya sākṣātkāra prayojaka tve suvarṇa rūpam tejaḥ dravyam pratyakṣam na syāt prabhāvat tasya anudbhūta sparśavat tvāt rūpam tu tasya udbhūtam eva kim tu upaṣṭambhaka pīta rūpa abhibhūtam abhibhavaḥ ca balavatsa jātīya saṃbandhaḥ evam andhakāre pītāgrahaṇe api abhibhavaḥ na ca evam andhakāre suvarṇa upalambha āpattiḥ abhibhūtasya api tejasaḥ grahāt na ca tejasi tejaḥ antaram vyañjakam iti vācyam rūpe gṛhyamāṇaḥ eva cakṣuṣā dravya grahāt suvarṇa rūpam abhibhavāt eva na upalabhyate upaṣṭambhaka rūpam ca āloka abhāvāt 
[043,vi]	atha yathā aruṇa kapila ādi rūpa abhibhūtam api vahni rūpam param ātmānam ca prakāśayati tathā kanakam api prakāśeta prakāśayet ca iti ced na tatra hi abhibhūta rūpa vahni saṃbaddhānabhibhūta rūpā vahni madhya ādi vyāpinī prabhā eva vyañjikā yat vā vahnau rūpa bhāsvara tve na abhibhūte kim tu śukla tva mātram suvarṇe tu rūpam abhibhūtam tena tad gata śukla tva bhāsvara tve anabhibhūte api vyakti agrahān na gṛhyete iti phala balāt kalpyate na ca pītim agurutva āśraya atiriktam tat asiddham asti hi suvarṇasya atyanta anala saṃyoge api pītam rūpam na tat vijātīyam tad anupapannam asati drava dravya saṃbandhe pārthive atyanta agni saṃyogasya pūrvarūpa vijātīya rūpa janakatva niyamāt jala saṃbandhe tad apagame ca paṭa ādau dāha ādāha darśanāt tat idam dhmāyamānam kanakam yadi atyanta agni saṃyogi pārthiva tve sati vijātīya rūpa pratibandhaka drava dravya saṃyuktam na syāt pūrvarūpa vijātīya rūpa vat syāt vahni saṃbaddha ghaṭa vat anyathā pārthivam na syāt jalam vā syāt agni saṃyogi vā na syāt 
[043,vii]	tat ayam prayogaḥ atyanta agni saṃyogi pītam vijātīya rūpa pratibandhaka drava dravya saṃyuktam atyanta agni saṃyogi tve sati pūrvarūpa vijātīya rūpa an adhikaraṇa pārthiva tvāt jala madhya sthita agni saṃyukta pīta paṭa vat yat vā pītam suvarṇam pīta rūpa atirikta rūpa utpatti pratibandhaka drava dravya saṃyuktam naktaṃdivam agni saṃyoge api pīta rūpa atirikta rūpa an āśraya tvāt tāvat paryantam agni saṃyukta jala madhya stha pīta paṭa vat na ca aprayojaka tvam virodhi drava dravya saṃbandham vinā pārthive atyanta agni saṃyogasya vijātīya rūpa janaka tvāt tat ca drava dravyam na jalam svābhāvika drava tva anāśraya tvāt na ca anudbhūtam tat śītala śilā tale agni saṃyogāt dāha darśanena anudbhūta drava tvasya dāha avirodhi tvāt naimittika drava tvāt ca na api tatas eva pārthiva tvam druta pārthivasya vijātīya rūpa pratibandhaka tve ghṛta ādau api tathā tva āpatteḥ tatra api rūpa parāvṛtti prasaṅgāt ca upaṣṭambhakasya api pārthiva tvena vijātīya rūpa apratibandhaka tvāt 
[043,viii]	yadi api tejaḥ antaram na naimittika drava tva adhikaraṇam na api vijātīya rūpa pratibandhakam kim tu tad janakam tathā api pratyakṣa dravya tvena tasya rūpavat tve pṛthivī jala anya tvena tejaḥ tvāt dharmi grāhaka māna siddham tathātvam pīta bhāga drava tvam api agni saṃyoge na naśyati druta tejaḥ pratibandhāt eva jala madhya stha agni saṃyukta ghṛta vat iti 
[043,ix]	atha yadi druta tejasaḥ vijātīya rūpa pratibandhaka tvam tadā jala stha paṭa vat druta suvarṇa madhya sthita paṭa ādeḥ api rūpa parāvṛttiḥ na syāt iti ced na loke suvarṇa tvena anubhūyamāne pīta dravye avinirbhāga vartinī upaṣṭambhake drutam tejaḥ vijātīyam rūpam pratibadhnāti na anyatra tathā eva anvaya vyatirekāt tarhi upaṣṭambhaka tvam anubhava siddham suvarṇasya iti asya āvaśyaka tvāt tasya eva svarūpa parāvṛttau pratibandhaka tvam astu kṛtam dṛṣṭa vijātīya tejaḥ kalpanayā iti ced na upaṣṭambhaka mātre hi vijātīya rūpa pratibandhaka svabhāva tvam druta tejasaḥ dharmi grāhaka māna siddha tvāt tasya tena eva rūpeṇa siddheḥ yadi drutam tejaḥ rūpa parāvṛtti pratibandhakam syāt paṭa ādi rūpa parāvṛttim api pratibadhnīyāt iti tarkasya tad viparyayasya ca siddhi asiddhi vyāhata tvāt anubhūyamāna suvarṇasya ca upaṣṭambhaka rūpa parāvṛtti pratibandhaka svabhāva tvam na dharmi grāhaka mānāt anyatas vā siddham yena pārthive asati virodhi drava dravya saṃbandhe agni saṃyogasya rūpa parāvartaka tvam anvaya vyatireka siddham paribhūyeta iti ācāryāḥ 
[043,x]	navīnāstu atyanta agni saṃyogena anucchidyamāna pratyakṣa drava tva adhikaraṇam taijasam jala pṛthivībhyām anya tve sati rūpavat tvāt vahni vat na ca asiddhiḥ pratyakṣa dravya tva adhikaraṇa tvena tasya rūpavat tvāt na ca tat jalam sāṃsiddhika drava tvānāśraya tvāt naimittika drava tva ādhāra tvāt sneha śūnya tvāt vā lākṣā vat snehe sati sneha drava tva adhīna saṃgraha prasaṅgāt na ca pārthivam atyanta agni saṃyoge api anucchidyamānam yat drava tvam tad adhikaraṇa tvāt jala paramāṇu vat asati virodhi drava dravya saṃbandhe iti viśeṣaṇam tena kvathyamāna jala stha ghṛtena na vyabhicāraḥ na ca aprayojaka tvam atyanta anala saṃyogena lākṣā ādi ghṛta ādi pṛthivī drava tva ucchede pṛthivī drava tva tvam eva prayojakam asati bādhake anugatasya prayojaka tve saṃbhavati tyāga ayogāt na ca ghṛta drava tva tva ādikam ananugamāt na api naimittika drava tva tvam drava tva tvam eva vā suvarṇe drava tva uccheda prasaṅgāt 
[044,i_044,ii]	atha apārthivam api sāṃsiddhika drava tvam taile janya jala antare ca atyanta agni saṃyogāt ucchidyate atas anugatam eva tṛṇa araṇi maṇi nyāyena drava tva uccheda prayojakam iti ced na pṛthivī drava tva ucchede pṛthivī drava tva tvam jala drava tva ucchede janya jala drava tva tvam drava tva mātra ucchede ca janya rasa vat drava tvam prayojakam lāghavāt etena vivāda viṣayaḥ pṛthivī naimittika drava tva āśraya tvāt ghṛta vat iti sat pratipakṣa tvam apāstam anukūla tarka abhāvena agni saṃyogāt drava tva uccheda prasaṅga lakṣaṇa pratikūla tarkeṇa ca hīna bala tvāt 
[044,iii]	atha naimittika drava tve pṛthivī tvam samavāyikāraṇa tāvacchedakam asati bādhake tyāga ayogāt iti ced na ghaṭa ādau api naimittika drava tva prasaṅgāt na ca ghṛta lākṣā ādiṣu pṛthivī tva avāntaram kiñcid ekam anugatam naimittika drava tva samavāyi kāraṇa tāvacchedakam asti pṛthivī niyata naimittika drava tvam katham apṛthivyām iti ced na tāvat tiryak gamana ūrdhva jvalana vat tat jāti niyatam ghaṭa ādau abhāvāt na api pṛthivītva avāntara jāti viśeṣa niyatam ghṛtam vihāya lākṣā ādiṣu api bhāvāt 
[044,iv_044,v]	atha upaṣṭambhake pītim agurutva āśraye pārthive atyanta agni saṃyogena anucchidyamāna drava tva ādhāra tvam anaikāntikam na hi tejaḥ drava tva daśāyām tat adravam eva āste pītam drutam iti pratīteḥ iti ced na tatra drava tva abhāvāt pārthiva drava tvasya atyanta agni saṃyogena ucchitti āpattyā bādhakena druta pratīteḥ bhrama tvāt jala madhya sthitam asīkṣa uda ādeḥ iva tad avayavānām drava dravya saṃbandhena praśithila saṃyoga āśraya tvāt na tu teṣām drava tvam na ca evam ghṛta ādau api tathā drava tve tatra bādhaka abhāvāt 
[044,vi]	anye tu upaṣṭambhake drava tvam utpadyate eva anubhavasya durapahnava tvāt atyanta agni saṃyogena tad ucchedaḥ tu na bhavati drava dravyasya tejasaḥ pratibandhaka tvāt na ca evam druta tejasi māna abhāvaḥ tathā hi pītam drava tva adhikaraṇam drava tva uccheda pratibandhaka drava dravya saṃyuktam atyanta agni saṃyoge api anucchidyamāna drava tva ādhāra pārthiva tvāt kvathyamāna jala madhya sthita ghṛta vat na ca aprayojaka tvam atyanta agni saṃyogena virodhi drava dravya saṃbandha asaṃbandhe pārthiva drava tva uccheda an uccheda darśanāt 
[044,vii]	atha vā rūpavat tve jala anya tve ca sati taijasa tva pārthiva tva saṃdehe vivāda adhyāsitam drava tva adhikaraṇam taijasam asati drava dravya saṃyoge atyanta agni saṃyoge api anucchinna anitya drava tva ādhāra tvāt yat na evam tat na evam yathā jalam ghṛtam vā iti vyatirekī na ca asādha araṇyam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām tasya doṣa tvāt 
[044,viii]	tathā hi yathā sādhya abhāva vat vyāvṛtta tvena pakṣe tasya sādhya sādhaka tvam tathā sādhya vat vyāvṛtta tvena sādhya abhāva sādhaka tā api syāt iti sat pratipakṣa utthāpaka tayā tasya doṣa tvam na ca sādhya abhāva sādhakasya pṛthivī tva siddhi paryavasāyinaḥ tulya bala tvam anukūla tarka abhāvena hīna bala tvāt yadi idam pārthivam syāt asati virodhi drava dravya saṃbandhe atyanta agni saṃyogena ucchidyamāna drava tvā adhikaraṇam syāt taila vat iti pratikūla tarkeṇa hīna bala tvāt 
[044,ix_044,x]	yadi idam jala anya rūpavat tve sati taijasam na syāt pārthivam syāt yadi ca pārthivam syāt atyanta agni saṃyogena ucchidyamānadratvā adhikaraṇam syāt iti anukūla tarka sadbhāvena pratikūla tarka abhāvena ca taijasatva sādhakasya adhika bala tvāt yadi ca asādhāraṇasya sādhya tad abhāva vat vyāvṛtta tvena tad ubhaya saṃśaya janakatayā doṣa tvam tathā api viśeṣa adarśana sahitasya saṃśāyaka tvam prakṛte ca anukūla tarka viśeṣa darśana saha kṛtasya vyatireki bhāvena sādhaka tvam tasmāt yadā sādhya tadabhāva koṭau na viśeṣa darśanam tadā asādhāraṇyasya doṣa tvam na ca evam śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda tvāt ityādikam api hetuḥ syāt viśeṣa darśana daśāyām iṣṭa tvāt 
[044,xi]	anye tu tejaḥ tvam na adrava rūpavat mātra vṛtti rūpavat vṛtti dravya tva sākṣāt vyāpya jāti tvāt pṛthivī tva vat yat vā tejaḥ tvam druta vṛtti rūpavat vṛtti dravya tva sākṣāt vyāpya jāti tvāt jala tva vat na ca rasa vat vṛtti tvam upādhiḥ rasavat tvam drava tu asamāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi adruta vṛtti dravya tva vyāpya dharma tvāt paṭatva vat iti druta tejassiddhau sādhya avyāpaka tvāt iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭena tejasi prasādhya vivāda adhyāsitam drutam taijasam atyanta agni saṃyogena anucchidyamāna aniti a drava tva adhikaraṇa tvāt na yat evam na tat evam yathā jalam iti vadanti 
[044,xii]	atha jhrādya anumāneṭa tejaḥ mātra āvṛtti tvam upādhiḥ na ca pakṣa itara tvam pradīpa tva ādeḥ api vyāvartya tvāt iti ced na balavat vipakṣa bādhakena vivāda viṣaye druta taijasa tva siddhau upādheḥ sādhya avyāpaka tvāt evam ca vivāda adhyāsite pārthiva tva taijasa tva sādhakāni yadi api bahūni anumānāni santi tathā api vipakṣa bādhaka tarkāt taijasa tva sādhakasya balavat tvam iti dhyeyam 
[044,xiii]	atha drutadrutatara ādeḥ kramaśas pratīteḥ prabala anala saṃyogena suvarṇa nāśāt tad drava tvam naśyati iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ na ca drava tva prāgabhāva asamāna adhikaraṇa drava tu a dhvaṃsa rūpaḥ ucchedaḥ na suvarṇe drava tva nāśe api agrima drava tvena utpādāt ghṛte ca tathā iti vācyam suvarṇe drava tva nāśe sati vinaṣṭa āśraye drava tva antarasya anutpādena drava tva prāgabhāva asamāna adhikaraṇa drava tva dhvaṃsasya sattvāt iti ced na suvarṇa drava tvam hi āśraya nāśāt vinaśyati na tu agni saṃyogāt yadi ca agni saṃyogāt vinaśyet tadā ghṛta vat na drava tva antaram utpadyeta drava tva ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya drava tva antara pratibandhaka tvāt tathā ca agni saṃyoge sati tad hetuka nāśa apratiyogi drava tva adhikaraṇa tvāt iti hetu arthaḥ athavā ghṛte drava tva uccheda samaye samāna adhikaraṇa drava tva sāmagrī samavadhānam na asti suvarṇe tu asti evam ca samāna adhikaraṇa drava tva sāmagrī samavahita agni saṃyoga janya dhvaṃsa pratiyogya vṛtti drava tva avāntara sāmānya vat drava tvam hetu arthaḥ 
[045,i_045,ii]	yat vā ghṛta paramāṇau agni saṃyoga daśāyām drava tva nāśe sati drava tva antaram na utpadyate tad ārabdha bhasmani drava tva abhāvāt evam suvarṇa paramāṇu drava tvam agni saṃyogāt ca yadi vinaśyet tadā tad ā ārabdha suvarṇam adravam syāt tathā suvarṇa ārambhakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ na pārthivāḥ atyanta agni saṃyogena anucchidyamāna drava tva adhikaraṇa tvāt jala paramāṇu vat taijasā vā tatas eva yat na evam tat na evam yathā ghṛta paramāṇuḥ iti vyatirekī jhrvāṭa evam apārthiva ārabdham taijasa ārabdham vā suvarṇam apārthivam taijasam vā atyanta anala saṃyoge api anucchidyamāna drava tva adhikaraṇa paramāṇu ārabdha tvāt iti anvaya vyatirekī ca iti 
[045,iii]	eka deśī tu drava tva adhikaraṇam na tejaḥ pīta vat na ca asiddhiḥ pītam drutam iti pratīteḥ pīta tve pārthiva tva āpattyā bādhakena pīta pratītiḥ bhramaḥ iti ced na śukla tve api apārthiva tva vat pīta tve api apārthiva tve bādhaka abhāvāt yathā naimittika drava tvam pṛthivī tve na tantram atiprasaṅgāt tathā pīta tve api gandha niyata tvam api naimittika drava tva vat eva pṛthivī jala anya tve sati rūpi tvena tejaḥ iti ced na aprayojaka tvāt anyathā jala tejaḥ anya tve sati sparśavat tvena vāyoḥ api pṛthivī tva āpatteḥ atha rūpa rasa gandhānām abhāvāt na tathātvam teṣām anudbhave ca pṛthivī udbhūta rūpa rasa gandha ādi anyatamavatī ityādi bahuvidha vyāpti virodhaḥ iti ced na tejaḥ adravam eva pratyakṣam tejaḥ pratyakṣa rūpa sparśa ādi anyatara vat eva sva para prakāśakam eva ityādi vyāpti virodhasya tejasi api sattvāt drava tva adhikaraṇam ca na pṛthivī iti tvayā eva sādhitam atas naimittika drava tva adhikaraṇam pītam suvarṇam dravya antaram eva iti āha 
[045,iv]	nanu indriya janya tvam sakhā ādi pratyakṣa avyāpakam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam iti ced na jñāta karaṇa ajanyaḥ sukha ādi anubhavaḥ indriya janyaḥ janya pratyakṣa tvāt rūpa pratyakṣa vat janya sākṣātkārasya indriya janya tvāt iti tatra api tad lakṣaṇa sattvāt sparśa ādi aviṣaya tvena tvac ādinā na artha antaram gandha rūpa rasa sparśeṣu ekaika mātra sākṣātkāra ajanaka tvena pṛthivī ādi bheda siddhau niḥsparśam lāghavān niravayavam ca manaḥ 
[045,v_045,vi]	tat ca vibhu jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt nitya indriya tvāt nitya tve sati dravya anārambhaka dravya tvāt viśeṣa guṇa śūnya dravya tvāt ātma ādi vat na ca mahat tvam upādhiḥ sādhana vyāpaka tvāt iti nanu sukha ādikam mūrta saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇaka guṇa vṛtti guṇa tva avāntara jāti yogi nitya vṛtti anitya viśeṣa guṇa tvāt śabda vat pākaja rūpa vat ca iti ced na anātma vṛtti tvasya śabda bhinna viśeṣa guṇa grāhaka indriya ajanya tvasya śabdasya dravya tvena mūrta vṛtti guṇa tvasya ca upādhi tvāt aprayojaka tvāt ca kāraṇe mūrta tvasya guru tvāt astu vā śarīra ātma saṃyoga janya tvena artha antaram 
[045,vii]	atha asamavāyi adhīnaḥ vibhu kāryāṇām prādeśika tva niyamaḥ iti vibhu manaḥ yogāt ātma mātre sukha ādeḥ utpattau niyata deśa tā na syāt atas aṇu manaḥ iti mā evam kim asamavāyi kāraṇam sva avacchinne vibhukāryam janayati iti niyamaḥ sva avacchinne janayati eva iti vā sva avacchinnaḥ eva janayati iti vā ādye sukha ādeḥ adhika deśa tve āpādaka abhāvaḥ dvitīye aṇumanassaṃyoge api sva avacchinne adhika deśe ca janayet niyāmaka abhāvāt antye tava api sukha ādeḥ aṇu mātra deśa tā āpattiḥ manaḥ vaibhave api avirodhaḥ ca 
[045,viii]	atha nimitta candana ādi anurodhena sukha ādau nyūna adhika deśa tā nimitta vāyu saṃyogāt iva śabde na tu asamavāyi anurodhāt tathā ca sukha ādikam tad avacchinnaḥ eva utpadyate iti ced hanta tarhi vaibhave api tathā astu na ca vibhukārya asamavāyī sva avacchinne kāryam janayati eva bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ iva śabdam iti candana ādi avacchinne api sukha ādikam utpadyeta iti vācyam tad deśīya candana sukhe hi tad deśīya candana saṃbandha sāpekṣaḥ asamavāyī hetuḥ iti katham tat nirapekṣaḥ tat kuryāt candanam ca sva avacchinne sukha janakam katham svān avacchinne api tat utpādayet katham vā tad deśīya candana sukham tad deśa candana saṃbandha janyam tena vinā eva utpadyeta 
[045,ix_045,x]	atha manaḥ vaibhave sukha ādi utpattau niyataḥ upādhiḥ vācyaḥ tena nānā nimitta samavadhāne api tad avacchedena ekadā sukha daḥkha ādiṣu ekam eva utpadyate na nānā eka avacchedena ekadā ekaḥ eva vibhu viśeṣa guṇaḥ utpadyate iti niyamāt nimittasya tu avacchedaka tve nānā sukha ādikam utpadyeta śabda vat iti ced na śrotre karṇa śaṣkulī avacchedena nānā nimittāt aneka śabda utpādāt anyathā kolāhala grahaḥ na syāt nānā avacchedena ekadā candana dahana ādi saṃbandhe sukha duḥkhayoḥ ca ekadā anubhava siddha tvena iṣṭa āpādanāt na ca tad yaugapadya pratyayaḥ bhramaḥ bādhaka abhāvāt na ca anyatra kramāt atra api krama anumānam anyatra kramasya nimitta krama adhīna tvāt 
[045,xi_045,xii]	evam ca vivāda viṣaya sukha duḥkhāni yugapad utpannā samavāyi kāraṇakāni yugapad utpadyamāna tvāt yugapad utpanna ghaṭa ādi vat abādhita anubhavāt ca na asiddhiḥ etena caraṇa duḥkham yadi śarīra avacchinnā samavāyi hetukam syāt śarīra vyāpakam syāt iti nirastam nimitta samavadhānasya tantra tve asya aprayojaka tvāt anyathā aṇu tva pakṣe śarīra vyāpakam sukha ādi na syāt ābhimānika abhyāsikamāna urathika sukheṣu jñāna icchā prayatna dveṣeṣu ca deśa aniyamaḥ śarīra avayaveṣu yat kriyāyām icchā tad avacchedena prayatnaḥ iti tatra eva ceṣṭā āvaśyaka tvāt aniyata deśa jñāna icchā ādau laghu tvāt ca anyathā aṇu tva pakṣe prayatnasya aṇu deśa tvam śarīra mātra deśa tvam vā syāt 
[045,xiii_046,ii]	anye tu sukha ādau tad nimitta avacchedena ātma manassaṃyogaḥ asamavāyī tanmātra sukha ādi upalambhāt na tu ātma mana ssaṃyoga mātram atiprasaṅgāt iti āhuḥ yāvati yat sukha ādi prāgabhāvaḥ tāvatī eva tad sukha ādikam utpadyate iti apare yat tu tad itara hetu sākalye tad vyāpaka tvena prāgabhāvasya āvaśyaka tvam iti tat na prāgabhāvasya ahetu tva āpatteḥ tad itara hetu sākalye tad abhāvena kārya abhāva abhāvāt 
[046,iii]	etena vyāpakam anavacchinnam na indriya m atiprasaṅgāt iti ākāśe karṇa śaṣkulī vat niyataḥ upādhiḥ vācyaḥ sa ca na śarīram tad avayava mātram vā niyataḥ tad avayavī vā ceṣṭā āśraya mātram vā nānā avayava avacchedena avyāpya vṛtti sukha ādi upalabdheḥ evam ca sūkṣmam indriyam upādhi tvena kalpanīyam tathā ca tat eva manaḥ kim upadheyena vibhunā tatra ca sarve eva hetavaḥ dharmi grāhaka māna bādhitāḥ iti nirastam 
[046,iv]	indriya tvena tasya śarīra mātrasya upādhi tve api nimitta vaśāt sukha ādeḥ niyata deśa tā upapatteḥ na ca ekadā aneka viṣaya indriya saṃbandhe yugapad jñāna anutpattyā indriya sahakāri tayā anumitam manaḥ aṇu tat eva sukha grāhakam indriyam lāghavāt iti tad vaibhava hetavaḥ bādhitāḥ iti vācyam bubhutsā vaśāt karaṇa dharma tvāt vā aṇu tva pakṣe śrotre aneka śabda samavāye api bubhutsita mātra śabda graha vat vyāsaṅga daśāyām yugapad jñāna anutpatteḥ upapatteḥ anyatra dīrgha śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇa ādau yugapad jñāna utpatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt iti 
[046,v_046,vi]	atra ucyate vyāsaṅga daśāyām indriyāṇām sva sva viṣaya saṃbandhe api ekasmāt jñānam na anyasmāt iti anubhava siddham atas yasya asaṃbandhāt na yugapad jñānāni tad indriya sahakāri krameṇa tat adhiṣṭhāyakam manaḥ tat eva sukha ādi grāhakam iti tasya dharmi grāhaka māna bādhitam vibhu tvam tathā hi cākṣuṣa jñānavataḥ maitrasya sva sva viṣaya saṃbaddhāni ghrāṇa rasana tvac śrotrāṇi sva sva viṣaya sākṣātkāra hetu saṃyoga śūnyāni tadānīm sva viṣaya sākṣātkārājanaka tvāt indriya asaṃbaddha ghaṭa vat 
[046,vii]	ekaikam vā pakṣaḥ anyathā hetu sākalye yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ na ca vaibhave api adṛṣṭa vilambāt vilambaḥ tad itara hetu sākalye tasya api sattvāt indriya antara vilopa prasaṅgāt ca na ca bubhutsā vaśāt kramaḥ dṛśyate hi nṛtya darśanavataḥ bubhutsātaḥ abhimata viṣaya antara jñānam iti vācyam sā hi na sva viṣaya jñāne hetuḥ abubhutsite api jñāna udayāt na api anya jñāna pratibandhikā ghaṭa bubhutsāyām api paṭa jñāna udayāt bubhutsā ca kriyā hetu manaḥ gocara prayatna dvārāḥ indriya antarāt ākṛṣya abhimata artha grāhiṇī indriya antare manaḥ niveśayantī bubhutsita grahe hetuḥ anya grahe pratibaṃndhikā ca na tu sākṣāt atas eva bubhutsā sattve api manaḥ gocara praṇidhāna abhāve sā na kiṃcitkarī 
[046,viii]	nanu indriya manassaṃyoga viśeṣaḥ eva viṣaya viśeṣa grahe hetuḥ kalpyatām na ca evam siddha kāraṇa bhāvasya viśeṣa kalpane hetu antara ucchedaḥ tasya api anvaya vyatireki tvāt iti ced na indriya manassaṃyoge hi viśeṣaḥ na jāti rūpaḥ anugata hetu abhāvāt jāti saṃkara prasaṅgāt ca na api sahakāri rūpaḥ tasya eva hetu tā āpatteḥ 
[046,ix]	atha astu karaṇa dharma tvena kriyā kramaḥ ekam karaṇam ekatra ekadā eka avacchedena tulya deśe vai eka jātīyām anekām kriyām na karoti kim tu ekām eva ekatra ityādi viśeṣaṇāt kuṭhāra agni saṃyoga śabdeṣu na vyabhicāraḥ iti ced tarhi cakṣuḥ ādi avacchedena bhinna deśīya śabda vat paramāṇau iva vijātīyām agni saṃyoga vat anekām kriyām kuryāt eva 
[046,x]	atha jñāna karaṇam ekatra ātmani ekadā ekam eva jñānam karoti samūha ālambana karaṇa vat katham anyathā nānā sāmagrī sattve samūha ālambanam ekam yat tu apara jñāna sāmagrī yadi tadā kārya avaśyaṃbhāvaḥ tat asattve kim karaṇa dharma tvena tasya sahakāri antara paryavasāyi tvāt iti tat na samūha ālambana sāmyāt karaṇasya ekadā eka mātra janaka tvena aparājanaka tayā tatra kāraṇa abhāvena eva sāmagrya sattvāt iti ced tarhi pañcasu yat ekam janayati na aparāṇi tatra niyāmakam āstheyam anyathā jñāna janane teṣām kalaham kaḥ samādadhyāt 
[046,xi]	kim ca evam yugapad jñānāni mā abhūvan yugapad jñānam tu kena vāryate eka samūha ālambana vat na ca cākṣuṣa tva ādi jāti saṃkara āpatteḥ na eka jñānam iti vācyam evam hi phala virodhena ekam api jñānam na janayet aviśeṣāt utpadyatām vā cākṣuṣa ādi vijātīyam jñānam sāmagrī sattvāt citra rūpavat phala balāt tatra tathā iti ced tarhi atra phala abhāve hetuḥ kalpyatām anyonya pratibandhakasya tattve vā jñānam eva na syāt na tu eka jñānam iti uktam 
[046,xii]	nanu cakṣuḥ ādi na saṃbhūya jana kam anya viṣaye anyasya asāmarthyāt śītam surabhi śubhram candanam iti atra iva kāraṇa antara anupanayanāt ca na ca sva sva viṣaya jñānāya udyatam indriyam kāraṇa antara sahakārāt tad tad viṣayam ādāya eva sva sva viṣayam jñāpayet iti vācyam bhinna viṣaya pramāṇānām saṃbhūya ajanaka tva niyamāt tat tat indriyam tad tat jñāna aṃśe janakam iti api na viṣayasya aṃśa tvāt iti ced 
[046,xiii]	mā evam na hi indriyāṇām saṃbhūyakāri tvam kim tvā arthaḥ samājaḥ pratyeka jñāna sāmagrī sattvāt ekadā nānā jñāna prasaktau karaṇa dharma tvena manaḥ tāvat gocarām ekām eva jñāna kriyām utpādayet samūha ālambana vat na ca eka kriyā jananadaśāyāma para viṣaya kriyāyām manaḥ na samartham iti katham tām janayet iti vācyam bhinna kriyā āyām asāmarthye api eka kriyāyām sāmarthyāt 
[046,xiv_046,xv]	vastutas tu viśeṣa abhāvāt ekām iva aparām api buddhim janayet aviśeṣāt na ca ekām api iti aneka jñāna utpattiḥ jñānān utpattiḥ vā na tu eka viṣaya jñāna utpattiḥ iti niyāmakam āstheyam samūha ālambane phala balena paraspara apekṣita tvena ekā eva sāmagrī nanu manaḥ aṇu tve katham mandaḥ api bubhutsitaḥ śabdaḥ gṛhyate na anyaḥ atha śabde bubhutsā eva itara graha pratibandhikāḥ agrahasya tad anuvidhānāt ananya gatika kārya darśanāt bubhutsita śabda graha sāmagrī eva vā balavatī iti yadi manyase tadā vaibhave api tatas eva yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ iti ced 
[047,i]	mā evam bubhutsā na rūpa ādi grahe hetuḥ na vai itara grahe pratibandhika iti ukta tvāt kim ca rūpa ādi sakala bubhutsāyām paraspara pratibandhāt ajñānam bubhutsā adhīnasāmagrī balavat tvāt vā sarveṣām jñānam syāt na tu ekasya pañca avadhānasya sarveṣām jñānam bhavati eva iti ced na tatra api krama anumānāt anyathā sarva bubhutsa adhīnapraṇidhāne api anyeṣām katham na syāt nanu aṇu tve api daśabhiḥ paṭhyamānāsu gāthāsu tāvat gocara bubhutsāyām praṇidhāne ca ukta rītyā sarveṣām jñānam ajñānam vā na tu eka jñānam iti ced atra kaścid śrotra manassaṃyoge ātma manassaṃyoge vā kaścid viśeṣaḥ kārya unneyaḥ kiṃcid śabda grahe hetuḥ tad anya grahe pratibandhakaḥ iti 
[047,ii_047,iii]	tat na vaibhave api indriya manassaṃyoga viśeṣasya tathā tve vyāsaṅga upapatteḥ anugata rūpa abhāvena prativyakti pratibandhaka tve hetu tve ca vyabhicārāt saṃyoge ca viśeṣasya jāti tve jāti saṃkaraḥ upādhi tve saḥ eva hetuḥ na manaḥ apare tu pratyakṣa anukūla indriya manassaṃyoga dvārā bubhutsā praṇidhānam ca pratyakṣa hetuḥ iti cākṣuṣa ādi bubhutsita grahe kḷpta tvāt tābhyām śrotre bubhutsita śabda avacchedena manaḥ saṃyujyate iti sa gṛhyate na anyaḥ kvacid praṇidhānam vinā eva tathā anyatra praṇidhāna adhīna kriyayā aśrūyamāṇa śabda avacchinna ātmanaḥ vibhajya bubhutsita śabda avacchedena manaḥ saṃyujyate iti tad grahaḥ na sarvasya iti 
[047,iv_047,v]	tad tuccham yugapad utpadyamānāsu viṃśatau gāthāsu tāvat gocara bubhutsāyām praṇidhāne ca tāvat gāthā avacchedena manassaṃyogāt i ugapad tāsām upalambha prasaṅgāt pratyeka sāmagrī sattvāt nikaṭa āhanyamāna ḍhakka ādi śabdānām śrotra vyāpaka tva niyamāt ca atha yatra kolāhale śrūyamāṇaḥ eva bubhutsita śabda grahaḥ tatra ubhaya śabda avacchedena manassaṃyogāt ubhaya grahaḥ kolāhale tu upekṣā jñānam tat iti tathā atrāpi iti ced tarhi kṛtam anayā kusṛṣṭyā abubhutsite upekṣā jñānam eva astu na ca tat api itas na śabda antaram aśrauṣam iti anubhavāt anyathā vaibhave api vyāsaṅga daśāyām itareṣām upekṣā jñānam eva iti 
[047,vi]	atra ucyate yadi api bubhutsā praṇidhāne na śabda graha mātre sahakāriṇī na vā itara graha pratibandhake tathā api nānā śabda samavāya daśāyām yaḥ śabda grahaḥ tatra tayoḥ tathā bhāvaḥ tathā eva tayoḥ anvaya vyatireka niyamāt yat vā kolāhale śrūyamāṇaḥ eva bubhutsita grahaḥ iti anye api kolāhala tvena tad viṣayāḥ eva bahūnām ca ekadā samavāye yugapad saṃnidhāne vā vyakti grahe tad gata gatvaka tva ādi grahaḥ na bhavati agṛhītaka tva ādi nānā śabdasya kolāhala buddhi viṣaya tvāt tasyām daśāyām bubhutsita śabdaka tva ādi jāti grahe bubhutsā eva śaraṇam eka kālīna bahu śabda bubhutsā ca na hetuḥ vyabhicārāt 
[047,vii_047,viii]	yat tu kolāhalāt anyatra ekadā nānā śabda grahe śrotram na samartham kim tu eka śabda grahe vinigamikā bubhutsā eva iti tat na eka gīyamāna apekṣayā ekadā nānā gīya mānasajātīya gīta ādiṣu sukha ādi vailakṣaṇya anubhavāt atha dīrdha śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇe katham pañca jñānāni kramaḥ tatra iti ced na jñānānām yaugapadya pratyayasya bādhakam vinā pramātvāt vyāsaṅgaḥ bādhakaḥ iti ced tarhi manaḥ avayavi aḥ tu tena saṃkoca vikāsābhyām ubhayam upapadyate iti kecid 
[047,ix_047,x]	tat na yadi hi saṃkoca vikāsa hetuḥ adṛṣṭam tarhi tatas eva tat ubhayam astu kṛtam manasā na api eka pañca bubhutsayā tau bhavataḥ tasyāḥ ahetu tvāt hetu tve vā astu vibhu manaḥ avayavitaḥ laghu tvāt atha yathā kvacid bubhutsayā kvacid tīvra viṣaya indriya saṃnikarṣāt indriya manassaṃyogaḥ evam mana ssaṃkoca vikāsayoḥ bubhutsādikam hetuḥ iti ced tarhi pañca bubhutsāyām praṇidhāne ca sarvadā sarveṣām pañca jñānāni jāyeran pañca avadhāna jñāne kramaḥ eva 
[047,xi]	etena aṇu manaḥ pañcatayam astu avayavitaḥ laghu tvāt bubhutsā ādi vaśāt teṣām ekapañca indriya saṃbandhāt ubhayam upapadyate iti nirastam pañca bubhutsāyām sarveṣām pañca indriya saṃbandhe vyāsaṅga anupapatteḥ katham tarhi dīrgha śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇe gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdān pratyemi iti anuvyavasāyaḥ kramika jñāna pañcatayena yugapad manassaṃnikarṣa abhāvāt iti ced na anu vyavasāyasya ekatva asiddheḥ anuvyavasāyāḥ pañca eva samaya saukṣmyāt teṣām kramaḥ na gṛhyate 
[047,xii]	atha vā kramikā anuvyavasāya āhita saṃskārāt pañca jñāna viṣaya smṛtau anubhava tva āropāt yugapad pratyemi iti anuvyavasāyaḥ vibhu tve hetu abhāvāt ātma manassaṃyoga abhāvāt na ātma sukha ādi upalambhaḥ syāt dravya tvena ātma saṃyogi tva sādhane tu aja saṃyoga siddhau tatas eva tad vibhāgi tve api sarvadā tayoḥ paraspara viruddha saṃyoga vibhāga prasaṅgaḥ 
[047,xiii]	nanu aṇu tve asamavāyi anurodhāt ceṣṭā hetu prayatnasya aṇu deśa tvam śarīra deśa mātra tvam vā syāt na tu śarīra tad ava yava deśa tvam yena kriyā niyamaḥ bhavet niyāmaka abhāvāt na ca nodana abhighātāt iva avyāpinaḥ api prayatnāt śarīra ādi kriyā atiprasaṅgāt evam ekadā viṃśati prayatna abhāvāt katham aṅgulīṣu viṃśatiḥ kriyāḥ na ca yaugapadya bhramaḥ bādhaka abhāvāt yugapad saṃnikarṣa abhāvena aṅgulyaḥ calanti iti samūha ālambana anupapatteḥ viṃśati jñānānām ekadā anu vyavasāya asaṃbhavāt agra paścāt bhāve vinigamaka abhāvāt ca krama utpāde ca bhrū nayana kara caraṇa ādi sakala śarīra avayavānām yugapad vicitra nānā karma samūha rūpam nṛtyam na pratyakṣam syāt tathā ca pratyeka karma janya sukhāt vilakṣaṇa sukha viśeṣaḥ na anubhūyeta iti 
[048,i]	atra brūmaḥ sukhe candana ādi vat cikīrṣā eva niyāmikā yat kriyāyām cikīrṣā sā kriyā tad cikīrṣā janyāt prayatnāt bhavati tatra śarīra kriyā api tad cikīrṣā janyā t aṇu mātra deśāt api prayatnāt bhavati atha vā yasya kriyāyām cikīrṣā tad avacchedena prayatnaḥ utpadyate tena śarīra avacchedena utpanna prayatnāt eva śarīra kriyā evam viṃśati kriyā cikīrṣā janyā t aṇu mātra deśāt api prayatnāt viṃśati kriyāḥ yugapad utpadyante athavā aṅgulī viṃśati kriyāyām cikīrṣā iti viṃśati avacchedena viṃśati prayatna ādi viṃśati kriyā hetavaḥ utpadyante evam nṛtya ādau api etat cikīrṣā anuvidhānāt kriyā prayatnayoḥ adhyavaseyam tat evam aṇu mana ssiddhau tad grāhyāḥ ātma viśeṣa guṇāḥ buddhi sukha ādayaḥ iti na avyāpakam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam 
[048,ii]	nanu vartamānam jñānam na mānasam kiṃtu svayam eva sva vyavahāra hetuḥ svasmin sati eva sva vyavahārāt na tu jñāna antaram apekṣate tad anvayatirekān anuvidhānāt jñāna antara viraha daśāyām sva virahāt eva sva vyavahāra virahāt svatas eva sva vyavahāra upapattau jñāna antara kalpane gauravāt ca ghaṭa ādi vyavahāre jñāna anvaya vyatirekāt aḥ tu tad apekṣā svīyam atītam anāgatam parakīyam ca jñānam sva vyavahāre jñāna antaram apekṣate eva vyavahāra kāle tad abhāvāt jñāna antara anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt ca 
[048,iii_048,iv]	nanu evam icchā ādikam api sva vyavahāra jñānam na apekṣeta jñāna tulya tayā svayam eva sva vyavahāra śakta tvāt iti ced na vyavahārasya jñāna janya tva niyamena icchā ādi vyavahāre jñāna apekṣaṇāt atha jñāna mātram na vyavahāra hetuḥ atiprasaṅgāt kiṃtu vyavahartavya viṣayam iti jñāna vyavahāraḥ api tad viṣaya jñāna antarāt bhavet iti ced satyam svasya eva sva viṣayaka tvāt yat vyavahāra anukūla śakti yogi yat jñānam tasya eva tad viṣayaka tvāt śaktiḥ ca padārtha antaram na kāraṇa tā iti na anyonya āśrayaḥ sva vyavahāre jñānam śaktam iti sva viṣayakam vyavahāra śakti samavāya ādayaḥ ca svabhāvataḥ eva tadīyāḥ saṃbandha antare api anavasthānāt svabhāvaḥ eva śaraṇam 
[048,v_048,vi]	etena bheda niyataḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ katham abhede iti nirastam sva vyavahāra śakta tvasya sva viṣaya tvasya abhede api saṃbhavāt astu vā jñānasya svabhāva viśeṣaḥ eva sva viṣaya tvam saṃbandham vinā eva svabhāva viśeṣāt yathā jñānam ghaṭīyam ghaṭa vyavahāra janana yogyam svīyam api tathā kaḥ asau svabhāva viśeṣaḥ iti ced na ākhyātum aśakyatve api anubhava siddhasya svabhāva viśeṣasya mādhurya ādi viśeṣa vat pratyākhyātum aśakyatvāt yadi api svabhāva viśeṣaḥ iti vākyena ākhyāyate eva tathā api padena ākhyātum aśakyatvāt 
[048,vii]	atha vyavahāraḥ vyavahartavya bhinna jñāna sādhyaḥ katham tena vinā syāt iti ced na vyavahāram prati vyavaharta vyajñāna tvena hetu tvāt na tu vyavahartavya bhinna jñāna tvena gauravāt samūha ālambanam ca ekaika vyavahāra janaka tvāt ekaika viṣayakam api na tu samūha viṣayakam eva atiriktasya tasya asattvena saṃnikarṣa abhāvāt 
[048,viii]	bhrama sthale rajata vyavahāra anukūlā śaktiḥ asti eva rajata jñāne kim tu doṣāt abhibhūtā eva sā jāyate iti na tayā rajate vyavahāraḥ rajata jñānam na śuktau pravartakam kim tu indriya janyam idaṃjñānam eva rajata arthi pravṛtti artham tu upasthita rajata bheda agraham apekṣate iti rajata jñānam kāraṇa tāvacchedakam evam ca sva viṣaya tvam sva prakāśa tvam na tu sva vyavahāre jñāna antara anapekṣa tvam gauravāt anyathā jñānasya svāviṣaya tvena saṃskāra abhāvāt smaraṇam na syāt 
[048,ix_048,x]	yat tu sva vyavahāre jñāna antara anapekṣa tvam uktam tad sva prakāśa tva nirvāhaka tayā pramāṇam ca sva prakāśe pratyakṣam eva sarvāḥ pratītaye idam aham jānāmi iti evam ākārāḥ jñātāram jñānam jñeyam ca ullikhantyaḥ jāyante tatra ātmā kartṛ tvena jñeyam karma tayā jñānam kriyā tvena bhāsate atas jñātṛ jñeya sva viṣayam jñānam anubhūyate iti tripuṭī pratyakṣa vādinaḥ 
[048,xi]	nanu idam iti vyāvasāyaḥ tat uttaram idam aham jānāmi iti anuvyavasāyaḥ mānasaḥ iti ced na sva prakāśa tvena upapattau jñāna antara kalpane gauravāt pariśeṣāt ca sva prakāśa tvam para prakāśa tve hi jñānam eva na sidhyet māna abhāvāt na hi tatra jñāta tā liṅgam atīta anāgatayoḥ tad abhāvāt na api mānasam pratyakṣam ajijñāsitasya mānasa tve jñāna avirāmāt anavasthānāt viṣaya antara asaṃcārat ca jijñāsitasya grāhya tve jñānam na mānasam jijñāsā grāhi a ātma dharma tvāt saṃskāra vat iti anumāna pratirodhaḥ atas eva jijñāsām vinā eva sukha ādīnām mānasa tvam 
[048,xii_048,xiii]	jijñāsā api jñāna sādhya iti anavasthā dharmi jñāna icchā ādibhiḥ jñānasya nāśāt ca na pratyakṣa tvam atha jñānam mānasa pratyakṣam pratyakṣa ātma guṇa tvāt ātma viśeṣa guṇa tve sati kṣaṇa mātra sthāyi tvāt sukha vat jñānam pratyakṣa janaka indriya saṃnikarṣa āśrayaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt sukha vat iti ced na mānasa tve anavasthānāt 
[049,i_049,ii]	atas eva cakṣuḥ janyam jñānam na cakṣuḥ janya jñāna viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt rāsana vat na etat jñāna viṣayaḥ vā etat janaka indriya saṃnikarṣān āśraya tvāt gagana vat cakṣuḥ na cākṣuṣa jñāna grāhakam bahis indriya tvāt rasana vat iti pratipakṣa anumānam apāstam para prakāśa tve anavasthayā jñāna asiddhau āśraya asiddheḥ sva prakāśa tvena tad siddhau dharmi grāhaka māna bādhāt kim ca sva vyavahāra śakta tvam sva viṣaya tvam tat ca sva saṃnikarṣā janya tve svājanya tve ca na viruddham na ca sva vyavahāre śakta tvasya abhāvaḥ eva sādhyaḥ aprayojaka tvāt sva saṃnikarṣā janye svājanye vyavahāra śakte ghaṭa ādau vyabhicārāt ca 
[049,iii]	atas eva sva prakāśa tvena pūrva anubhava viṣaya tā tat tānubhūta mātra viṣaye smaraṇe utsargataḥ bhāsate jñāna antarasya anāvaśyaka tvāt svasya svājanya tve katham sva karmatā iti ced na atīta anāgatayoḥ iva sva viṣaya tvam na tu karma tvam viṣaya tvam ca abhede api sva vyavahāra śakta tvasya jñāna svabhāva viśeṣasya vā viṣaya tvāt na ca adhīkarma tayā śaśaśrṛṅga vat asattvam tasya kadāpi aprakāśāt dhī janya vyavahāra bhāgi tvam karma tvam sva prakāśe api tad anya phala bhāgi tvam ca ghaṭe api asiddham jñāta tā niṣedhāt jñāna anapekṣa indriya saṃnikarṣa jam jñānam pratyakṣam atas sarvam jñānam jñāna anapekṣa ātma manassaṃnikarṣa janya tvena sva ātmani pratyakṣam viśiṣṭa pratyakṣam ca na viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam nirvikalpaka niṣedhāt 
[049,iv_049,v]	sa vikalpaka tvena jñāna ajanya jñānam vā pratyakṣam tena nirvikalpaka janyam jāti viśiṣṭa jñānam pratyakṣam na tu asādhāraṇa indriya ādi karaṇakam tena vinā api anumiti ādau sva ātma prakāśāt indriya ādikam tu artha prakāśaḥ eva hetuḥ tasya eva tad pratibaddha hetu janya tvāt iti atra ucyate pratyakṣam na sva prakāśe pramāṇam vyavasāyānām idam aham jānāmi iti ākāra asiddheḥ na ca evam anubhava virodhaḥ artha niścayena pravṛtti ādi darśanāt vyavasāyasya artha viṣaya tva mātram anubhūyate na tu sva viṣaya tvam api gauraveṇa tasya sva viṣaya bhāna tayā pravṛtti ahetutvāt anubhavaḥ api idam rajatam iti ādi eva 
[049,vi_049,vii]	na ca evam idam aham jānāmi iti anubhava apalāpe upekṣaṇīyatā vyavasāya uttara kālam tad upagamāt idam rajatam iti ādi laukika anubhavāt vyavasāyasya tat ākāra tām niṣedhāmaḥ na tu anuvyavasāyasya nanu bhinna anuvyavasāye anavasthānāt vyavasāyaḥ eva anuvyavasāyaḥ iti ced tarhi para prakāśe bādhakāt sva prakāśa tva siddhau sarva pratītīnām idam aham jānāmi iti ākāra tā siddhiḥ tathā ca sva prakāśa tva asiddhau sarva pratītīnām idam aham jānāmi iti ākāra tvam asiddham iti na sā pratītiḥ sva prakāśa tve pramāṇam 
[049,viii]	api ca kriyāyāḥ kṛteḥ vā samavāyi tvam kartṛ tvam para samaveta kriyā phala śali tvam karaṇa vyāpāra viṣaya tvam vā karma tvam dhātvartha tvam anyat vā kriyā tvam idam aham jānāmi iti vyavasāye na bhāsate tad bodhaka indriya saṃnikarṣa abhāvāt kim tu idaṃviṣaya ka jñāna tva viśiṣṭasya jñānasya vaiśiṣṭyam ātmani bhāsate na ca sva prakāśe vyavasāye tādṛśam svasya vaiśiṣṭyam bhāsitum arhati pūrvam viśeṣaṇasya tasya ajñānāt tasmāt idam aham jānāmi iti na vyavasāyaḥ kiṃtu anuvyavasāyaḥ 
[049,ix]	syāt etat kartṛ tva ādi jñāna vaiśiṣṭyam ātmani mā jñāyi vyavahārasya sva viṣaya ka jñāna sādhya tva siddhau tat eva jñānam sva viṣayakam kalpyate lāghavāt jñāna vitti vedyaḥ ātmā api tad viṣayaḥ iti ātma viṣaya tvam sarva vittīnām iti ced na sva janaka indriya saṃnikarṣān āśraya tvena svasya svāviṣaya tvāt viṣaya tva niyāmaka indriya saṃnikarṣa ādeḥ abhāve sva viṣaya tva anupapatteḥ kāraṇam vinā kārya anutpādāt pratyakṣa ajanakasya pratyakṣa viṣaya tva anupapateḥ ca ātma dharma pratyāsatti anāśraye pratyakṣa viṣaya tāyāḥ janakatva vyāpta tvāt jñānasya pratyakṣa tvena indriya saṃnikarṣa āśraya tvāt manassaṃnikarṣa janya tvena māna satvam 
[049,x_049,xi]	tat ayam prayogaḥ vivāda adhyāsitam indriya janyam jñānam na etat jñāna viṣaya āśrayaḥ etat janaka indriya saṃnikarṣān āśraya tvāt etat ajanaka tvāt vā asaṃnikṛṣṭa vat na etat jñāna viṣayakam vā ātma dharma pratyāsatti anāśraya tve sati etat ajanya tve ca sati sākṣātkāri tvāt pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ jñānam sva pratyakṣa janaka indriya saṃnikarṣa āśrayaḥ pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt iti manassaṃnikarṣa grāhyam cākṣuṣam jñānam na cakṣuḥ janya jñāna viṣayaḥ cakṣuḥ asaṃnikṛṣṭa tvāt ghaṭa vat jñānam prameyam eva iti vyāpti jñānam jñāna tva pratyāsattyā sva viṣayam īśvara jñānam ahetuka tvena sarva viṣaya tvāt sva prakāśam 
[049,xii]	nanu para prakāśaka tve jñānam eva na sidhyet anavasthānāt iti dharmi grāhaka mānāt sva prakāśa tva siddhau ananya gatika tayā svasya asaṃnikṛṣṭasya api pratyakṣa viṣaya tvam atas dharmi grāhaka māna bādhitāḥ tvadīya hetavaḥ iti ced na vitteḥ avaśya vedya tva abhāvena anavasthā vigamāt saṃyukta samavāyena manaḥ vedya tva abhāvāt apekṣaṇīya antara abhāvāt ca utpannā eva kutas na avaśya vedyā iti ced na sukha ādi tad buddhi ādi sāmagryā pratibandhāt viṣaya antara saṃcāra darśanena tasyāḥ balavat tvāt anudbhavāt iti kecid 
[049,xiii]	yogi ātma viśeṣa guṇa tvāt jñāna tvāt jñānam pratyakṣam eva iti vyāpteḥ vitteḥ avaśya vedya tvena sva prakāśa tvam iti ced na vyāpteḥ asiddheḥ para prakāśaka tve anavasthānāt sva prakāśe kāraṇa anupapatteḥ saṃnikṛṣṭam eva pratyakṣam tat viṣaya janyam eva pratyakṣam iti vyāpteḥ ca anyathā kāraṇam vinā kāryān utpatti vyāpteḥ vinigamakam kāraṇa sattve api pratibandhāt kārya anutpāde kāraṇa tvam apratyūhyam kḷpta kāraṇam vinā kārya utpāde kāraṇa tā bhaṅgaḥ kārya anutpādaḥ ca 
[049,xiv_049,xv]	api ca para prakāśe anavasthānāt pariśeṣa anumānena jñānasya sva prakāśa tvam tathā ca sva prakāśa tva anumiteḥ api sva prakāśa tvam anum iti antaragamyam evam tasya api iti anavasthā sva prakāśa tva anumiti paramparā dvārā tava api syāt viṣaya antara saṃcārasya pratibandhaka tvam yāvat jijñāsam vā sva prakāśa tva anumitiḥ iti yadi tulyam para prakāśa tve api na ca jñānam sva prakāśam iti anumityā sva prakāśa tvam api sāmānya pratyāsattyā viṣayīkṛtam iti vācyam paratas pakṣe api tulya tvāt tvayā tad anabhyupagamāt ca 
[050,i]	kim ca anum iti ādau jāti saṅkarāt na pratyakṣa tvam na ca jñāna sāpekṣam manaḥ janakam iti anumiti viṣaya vat ātmani na tat pratyakṣam tasya sva viṣaya tve jñānān apekṣā iti ced na jñānam jñāna janyam tat ca sva viṣaye sva ātmani ekam eva iti katham tad apekṣam tad anapekṣam ca viruddha tvāt na ca jñāna bhinna viṣaya tvam sa apekṣam tathā tve bahis jñānam pratyakṣam na syāt 
[050,ii]	atha anyasya anya viṣaya tve saṃnikarṣa ādiḥ niyāmakaḥ sva viṣaya tve kim tena anatiprasaṅgāt saṃnikarṣasya ananugamāt ca vyavahāre śakta tvam viṣaya tvam abhede saṃnikarṣam vinā api iti ced na anyatra pratyakṣa mātre saṃnikarṣasya hetu tvāt anyathā ananugamāpattiḥ atha yā vittiḥ na vedyā sā pramāṇa abhāvāt asatī iti tad adhīna sattvasya viṣaya paryantasya asattvam syāt iti ced na avirala lagna tad vitti vitti dhārā na abhyupeyate kim nāma kenacid kadācid kācid vittiḥ vyavahāra smaraṇa liṅga ādinā pratīyate iti sarvā pramāṇa siddhā eva iti abhyupagamāt 
[050,iii]	atha syāt evam yadi ghaṭaḥ ayam ghaṭam aham jānāmi iti atas adhikā ghaṭa vat vitti dhārā vāhi viṣaya śata bhāra mantharā kācid vittiḥ asmad ādeḥ utpadyamānā anubhūyeta na ca evam iti ced na anuvyavasāyaḥ viṣaya mātra nirūpyaḥ na tu tad viṣaya paraṃparā nirūpyaḥ gauravāt tathā ca jñāna jñāna tvena sarvāḥ vittiḥ asmad ādeḥ utpadyamānāḥ anubhūyate eva na ca evam anirmokṣaḥ yoga ja dharma pratyāsattyā sāmānya lakṣaṇayā vā vyāpti jñāna rūpasya ananu vyavasāyasya api sva viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt na ca tad vyavahāra śakta tvam tat viṣaya tvam tad viṣaya tvena tad vyavahāra kāraṇa tva grahe sati tad śakta tva jñānam tad śakta tvam ca tat viṣaya tvam iti anyonya āśrayāt kāraṇa tva graham vinā śakteḥ agrahāt tvad mate api rajata jñānasya śukti viṣaya tva āpatteḥ ca rajata arthi pravṛttau rajata jñānam hetuḥ na tu tad avacchedakam iti ukta tvāt lāghavena sva viṣaye jñānasya pravartaka tvam sarvaiḥ eva adya pravṛttau tathā avagamāt iti ced hanta evam anyathā ākhyātiḥ astu na tu anyathā siddha rajata jñānasya apravartaka tvam iti 
[050,iv_050,v]	etena yathā tad guṇa saṃvijñāna bahu vrīhi siddham kuṭādi padam aśakyam api kuṭam gaṇam ādāya eva pradhānam anya padārtham bodhayati tathā jñānam aviṣayam api ātmānam ādāya eva sva viṣaye vyavahāram karoti saṃskāram ca sva janya vyavahāra viṣaye jñānasya saṃskāra janaka tvāt sva janya vyavahāra viṣayaḥ sva ātmā viṣayaḥ ca iti prācīnam guru matam apāstam anyatra lāghavena jñānasya sva viṣaye vyavahāra saṃskāra janaka tva kalpanāt sva viṣaye sva ātmani vyavahāra saṃskāra ajanaka tvāt vyavahāra saṃskārayoḥ sva viṣaya jñāna sādhya tvena sva aviṣayaka jñāna asādhya tvāt 
[050,vi]	nanu jñānasya mānasa tve katham jānāmi iti viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ jñāna tva nirvikalpaka janya jñā na kṣaṇe viśeṣya abhāvena pratyakṣān utpatteḥ iti ced na jñāna nā śa kṣaṇe eva jñāne jñāna tva viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ viśeṣyasya pūrva kṣaṇa sattvāt pratyakṣe sva samaya varti tayā gauraveṇa viśeṣyasya ahetutvāt jānāmi iti vartamāna tvena sthūlaḥ upādhiḥ bhāsate na tu kṣaṇaḥ tasya atīndriya tvāt tatas jñāna viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ ātmani viśeṣaṇa jñānasya pūrva sattvāt viśeṣaṇam ca na viśiṣṭa pratyaya hetuḥ gauravāt kim tu tat jñānam āvaśyaka tvāt atas eva tat tām vinā api tad buddheḥ pratyabhijñā 
[050,vii]	yat tu vyavasāyana aśakṣaṇa utpanna vyavasāya antare jñāna tva viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ iti tat na tad hetoḥ abhāvāt anuminomi iti ādau anuvyavasāye anumiti tva abhāvāt ca yat vā jñānam jñāna tvam ca nirvikalpake bhāsate tatas jñāna tva vaiśiṣṭyam jñāne jñāna vaiśiṣṭyam ca ātmani bhāsate viśeṣye viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇa antaram ca bhāsate iti eva hi viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya arthaḥ 
[050,viii]	vastutas tu jñānam abhāvaḥ iva viśiṣṭa jñāna viṣayaḥ eva anuvyavasāyasya viṣaya rūpa viśeṣaṇa viṣaya kavya vasāya sādhya tvena viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagrī sattvāt jñāna tvam api tatra bhāsate tad jñāna sāmagrī sattvāt aṃśe tad sa prakārakam niṣprakārakam ca iti narasiṃha ākāram tatra eva viśiṣṭa jñāne jñāna tva vaiśiṣṭyam bhāsate anuminomi iti ādau tu na tathā anuvyavasāye anumiti tva abhāvāt iti 
[050,ix]	tat ca pratyakṣam dvividham nirvikalpakam sa vikalpakam ca iti tatra nāma jāti ādi yojanā rahitam vaiśiṣṭyānavagāhi niṣprakārakam nirvikalpakam nanu jñāna tvam sa vikalpaka bhinna vṛtti iti atra kim mānam na pratyakṣam asiddheḥ atīndriya tva abhyupagamāt ca na ca vyavahāraḥ tasya sa vikalpaka sādhya tvāt na api idam na vivecitam pūrvam adhunā vivecayāmi iti anubhava pramāṇaka ava ālocana vikalpau bahu viśeṣaṇa jñāna ajñānābhyām tad upapatteḥ 
[050,x]	nanu gauḥ iti pratyakṣam viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt anumiti vat iti atha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya jñāna sāmagrītaḥ sa ākāṅkṣa ubhaya viṣayam ekam viśiṣṭa jñānam tatra pratyakṣe yogya indriya saṃnikarṣāt anumitau pakṣa dharma tā balāt vyāpaka tva avacchedaka prakāreṇa śābde yogyatā ādi vaśāt padārtha tāvacchedaka rūpeṇa apūrvam eva viśeṣaṇam bhāsate upamitau api evam eva iti na kvāpi viśeṣaṇa jñānam janakam na ca pratyabhijñāyām tat ta anubhavaḥ tathā tat tānubhave api saṃskārasya anudbodhāt vilopāt vā pratyabhijñāna anutpādena udbuddhaḥ saṃskāraḥ eva pratyāsatti tayā viśeṣaṇa jñāna artham indriya sahakārī surabhi candanam iti ādau api viśeṣaṇa jñāna artham tat jñānam pratyāsatti sthānīyam indriya sahakāri bhramaḥ viśiṣṭa jñānam eva na asti iti ced 
[050,xi]	ucyate sādhya prasiddhi padārtha upasthiti vācya tva jñāna tatta anubhavānām anum iti ādi hetu tvam sādhya prasiddhi ādikam vinā anumiti ādeḥ asaṃbhavāt sādhya ādikam ca viśeṣaṇam iti tat jñāna manum iti ādi hetuḥ yadi api anumiti ādi pratyekam prati sādhya ādi viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena na kāraṇa tā tathā api viśiṣṭa jñāna mātram prati viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena kāraṇa tā bādhaka abhāvāt 
[051,i]	syāt etat vahnimān itya ādi jñānam prati vahni jñānasya na viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena kāraṇa tā dravya tvena vahni jñāne api vahnimān iti jñāna abhāvāt kim tu viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñāna tvena atas na viśiṣṭa jñāne viśeṣaṇa jñānam hetuḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvam api tatra asti iti ced na tasya atiprasakta tvāt anyathā siddheḥ ca na ca tādṛśa viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvam sādhyam bādhāt iti 
[051,ii_051,iii]	tat na viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñānam prati hi viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakārakam jñānam kāraṇam ubhaya siddham atas viśiṣṭa jñāna mātram prati viśeṣaṇa jñānam hetuḥ yad viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad sāmānyayoḥ api bādhakam vinā kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamāt anyathā sāmānya kārya ucchedaḥ na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa sāmagrī viraheṇa tad tad kārya viśeṣān udayāt na ca parokṣa tvam upādhiḥ pratyabhijñāyām sādhya avyāpaka tvāt na api viśiṣṭa viśeṣaṇaka tvam pakṣa itara tvāt iti mā evam tava api smṛti vat pūrva anubhavasya saṃskāra dvārā janaka tvāt siddha sādhanāt na ca avyavahita viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvam sādhyam aprayojaka tvāt pratyabhijñāvat smṛtyā eva upapatteḥ vā na api tatas eva avyavahita viśeṣaṇa anubhava janya tvam sādhyam aprasiddheḥ pratyabhijñāna ādau vyabhicārāt ca
