[051,iv]	atha tad kāla utpanna rūpa ādi viśiṣṭa pratyakṣe saṃskāra abhāvena smaraṇa abhāvāt pakṣa dharmatā balena nirvikalpaka siddhau anyatra api sāmagrī taulyāt tad siddhiḥ iti ced na pratyutpanna viśeṣaṇa sthale hi śukla tva ādi viśiṣṭa śukla vaiśiṣṭya bodhaḥ vā aviśiṣṭa tad viśiṣṭa bodhaḥ vā ādye śukla tva ādi smaraṇam prathamam tatas pratyakṣeṇa tad viśiṣṭa śukla bodhaḥ tatas śukla tva ādi viśiṣṭa śuklāḥ divaiśiṣṭya bodhaḥ dravyaḥ iti kim anupapannam śukla tva ādi jāti smaraṇam eva vā sāmānya lakṣaṇayā sakala rūpa ādi viṣayam astu dvitīye ananubhavaḥ na hi śukla tva ādi pratyaya vilakṣaṇam śukla rūpa ādi viśiṣṭa bodham kaścid anubhavati 
[051,v^1]	atha jāgara ādi aviśiṣṭa anubhavaḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyaḥ viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt na ca tatra saṃskāra dvārā pūrva viśeṣaṇa anubhavaḥ tad janya viśeṣaṇa smaraṇam vā tatra saṃbhavati udbodhakam vinā saṃskārasya smaraṇe viśiṣṭa bodhe vā sāmarthya abhāvāt iti udbodhakam vaktavyam udbodhakam ca anyatra jñānam dṛṣṭam iti tat eva vācyam na ca tad viśiṣṭa jñānam eva tatra api viśeṣaṇa jñāna apekṣāyām anavasthā patteḥ iti ālocana siddhiḥ iti tat na sati api jñāne saṃskārān udbodhāt yasmāt phalam bhavati sa jñāna viśeṣaḥ tathā iti ced 
[051,v^2]	na ananugata tvāt yad anantaram phalam dṛśyate tat eva ananugatam api udbodhakam kalpyate phala balāt iti ced tarhi jāgara kāraṇa anantaram saṃskāra udbodhaḥ asti iti tat eva kāraṇam astu kḷpta tvāt atas eva saṃskāra udbodhe na niyataḥ hetuḥ iti sadṛśa adṛṣṭa cintā ādyāḥ smṛti bodhakā iti āhuḥ evam ca praṇidhāna ādi sūtram api saṃgacchate api ca viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt iti atra vyavacchedyam aviśiṣṭa jñānam tat ca aprasiddham siddhau vā vyartham anumānam jñāna tvam ca svataḥ asiddha vyāptikam nirvikalpake vyabhicārāt anavasthā pātāt ca 
[051,vi]	kim ca viśiṣṭa jñāna tvam na tāvat vastu gatyā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya viṣaya ka jñāna tvam ālocanena vyabhicārāt na api viśeṣaṇa tva viṣayaka tvam atad vyāvṛtti bodha janaka jñāna viṣaya tvasya viśeṣaṇa tvasya tatra aprakāśāt na api vaiśiṣṭya viṣaya ka jñāna tvam tathā sati gauḥ iti vikalpe vaiśiṣṭyam viśeṣaṇam iti ālocanasya api tad viṣaya tvena viśiṣṭa jñāna tve anavasthā pātāt iti 
[051,vii]	na api sa prakāraka jñāna tvam prakāraḥ ca viṣaya tā viśeṣaḥ iti vācyam jñāna viṣaya svarūpa atiriktāyāḥ viṣaya tāyāḥ abhāvāt na ca viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvam sa prakāra tvam yad viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam yat saḥ eva tatra prakāraḥ iti gauḥ iti vikalpe tasya eva sādhya tvāt īśvara jñānasya niṣprakāraka tva āpātāt ca na api atad vyāvṛtti viṣaya tvam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvam apohavāt anirāsena gauḥ iti vikalpe tathā tva asiddheḥ na api atad vyāvṛtti bodha janaka tvam tat ālocana vyāvṛtta anugata rūpam antareṇa atad vyāvṛtta bodha janaka tvasya grahītum aśakyatvāt na ca gauḥ iti jñānam etat anya sa vikalpakāni ajñāna bhinnam prameya tvāt yat vā cakṣuḥ cākṣuṣa sa vikalpaka jñāna atirakta jñāna janakam indriya tvāt iti tad siddhiḥ aprayojaka tvāt ubhayatra sa vikalpaka pada anantaram nirvikalpaka ādi pada prakṣepeṇa tṛtīya ādi jñāna siddhi prasaṅgāt ca iti 
[051,viii_051,ix]	atra ucyate prāthamikam gauḥ iti pratyakṣam jñānam janya viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam janya viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt anumiti vat na ca smaraṇam tatra saṃbhavati tad janmani tena go tvasya ananubhavāt atha yathā bālasya adya pravṛtti balāt prāc bhavīya saṃskārāt vyāpti smaraṇam tathā iha api janmāntarīya saṃskārāt go tva smaraṇam astu prāthamika viśiṣṭa jñāna balāt iti ced na jīvana adṛṣṭena tatra saṃskāra udbodhāt tathā astu iha tu na vilakṣaṇam udbodhakam asti atas go tva asaṃnikarṣe api go tva smaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ yaḥ eva go tva indriya saṃnikarṣaḥ tava nirvikalpake hetuḥ saḥ eva saṃskāra udbodhakaḥ iti ced tarhi atra kḷpta kāraṇa bhāvāt go tva indriya saṃnikarṣāt go tva anubhavaḥ eva syāt smaraṇa sāmagrītaḥ anubhava sām agryāḥ balavat tvāt na ca tad viśiṣṭa jñānam pūrvam viśeṣaṇa jñāna abhāvāt iti arthān nirvikalpakam atas eva na tatra jñāna tvena viśiṣṭa jñāna tva anumānam kāraṇa bādhena bādhāt yadi ca anubhava sām agrītaḥ smaraṇam tadā nityānām vaidika arthānām ca smaraṇam syāt na tu anubhavaḥ 
[051,x_052,i]	na ca go tva jñānam go tva jñāna janyam janya jñāna janyam janya viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam ca iti anyatra darśanāt prathamam na go tva anubhavaḥ iti vācyam ekasya eva janya janaka tvā anavacchedaka tvāt anavasthā pātāt ca nanu gauḥ iti atra go tva vaiśiṣṭyam gavi bhāsate tathā ca tat viṣayakam jñānam syāt tat ca nirvikalpakam iti ced go tvam hi tatra viśeṣaṇam na tu tad vaiśiṣṭyam nanu tathābhūta viśeṣaṇa dhī janya viśiṣṭa jñāne viśeṣaṇam svadharma viśiṣṭam katham bhāseta pūrvam tasya anavagamāt avagame vā tasya api viśeṣaṇa antaravataḥ viśeṣaṇam iti anavasthā iti ced na gauḥ iti viśiṣṭa jñāne viśiṣṭasya go tvasya ābhānāt 
[052,ii]	atha sarvam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇa vat eva go tva ādau api vyakti ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tvāt iti ced astu tathā kim tu viśeṣaṇam viśeṣaṇa vat eva bhāseta iti na niyamaḥ anyathā gauḥ iti jñāne viśeṣaṇa tad viśeṣaṇa ananta paraṃpara aviṣaya tve viṣaya aparyavasāna prasaṅgaḥ kvacid nirviśeṣaṇasya api bhāne prathamatas api tathā syāt aviśeṣāt na ca viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt iti atra hetoḥ vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam yena viśeṣaṇena vinā vyāptiḥ grahītum na śakyate tasya eva sārthaka tvāt vyabhicāra vārakasya api sārthaka tve etat eva mūlam iha api jñāna tva viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvayoḥ viśeṣaṇam vinā vyāptiḥ grahītum na śakyate anavasthānāt sāmānyatas vyabhicāra avagamāt 
[052,iii_052,iv]	atas eva cakṣuḥ taijasa tva ādi sādhane rūpa ādiṣu madhye rūpasya eva vyañjaka tvāt ityādau asiddhivārakam api viśeṣaṇam sārthakam tena vinā rūpasya eva vyañjaka tva āditi asya aprasiddheḥ vyāpti agrahāt viśeṣaṇam vinā api yatra vyāpti grahaḥ tatra vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam yathā nīladhūma tva śarīra ajanya tva ādau yasya yatra yaḥ saṃbandhaḥ saḥ eva tatra tasya vaiśiṣṭyam tena hi sva asaṃbaddhebhyaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ bodhyate yathā daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti jñāne daṇḍa saṃbandhaḥ puruṣe avagataḥ iti tena ayam adaṇḍa vyāvṛttaḥ bodhyate tathā gauḥ iti vikalpe api tathā ca viśeṣaṇa vat viśeṣya jñāna tvam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvam etat eva ātad vyāvṛtta bodha janaka tā avacchedakam 
[052,v]	nanu daṇḍa puruṣa saṃbandhāḥ iti atra api daṇḍa saṃbandhaḥ puruṣe avagataḥ iti tatas api adaṇḍa vyāvṛtta puruṣa bodhaḥ syāt iti ced bhavati eva daṇḍa saṃbandhaḥ eva puruṣe daṇḍa jñānam vinā na jñāyate iti brūmaḥ yatra viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagrī na asti tatra nirvikalpakam jñāna karaṇa janye sarvatra viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvāt na tat iti pratyakṣam eva etat iti 
[052,vi]	atas eva abhāve na nirvikalpakam tad buddhau pratiyogi adhikaraṇa jñānayoḥ kāraṇa tvena tad ubhaya viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagrī niyamāt yadi abhāve na nirvikalpakam tadā ghaṭa abhāvavat bhū talam iti jñānam na syāt viśeṣaṇa jñānam vinā tad abhāvāt bhāve vā na nirvikalpaka siddhiḥ viśiṣṭa jñāna tvasya tatra eva vyabhicārāt iti ced na prathamam bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti buddhiḥ tatra bhū talam viśeṣaṇam abhāvaḥ viśeṣyaḥ viśeṣya jñānam ca na kāraṇam paścāt bhū tala viśeṣyakam ghaṭa abhāva vat iti jñānam 
[052,vii_052,viii]	nanu indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tayā abhāvaḥ gṛhyate iti uktam atas katham sa viśeṣyaḥ iti ced bhū tala viśeṣaṇa tayā svabhāva pratyāsattyā gṛhyate iti tad arthaḥ na tu abhāvasya viśeṣaṇa tayā bhāmam iti atas eva vāyau rūpa abhāvaḥ iti pratīteḥ cākṣuṣa tvam uktam ācāryaiḥ ayogya viśeṣye indriyasya asāmarthyāt jñāna tve ca nirvikalpakam viṣaya viśiṣṭa tva aṃśe sa vikalpakam api anuvyavasāyasya vyavasāya janya tvena niyamataḥ pūrvam viṣaya rūpa viśeṣaṇa bhānāt tatra eva jñāne tat eva jñānam niṣprakārakam sa prakārakam ca iti na viruddham aṃśa bhedam ādāya avirodhāt atas eva nirvikalpaka tva savikalpaka tve na jātī cākṣuṣa tva ādinā saṃkara āpatteḥ gauḥ iti sa vikalpakam api go tva aṃśe nirvikalpakam eva tatra prakāra ābhānāt bhāne vā anavasthā nirvikalpakā siddhiḥ ca 
[052,ix_052,x]	prakāraḥ ca dvividhaḥ viśeṣaṇa upalakṣaṇa bhedāt nanu vyāvartaka tva aviśeṣe katham tayoḥ bhedaḥ vyāvartaka tve sati sat viśeṣaṇam asat upalakṣaṇam yathā daṇḍī puruṣaḥ kuruṇā kṣetram iti ced na kāka vat devadatta gṛham jaṭābhiḥ tāpasaḥ iti ādau upari bhrāmyataḥ kākasya jaṭā ādeḥ asattve api aviśeṣaṇa tvāt upalakṣaṇa tvāt ca 
[052,xi_052,xii]	etena vyāvṛtti bodha kāle vyāvartakam sat viśeṣaṇam asat upalakṣaṇam tena kāka ādīnām vyāvṛtti bodha samaye satām viśeṣaṇa tvam eva vyāvṛtti bodha samaye asatām upalakṣaṇa tvam atas eva kākaiḥ jaṭābhiḥ kuruṇā iti ādau itthaṃbhūta lakṣaṇe tṛtīyā iti nirastam vyāvṛtti bodha samaye sataḥ api upari bhramataḥ kāka ādeḥ aviśeṣaṇa tvāt upalakṣaṇa tvāt ca 
[052,xiii]	na api viśeṣya vṛtti tve sati pratyāyya vyāvṛtti samāna adhikaraṇa tve sati vyāvartakam viśeṣaṇam yat vā yatra viśeṣya tva avacchedena vyāvṛttyā vā yad samāna adhikaraṇa tvena pratīyate tatra tad viśeṣaṇam viśeṣya tvam ca pratyāyya vyāvṛtti adhikaraṇam iti jaṭābhiḥ tāpasaḥ iti ādau jaṭā dau atiprasaṅgāt na hi tāpase na jaṭā vartate 
[052,xiv_052,xv]	na api viśeṣya samāna vibhaktika tvam viśeṣaṇa tvam kāka vat devadatta gṛham iti ādau upalakṣaṇe api gata tvāt anabhidhāna daśa āyāma viśeṣaṇatva apātāt ca atha vyāvartaka tve sati viśiṣṭa dhī viṣaya tvam viśeṣaṇa tvam viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ ca na viśeṣaṇa tva gocarāḥ gauravāt kiṃtu viśeṣaṇa viṣayā viśeṣaṇa upalakṣaṇa saṃdeha anupapatteḥ 
[053,i]	atas eva cākṣuṣa tva ādi virodhaḥ upalakṣaṇa tve tu upalakṣitam saṃsthāna ādi viśiṣṭa dhī viṣayaḥ na kākavat tvam tad abhāve api tad gṛha pratīteḥ tādrūpyāt anyathā bhramatvā āpatteḥ na ca śabda upasthāpitasya katham śābda jñāna bahirbhāvaḥ iti vācyam tathā eva vyutpatteḥ na hi gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti atra pravāhaḥ api tīra avacchedaka tayā bhāsate kiṃtu tīra tvena tīra viśeṣaḥ eva anyathā ajahatsva artha asāmyāt na ca evam upalakṣaṇa padasya lākṣaṇika tvam aśakyasya saṃsthāna ādeḥ upasthāpanāt iti vācyam upalakṣaṇa buddhi upasthāpita kāraṇa antara janya saṃsthāna upasthityā tad anvaye tātparyāt iti 
[053,ii_053,iv]	mā evam tathā vyutpatteḥ asiddheḥ na hi upalakṣaṇa padātiriktam upalakṣya upasthāpakam asti iti upalakṣaṇa padam sva artham upasthāpya upalakṣyam upasthāpayati iti lakṣaṇā eva syāt anyathā lakṣaṇa ucchedaḥ ghaṭaḥ na asti iti atra upalakṣaṇasya pratiyoginaḥ abhāva dhī viṣaya tvāt niyata upalakṣya abhāvāt ca na api vyāvartaka tve sati kriyā anvayi viśeṣaṇam anyat upalakṣaṇam kriyā hīne subhagaḥ ayam daṇḍī mahā bāhuḥ iti ādau daṇḍa ādeḥ aviśeṣaṇa tva āpātāt paraṃparayā upalakṣaṇe api kriyā anvayitvāt ca atha atad vyāvṛttiḥ vaiśiṣṭyam tathā ca viśiṣṭa jñāne atad vyāvṛttiḥ viṣayaḥ na viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā tathā ca viśiṣṭa dhī kāraṇa jñāna viṣaya tve sati pratyāyya vyāvṛtti samāna adhikaraṇam viśeṣaṇam iti 
[053,v]	tat na nīlam utpalam iti ādāvanīla anullekhe atad vyāvṛtti anullekhāt nīlam jānāmi iti anuvyavasāya virodhāt apohāpātāt ca atha vyāvartakam sākṣāt saṃbaddham nīla ādi paraṃpara asaṃbaddham gṛha upari bhramat kāka ādi tatra vyāvartanīyam adhitiṣṭhati yat hi sākṣāt eva tad viśeṣaṇam atas viparītam anyat daṇḍī pumān iti viśeṣaṇam atra daṇḍaḥ puṃso na jātiḥ anudaṇḍam asau ca tasya iti saṃbandhi dvaya atirikta sambandha ghaṭaka abhāve sati saṃbandhaḥ eva sākṣāt saṃbandhaḥ sa ca saṃyoga samavāya svarūpa saṃbandha sādhāraṇaḥ jñāne viṣayasya adhikaraṇe abhāvasya saṃbandhini samavāyasya asti iti teṣām api viśeṣaṇa tvam iti śiva āditya miśrāḥ 
[053,vi_053,vii]	tat na gaura nityaḥ rūpavān calati rūpavati rasaḥ iti ādau jāte rūpasya ca sākṣāt saṃbandhe api upalakṣaṇa tvāt lohitaḥ sphaṭikaḥ ityādau paraṃparā saṃbandhe api lohita tvasya viśeṣaṇa tvāt atha anvaya pratiyogi upasthāpaka tayā anvitam upalakṣaṇam sākṣāt anvitam viśeṣaṇam kāka ādeḥ saṃsthāna ādi upasthāpaka tayā upayogāt atathātve daṇḍa ādi vat viśeṣaṇa tvam eva iti ced na upalakṣaṇasya lākṣaṇika tva āpatteḥ pratiyeginaḥ abhāve dharma antarān upanayāt ca 
[053,viii_053,ix]	atha vyāvṛtti buddhi samaye viśeṣya saṃbaddham vyavartakam viśeṣaṇam tadānīm viśeṣya asaṃbaddham vyāvartakam upalakṣaṇam na ca jaṭā yadā yatra asti tadā tatra upalakṣaṇam atas eva tatra eva tat eva saṃbandha samaye viśeṣaṇam asaṃbandha samaye upalakṣaṇam iti tat na rūpavati ghaṭe rasaḥ iti ādau rūpasya viśeṣaṇa tva prasaṅgāt daṇḍī ā āsīt iti ādau atīte daṇḍasya aviśeṣaṇa tva apātāt ca 
[053,x_053,xi]	etena yatra yat viśeṣya tāvacchedaka dharmeṇa vyāvṛttyā vā samāna adhikaraṇa tvena pratīyate tatra tat viśeṣaṇam iti api pratyuktam atra ucyate daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti jñāna anantaram daṇḍavatya daṇḍa vyāvṛttiḥ avagamyate iti pratyāyya vyāvṛtti adhikaraṇa tā puruṣasya daṇḍena avacchidyate na puruṣa tvena ati vyāpteḥ upalakṣaṇe tu gṛha tāpasa ādi niṣṭha pratyāyya vyāvṛtti adhikaraṇa tā na kāka jaṭa ādibhiḥ avacchidyate tat abhāvavatī api vyāvṛtti pratīteḥ kim tu saṃsthāna viśeṣavatvādinā 
[053,xii]	evam ca pratyāyya vyāvṛtti adhikaraṇa tāvacchedaka tve sati vyāvartakam viśeṣaṇam tad anya vyāvartakam upalakṣaṇam vyāvṛtti ullekha anantaram eva viśeṣaṇa tva buddhiḥ tad āhuḥ ācāryāḥ sat asat vā samāna adhikaraṇam vyavacchedakam viśeṣaṇam vyadhikaraṇam upalakṣaṇam iti asya arthaḥ sva adhikaraṇa mātra vṛtti vyāvṛtti bodhaka tvam sva avacchinna adhikaraṇa tā kavyāvṛtti bodhaka tvam sva an adhikaraṇa adhikaraṇa kavya āvṛttya bodhaka tve sati vyāvṛtti bodhaka tvam vā iti upalakṣaṇam tu sva an adhikaraṇe api vyāvṛttim bodhayati 
[053,xiii]	athavā vivakṣita anvaya pratiyogi ta avacchedakam viśeṣaṇam daṇḍinam ānayā ityādau daṇḍaḥ tathā tad anavacchedakam upalakṣaṇam kākena devadattasya gṛhāḥ ityādau kākaḥ na gṛhasya devadatta anvaya pratiyogi tāvacchedakaḥ tad viraha daśāyām api devadatta anvaya avagamāt kim tu gṛha viśeṣaḥ eva upalakṣaṇa paricitaḥ atas eva anvaya apratiyogi tve api na upalakṣaṇa vaiyarthyam 
[053,xiv]	yat vā yat anvita tayā jñātaḥ eva viśeṣye tātparya viṣaya itara anvaya dhīḥ tad vyavacchedakam viśeṣaṇam anevaṃbhūtam tad upalakṣaṇam upalakṣaṇān avacchinne api upalakṣye tātparya viṣayībhūta anvaya bodhāt ayam eva kārya anvayi viśeṣaṇam tad ananvayi upalakṣaṇam iti asya arthaḥ na tu tātparya viṣayībhūta viśeṣya anvaya bodha viṣaya tvam viśiṣṭa jñāna viṣaya tvam vā pratiyogi abhāva buddhi viṣayaḥ iti mate tad abhāvāt 
[054,i_054,ii]	yat vā viśeṣya anvayinā yasya avaśyam anvayaḥ tad avacchedakam viśeṣaṇam tat anyat upalakṣaṇam iti tatra upalakṣya viśeṣya mātra anvayāt yat vyāvartakam viśeṣya anvayinā anvīyate tad viśeṣaṇam tat anyat upalakṣaṇam iti vā yat vā tātparya viṣaya anvaya pratiyogī uddeśya anvaya pratiyogī vā dharmaḥ viśeṣaṇam tad anyat upalakṣaṇam iti alam vistareṇa 
[054,iii_054,iv]	sa vikalpakam ca viśiṣṭa jñānam yathā gauḥ ayam iti tat ca sāmānya ādīnām parama artha sattvena artha ja tvāt indriyaja tvāt ca pratyakṣam kvacid saṃskāra sahakāri vaśena tat tāviśiṣṭasya idantā viśiṣṭā bheda ullekhī aindriyakaḥ vikalpaḥ nanu eka kārya sahakāri tvam anyatra pratyabhijñānam tu na ekam jñānam tad aṃśe pārokṣyasya idam aṃśe ca apārokṣyasya anubhavena viruddha dharma saṃsargāt na ca idam yathārtham aneka deśa kāla saṃbandhasya ekatra bādhāt eka kāla ādi saṃsarga tadabhāva vyavaccheda vat tad avinābhūta kāla antara ādi saṃbandha vyavacchedāt tat ayathārtha tve bahu viplaveta iti ced na pārokṣya apārokṣyayoḥ iha asiddheḥ indriya janya tvena aparokṣa tva niyamāt tat ta aṃśasya ca smṛti upanīta tvāt indriya saṃbaddha viśeṣaṇa tā pratyāsatteḥ na ca eka kāla saṃbandhaḥ kāla antara saṃbandha abhāvau inābhūtaḥ ekasmin nānā ādiś saṃbandhasya jñāne aneka viṣaya tvasya ca vyāghāta āpatteḥ sākṣātkaromi iti anuvyavasāye bādhaka abhāvāt ca 
[054,v]	nanu kā iyam tat tā na tāvat atīta samaya saṃbandhaḥ anāgata gocara smṛti pratyabhijñayoḥ tad ta ullekhāt pratyakṣa anubhūyamāna ghaṭa ādau atīta samaya avaccheda anumāne tad tādhī vi apadeśayoḥ abhāvāt atīta samaya saṃbandha avagame api saḥ ayam na vā iti saṃśayāt sa na ayam iti viparyayāt tad abhāva avagame api saḥ ayam iti pratīteḥ atīta samaya viśiṣṭaḥ saḥ iti saha prayogāt kāle tad abhāvāt ca etena jñāta dharma antara vaiśiṣṭyam tat ta iti nirastam 
[054,vi_054,vii]	na ca tad vṛtti guṇa ādikam eva tat tā tad avagame api tad anavagamāt tad anavagame api tad avagamāt ca na api atīta jñāna vaiśiṣṭyam pareṇa jñātaḥ iti jñāne api saḥ iti prayoga abhāvāt na api etat janma atīta sva jñāna vaiśiṣṭyam tad avagame api tat ta asaṃśaya viparyaya darśanāt atīta jñāna viśiṣṭaḥ saḥ iti saha prayogāt atīta anubhava viṣaya tvasya anubhava aviṣaya tvena smṛtyā tad ullekha anupapatteḥ ca 
[054,viii_054,ix]	yat tu atīta anubhava viṣaya tvam tat tā tat ca anubhava aviṣaya tvena yadā jñāna antareṇa gṛhyate tadā sa ghaṭaḥ iti smaraṇam no ced pramuṣṭa tattākam ghaṭaḥ iti tat na atīta anubhava viṣaya tvasya anumitau bhāne api saḥ iti dhī vyapadeśayoḥ abhāvāt atīta anubhava viṣaya tva niścaye api tat ta asaṃśaya viparyaya darśanāt saha prayoga anupapatteḥ jñāna antareṇa atīta anubhava viṣaya tva grahe tad ta ullekhā patteḥ ca 
[054,x_054,xi]	atha atīta dharma vaiśiṣṭyam tat tā sa dharmaḥ kvacid samayaḥ kvacid jñāna ādiḥ na ca atīta dharma viśiṣṭaḥ saḥ iti saha prayoga anupapattiḥ dharma viśeṣam ādāya tad upapatteḥ tad apratītau api saḥ iti pratītiḥ asiddhā eva na ca atīta dharma viśiṣṭa pratītau api sa na vā iti saṃśayāt sa na ayam iti viparyayāt ca na evam iti vācyam niścita dharma itara dharma viśeṣa viṣaya tvena tayoḥ upapatteḥ iti ced mā evam yadi vastu gatyā yaḥ atītaḥ dharmaḥ tad vaiśiṣṭyam tat tā tadā anubhave api tad viṣaya tvāt tad ta ullekhāpattiḥ na api atīta tvena yaḥ bhāsate dharmaḥ tad vaiśiṣṭyam bhāsamāna dharmasya atīta tvena anubhava aviṣaya tvāt pratyuta vartamāna tvena anubhavāt smṛtau tad ullekhā anupapatteḥ ca 
[054,xii]	na ca anubhava anantaram yadā jñāna antareṇa atīta dharma vaiśiṣṭya bhānam tadā smṛtau tad ta ullekhaḥ na anyadā iti vācyam atīta dharmasya anumitau tad ta ullekhā patteḥ idantā api na tanmātra vṛtti guṇa ādikam anumāna ādinā tad avagame api ayam iti vyapadeśa abhāvāt pratyakṣeṇa tad avagame ayam iti vyapadeśaḥ iti ced na vācyasya pramāṇa gocara tayā vyapadeśasya niyantum aśakyatvāt guṇa ādau api tad nirvacane ananugamāt na ca etat vyakti āśraya tvam idam etat oḥ paryāya tvāt na api pratyakṣa jñāna gocara tvam acākṣuṣa tva āpatteḥ atīte tad anumāne ayam iti buddhi vyapadeśa abhāvāt smṛtyā api tad ullekhā patteḥ ca 
[054,xiii]	atra kecid āhuḥ tat tedante smṛti anubhava bhāsinyau akhaṇḍe eva upādhī kḷpta dharma atirekiṇau evam ced antā saṃskāreṇa idantā eva tad tayā smaryate na ca tat tāyāḥ kvacid anārope katham āropaḥ iti vācyam pratyabhijñāyām tat ta aṃśe yathārtha tvāt idantān ullekhī anubhava prabhava smaraṇe dharma antaram eva tad tayā bhāsate atas eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti na smaraṇam atas eva sarvā smṛtiḥ ayathārthāḥ ayathārtha anubhavā ca hari hara ādi anucintanam ca kavi kāvya mūla jñāna vat manoratha jñāna vat ca sa ākāṅkṣa padārtha jñāna prabhavam anubhava rūpam eva iti 
[054,xiv_055,ii]	tat na smṛteḥ pūrvam idanta upasthitim vinā tatra tat tāra upāsaṃbhavāt kim ca tat ta aṃśe ananubhūta gocara tvena smṛteḥ saṃskāra sīmā laṅghane idantā tad tayā smaryate iti atra māna abhāvāt ghaṭaḥ eva tat tayā smaryate iti astu lāghavāt iti atra ucyate anubhave kālaḥ dharma antaram vā yaḥ vartamāna tvena viṣayaḥ saḥ eva smaraṇasya anubhava smaraṇayoḥ eka viṣaya tve api smaraṇe tatra tad śabda prayogaḥ saṃskāra jajñānasya eva tad śabda prayoga hetu tvāt atas eva pratyabhijñāne tatra tad śabda prayogaḥ pratyakṣa anubhave tatra eva idaṃśabda prayogaḥ na tu viṣaya kṛtaḥ anubhava smaraṇayoḥ viśeṣaḥ atas eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti anubhavāt ayam ghaṭaḥ iti na smaraṇam sa ghaṭaḥ iti smaraṇa kāraṇam sa ghaṭaḥ iti na anubhavaḥ 
[055,iii]	yat vā ayam ghaṭaḥ iti atra yat dharma vaiśiṣṭyam bhāsate tasya atīta tvam tat tā tad vaiśiṣṭyam ananubhūtam api smṛti viṣayaḥ idantā viśiṣṭa gocara saṃskārāt katham tat tāsmṛtiḥ iti ced na sa ghaṭaḥ iti smṛtim pratyanubhavasya hetu tva nirvāhaka tayā saṃskārasya tathā eva kalpanāt ayam ghaṭaḥ iti smṛteḥ sa ghaṭaḥ iti anubhavasya adarśanāt ca samāna viṣaya tvena smṛteḥ ayam ghaṭaḥ iti smṛtiḥ na sa ghaṭaḥ iti na anubhavaḥ ca syāt na ca evam smṛtiḥ ananubhūta tatta aṃśe anubhavaḥ syāt saṃskāra asādhāraṇa kāraṇaka tvena smṛti tvāt saha prayogaḥ ca dharma viśeṣam ādāya pratividheyaḥ atas eva saṃskāra hetu anubhava prāmāṇya pāratantryeṇa yathārtha tve api smṛtiḥ apramā iti sarva tantrasi dvāntaḥ 
[055,iv_055,v]	yat vā na iyam yathārthā tathā hi smṛtiḥ sva viṣaya vartamāna tva viṣayāḥ atīta anāgatā gocara pratīti tvāt pratyabhijñāvat pratīti tvāt vā ghaṭaḥ asti iti pratīti vat pratīteḥ samaya viśeṣa viṣaya tva niyamāt jñāna sāmagrī mahimnā ca ananubhūte api samaya aṃśe smṛtiḥ na tatra saṃskāra vyāpāraḥ anyathā siddha tvāt atas eva pāka rakte śyāmaḥ ayam iti dhiyaḥ ayathārtha tva vyavahāraḥ laukikānām śyāma tvasya vartamāna tvena avagamāt 
[055,vi_055,vii]	etena śyāma dhīḥ tatra yathārtha eva ghaṭe kadācid tat sattvāt idānīm ayam śyāmaḥ iti ākāraḥ eva na iti apāstam atas eva atīta anāgata vahni agocara tve vidyamāna dhūmena parvate vahniḥ iti anumiteḥ vartamāna vahni viṣaya tvāt idānīm vahni niścayena vahni arthi pravṛttiḥ anyathā idānīm tad saṃdehe pravṛttiḥ na syāt yadā dhūmaḥ tadā vahniḥ iti vyāptau api tad ajñāna daśāyām pravṛtteḥ anyathā anupapatteḥ 
[055,viii]	yat vā sa ghaṭaḥ iti smṛtau tat tā viśiṣṭasya vartamāna tā bhāsate saṃskārasya vartamāna jñāna sāmagrī sahitasya eva hetu tvāt saḥ ayam idānīm ityādau tathā kalpanāt gehe sa ghaṭaḥ iti smaraṇāt niśśaṅka pravṛtteḥ ca anyathā tat tā viśiṣṭasya idānīm saṃdehe sā na syāt na ca vartamāna tva aṃśe ananubhūta viṣaya tvam vartamāna tvena anāgata vartamānasya pūrvam anubhavāt 
[055,ix_055,x]	evam ca smṛteḥ tathābhūtasya vartamāna tā viṣayaḥ tatra viśeṣyasya viśeṣaṇasya vā vartamāna tva abhāvāt smṛtiḥ ayathārtha eva na ca pūrvam tathā āsīt arthaḥ iti tat yathārtha tvam pāka rakte śyāmaḥ ayam iti jñānasya yathārtha tva prasaṅgāt pramuṣṭa tattā aṃśe ca smaraṇe avidyamāna dharma avacchedaḥ na bhāsate tad āhuḥ ācāryāḥ smṛteḥ yāthārthyam api kutas iti 
[055,xi_055,xii]	pratyakṣa upajīvaka tvāt pratyakṣa anantaram bahu vādi sammata tvāt upamānāt prāc anumānam nirūpyate tatra vyāpti viśiṣṭa pakṣa dharma tā jñāna janyam jñānam anumitiḥ tad karaṇam anumānam tat ca liṅga parām arśaḥ na tu parāmṛśyamānam liṅgam iti vakṣyate atha anumānam na pramāṇam yogyā upādhīnām yogyā anupalabdhyā abhāva niścaye api ayogya upādhi śaṅkayā vyabhicāra saṃśayāt śataśas sahacaritayoḥ api vyabhicāra upalabdheḥ ca loke dhūma ādi darśana anantaram vahni ādi vyavahāraḥ ca sambhāvanā mātrāt saṃvādena ca prāmāṇya abhimānāt iti na apratyakṣam pramāṇam iti 
[055,xiii_055,xiv]	na apramāṇa sādharmyeṇa aprāmāṇya sādhane dṛṣṭa sādharmyasya anumāna tvāt etad vākyasya sandigdha viparyasta anyataram pratyarthavat tvā tayoḥ ca parakīyayoḥ apratyakṣa tvāt anumānam apramāṇam iti vākyasya prāmāṇya aprāmāṇayoḥ vyāghātāt ca api ca anumāna aprāmāṇye pratyakṣasya api apramāṇa tā āpatteḥ prāmāṇyasya anumeya tvāt svatas ca prāmāṇya grahe tad saṃśaya anupapatteḥ vyāpti graha upāyaḥ ca vakṣyate 
[056,i]	nanu anumiti hetu vyāpti jñāne kā vyāptiḥ na tāvat avyabhicarita tvam tat hi na sādhya abhāva vat avṛtti tvam sādhya vat bhinna sādhya abhāva vat avṛtti tvam sādhya vat pratiyogikān yonya abhāva āsāmānādhikaraṇyam sakala sādhya abhāva vat niṣṭhā abhāva pratiyogi tvam sādhya vadanyāvṛtti tvam vā kevalān vayinī a bhāvāt 
[056,ii]	na api sādhyāsā mānādhikaraṇyā anadhikaraṇa tvam sādhya vaiyadhi karaṇyānadhikaraṇa tvam vā tat ubhayam api sādhyān adhikaraṇān adhikaraṇa tvam tat ca tatra yad kiñcit sādhyān adhikaraṇa adhikaraṇe dhūme ca aprasiddham 
[056,iii]	atha idam vācyam jñeya tvāt ityādau samavāyitayā vācya tva abhāvaḥ ghaṭaḥ eva prasiddhaḥ vyadhikaraṇa dharma avacchinna pratiyogi tākā bhāvasya kevala anvayitvāt na ca evam ghaṭaḥ eva vyabhicāraḥ sādhya tāvacchedaka avacchinna pratiyogi tāka sādhya abhāva vat vṛtti tvam hi vyabhicāraḥ na ca vācya tva abhāvaḥ tādṛśaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ced tarhi tādṛśa sādhya abhāva sāmāna adhikaraṇyā bhāvaḥ vyāptiḥ tathā ca aprasiddhiḥ pratiyogi avṛttiḥ ca dharmaḥ na pratiyogi ta avacchedakaḥ tad viśiṣṭa jñānasya abhāva dhī hetutvāt anyathā tad nirvikalpakāt api ghaṭaḥ na asti iti buddhi āpatteḥ gavi śaśa śṛṅgam na asti iti pratateḥ aprasiddheḥ śaśaśṛṅgam na asti iti ca śaśe śṛṅga abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[056,iv^1]	atha sādhyāsā mānādhikaraṇyā an adhikaraṇa tve sati sādhikaraṇa tvam vyāptiḥ kevala anvayini sādhyāsāmānādhikaraṇyam niradhikaraṇe ākāśa ādau prasiddham iti ced na sādhyāsāmānādhikaraṇyam hi na sādhyān adhikaraṇa adhikaraṇa tvam sādhya adhikaraṇa anadhikaraṇa tvam vā kevala anvayini yat kiṃcid sādhya adhikaraṇa an adhikaraṇe dhūme ca avyāpteḥ na api sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāvā pratiyogi sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam parvatīya vahneḥ mahānasīya dhūma samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvāt dravya tva ādeḥ avyāpya vṛtti avyāpya ta āpatteḥ ca na ca pratiyogi virodhi tvam vyāpya vṛtti tvam vā abhāva viśeṣaṇam deyam saṃyoga ādau sādhye sattva ādeḥ anaikāntika tva abhāva prasaṅgāt na hi pratiyogi virodhī saṃyoga ādeḥ aparaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ asti 
[056,iv^2]	adhikaraṇa bhedena abhāva bheda abhāvāt na api sādhana vat niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva apratiyogi sādhyavat katvam vyāptiḥ mūle vṛkṣaḥ kapi saṃyogavān na itya bādhita pratīteḥ tad anyonya abhāvasya api tatra sattvāt na ca evam bheda abhedaḥ avacchedaka bhedena tad sattva abhyupagamāt sādhana vat niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva apratiyogi sādhya vadyasya iti ṣaṣṭhī artha vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva anirūpaṇāt sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāpti nirūpya tvāt vahnimat parvatasya dhūma vat mahānasa niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva pratiyogi tvāt ca viśeṣa abhāva kūṭāt eva abhāva vyavahāra upapattau sāmānya abhāve māna abhāvāt na api sādhana samāna adhikaraṇa yāvat dharma nirūpita vaiyadhi karaṇyān adhikaraṇa sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam sādhana samāna adhikaraṇasya prameya tva ādeḥ vaiyadhi karaṇya aprasiddheḥ mahānasa ādau samavāyitayā vahni vahnim atoḥ atyantān yonya abhāvayoḥ sattvāt dhūma ādau api ukta lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ca 
[056,v]	atha anaupādhikaḥ sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ upādhiḥ ca sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpakaḥ vyāpaka tvam tu tadvat niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam vyabhicāre ca avaśyam upādhiḥ pratiyogi tvam na virodhi tvam saha anavasthāna niyama lakṣaṇam go tva aśva tvayoḥ atathātvāt anyonya abhāva pratiyogini asattvāt ca kim tu yathā adhikaraṇa abhāvayoḥ sva rūpa viśeṣaḥ sambandhaḥ tathā pratiyogi tvam anuyogi tvam api abhāva viraha āma tvam vā iti ced 
[056,vi]	yat kiṃcid sādhya vyāpaka sādhana avyāpaka dharma niṣedhaḥ na dhūma ādau prakṛta sādhya vyāpaka sādhana avyāpaka dharmaḥ ca siddhi asiddhibhyām na niṣeddhum śakyaḥ yāvat sādhya vyāpake prameya tva ādau sādhana avyāpaka tvam yāvat sādhana avyāpake ca ghaṭa tva ādau sādhya vyāpaka tvam niṣidhyate iti ced na vyadhikaraṇa tvāt 
[056,vii_056,viii]	yāvat sādhana avyāpakam avyāpakam yat sādhyasya yāvat sādhya vyāpakam vyāpakam vā yasya tattvam tat iti ced na sa upādheḥ api tathātvāt tathā hi sādhanasya vahneḥ avyāpakam yāvat ārdra indhanam tat pratyekam avyāpakam sādhya dhūmasya dvitīye sādhya dhūmasya vyāpakam ārdra indhanam tat vyāpakam mahānasīya vahneḥ na api sādhyam yāvat vyabhicāri tat avyabhicāri tvam anaupādhika tvam sādhya avyabhicāri tvasya eva gamaka tva sambhavāt tat ca dūṣitam 
[056,ix]	na api kātsrnyena sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ eka vyaktike tad abhāvāt nānā vyaktike api sakala dhūma sambandhasya pratyeka vahnau abhāvāt atas eva na kātsrnyena sādhyena sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ viṣam avyāpte tad abhāvāt ca na ca yāvat sādhana āśraya āśrita sādhya sambandhaḥ sādhana āśraya mahānasa ādau sakale pratyekam vahneḥ āśrita tva abhāvāt 
[056,x_057,i]	na api sādhana samāna adhikaraṇa yāvat dharma samāna adhikaraṇa sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam yāvat dharma sāmānādhikaraṇyam hi yāvat dharma adhikaraṇa adhikaraṇa tvam tat ca aprasiddham na api svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ vyāptiḥ svabhāva janya tve tad āśrita tva ādau vā avyāpti ati vyāpteḥ na api avinābhāvaḥ kevalān vayinī a bhāvāt atha sambandha mātram vyāptiḥ vyabhicāri sambandhasya api kenacid saha vyāpti tvāt dhūma ādi vyāptiḥ tu viśiṣya eva vaktavyā iti 
[057,ii_057,iii]	tat na liṅga parāmarśa viṣaya vyāpti svarūpa nirūpaṇa prastāve lakṣaṇa abhidhānasya artha antara tvāt na ca sambandha mātram tathā tad bodhāt anum iti anutpatteḥ na api vyāpti pada pravṛtti nimittam idam sambandha jñāne api vyāpti pada aprayogāt kevala anvayini kevalānvayi saṃmbandhaḥ vyatirekiṇi sādhya vadanyāvṛtti tvam vyāptiḥ etayoḥ anumiti viśeṣa janaka tvam anumiti mātre pakṣa dharma tā eva prayojikā na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa sāmagrī sahitāyāḥ eva sāmānya sāmagryāḥ kārya janaka tva niyamāt iti kecid 
[057,iv]	tat api na sādhya vadanyāvṛtti tvasya dhūme asattvāt vahnimat parvatāni asmin dhūma sattvāt na ca sakala sādhya vadanyāvṛtti tvam vahnimatām pratyekam tathātvāt sarvatra lakṣaṇe sādhya tva sādhana tva tad abhimata tvānām vyāpti nirūpya tvena ātma āśrayaḥ sādhya tvam hi na siddhi karma tvam siṣā dhayiṣā viṣaya tvam vā mahānasīya vahnau tad abhāvāt na ca sāmānyatas vyāpti avagamaḥ asti eva parasya katham anyathā dūṣaṇena asādhaka tām sādhayet iti vācyam sva artha anumāna upayogi vyāpti svarūpa nirūpaṇam vinā kathā yāma praveśāt iti 
[057,v]	atra ucyate pratiyogi asamāna adhikaraṇa yat samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka avacchinnam yat na bhavati tena samam tasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam vyāptiḥ 
[057,vi]	anya niṣṭha vahneḥ dhūmavat parvata vṛtti atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve api tad pratiyogitā na vahni tvena avacchidyate dhūmavati vahniḥ na asti iti apratīteḥ sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tākā bhāvaḥ pṛthak eva anyathā sakala prasiddha rūpa abhāve prasiddha rūpa vat anya tve ca avagate vāyau rūpam na vā vāyuḥ rūpavān na vā iti saṃśayaḥ na syāt viśeṣa abhāva kūṭasya niścita tvāt 
[057,vii]	yat vā pratiyogi vyadhikaraṇa sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyoginā sāmānādhikaraṇyam yad samāna adhikaraṇānyonya abhāva pratiyogi yadvat na bhavati tena samam tasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam vā sva samāna adhikaraṇa anyonya abhāva apratiyogiyadvatka tvam vā anya vṛtti vahni tadvatoḥ anya vṛtti dhūma vat niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva anyonya abhāva pratiyogi tvāt vyadhikaraṇa vahni dhūmayoḥ na vyāptiḥ kiṃtu tad tad dhūmasya samāna adhikaraṇa tad tad vahninā na ca evam dhūma mātre na vyāptiḥ iti vācyam sarva dhūmavyakteḥ tathā tvena dhūma mātrasya vyāpya tvāt dhūma sambandhi vahniḥ tat vyāpyaḥ eva yugapad utpanna vinaṣṭayoḥ ca vyāptiḥ eva karmaṇi ca saṃyoga abhāvaḥ pratiyogi asamāna adhikaraṇaḥ 
[057,viii_057,x]	yat vā pratiyogi vaiyadhi karaṇyā avacchedaka avacchinna tvam atyanta abhāva viśeṣaṇam karmaṇi ca saṃyoga abhāvasya pratiyogi vaiyadhikaraṇyā avacchedaka avacchinna tvam eva na ca anyonya abhāvasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam abhedasya ābādhita pratyabhijñānāt vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva ajñāne api vastu sataḥ tathā tvena ajñāyamānasya sambandha tvena eva bhātasya ṣaṣṭhī artha tvam na ca evam ananugamaḥ doṣāya kasya kā vyāptiḥ iti ananugatasya eva lakṣya tvāt atha dhūmavati vahni hradau na staḥ dhūmavān vahnimat hradau na bhavati iti pratīteḥ vyāsa jya vṛtti pratiyogikau vahni vahnim atoḥ atyantānyonya abhāvau dhūmavati vidyeta iti katham ete lakṣaṇe iti ced na tādṛśa abhāva anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā tatra tat ubhayam pratiyogi na vahni vahnimantau 
[057,xi]	atha vā anaupādhika tvam vyāptiḥ tat ca yāvat svasamāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka avacchinnam yat tad pratiyogikātyānta abhāva samāna adhikaraṇam yat tena samam sāmānādhikaraṇyam na hi evam sa upādhiḥ tatra sādhana samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyoginaḥ ārdra indhana vat tva ādeḥ upādheḥ yaḥ atyantā bhāvaḥ tena samam sādhyasya dhūma ādeḥ sāmānādhikaraṇya abhāvāt upādheḥ sādhya vyāpaka tvāt etat eva yāvat su avyabhicāri vyabhicāri sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam anaupādhika tvam gīyate 
[058,i_058,iii]	yat vā yāvat yat samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyogi pratiyogika atyanta abhāva sāmānādhikaraṇyam yasya tasya tat eva anaupādhika tvam sa upādhau tu sādhya vat niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva apratiyoginaḥ upādheḥ yaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ tena samam hetoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam upādheḥ sādhana avyāpaka tvāt yat vā yad sambandhi tāvacchedaka rūpavat tvam yasya tasya sā vyāptiḥ tathā hi dhūmasya vahni sambandhi tve dhūma tvam avacchedakam dhūma mātrasya vahni sambandhi tvāt vahneḥ tu dhūma sambandhe na vahni tvam avacchedakam dhūma asambandhini gata tvāt na hi ati prasaktam avacchedakam saṃyoga ādau tathā tva adarśanāt kiṃtu vahnau ārdra indhana prabhava vahni tvam dhūma sambandhi tāvacchedakam tādṛśam ca vyāpyam eva athavā yat sāmāna adhikaraṇyā avacchedaka avacchinnam yasya svarūpam tat tasya vyāpyam vahni sāmānādhikaraṇyam hi dhūme dhūma tvena avacchidyate sa upādhau tu upādhinā 
[058,iv_058,v]	atas eva sādhana tāvacchedaka bhinnena yena sādhana tā abhimate sādhya sambandhaḥ avacchidyate saḥ eva tatra sādhane viśeṣaṇam upādhiḥ iti vadanti atas eva ca tatra sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka tvam lakṣaṇam dhruvam vyabhicāriṇi sādhane ekatra sādhya tad abhāvayoḥ virodhena avacchedaka bhedam vinā tad ubhaya sambandha abhāvāt avaśyam sādhya sambandhi tā avacchedakam asti tat eva ca sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpakam sādhana avyāpakam tatra upādhiḥ 
[058,vi_058,viii]	atas eva vyabhicāre ca avaśyam upādhiḥ iti saṃgacchate anyathā vyabhicārāt eva tatra āgamaka tvena vyabhicāreṇa na tad anumānam aprayojaka tvāt atas eva ca tasya sādhya sambandhi tāvacchedaka rūpa lakṣaṇa avyāptiḥ sādhana tā abhimate cakāsti iti sphaṭike japā kusuma vat upādhiḥ asau ucyate lakṣaṇam tu sādhya sādhana sambandha vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tvam viṣam avyāptaḥ tu na upādhipad a vācyaḥ pravṛtti nimitta abhāvāt dūṣaka tā ca tasya vyabhicāra unnāyaka tayā na ca vyabhicāra unnāyaka tvam eva aupādhika tvam aprayojaka sādhya vyāpaka vyabhicāriṇaḥ api upādhi tva āpatteḥ iti 
[058,ix_058,x]	sā iyam vyāptiḥ na bhūyas darśana gamyā darśanānām pratyekam ahetu tvāt āśu vināśinām kramikāṇām melakā bhāvāt na ca tāvat darśana janya saṃskārāḥ indriya saha kṛtāḥ vyāpti dhīhetavaḥ pratyabhijñāyām indriyasya tathā tva kalpanāt iti vācyam samāna viṣaye smaraṇe pratyabhijñāne ca saṃskāraḥ hetuḥ atas katham saṃskāreṇa vyāpti jñānam janyeta anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ kim ca sambandha bhūyas darśanam bhūyassu sthāneṣu darśanam bhūyasām vā darśanam bhūyāṃsi vā darśanāni na tathā ekatra rūpa rasayoḥ dravya tva ghaṭa tvayoḥ ca vyāpti grahāt ekatra eva dhārāvāhike tad hī prasaṅgāt bhūyaḥ tvasya tri catur ādi tvena ananugamāt ca 
[058,xi]	api ca pārthiva tva lauha lekhya tva ādau śataśas darśane api vyāpti agrahāt tarka saha kṛtam tathā iti ced tarhi sahacāra darśana vyābhicāra adarśana sahakṛtaḥ saḥ eva vyāpti grāhakaḥ astu āvaśyaka tvāt kim bhūyas darśanena na ca tena vinā tarkaḥ eva na avatarati prathama darśane vyutpannasya tarka sambhavāt na ca evam eva astu tarkasya vyāpti graha mūlaka tvena anavasthānāt jāta mātrasya pravṛtti nivṛtti hetu anumiti janaka vyāpti jñānam tarkam vinā eva atas na anavasthā iti ced tarhi vyabhicārāt saḥ api na vyāpti grahe hetuḥ na ca etat buddhau avāntara jātiḥ asti sāmānya pratyāsattyā sarva upasaṃhārāt avinā bhāva grahaḥ sāmānya rūpa tā ca na sakṛt darśana gamya iti bhūyas darśana apekṣā iti ced na sāmānyasya hi pratyāsatti tvam lāghavāt na tu sāmānyatayā jñātasya tad anabhyupagamāt ca na ca kākatālīya tva ādi śaṅkā vyudāsa artham dvitīya ādi darśana apekṣā iti vācyam dvitīya ādi darśane api śaṅkā tādavasthyāt 
[058,xii_058,xiv]	nanu anaupādhika tva jñānam vyāpti jñāne hetuḥ tad deśa kāla tatra avasthita ghaṭa ādīnām upādhi tva śaṅkā nirāsaḥ kasyacid sādhana vyāpaka tva jñānena kasyacid sādhya avyāpaka tva jñānena syāt tat ca bhūyas darśanam vinā na avatarati iti ced na ayogyā upādhi vyatirekasya anumāna adhīna jñāna tvena anavasthā pātāt atha sādhya sādhana sahacarita dharma antarāṇām upādhi tva saṃśaye na vyāpti grahaḥ atas teṣām anupādhi tva jñānam bhūyas darśana adhīna sādhya avyāpaka tva jñāne satī iti etad artham bhūyas darśana apekṣā atas eva yāvatā darśanena tat niścayaḥ tāvat bhūyas darśanam hetuḥ iti na vāra saṅkhyā niyamaḥ na vā an anugamaḥ 
[059,i]	yadi api ca anyasya sādhya vyāpaka tva sādhana avyāpaka tva saṃśayaḥ na anya vyāpti graha pratibandhakaḥ tathā api tad ā ahita vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ pratibandhakaḥ iti tad vidhūnanam āvaśyakam iti ced na ayogya upādhi saṃśaya adhīna vyabhicāra saṃśayasya tathā api anucchedāt sa ca na bhūyas darśanāt na api anumānāt iti uktam api ca bhūyas darśana āhita saṃskāraḥ na bahis indriya sahakārī tat vyāpāram vinā api ca sahacāra ādi jñānavataḥ vyāpti grahāt 
[059,ii]	na api manasaḥ indriya ādi vat bhūyas darśana janya saṃskārasya tad janya smaraṇasya vā pramāṇa antaratva āpatteḥ tasmāt pariśeṣāt sakṛt darśana gamyā sā tathā hi upādhi abhāvaḥ vyāptiḥ abhāvaḥ ca kevala adhikaraṇam tad kāla sambandhaḥ vā sva prakāśa rūpam tat jñānam vā tat ca prathama darśanena avagatam eva cakṣuḥ ādinā na ca adhikaḥ tad abhāvaḥ asti na ca pratiyogi jñānam adhikaraṇa ādi jñāna janakam yena upādhi jñānam vinā tat na syāt evam upādhi abhāve jñāte kiṃcid na jñātum avaśiṣyate upādhi abhāva vyavahāraḥ tu tat hiyam apekṣate dīrgha tva ādi vyavahāraḥ iva avadhi jñānam na ca evam rāsabha sambandha tulya vahni dhūma sambandha jñānāt eva anumitiḥ syāt iti vācyam upādhi smaraṇe sati upādhi tad vyāpya itara sakala tad upalambhaka samavadhāne ca upādhi anupalambha sahitasya kevala adhikaraṇa jñānasya anumiti hetu tvāt tad vyavahāra hetu tvāt ca 
[059,iii_059,iv]	nanu evam prathama darśanena vyāpti niścayāt viśeṣa darśane sati rāsabha ādi saṃśaya vat tad saṃśayaḥ na syāt iti ced vyāpti jñāna anantaram kim vidyamānaḥ eva upādhiḥ maya upādhi tvena na jñātaḥ iti śaṅkayā gṛhīta vyāptau api saṃśayaḥ atas tatra bhūyas darśanena upādhi nirāsa dvārā vyāpti abhāva śaṅkā apanīyate yat vā jñāna prāmāṇya saṃśayāt vyāpti saṃśayaḥ yathā ghaṭa jñāna sāmagryām satyām ghaṭa jñāne sati tad prāmāṇya saṃśaya āhitaḥ tad saṃśayaḥ na tu ac rima saṃśaya anurodhena tatra ghaṭa jñānam eva na vṛttam iti kalpyate tathā iha api upādhi abhāvasya vyāpti tvāt tasya ca kevala adhikaraṇa rūpasya prathama darśane api niścita tvāt vyāpti grāhaka antarasya abhāvāt ca pariśeṣeṇa sakṛt darśanasya vyāpti grāhaka tvāt tad niścaye prāmāṇya saṃśayāt eva tad saṃśayaḥ 
[059,v_059,vi]	na ca evam rāsabhe api prathamam vyāpti paricchedaḥ syāt iti vācyam tatra vyāpteḥ abhāvāt pratyakṣe viṣayasya hetu tvāt kvacid asaṃsarga āgrahāt tathā vyavahāraḥ doṣa māhātmyāt na ca atra api tathā ārope sati nimitta anusaraṇam na tu nimittam asti iti āropaḥ iti abhyupagamāt kecid tu sādhana vat niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva apratiyogi sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam sādhana vat niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva apratigogi sādhyavat katvam vā vyāptiḥ tat ubhayam api yogyam pratyakṣeṇa vahni dhūma sambandha anubhavena prathamam avagatam eva mahānase yaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ vā avagataḥ tasya pratiyogī na vahniḥ na vā vahnimān iti anubhavāt rāsabhe tathā avagame api agre sa bādhyate iti tat na evam hi tad vahni tad dhūmayoḥ eva vyāptiḥ syāt na tu dhūma tva vahni tva avacchedena na ca tad anumāna upayogi vahni tvam vahnimat tvam vā na pratiyogita avacchedakam iti prathamatas jñātum aśakyam eva iti 
[059,vii^1]	mā evam prakṛta sādhya vyāpaka sādhana avyāpakaḥ vā sādhana tva abhimatena samam prakṛta sādhya sambandhi tā avacchedakam viśeṣaṇam vā upādhiḥ ubhayathā api tad abhāvaḥ na vyāptiḥ siddhi asiddhibhyām tad niṣedha anupapatteḥ kim tu yāvat svavyabhicāri vyabhicāri sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyam anaupādhika tvam tasya ca prathamam jñātum aśakyatvāt kim ca na vastu gatyā vyāpteḥ jñānam hetuḥ kim tu vyāpti tvena tat ca upādhya bhāva tvam na ca upādheḥ ajñāne tad abhāva tvena jñānam sambhavati viśeṣaṇa jñāna sādhya tvāt viśiṣṭa jñānasya na ca niyamataḥ prathamam upādhi dhīḥ asti yat ca uktam 
[059,vii^2_059,viii]	pratiyogi jñānam vyavahāra hetuḥ na abhāva jñāne iti astu tāvat evam tathā api tad abhāvaḥ mā vyavahāri upādhi abhāva jñāna adhīnā anumitiḥ syāt eva upādhi jñānam vinā api na ca evam vastutas tu viśeṣa adarśane sahacāra ādi sādhāraṇa dharma darśanāt vyabhicāra saṃśayāt prathama darśane na vyāpti niścayaḥ atha vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ na avyabhicāra niścaya pratibandhakaḥ grāhya saṃśayasya niścaya apratibandhaka tvāt anyathā saṃśaya uttaram kvāpi niścayaḥ na syāt iti ced na vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ pratibandhakaḥ iti brūmaḥ kim tu viśeṣa adarśane sati sahacāra ādi sādhāraṇa dharma darśanāt saṃśayaḥ syāt na tu saṃśaya sāmagrītaḥ niścayaḥ iti kim ca yat hī sāmagrī yatra pratibandhikā viśeṣa adarśane tatra tat hīrapi iti vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ api pratibandhakaḥ evam bhūyas darśanam api saṃśāyakam tarkaḥ tu anavasthā graste eva iti katham vyāpti grahaḥ 
[059,ix_059,x]	atra ucyate vyabhicāra jñāna viraha saha kṛtam sahacāra darśanam vyāpti grāhakam jñānam niścayaḥ śaṅkā ca sā ca kvacid upādhi sandehāt kvacid viśeṣa adarśana sahita sādhāraṇa dharma darśanāt tad virahaḥ ca kvacid vipakṣa bādhaka tarkāt kvacid svatassiddhaḥ eva tarkasya vyāpti graha mūlaka tvena anavasthā iti ced na yāvat āśaṅkam tarka anusaraṇāt yatra ca vyāghātena śaṅkā eva na avatarati tatra tarkam vinā eva vyāpti grahaḥ 
[060,i]	tathā hi dhūmaḥ yadi vahni asamavahita ājanya tve sati vahni samavahitā janyaḥ syāt na utpannaḥ syāt iti atra kim dhūmaḥ avahneḥ eva bhaviṣyati kvacid vahnim vinā api bhaviṣyati ahetukaḥ eva vā utpatsyate iti śaṅkā syāt sarvatra sva kriyā vyāghātaḥ syāt yadi hi gṛhīta anvaya vyatirekam hetum vinā api kārya utpattim śaṅketa tadā svayam eva dhūma artham vahneḥ tṛpti artham bhojanasya para pratipatti artham śabdasya ca upādānam niyamataḥ katham kuryāt tena vinā api tad sambhavāt tasmāt tat tad upādānam eva tādṛśa śaṅkā pratibandhakam śaṅkāyām na niyata upādānam niyata upādāne ca na śaṅkā tat idam uktam tat eva hi āśaṅkyate yasmin āśaṅkyamāne sva kriyā vyāghātaḥ na bhavati iti na hi saṃbhavati svayam vahni ādikam dhūma ādi kārya artham niyamataḥ upādatte tad kāraṇam tat noti āśaṅkyate ca iti 
[060,ii_060,iii]	etena vyāghātaḥ virodhaḥ sa ca saha anavasthāna niyamaḥ iti tatra api anavasthā iti nirastam sva kriyāyāḥ eva śaṅkā pratibandhaka tvāt atas eva vyāghātaḥ yadi śaṅkā asti na ced śaṅkā tatas tarām vyāghāta avadhiḥ āśaṅkā tarkaḥ śaṅkā avadhiḥ kutas iti khaṇḍanakāra matam api apāstam na hi vyāghātaḥ śaṅkā āśritaḥ kim tu sva kriyā eva śaṅkā pratibandhika iti na vā viśeṣa darśanāt kvacid śaṅkā nivṛttiḥ evam syāt na ca etādṛśa tarka avatāraḥ bhūyas darśanam vinā iti bhūyas darśana ādaraḥ na tu sa svatas eva prayojakaḥ 
[060,iv_060,v]	atas eva na tat āhita saṃskāraḥ māna antaram tarkasya apramātvāt tat ca pratyakṣa vyāpti jñāne hetuḥ tad abhāve api śabda anumānābhyām tad grahāt nanu sahacāra darśana vyabhicāra adarśana vat vyabhicāra śaṅkā viraha anukūla tarkayoḥ jñānam vyabhicāri sādhāraṇam iti na tatas api vyāpti niścayaḥ iti ced na sva rūpa satoḥ eva tayoḥ vyāpti grāhaka tvāt sat tarkāt vyāpti pramā tad ābhāsāt tad apramā viśeṣa darśana satya tva asatya tvābhyām puruṣa jñānam iva 
[060,vi_060,viii]	apare tu yatra tarke vyāpti anubhavaḥ mūlam tatra tarka antara apekṣā yatra tu vyāpti smaraṇam hetuḥ tatra na tarka antara apekṣā iti na anavasthā asti ca jāta mātrāṇāḥ miṣṭa aniṣṭa sādhana tā anumiti hetu vyāpti smaraṇam tadānīm vyāpti anubhāvaka abhāvāt tad mūla anubhava mūlā ca agre api vyāpti smaraṇa paramparā iti yat tu anādi siddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva virodha ādi mūlāḥ kecid tarkāḥ iti tat na pramāṇa anuyoge anumānaḥ eva paryavasānāt na ca vyāpti grahānyatha anupapattyā eva tarkasya anādi siddha vyāptika tva jñānam iti vācyam anupapatteḥ api anumāna tvāt anye tu vipakṣa bādhaka tarkāt anaupādhika tva grahaḥ eva tad adhīnaḥ vyāpti grahaḥ iti tat api na tarkasya apramāṇa tvāt vyabhicāra ādi śaṅkā nirāsa dvārā pratyakṣa ādi sahakārī saḥ iti ced na anavasthā abhayena tarkam vinā vyāghātāt yatra śaṅkā virahaḥ tatra vyāpti grahe tarkasya vyabhicārāt 
[060,ix_060,x]	yat tu yogyānām upādhīnām yogyā anupalabdhyā abhāva grahaḥ ayogyānām tu sādhya avyāpaka tva sādhana vyāpaka tva sādha nāt abhāva grahaḥ iti anaupādhika tvam manasā sugraham iti tad tuccham anumānena tad sādhane anavasthānāt pramāṇa antarasya abhāvāt ye ca anukūla tarkam vinā eva sahacāra ādi darśana mātreṇa vyāpti graham vadanti teṣām pakṣa itara tvasya sādhya vyāpaka tva grahe anumāna mātram ucchidyeta anumāna mātra ucchedaka tvāt eva pakṣa itaraḥ na upādhiḥ iti ced bhrāntaḥ asi na hi vayam upādhi tvena tasya doṣa tvam ācakṣmahe sādhya vyāpaka tvena tad vyatirekāt pakṣe sādhya vyāvartaka tayā vyāpaka vyatireke vyāpya vyatirekasya vajra lepa tvāt ca api ca kara vahni saṃyogaḥ śakti atiriktā atīndriya dharma samavāyī janakatvāditi atra aprayojaka tvāt na sādhakam tatra vyāptasya pakṣa dharma tve kim aprayojakam nāma tasmāt vipakṣa bādhaka tarka abhāvāt na tatra vyāpti grahaḥ iti aprayojaka tvam iti 
[060,xi]	ukta vyāpti prakāreṣu anyonya abhāva garbhā eva vyāptiḥ anumiti hetuḥ lāghavāt atas na ananugamaḥ anaupādhika tvam tu tad lakṣaṇam nanu evam upādhiḥ asiddhi upajīvya tvena vyabhicāra vadha itvābhāsa antaram syāt na tu vyāpti abhāva tvena asiddhiḥ iti ced tat jñānam upajīvyam api na svatas dūṣakam na hi anyasya sādhya vyāpaka tva sādhana avyāpaka tva jñānam anyasya sādhya vyāpya tva jñāne pratibandhakam ati prasakteḥ vyabhicāra ajñānasya tadhetu tvāt tat buddhiḥ tathā na ca anaupādhika tva jñānam vyāpti jñāna hetuḥ iti uktam tathā ca vyabhicāra jñāna dvārā sa dūṣakaḥ evam ca para mukha nirīkṣaka tayā siddha sādhana vat na pṛthak na ca evam avyabhicārasya vyāpti tve vyabhicāraḥ tad abhāva tvena asiddhiḥ syāt iti vācyam sādhya abhāvavat vṛtti tvam hi vyabhicāraḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca na avi abhicāraḥ kevalān vayinī a bhāvāt kim tu sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyogi sāmānādhikaraṇyam na ca anayoḥ paraspara viraha tvam iti 
[061,i^1]	vyāpti grahaḥ ca sāmānya lakṣaṇa apratyāsattyā sakala dhūma viṣayakaḥ katham anyathā parvatīya dhūme vyāpti agrahe tasmāt anumitiḥ sā ca indriya sambaddha viśeṣaṇa tā atiriktā eva vā tad viśeṣyaka pratyakṣe tad indriya saṃnikarṣasya hetu tvena anāgata ādau saṃyoga ādeḥ abhāvāt iti vadanti tad apare na manyante tathā hi dhūma tvā avacchinnā vyāptiḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa dhūma viṣaye dhūma tvena pratyakṣeṇa jñāyate tatas smṛtā sā tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśe pakṣa niṣṭha dhūma vṛtti tayā jñāyate tatas anumitiḥ tad anabhyupagame api sannikṛṣṭa dhūma viṣaye dhūma tvena dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpya iti anubhavaḥ tathā eva vyāpti smaraṇam tatas dhūmavān ayam iti vyāpti smṛti prakāreṇa dhūma tvena pakṣa vṛtti dhūma jñānāt anumitiḥ vyāpti anubhava tad smaraṇa pakṣa dharma tā jñānānām eka prakāraka tvena anumiti hetu tvāt gavā ādi padeṣu api śakti anubhava tad smaraṇa vākya artha anubhavānām eka prakāraka tvena hetu hetum at bhāvaḥ iti apūrve vakṣyate tatra yogyatā ādi balāt apūrva vyakti lābhaḥ anumāne tu pakṣa dharma tā balāt dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpya iti anubhavaḥ 
[061,i^2]	na tu sarvaḥ dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpya iti yena sarva bhānā artham tad svīkāraḥ atha vahnimānayam iti anumitiḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna sādhya aviśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt iti parvatīya vahni bhānā artham tad kalpane dhūme api tathā kvacid dhūmasya api vyāpaka tvāt iti ced na viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñāne viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñānasya āvaśyaka tvena hetu tvāt tat ca vṛttam eva na tu viśeṣaṇa jñānam api tathā gauravāt gauḥ ayam iti viśiṣṭa jñāne yugapad viśeṣye viśeṣaṇe saṃnikarṣaḥ eva kāraṇam na tu nirvikalpakam māna abhāvāt viśiṣṭa jñāna tvam eva mānam iti ced na ddaṣṭānta abhāvāt daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti atra viśeṣaṇa dhī janyatva anabhyupagamāt viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñāna tvāt api ca prameya tvena vyāptim paricchindan sarvajñaḥ syāt tathā ca parakīya jñāna viṣaye ghaṭa tvam na vā iti saṃśayaḥ na syāt prameya tvena tad anyatara niścayāt prameya tvena ghaṭam jānāti eva ghaṭa tvam tasya na jānāti iti ced na tat kim ghaṭa tvam na prameyam yena tat na jānīyāt sakala ghaṭa vṛtti dharmasya prameyat tvena tad ajñāna asambhavāt 
[061,ii]	ucyate yadi sāmānya lakṣaṇāḥ na asti tadā anukūla tarka ādikam vinā dhūma ādau vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ na syāt prasiddha dhūme vahni sambandha avagamāt kāla antarīya deśa antarīya dhūmasya māna abhāvena ajñānāt sāmānyena tu sakala dhūma upasthitau viśeṣa adarśanena saṃśayaḥ yujyate yat tu pāka ādau cikīrṣā sukha ādau icchā na syāt siddhe icchā virahāt asiddhi asya ajñānāt tasmāt sukha tva ādinā jñāteṣu sarveṣu siddham vihāya asiddhe icchā bhavati iti abhyupeyam tat na prasiddhasya ajñāne api siddha gocara jñānāt eva icchā pravṛtti svābhāvyāt asiddhe tayoḥ utpatteḥ na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ samāna prakāraka tvena jñāna icchā kṛtīnām kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt na tu samāna viṣaya tvena api kvacid api akalpanāt samāna viṣayaka tve sati api samāna prakāraka jñāna abhāvena icchā kṛtyoḥ abhāvāt tasya āvaśyaka tvena gauravāt ca iti para siddhāntāt na ca sarvajña tve saṃśayaḥ na syāt iti doṣaḥ ghaṭaḥ saḥ iti ghaṭa tva prakārakam hi jñānam saṃśaya virodhi tat ca na vṛttam sva sāmagrī virahāt atas ghaṭa tva ādi sakala viśeṣa jñāne api sa ghaṭaḥ na vā iti saṃśayaḥ iti 
[061,iii^1]	upādhi jñānāt vyabhicāra jñāne sati na vyāpti niścayaḥ iti upādhiḥ nirūpyate tatra upādhiḥ sādhya tva abhimata vyāpaka tve sati sādhana tva abhimatā vyāpakaḥ anaupādhika tva jñānam ca na vyāpti jñāne hetuḥ atas vyāpaka tva ādi jñāne na anyonya āśrayaḥ yat vā vyāpaka tvam tadvat niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam tad pratiyogi tvam ca avyāpaka tvam pratiyogi tvam ca tad adhikaraṇān adhikaraṇa tvam iti vadanti tat na sādhana pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka upādhi avyāpteḥ na ca tayoḥ anupādhi tvam dūṣaka tā bīja sāmyāt mitra atanaya tvena śyāma tva sādhane śāka pāka ja tvasya pratyakṣa sparśa āśraya tvena vāyoḥ pratyakṣa tve sādhye udbhūta rūpavat tvasya ca śāstre prayojaka tvena upādhi tva svīkārāt ca iti pakṣa itare ati vyāptiḥ ca na ca vyatireke parvata itara anyatvāt iti atra itara anyatvasya asiddhi vāraṇa artham parvata padam viśeṣaṇam iti vyatireke vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt na saḥ upādhiḥ bādha unnītasya api anupādhita āpatteḥ na ceṣṭāpattiḥ 
[061,iii^2]	itara anyatvasya aprasiddhyā viśeṣaṇam vinā vyāpti agraheṇa tat sārthaka tvāt vastu gatyā sādhya vyāpakaḥ pakṣetaraḥ upādhiḥ iti ced astu tathā tathā api pakṣa atirikte sādhya vyāpaka tā grahāt upādheḥ dūṣaka tvam tat ca tatra api asti anyathā pakṣe sādhya sandehāt anupādhi tve upādhi mātram ucchidyeta vipakṣa avyāvartaka viśeṣaṇa śūnya tvam viśeṣaṇam tena bādha unnīta pakṣa itarasya parigrahaḥ tatra pakṣasya eva vipakṣa tvāt na tu parvata itara tva ādeḥ iti ced na na hi vastu vipakṣa avyāvartaka viśeṣaṇa śūnyam 
[061,iii^3]	sarvatra prameya tva ādeḥ sattvāt tatra upātta iti viśeṣaṇe siddhi asiddhi vyāghātaḥ tathā api ca sādhya vyāpaka tva sādhana avyāpaka tve tatra staḥ iti tad vyāvṛttyā pakṣe sādhya vyāvṛttiḥ atas hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ eva vyabhicāre ca avaśyam upādhiḥ iti pakṣetaraḥ eva tatra upādhiḥ syāt tāvat mātrasya eva dūṣaka tvāt ca vyartham viśeṣaṇam atas eva anumāna mātra ucchedaka tayā jāti tvāt na pakṣa itaraḥ upādhiḥ iti apāstam dūṣaṇa samartha tvena jāti tva abhāvāt etena pakṣa itara vyāvṛtti artham prakāra antaram api nirastam upādhi tva abhāve api dūṣaṇa samartha tvāt 
[061,iv]	atha upādhiḥ sva vyatirekeṇa sat pratipakṣa utthāpaka tayā dūṣaṇam pakṣa itara tva vyatirekaḥ ca na sādhya abhāva sādhakaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt na tu vyabhicāra unnāyaka tayā dūṣaṇam yathā hi sādhya vyāpaka upādhya vyāpya tayā hetoḥ sādhya avyāpya tvam tathā sādhya vyāpya hetu avyāpaka tayā upādheḥ na sādhya vyāpaka tvam api sidhyet vyāpti grāhakasya ubhayatra api sāmyena vinigamaka virahāt tasmāt yathā sādhya vyāpyena hetunā sādhyam sādhanīyam tathā sādhya vyāpaka upa adhi vyāvṛttyā sādhya abhāvaḥ api sādhanīyaḥ vyāpti graha taulyāt iti dūṣaka tā bījam saḥ ayam sat pratipakṣaḥ eva iti 
[061,v^1]	mā evam evam hi sat pratipakṣe upādhi udbhāvanam na syāt sa pratipakṣa antara vat kim ca evam bodha unnītaḥ api pakṣa itaraḥ na upādhiḥ syāt vyatireke asādhāraṇyāt nanu bādhe na upādhi niyamaḥ dhūmena hrade vahni sādhane tad abhāvāt na tu hetumati pakṣe bādhe pakṣa itara upādhi niyamaḥ pratyakṣe vahnau kṛtaka tvena anuṣṇa tve sādhye atejaḥ tu ādeḥ upādhi tva sambhavāt iti ced na tejaḥ mātra pakṣa tve atejaḥ tvam vinā anyasya upādheḥ abhāvāt kim ca parvata avayava vṛtti anya tvam parvata itara dravya tvam hṛd aparvata saṃyoga anādhāra tvam hṛd aparvata anyatva ādikam upādhiḥ syāt eva vyatireke asādha araṇya abhāvāt vyatirekiṇā sat pratipakṣa sambhavāt ca na ca asādha araṇyam 
[061,v^2]	tasya api sat pratipakṣa utthāpaka tayā doṣa tvāt tasmāt ubhayoḥ api vyāpti grāhaka sāmye virodhāt na vyāpti niścayaḥ kim tu ubhayatra vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ tathā ca vyabhicāra saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvena upādheḥ dūṣaka tvam tat ca pakṣa itare api asti tat uktam upādheḥ eva vyabhicāra śaṅkā iti bhavatu vā ukta nyāyena sakala anumāna bhaṅga bhiyā pakṣetaraḥ anupādhiḥ tathā api lakṣaṇam ativyāpakam na api sādhya samavyāpta tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tvam upādhi tvam dūṣaka tā bījasya vyabhicāra unnayanasya sat pratipakṣasya vā sāmyena viṣam avyāptasya api upādhi tvāt tathā dūṣaka tāyām sādhya vyāpya tvasya aprayojaka tvāt ca 
[062,i]	atha sādhya prayojakaḥ dharmaḥ upādhiḥ prayojaka tvam ca na nyūna adhika deśa vṛtteḥ tasmin sati abhavataḥ tena vinā api bhavataḥ tad aprayojaka tvāt anyathā pakṣa itarasya api upādhi tva prasaṅgāt iti ced na dūṣaṇa aupayikam hi prayojaka tvam iha vivakṣitam tat ca sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tvam eva iti tat eva prayojakam na tu adhikam vyartha tvāt 
[062,ii]	atha upādhiḥ saḥ ucyate yat dharmaḥ anyatra pratibimbate yathā japā kusumam sphaṭika lauhitye upādhiḥ tathā ca upādhi vṛtti vyāpya tvam hetu tva abhimate cakāsti tena asau upādhiḥ na ca vyāpya tva mātreṇa dūṣaka tvam iti sādhya vyāpaka tā āpīṣyate tathā ca samavyāptaḥ eva upādhiḥ iti ced tat kim viṣam avyāptasya dūṣa ka tā bīja abhāva anna upādhi śabda vācya tvam tathātve api upādhi pada pravṛtti nimitta abhāvāt vā na ādyaḥ tasya api vyabhicāra ādi unnāyaka tvāt na aparaḥ na hi loke samavyāptaḥ eva anyatra svadharma pratibimba janake eva upādhi pada prayogaḥ lābha ādi upādhinā kṛtam ityādau lābha ādau api upādhi pada prayogāt kim ca na śāstre laukika vyavahāra artham upādhi vyutpādanam kintu anumāna dūṣaṇa artham tat ca sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tva mātram iti śāstre tathā eva upādhi pada prayogaḥ 
[062,iii^1]	anye tu yat abhāvaḥ vyabhicāra virodhī saḥ upādhiḥ na ca viṣam avyāptasya abhāvaḥ vyabhicāram viruṇāt hi tasya abhāve api vyabhicārāt asti hi anitya tva vyāpakam prameya tvam tat vyāpyam ca guṇa tvam na ca anitya tva guṇa tvayoḥ vyāptiḥ asti samavyāptikasya ca vyatirekaḥ tathā na hi sādhya vyāpaka vyāpyībhūtasya vyāpyam yat tat sādhyam vyabhicarati vyabhicāre ca antataḥsādhyam eva upādhiḥ abhede api vyāpya vyāpaka tvāt sādhana avyāpaka tvāt ca iti svīcakruḥ tat na tava api hi avyabhicāre sādhya vyāpya vyāpya tvam tantram āvaśyaka tvāt lāghavāt ca na sādhya vyāpaka vyāpya tvam api 
[062,iii^2]	bhavatā eva vyabhicārasya darśita tvāt na ca sādhya vyāpya vyāpya tvam eva anaupādhika tvam sādhya vyāpyam iti atra api hi anaupādhika tvam tat eva vācyam tathā ca anavasthā iti anaupādhika tve ca vyāpti lakṣaṇe yāvat iti padam sādhya vyāpaka tve viśeṣaṇam dattam eva kim ca yasmin sati anumitiḥ na bhavati tat eva tatra dūṣaṇam na tu yat vyatireke bhavati eva iti etat garbham viruddha tva ādeḥ api adoṣa tva āpatteḥ na api pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tvanam upādhi tvam sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka upādhya vyāpanāt śabdaḥ abhidheyaḥ prameya tvāt iti atra aśrāvaṇa tvasya upādhi tva āpatteḥ ca śabda dharma guṇa tva avacchinna abhidheya tvam yatra rūpa ādau tatra aśrāvaṇa tvam vyāpakam pakṣe prameya tvasya sādhanasya avyāpakam hi tat ārdra indhanavat tva ādau upādhau pakṣa niyata tāddaśa dharma abhāvāt ca atha sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpakaḥ upādhiḥ tena dhvaṃsasya janya tvena dhvaṃsa pratiyogi tve sādhye sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpakam bhāva tvam upādhiḥ 
[062,iii^3]	śyāma tve śāka pākaja tvam upādhiḥ iti tat na pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka upādhya vyāpanāt jalam prameyam rasava tvāt iti atra rasavatva avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka pṛthivī tvasya upādhi tva prasaṅgāt sa upādhi tvāt asādhakam iti atra sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka vyabhicāri tve sādhana avacchinna iti asya vyartha tva prasaṅgāt ca kim ca pakṣa dvaye api viśiṣṭa sādhya vyabhicāram viśiṣṭa sādhya vyatirekam vā prasādhya paścāt kevala sādhya vyabhicāraḥ kevala sādhya vyatirekaḥ vā sādhanīyaḥ tathā ca artha antaram kevala sādhye hi vivādaḥ na tu viśiṣṭe atha prakṛta sādhya vyabhicāra siddhi artham viśiṣṭa sādhya vyabhicāraḥ sādhyaḥ iti ced na aprāpta kāla tvāt prathamam sādhya vyabhicāraḥ eva udbhāvyaḥ tatra asiddhau upādhiḥ iti ced tarhi prakṛta anumāne na upādhiḥ dūṣaṇam syāt kim ca sādhya vyabhicāra hetu tvena pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka vyabhicāraḥ eva upanyasanīyaḥ na upādhiḥ syāt etat paryavasita sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpakaḥ upādhiḥ 
[062,iii^4]	paryavasitam sādhyam pakṣa dharmatā bala labhyam yathā śabdaḥ anitya tva atirikta śabda dharma atirikta dharmavān meya tvāt iti atra paryavasitam yat sādhyam anitya tvam tasya vyāpakam kṛtaka tvam upādhiḥ yadi ca tathā eva kṛtaka tvam api śabde sādhyate tadā anitya tvam upādhiḥ tat uktam vādyukta sādhya niyama cyutaḥ api kathakaiḥ upādhiḥ udbhāvyaḥ paryavasitam niyamayan dūṣa kata bīja sāmrājyāt iti anena pakṣa dharma sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka upādhiḥ saṃgṛhyate tāddaśa sādhyasya paryavasita tvāt iti tat na evam hi dvi aṇukasya sāvayava tve siddhe dvi aṇukam anitya dravyā samavetam janya mahat tva anadhikaraṇa dravya tvāt iti atra nisparśa dravya samaveta tvam upādhiḥ syāt bhavati hi nitya dravya samaveta tvam paryavasitam sādhyam tasya vyāpakam sādhana avyāpakam ca kim ca pakṣa dharmatā bala labhya sādhya siddhau niṣphalaḥ upādhiḥ tad asiddhau ca kasya vyāpakaḥ na hi sa upādhau pakṣa dharma tā balāt sādhyam sidhyati yasya vyāpakaḥ upādhiḥ syāt iti 
[062,iv]	atra ucyate yat vyabhicāri tvena sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāri tvam saḥ upādhiḥ lakṣaṇam tu paryavasita sādhya vyāpaka tve sati sādhana avyāpaka tvam yat dharma avacchedena sādhyam prasiddham tad avacchinnam paryavasitam sādhyam sa ca dharmaḥ kvacid sādhanam eva kvacid dravya tva ādi kvacid mahānasa tva ādi tathā hi samavyāptasya viṣam avyāptasya vā sādhya vyāpakasya vyabhicāreṇa sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāraḥ sphuṭaḥ eva vyāpaka vyabhicāriṇaḥ tad vyāpya vyabhicāra niyamāt sādhana avacchinna pakṣa dharma avacchinna sādhya vyāpakayoḥ vyabhicāri tvena sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāri tvam eva yathā dhvaṃsasya anitya tve sādhye bhāva tvasya vāyoḥ pratyakṣa tve sādhye udbhūta rūpavat tvasya ca viśeṣaṇa avyabhicāriṇi sādhane viśiṣṭa vyabhicārasya viśeṣya vyabhicāri tva niyamāt atas eva na artha antaram viśeṣaṇa avyabhicāri tvena jñāte sādhane viśiṣṭa vyabhicāraḥ sidhyan viśeṣī asādhya vyabhicāram ādāya eva sidhyati pakṣa dharma tā balāt anyathā pratīteḥ aparyavasānāt na ca pakṣa dharma tā balāt prakṛta siddhau artha antaram 
[062,v_062,vi]	yat vā pratyakṣa sparśa āśraya tvam pratyakṣa tva vyabhicāri dravya tva avyabhicāri tve sati dravya pratyakṣa tva vyāpaka vyabhicāri tvāt mahattva vat tathā mitrātanaya tvam śyāma tva vyabhicāri mitra atanayatva avyabhicāri tve sati śyāma mitra atanaya tva vyāpaka vyabhicāri tvāt aghaṭa tva vat avyabhicāraḥ ca tad samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam tat ca abhede api yat vā yaḥ sādhana vyabhicārī sādhya vyabhicāra unnāyakaḥ saḥ upādhiḥ tattvam ca sākṣāt paramparayā vā iti na artha antaram 
[063,i]	kiṃca artha antarasya puruṣa doṣa tayā ābhāsa antarasya tatra abhāvāt upādhiḥ eva bhāva tva ādikam doṣaḥ na ca evam śabdaḥ abhidheyaḥ prameya tvāt iti atra aśrāvaṇa tvam jalam prameyam rasavat tvāt iti atra pṛthivī tvam upādhiḥ syāt kevala anvayitva sādhaka pramāṇena tatra sādhya siddheḥ upādheḥ viśiṣṭa avyāpaka tvāt na ca pakṣa itare sva vyāghātaka tvena anupādhau ati vyāptiḥ tatra anukūla tarka abhāvena sādhya vyāpaka tva aniścayāt sahacāra darśana ādeḥ tena vinā saṃśāyaka tvāt iti uktam 
[063,ii]	bādha unnīte ca anukūla tarkaḥ asti eva iti evam parvata avayava vṛtti anya tva ādeḥ api na upādhi tvam pakṣa mātra vyāvartaka viśeṣaṇavat tvāt atas eva dhūme ārdra indhana prabhava vahnimat tvam dravya bahis indriya pratyakṣa tve udbhūta rūpavat tvam mitra atanaya śyāma tve śāka pākaja tvam janyā nitya tve bhāva tvam upādhiḥ tat utkarṣeṇa sādhya utkarṣāt ananyathā siddha anvaya vyatirekataḥ vaidyakāt kāraṇa tā avagamena ghaṭa unmajjana prasaṅgena sādhya vyāpaka tā niścayāt tat kim kārya kāraṇayoḥ eva vyāptiḥ tathā ca bahudhā vyākulī syāt iti ced na tad upajīvyāni eṣām api anukūla tarkeṇa vyāpti grahāt yatra sādhya upādhyoḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ vā vyāpti grāhaka sāmyāt na ekatra vyāpti niścayaḥ tatra sandigdha upādhi tvam vyabhicāra saṃśaya upadhāyaka tvāt yadā ca tādṛśī ekatra anukūla tarka avatāraḥ tadā hetu tvam upādhi tvam vā niścitam pakṣetarasya sva vyāghātaka tvena na hetu vyabhicāra saṃśāyaka tvam atas na saṃdigdha upādhiḥ api saḥ 
[063,iii_063,iv]	yat tu pakṣa itarasya yathā sādhya vyāpaka tvam tathā sādhya abhāva vyāpaka tvam api grāhaka sāmyāt tathā ca ubhaya vyāpaka nivṛttyā sādhya tad abhāvābhyām pakṣe nivartitavyam na ca evam tathā ca pakṣa itaraḥ sādhya vyāpaka tā saṃśayena sandigdhaḥ katham param dūṣayet iti tat na tathā hi sādhya vyāpaka tā pakṣam ālambya hetu vyabhicāra saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvena dūṣaṇam syāt eva 
[063,v_063,vi]	nanu yatra upādhiḥ tatra anukūla tarkaḥ yadi na asti tadā tad abhāvena eva vyāpteḥ agrahaḥ atha asti tadā sādhya vyāpya avyāpaka tvena upādhiḥ sādhya avyāpaka tva niścayāt na upādhiḥ iti ubhayathā api na upādhiḥ dūṣaṇam na ca vyāpti abhāva vyāpyam ubhayam atas upādhiḥ api tad abhāva unnayanena doṣaḥ iti vācyam upādheḥ ātma lābha artham anukūla tarka abhāva upajīvaka tvena tasya eva doṣa tvāt iti ced na sa upādhau ekatra sādhya tad abhāva sambandhasya viruddha tvāt avacchedaka bhedena tad ubhaya sambandhaḥ vācyaḥ tathā ca sādhanesādhya sambandhi tāvacchedaka rūpam anukūla tarkā bhāva upajīvanam antareṇa upādhiḥ āvaśyakaḥ tathā anukūla tarka abhāvaḥ api āvaśyakaḥ iti ubhayoḥ api vinigamaka abhāvāt dūṣaka tvam 
[063,vii]	anye tu yat vyāvṛttyā yasya sādhanasya sādhyam nivartate sa dharmaḥ tatra hetau upādhiḥ sa ca dharmaḥ yasya abhāvāt pakṣe sādhya sādhana sambandha abhāvaḥ yathā ārdra indhanavat tvam vyāvartate hi tad vyāvṛttyā dhūmavat tvamayaḥ golake atas eva tatra sādhya sādhana saṃbandha abhāvaḥ pakṣe evam bhāva tva vyāvṛttyā dhvaṃse janya tva anitya tvayoḥ sambandhaḥ nivartamānaḥ pakṣa dharma tā balāt anitya tva abhāvam ādāya sidhyati tathā vāyau udbhūta rūpavat tvam nivartamānam bahis dravya tve sati pratyakṣa tvam nivartayat pratyakṣa tva abhāvam ādāya sidhyati tathā ca ubhayatra api pakṣe sādhya abhāva siddhyā sādhya sādhana sambandha abhāvaḥ asti iti atas eva bādhānunnīta pakṣa itarasya anupādhi tvam sva vyāghātaka tvena tad vyatirekasya sādhya avyāvartaka tvāt iti 
[063,viii_063,ix]	yat tu upādhi mātrasya lakṣaṇam vyatireki dharma tvam pakṣetaraḥ api kvacid upādhiḥ tat tad upādheḥ tu tad tad sādhya vyāpaka tve sati tad tad sādhana avyāpaka tvam na ca vahni dhūma sambandha upādhiḥ pakṣetara tvam syāt iti vācyam āpādya aprasiddheḥ iti tat na anumiti pratibandhaka jñāna viṣaya tā avacchedakam upādhi tvam iha nirūpyam tat ca na vyatireki tvam atiprasaṅgāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇe vahni dhūma sambandhe pakṣa itaratvasya upādhi tva prasaṅgāt ca 
[063,x_063,xi]	kecitu sādhana vyāpakaḥ api upādhiḥ kvacid yatra pakṣa āvṛttiḥ hetuḥ yathā karakā pṛthivī kaṭhina saṃyoga āditi atra anuṣṇa aśīta sparśavat tvam na ca tatra svarūpa asiddhiḥ eva doṣaḥ sarvatra upādheḥ dūṣaṇa antara saṃkarāt iti āhuḥ sādhyam ca na upādhiḥ vyabhicāra sādhane sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvāt anumiti mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt ca 
[063,xii^1]	sa ca ayam dvividhaḥ niścitaḥ sandigdhaḥ ca sādhya vyāpaka tvena sādhana avyāpaka tvena ca niścitaḥ vyabhicāra niścaya ādhāyaka tayā niścita upādhiḥ yathā vahnimat tvena dhūmavat tve sādhye ārdra indhana prabhava vahnimat tvam yatra ca sādhana avyāpaka tva san deha ssādhya vyāpaka tva saṃśayaḥ vā tad ubhaya sandehaḥ vā tatra hetu vyabhicāra saṃśaya ādhāyaka tayā sandigdha upādhiḥ yathā mitra atanaya tvena śyāma tve sādhye śāka ādi āhāra pariṇati ja tvam na ca tena eva hetunā śāka pākaja tvam api sādhyam tatra śyāma tvasya upādhi tvāt ubhayasya api sādhane artha antaram śyāma tva mātre hi vivādaḥ na tu ubhayatra na
[063,xii^2_064,ii]	ca evam dhūmāt vahni anumāne api vahni sāmagrī upādhiḥ syāt tatra vahninā iva tad sāmagrya api samam dhūmasya anaupādhika tva niścayāt atra tu mitra atanaya tva vyāpya śyāma sāmagryā sthātavyam iti atra kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādīnām vyāpti grāhakāṇām abhāvāt atas eva sādhya sāmagryā saha hetoḥ api yatra vyāpti grāhakam asti tatra sāmagrī na upādhiḥ yatra tu tat na asti tatra sā api upādhiḥ iti abhisandhāya sāmagrī ca kvacid na upādhiḥ na tu sarvatra iti uktam yathā tulya yogakṣemayoḥ upādheḥ vyāpaka tā āsandehe īśvara anumāne śarīra janya tva aṇu tva ādiḥ yathā ca śākapāka janya tvasya sādhya vyāpaka tā āsandehe mitra atanaya tve yat tu upādhi sandehaḥ na upādhiḥ na vā hetvābhāsa antaram iti tad udbhāvane niranuyojya anuyogaḥ iti tat na sandigdha anaikāntika vat vyabhicāra saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvena dūṣaka tvāt upādheḥ iva vyabhicāra niścaya ādhāyaka tayā 
[064,iii]	idānīm upādheḥ dūṣaka tā bījam nirūpyate na api asya vyatireka dvārā sat pratipakṣa tvena dūṣaka tvam tadā hi sat pratipakṣe sat pratipakṣa antara vat upādheḥ udbhāvanam na syāt na ca pratipakṣa bāhulyena adhika bala artham udbhāvanam śatam api andhānām na paśyati iti nyāyāt ekena api bahūnām pratibandhāt ca vyāpti pakṣa dharmate hi balam tat ca tulyam eva na tu bhūyaḥ tvam api ekasmāt api anumiti darśanāt sandigdha upādheḥ adūṣaka tā āpatteḥ ca tad vyatirekasya pakṣe sandigdha tvāt 
[064,iv]	api ca evam bādha unnīta pakṣa itarasya upādhi tvam na syāt vyatireke asādhāraṇyāt pakṣa vṛttiḥ ca upādhiḥ na syāt yathā ghaṭaḥ anityaḥ dravya tvāt iti atra kāryatvam andhakāraḥ dravyam svātantryeṇa pratīyamāna tvāt iti atra aśrāvaṇa tvam tad vyatirekasya pakṣa āvṛtti tvāt na ca na ayam upādhiḥ tad lakṣaṇa sattvāt anyathā api dūṣaka tva sambhavāt ca 
[064,v^1]	kiṃca sādhya vyāpya avyāpaka tvena upādheḥ sādhya avyāpaka tve tad vyatirekeṇa katham sat pratipakṣaḥ na hi avyāpaka vyatirekāt avyāpya vyatirekaḥ na api vyāpti viraha rūpa tayā asiddha tvena anaupādhika tvasya vyāpti tva nirāsāt na api anaupādhika tva jñānasya vyāpti dhīhetu tvasya tattvena vyāpti jñāna kāraṇa vighaṭaka tayā vyāpya tva asiddhau antarbhāvaḥ na hi anyasya sādhya vyāpaka tva sādhana avyāpaka tva jñānam anya vyāpti jñānam prati pratibandhakam iti uktam na ca sādhya vyāpaka avyāpya tva jñāne vidyamāne sādhanasya sādhya vyāpya tva jñānam na utpattum arhati iti vācyam na hi sādhya vyāpaka vyāpya tva jñānam vyāpti jñāna kāraṇam 
[064,v^2]	yena tad pratibandhakam syāt kiṃtu sādhya vyāpaka vyabhicāri tvena sādhya vyabhicāri tva jñāna dvārā na api vyabhicāra unnāyaka tvena yathā hi sādhya vyāpaka vyabhicāritayā sādhanasya sādhya vyabhicāri tvam anumeyam tathā sādhya vyāpya vyabhicāri tvena sādhya vyabhicāri tvam upādheḥ api anumeyam vyāpti grāhaka sāmyāt na api sādhya vyāpaka avyāpya tvena vyāpti viraha unnāyaka tayā sādhya vyāpya avyāpaka tvena upādheḥ eva sādhya avyāpaka tva sādhanāt tasmāt upādhiḥ hetvābhāsa antaram iti 
[064,vi_064,vii]	ucyate ārdra indhanavat tva ādeḥ tarka ādinā sādhya vyāpaka tva sādhana avyāpaka tve niścite dūṣaka tā bīja cintanam yadi hi sādhya sādhana sahacāra darśanena upādhau sādhya vyāpaka tā niścayaḥ eva na asti tadā upādhi tva niścaya abhāvāt dūṣaka tā eva na asti iti kva bahirbhāva antar bhāva cintā kim ca sat pratipakṣa tayā vyāpya tva asiddha tayā svātantryeṇa vā yadi doṣa tvam sarvathā sādhya vyāpaka tā niścayaḥ vācyaḥ tena vinā teṣām abhāvāt tasmāt upādhi niścayāt vyabhicāra niścayaḥ tad saṃśayāt tad saṃśayaḥ iti vyabhicāra jñāna dvārā sādhya vyāpaka avyāpya tvena vyāpti viraha unnāyaka tayā vā upādheḥ dūṣaka tvam yat vā sādhya vyāpaka abhāva vat vṛtti tayā sādhya vyabhicāri tvam unneyam na ca sādhana abhāva vat vṛtti tvam upādhiḥ iti vācyam upādhi mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt sat pratipakṣe pūrva sādhana vyatireka vat avṛtti gagana ādau sādhya avyāpaka tvāt saṃyoga ādau hetau sādhana vyāpaka tvāt ca 
[064,viii^1]	atha upādhi ābhāsaḥ asādharaṇa viparyayaḥ yathā anvavyatirekiṇi sādhye bādha unnīta anya pakṣa itara tvam aprasiddha sādhya viparyayaḥ yathā kevala anvayini sādhye pakṣetara tva ādiḥ bādhita sādhya viparyayaḥ yathā vahniḥ uṣṇaḥ tejaḥ tu āditi atra akṛtaka tvam pakṣa avyāpaka viparyayaḥ yathā kṣiti ādikam sa kartṛkam kāryatva āditi atra aṇu vyatirikta tvam atra aṇu vyatirekasya kṣiti ādeḥ eka deśa vṛttyā bhāga asiddheḥ pūrva sādhana vyatirekaḥ yathā śarkarā rasaḥ anityaḥ anitya vṛtti guṇa tvāt 
[064,viii^2]	rasaḥ nityaḥ rasanā indriya janya nirvikalpaka viṣaya tvāt rasa tva vat iti ādau pūrva sādhana tāyāḥ prayoga anurodhi tvena avyavasthita tvāt kadācid nitya tva sādhana vyatirekasya upādhi tvam kadācid anitya tva sādhana vyatirekitvasya iti vastu vyavasthā na syāt upādheḥ nitya doṣa tvāt ca na hi yat yena sa upādhi sambaddham tat tena anupādhi tva sambaddham sambhavati na tu sat pratipakṣa ucchedaḥ pūrva sādhana vyatirekasya anupādhi tve bījam sthāpanāyāḥ yathābhāsa tvam tatra pūrva sādhana vyatirekasya sādhya vyāpaka tvena anupādhi tvāt na ca pūrva hetoḥ tatas eva asādhaka tvāt sat pratipakṣa vaiyarthyam tatra iti vācyam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām sat pratipakṣa sambhavāt pūrva sādhana vyāpya vyatirekaḥ yathā akartṛkatva anumāne nitya tva ādiḥ pakṣa vipakṣa anyatara anyaḥ yathā prasiddha anumāne parvata jala hradānya tara anyatvam pakṣa itara sādhya abhāvaḥ yathā atra eva parvata itara agrimat tvam na ca atra vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam dūṣaṇam tattve api upādheḥ ābhāsa tvāt tad tulyam ca yathā atra eva parvata itara indhanavat tvam evam vahni sāmagrya ādikam ūhyam 
[065,i^1]	vyāpti anantaram pakṣa dharma tā nirūpyate tatra na tāvat saṃdigdha sādhya dharma tvam pakṣa tvam saṃdehaḥ hi na viśeṣaṇam parāmarśa pūrvam liṅga darśana vyāpti smaraṇa ādinā tasya nāśāt na upalakṣaṇam avyāvartaka tā āpatteḥ na api sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ubhaya abhāvasya pratyeka sattve api sattvāt na api abhāva dvayam tathā bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvasya vyartha tvāt hrada ādeḥ pakṣatve api bādha hetu asiddhi ādeḥ āvaśyaka tvena anumiti anutpādāt na api sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ iti śrutyā samāna viṣayaka śravaṇa anantaram manana bodhanāt pratyakṣat daṣṭe api anumāna darśanāt eka liṅga avagate api liṅga antareṇa tad anumānāt ca mantavyaḥ ca upapattibhiḥ iti smaraṇāt atha siṣā dhayiṣita sādhya dharmā dharmī pakṣaḥ tathā hi mumukṣoḥ śabdāt ātma avagame api mananasya mokṣa upāya tvena siddhi viśeṣa anumiti icchayā ātma anumānam atas eva pratyakṣa parikalitam api artham anumānena bubhutsante tarkarasikāḥ na hi kariṇi ddaṣṭe cītkāreṇa tam anumimate anumātāraḥ iti vācaspati vacanayoḥ avirodhaḥ 
[065,i^2]	anumitsā ta dvirahābhyām tat upapatteḥ iti ced na sandeha vat parāmarśa pūrvam siṣā dhayiṣāyāḥ api abhāvāt yogyatāyāḥ ca anirūpaṇāt siṣā dhayiṣā virahe api ghana garjitena megha anumānāt sva kāraṇa adhīna tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśa balena anapekṣita anumāna darśanāt ca iti ucyate siṣā dhayiṣā viraha saha kṛta sādhaka pramāṇa bhāvaḥ yatra asti sa pakṣaḥ tena siṣā dhayiṣā viraha saha kṛtam sādhaka pramāṇam yatra asti sa na pakṣaḥ yatra sādhaka pramāṇe satyasati vā siṣā dhayiṣā yatra vā ubhaya abhāvaḥ tatra viśiṣṭa abhāvāt pakṣa tvam yadi api pakṣatvasya kevala anvayitvāt na asya bhedaka tvam tathā api pakṣa pada pravṛtti nimittam uktam 
[065,ii_065,iii^1]	pakṣa dharmasya vyāpti viśiṣṭa jñāna m anum iti hetaḥ nanu vyāpya tāvacchedaka prakāreṇa vyāpti smaraṇam pakṣa dharma tā jñānam tathā lāghavāt parāmarśa hetu tvena āvaśyaka tvāt ca evam dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpyaḥ dhūmavān aḥ ca ayam iti jñāna dvayāt eva anumitiḥ astu na ca anumitim prati vyāpya tva jñānam eva hetuḥ lāghavāt upajīvya tvāt ca iti vācyam tasya anumiteḥ pūrvam asiddhau yugapad upasthiti abhāvāt atha yathā tat tā viśiṣṭa smaraṇe sati indriya saṃnikṛṣṭe saḥ eva ayam iti abheda pratyayaḥ bhavati tathā indriya saṃnikṛṣṭe dhūme vahni vyāpya dhūma smaraṇe dhūma tva sādhāraṇa dharma darśanāt vyāpyaḥ ayam iti abheda pratyayaḥ syāt sāmagryā vṛtta tvāt iti saḥ eva anumiti hetuḥ iti ced na pratyakṣa sāmagrītaḥ anumiti sāmagryā balavat tvāt anumitiḥ eva utpadyate na tu vyāpya abheda pratyakṣam anyathā tava api parāmarśa anantaram tad anu vyavasāyaḥ vā bhavet na tu anumitiḥ eva atha vahni vyāpyaḥ dhūmaḥ iti smarataḥ parvatīya dhūma indriya saṃnikarṣeṇa prathamatas eva vyāpti dhūma tvayoḥ vaiśiṣṭyam yatra bhāsate viśeṣaṇa jñānasya pūrvam vṛtta tvāt tatra 
[065,iii^2]	yatra vā āpta vākyāt vahni vyāpi avān ayam iti jñānam tatra ubhayatra api lāghavāt pakṣa dharma vyāpya tva jñāna hetu tva kalpanāt anyatra api tathā iti ced na indriya asaṃnikṛṣṭe atīndriye ca liṅge pratyakṣa viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagrī virahāt tena vinā anumiti anutpāda āpatteḥ asmad ukta sāmagryāḥ ca tatra api sattvāt na ca anumāna ādinā tatra parāmarśaḥ anavasthānāt atha yathā saḥ devadattaḥ gauraḥ na vā 
[065,iii^3]	paramāṇu guru tva adhikaraṇam na vā iti saṃśayaḥ bahis asvatantreṇa api manasā koṭi smaraṇa viśeṣa adarśana ādi sahakāri vaśāt janyate yathā vā nidrā sahakāreṇa bāhya svapna anubhavaḥ tathā iha api jñāna antara upanīta viśeṣye vyāpti smaraṇa saha kṛtena manasā parāmarśaḥ janyate tad anantaram anumiti darśanāt iti ced na vyāpti smaraṇa ādeḥ pramāṇa antara tā āpatteḥ tat eva hi pramāṇa antaram yat asādhāraṇam sahakārya āsādya manaḥ bahis gocara pramām janayati yathā indriya ādi saṃśaya svapnau tu na preme iti na nidrā ādeḥ pramāṇa antara tvam na ca tava api katham sa dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpya iti vyavahāraḥ 
[065,iii^4]	tadānīm tad vyāpya tva anubhāvaka abhāvāt iti vācyam tatra smṛta dhūme dhūma tvena vahni vyāpyatva anumānāt na ca tvad mate dhūma tvena vyāpya tva anubhavaḥ sambhavati atas eva yaḥ vahni vyāpyavān saḥ avaśyam vahnimān iti vyāpti jñānavataḥ anumitiḥ na anyathā atha parvatīya dhūme jñāte vahni vyāpyaḥ ayam na vā iti saṃśaye api anumitiḥ syāt iti ced na dhūmaḥ vahni vyāpya iti smaraṇe vidyamāne dhūma tva jñānasya viśeṣa darśana tvena saṃśaya abhāvāt anyathā parāmarśaḥ api kutas na syāt saṃśayena pratibandhāt iti ced tulyam na ca sāmānya niścayasya sāmānya saṃśaya nivartaka tvāt dhūma sāmānye saṃśayaḥ mā bhūt 
[065,iii^5]	viśeṣa saṃśayaḥ tu viśeṣa niścaya nivartanīyaḥ iti dhūma viśeṣe saṃśaya nirāsa artham pṛthak vyāpti niścayaḥ vācyaḥ iti vācyam yatra hi yat vyāvartaka dharma darśanam tatra na tad saṃśayaḥ tat ca sāmānye viśeṣe vā iti vastutas tu dhūma tva puraskāreṇa vyāpti smaraṇe pakṣa dharma tā jñāne ca anumitiḥ bhavati eva nanu bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā ubhayathā api prameyam iti atra bhāva tva abhāva tvayoḥ vyāpyatāvaccheda kayoḥ agrahāt anumānam na syāt tad anya anyatva rūpasya antara tvasya liṅga tva abhāvāt iti ced na bhāva tva abhāva tva anyāni adharmavat tvasya liṅga tvāt evam dhūma āloka anyatara tvam api liṅgam atha yat vyatireka jñānam yat utpatti pratibandhakam tat tad niścaya sādhyam tathā ca pakṣa dharmasya vyāpya bheda jñānam anumiti pratibandhakam atas vyāpya abheda jñānam tat hetuḥ siddhyati iti ced na dhūma tva puraskāreṇa vyāpti smaraṇa pakṣa dharmatā jñāne sati viśeṣa darśanāt na dhūme vyāpya bheda jñānam 
[065,iii^6]	kim tu anumiteḥ eva tatra utpattiḥ tad sāmagrī sattvāt atas na vyāpya bheda jñānam anumiti pratibandhakam yena vyāpya abheda jñānam tat hetuḥ syāt na ca dhūma tva puraskāreṇa vyāpti smaraṇa pakṣa dharma tā jñāne iyam dhūma vyaktiḥ vahni vyāpyā na iti bhrāmyataḥ anumiti āpattiḥ atas viśiṣṭa jñānam tat hetuḥ iti vācyam dhūma tvasya viśeṣasya darśanena tādṛśa bhramānutpatteḥ tatra anumiti sadbhāvāt eva anyathā niścaya sāmagryām satyām bhrama anantaram parāmarśaḥ eva kutas na bhavati astu vā vyāpya tayā pakṣa dharma tayā ca avagatasya bheda agrahaḥ eva anumiti hetuḥ parāmarśa hetu tayā tasya āvaśyaka tvāt atas eva āsat nikṛṣṭa dhūma jñānāt api anumitiḥ na ca evam gauravam tadā viśiṣṭa jñāna anupasthiteḥ na ca janaka jñāna avirodhinaḥ jñānasya apratibandhaka tvāt bheda grahaḥ na pratibandhakaḥ iti vācyam abheda jñānasya ajanaka tvāt tvayā api liṅga parāmarśe tādṛśasya pratibandhaka tva svīkārāt ca 
[065,iv]	atha go tvam madhura tva avāntara jātiḥ vā liṅgam na syāt tad gata dharma antarasya abhāvāt atas eva tasya vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti ced na vyakteḥ eva tatra prakāra tvāt na hi gauḥ gotvam iti jñānayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ anyathā go tvam iti jñānasya nirvikalpaka tva āpattyā vyāpya tva grahe parāmarśe ca anupayogāt gavetara āvṛtti tve sati sakala go vṛtti tvam go tva tvam iti anubhavāt ca na ca evam anavasthā tad itara vṛtti tve sati tad vṛtti tvasya anubhavena apalāpa asambhavāt 
[066,i^1]	atra ucyate ayam ālokaḥ dhūmaḥ vai ubhayathā api vahni vyāpya iti jñānam tatas anumitiḥ na ca dhūma tvena āloka tvena vā tatra niścayaḥ atha tad anya anya tvam eva tatra liṅgam na ca tad ajñāna daśāyām anumiti darśanāt na tathā iti vācyam dhūma ālokānya anyatva jñānam vinā tava api tatra vyāpya tva aniścayena tad artham tad bodha āvaśyaka tvāt iti ced na na hi dhūma ālokānya anya tvam dhūmānya anya tvam vā vyāpya tāvacchedakam gauravāt vyabhicārāḥ vāraka viśeṣaṇavat tvāt ca kim tu dhūma tva ādikam tat ca tatra saṃdigdham eva nanu tad anyā anyat vahni vyāpyam eva vyabhicāra abhāvena vyāpti viraha sādhanasya bādhita tvāt puruṣaḥ tu tatra nīladhūmavat tvāt iti atreva adhikena nigṛhyate na tu vyāpya tva asiddhyā iti ced na tad anyā anyat dhūma āloka svarūpam eva tat ca vyāpyam iti satyam na ca vastu gatyā vyāpya jñānāt anumitiḥ atiprasaṅgāt kim tu vyāpya tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñānāt na ca tad anya anya tvam vahni vyāpya tāvacchedakam iti uktam na ca tad anya anya tvāt vahni vyāpya tvam api tatra na anumeyam 
[066,i^2]	vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt iti vācyam pratyakṣam hi tad anya anyatva viśeṣa darśanāt vyāpya tva jñānam janayati viśeṣaṇa jñāna viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya indriya saṃnikarṣa tada saṃsarga āgraha viśeṣa darśanānām sattvena vahni vyāpya tva pratyakṣa sattvāt na ca evam na pratyakṣe api tad anya anyatva jñānam sahakārī iti vācyam anvaya vyatirekābhyām guroḥ api tasya viśeṣa darśana tvena pratyakṣa sahakāri tvāt tasmāt tat anya anyatva jñānam tatra vyāpya tā jñāna upakṣīṇam na tu sākṣāt anumiti hetuḥ iti kim ca vahni vyāpi avān ayam iti śābda jñāne vyāpyattva jñānam kāraṇam iti anyatra api tathā 
[066,ii^1]	atha vahni vyāpya tvam api vahni vyāpya tāvacchedakam tathā hi vahninirūpitā dhūma ādi pratyeka vṛttiḥ eva vyāptiḥ vyāpti tvena sakala dhūma ādi vṛtti vyāpti avacchedikā āśraya bhedena ca vyāpti bhedāt iti ced na sakala dhūma ādi vṛtti vyāptau māna abhāvāt yatra vahni vyāpyaḥ tatra vahniḥ iti vyāpti buddhau śābda vyāpya tva buddhau ca pratyeka vṛtti vyāpti āśrayatvasya eva viṣaya tvāt pratyeka vṛtti vyāpti jñānam vinā tad bodha abhāvāt api ca yatra dhūma tu a vyāptyoḥ vaiśiṣṭyam prathamam eva pratyakṣeṇa yugapad pakṣa dharme bhāsate tatra lāghavāt vyāpya tva jñāna tvam eva kāraṇa tāvacchedakam na ca evam atirikta viśiṣṭa jñāna kāraṇa tve gauravam doṣāya sa pramāṇaka tvāt kāraṇa tā graha daśāyām phala mukha gauravasya siddhi asiddhi bhyām adoṣa tvāt na ca asaṃnikṛṣṭe dhūme tad abhāvaḥ 
[066,ii^2]	bhavat matā anumiti hetu vyāpti smaraṇa dhūma tva jñāna sahitena manasā tad utpādāt yathā paramāṇuḥ niravayava dravyam nitya parimāṇavat tvāt ākāśa vat ityādau pratyeka anumāna upanīta atīndriya sādhya sādhanayoḥ ākāśa vṛtti tayā smaraṇe vyabhicāra ajñāne manasā vyāpti anubhavaḥ anumānayoḥ pratyeka tad ubhaya sahacāra viṣaya tvena vyāpti agrāhaka tvāt na ca atīndriya vyāpya tvam atīndriye anumeyam tatra api vyāpti grāhaka abhāvāt na ca tad upanaya sahitasya manasaḥ bahis artha pramā hetu tve upanayasya pramāṇa antara tvam indriya ādeḥ saṃnikarṣa vat upanayasya niyata vyāpāra abhāvena pramāya ām akaraṇa tvāt sahakāritā ca tad abhāve api bhavati bahis indriya liṅga sādṛśya ādi vyāpāram vinā api cintā upanīta padārthānām bādhakān avatāre saṃsarga anubhavasya sakala jana siddha tvāt katham anyathā kavi kā vya ādikam iti 
[066,iii]	syāt etat pakṣa dharmasya vyāpya tā jñānam na indriyeṇa vahneḥ asaṃnikarṣe tat niyata sāmānādhikaraṇyasya vyāpya tvasya asyogya tvāt na ca dhūma tvena sakala dhūma vyāpya tau agamāt dhūma viśeṣe saṃskārāt smaraṇāt vā upanīta vyāpya abheda grahaḥ pratyabhijñāne tat tā viśiṣṭasya iva iti vācyam evam hi dhūmavat tvena vahnimat tva jñānāt dhūma vat viśeṣe parvate saṃskāra vaśāt pratyakṣeṇa vyāpti jñāna apekṣeṇa vahni mada bheda grahaḥ vahnimat tva saṃsarga grahaḥ vā astu kim anumānena 
[066,iv_066,v]	pṛthak vahnimat tva smaraṇam tatra na asti kim tu vyāpti avacchedaka tayā iti ced na vahnimān na vā iti saṃśaya anurodhena svatantra vahnimat tva smaraṇāt na ca viśiṣṭa jñāne svatantra viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena hetu tvam gauravāt atha yaḥ yatra viśiṣya pūrvam avagataḥ sa tatra saṃskāra vaśāt yathārtha pratyakṣe bhāsate yathā tat ta apratyabhijñāne na ca parvate viśiṣya purā vahniḥ avagataḥ yatra candane saurabham upalabdham tatra saṃskāra vaśāt cakṣuṣā surabhi candanam iti jñānam anyathā anumitiḥ iti ced tarhi pakṣa dharma dhūme api na purā viśiṣya vyāptiḥ avagata iti katham saṃskāra vaśāt tad gata vyāpti bodhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa
