[066,vi]	na ca sahacāra darśana janya saṃskāra sahitena indriyeṇa vyabhicāra jñāna abhāve sati mahānasīya dhūma vat parvatīya dhūme vyāpti avagamaḥ vahneḥ tu na pratyakṣa sāmagrī saṃnikarṣa abhāvāt iti vācyam hetu sādhya sākṣātkāram vinā pratyakṣeṇa vyāpti agrahāt na ca parvate vahni sākṣātkāraḥ na ca pakṣa dharmasya sādhya sāmāna adhikaraṇya viśeṣaḥ vyāptiḥ pakṣe sādhya graham vinā iti uktam 
[066,vii_066,ix]	ucyate viśeṣaṇa jñānam tasya viśeṣye sambandhaḥ tayoḥ asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ viśeṣa darśanam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya indriya saṃnikarṣaḥ gaurayam ityādi yathārtha viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa kāraṇam asti ca atra api vyāpti smaraṇam smṛta vyāpteḥ pakṣa vṛtti dhūme sattvam ekā eva hi sā vyāptiḥ tayoḥ asaṃsarga āgrahaḥ dhūma tva viśeṣa darśanam vyāpti viśiṣṭa dhūma indriya saṃnikarṣaḥ ca vyāpti viśiṣṭa jñāna kāraṇam na ca vahni viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagrī vahneḥ asaṃnikarṣāt kaścid tu dhūma tve paramparā sambandhena vahni vyāpya tvam pūrvam gṛhītam tathā ca saṃskāra upanītam vahni vyāpya tvam paramparā sambandhena pakṣa vṛtti dhūma tve pratyabhijñāyate tad vṛtti tvena pūrvam anubhavāt evam ca dhūma tva vyāpya tva parāmarśāt eva anumitiḥ iti prāha 
[066,x]	bhavatu tāvat evam tathā api jātiḥ eva liṅgam syāt na tu vyaktiḥ tathā ca sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyaktau vyāpti graha artham sāmānya lakṣaṇa pratyāsatti vyutpāda nam aphalam syāt dṛśyate ca paramparā sambandha jñānam vinā jāti vyāptim aviduṣaḥ api dhūmāt vahni anumānam na hi vyāpya tāvacchedaka tayā bhāsamānasya avaśyam vyāpya tā grahaḥ māna abhavāt tasmāt pakṣa dharme vyāpti viśiṣṭa jñānam tad anantaram viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñānam pakṣe vā tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśaḥ 
[067,i_067,ii]	anye tu sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam vyāpaka tvam tad sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vyāpya tvam tathā ca lāghavāt vyāpaka tā jñānam anumiti hetuḥ sādhyasya pakṣa dharma vyāpaka tā jñānam ca parāmarśaḥ na tu sādhya vyāptasya pakṣa dharma tā jñānam sādhya vyāpya vat pakṣa jñānam vā gauravāt atas eva yaḥ yaḥ dhūmavān sa saḥ agnimān iti udāharaṇa vākye sādhya ayoga vyavacchedena dhūma vyāpaka tā vahneḥ upadarśyate anyathā vahnimān ā iva dhūmavān iti anya yoga vyavacchedena udāharaṇa śarīram syāt doṣaḥ api vyabhicāra ādiḥ na pakṣa dharma vyāpakam sādhyam iti eva udbhāvyaḥ 
[067,iii]	atha parvata vṛtti dhūma vyāpakaḥ vahniḥ iti parāmarśaḥ yadi tadā parvatīya dhūmam prati vyāpaka tāyāḥ parvata dhūma sāmānādhikaraṇya naiyatyāt parvata vahniḥ parāmarśa viṣayaḥ eva iti kim anumeyam iti ced tarhi parvatīya dhūme niyata sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇyasya vyāpya tvasya jñānam sādhya sāmāna adhikaraṇya bhāna niyatam iti vyāpya tva bhāne api tulyam yadi ca smṛtā vyāptiḥ dhūme avagamyate tadā vyāpaka tve api samānam 
[067,iv_067,v]	vastutas tu vyāpaka tvam tadvat niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam na tu dhūma sāmānādhikaraṇyam vyāpya tvam tu sāmānādhikaraṇya viśeṣaḥ iti tava eva anumitiḥ aphalā syāt na ca evam parāmarśasya cākṣuṣa tvam na syāt vyāpakasya viśeṣyasya indriya asaṃnikarṣāt iti vācyam iṣṭa tvāt asaṃnikṛṣṭa dhūma ādau iva mānasaḥ eva hi sarvatra parāmarśaḥ cakṣuḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam ca pakṣa vṛtti dhūma upanaya upakṣīṇam atha janaka jñāne upasarjana tayā bhātasya pakṣasya parvata ādeḥ anumitau prādhānyena bhānam na syāt na hi janaka jñāne upasarjana tayā avagatam janya jñāne prādhānyena bhāsate tathā adarśanāt na ca anumiteḥ tathā atvam asiddham parvataḥ ayam vahnimān iti anumiteḥ loka siddha tvāt iti ced 
[067,vi]	na puruṣasya daṇḍaḥ iti jñāna anantaram daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti jñāna janya jñāna darśanāt anyathā tava api katham pakṣa viśeṣyaka tva niyamaḥ na hi kāraṇībhūta jñāne yat viśeṣya tayā bhāsate tat kāryībhūte api tathā iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti jñāna janye ghaṭa abhāvavat bhū talam iti jñāne tava ca vyabhicārāt tasmāt pakṣa vṛtti liṅga parāmarśasya ayam svabhāvaḥ yat sva āśraya viśeṣyikām anumitim janayati na atathā bhūtām evam mama api tulyam iti 
[067,vii]	evam liṅga parāmarśaḥ kāraṇam na tu parāmṛśyamānam liṅgam atha parāmarśa mātram na hetuḥ api tu liṅga parāmarśaḥ tathā ca liṅgam api hetuḥ viśiṣṭa kāraṇa tā grāhaka mānena bādhakam vinā viśeṣaṇasya api hetu tva grahāt na ca liṅgam parāmarśa paricāyaka tvena anyathā siddham paricaye viśeṣaṇa antara abhāvena liṅgam eva viśeṣakam tathā ca ananyathā asiddha tvāt tat api hetuḥ anyathā paricāyaka tayā saṃyogena anyathā siddham indriyam api kāraṇam na syāt 
[067,viii_067,xi]	api ca dhūmavān vahnimān iti dhūma samāna kāla vahni viṣayā dhūma viśeṣaṇikā anumitiḥ jñāyamāna viśeṣaṇa janyā viśeṣaṇa samāna kāla tayā viśeṣya viṣaye aśābda viśiṣṭa bhāna tvāt daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti viśiṣṭa pratyaya vat atas eva jñāyamāna viśeṣaṇa janya tvena viśeṣaṇa kāla vṛtti tayā viśeṣya bhāna naiyatyam yathā daṇḍī puruṣaḥ iti pratyakṣe tena dhūma samāna kālīna vahni siddhiḥ anyathā tad tad dhūma kāla vṛtti vahni anumānam na syāt samaya viśeṣam antar bhāvya vyāpti agrahāt kim ca liṅga karaṇa tva pakṣe parāmarśaḥ eva tad vyāpāraḥ parāmarśasya tu na vyāpāra antaram asti carama kāraṇa tvāt iti na tat karaṇam atra ucyate atīta anāgata dhūma ādi jñāne api anumiti darśanāt na liṅgam tad hetuḥ vyāpāra pūrva varti tayoḥ abhāvāt 
[067,xii]	na ca vidyamānam liṅga antaram eva tad hetuḥ tadā tasya aparāmarśāt parāmarśa aviṣayasya kāraṇa tā grāhaka abhāvāt bhāvini pakṣe vyakti aikyam eva vā yatra liṅgam tatra liṅga antara abhāvāt ca yadi ca vartamānam eva tatra liṅgam tadā vartamāna vahni anumāna upapattiḥ atha bhāvi bhūtam vā dhūma ādi na liṅgam kim tu tad prāc abhāvaḥ tad dhvaṃsaḥ ca vartamānaḥ eva tayoḥ api vahni samāna deśa tvāt iti ced na atīta bhāvi dina vṛtti tayā niścitāt vartamāna tayā sandigdhāt dhūmāt anumitau hi na prāc abhāva dhvaṃsau liṅge tayoḥ saṃdigdha tvāt na api dhūmaḥ tasya āvartamāna tvāt 
[067,xiii_067,xiv]	kim ca bhūta bhā vivartamāna tva aviṣayāt parvate dhūmaḥ iti jñānāt yatra anumānam tatra kā gatiḥ sarvatra prāc abhāva ādi anyatamava tvam dhūma ādi atyanta abhāva abhāvavat tvam vā liṅgam iti ced na vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvena teṣām aliṅga tvāt anyatamatva ajñāne api dhūma jñānāt anumitisattvāt ca api ca dhūma prāc abhāva ādi na liṅgam na vā tad dhīra numiti kāraṇam prāc abhāva ādīnām vyartha tvāt āvaśyaka dhūma ādi jñānāt eva anumiti sambhavāt ca kim ca liṅgam na anumiti mātre hetuḥ liṅgam vinā api dhūlī paṭalāt liṅga bhrameṇa anum iti utpatteḥ na api liṅgam pramā anu mitau parāmarśaḥ anumiti mātre hetuḥ tad viśeṣa pramātvā pramātvābhyām eva anumiti tathā tvāt yat sāmānye yat sāmānyam prayojakam tad viśeṣe tad viśeṣasya prayojaka tvāt 
[068,i]	atha parāmarśasya pramātvam vidyamāna liṅga viṣaya tvam tathā ca āyātam liṅgasya pramānum iti hetu tvam iti ced na bhāvinā bhūtena vā yadā kadācid vidyamānena api liṅgena parāmarśa pramātu a sambhavāt na anumiti pūrva samaye tad pramātvā anurodhena liṅgasya sattvam kāraṇa tvam vā dhūmakālīna vahni anumānam ca yadā yatra dhūmaḥ tadā tatra vahniḥ iti vyāpti jñānāt eva 
[068,ii_068,iii]	atha vā dhūma kālaḥ pakṣa tāvat chedakaḥ pakṣa tā avacchedaka dharma samāna adhikaraṇam ca pakṣa dharma tā balāt sādhyam sidhyati iti dhūmakālīna vahni siddhiḥ yat tu vyāpāra abhāvāt na parāmarśaḥ karaṇam iti tathā eva kim tu vyāpti jñānam karaṇam parāmarśaḥ vyāpāraḥ na ca parāmarśasya saṃskāraḥ vyāpāraḥ parāmarśasya carama kāraṇa tvena saṃskāra utpādana samaye anum iti utpādanāt na api tarkaḥ vyāpti grāhakasya viṣaya pariśodhakasya vā tasya tad ajanya tvāt iti 
[068,iv_068,v]	tat ca anumānam trividham kevala anvayi kevala vyatirekyā anvaya vyatireki bhedāt tatra asat vipakṣam kevala anvayi tathā hi kevala anvayinaḥ abhidheya tvasya na vipakṣaḥ abhidhāne anabhidhāne ca vipakṣa tva vyāghātāt atha yathā ākāśa śabdāt śabda āśraya tvam anabhidheyam api upatiṣṭhate tathā abhidheya tva vipakṣasya anabhidheya tve api padāt upasthitiḥ syāt evam ca abhidheya tvam kutas api vyāvṛttam dharma tvāt go tva vat iti ced na vyāvṛt tattvasya avyāvṛtta tve vyāvṛtta tvam eva kevala anvayi vyāvṛtta tve atas eva vyāvṛttam vyāvṛtta tvam tat eva kevala anvayī iti dharma tvasya anaikāntika tvāt evam atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvasya atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tve atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam eva kevala anvayi atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve yat niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi anta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tat eva kevala anvayi na ca atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam vyāvṛtta tvam ca nānā iti vācyam anugata pratīti balena go tva vat tayoḥ siddheḥ 
[068,vi_068,vii]	atra na tāvat avyāpya vṛtti atyanta abhāvaḥ kevala anvayī tasya pratiyogi avacchinne api atyanta abhāvāt atyanta abhāva apratiyoginaḥ ca kevala anvayitvāt na api āśraya nāśa janya guṇa nāśa atyanta abhāvaḥ tasya nāśasya sarvatra atyanta abhāvāt iti vācyam yatra hi pratiyogi prāgabhāvaḥ vartate tatra na tad atyanta abhāvaḥ vartate tathā ca nāśasya prāgabhāvaḥ yatra nāśa pratiyogi samāna deśe vartate tatra katham nāśa atyanta abhāvaḥ vartatām tarhi nāśasya tatra vṛttiḥ syāt iti ced na pūrvam tatra nāśa prāga bhāvasya eva sattvāt uttara kāle āśrayasya eva abhāvāt na api ākāśa atyanta abhāvaḥ kevala anvayī tasya api pratiyogi rūpa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvāt abhāva atyanta abhāvasya bhāva tvāt atha abhāva atyanta abhāvaḥ na pratiyogi rūpaḥ tathā sati anyonya abhāva atyanta abhāvaḥ pratiyogi rūpaḥ iti pratiyogi samāna deśaḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ na syāt iti ced na atyanta abhāva atyanta abhāvaḥ pratiyogi eva anyonya abhāva atyanta abhāvaḥ tu pratiyogi vṛtti rasādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
[068,viii]	ucyate vṛttimat atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam kevala anvayitvam ākāśa atyanta abhāvaḥ yadi api pratiyogi rūpa atyanta abhāva pratiyogī tathā api na sa vṛttimān iti ākāśa atyanta abhāvaḥ eva kevala anvayī tathā prameya tva abhidheya tva ādi kevala anvayi vṛttimataḥ atyanta abhāvasya apratiyogi tvāt nanu prameya tvam pramāviṣayatvam tat ca na kevala anvayi pramāyāḥ viṣaya tvasya ca ananugamāt iti vācyam pramā tvam eva hi paramparā sambandhāt ghaṭa ādau prameya tvam anugatam pramājātīya viṣaya tvam vā tathā api kevala anvayini saṃśaya abhāvāt katham anumitiḥ prameya tvam atra vartate na vā iti saṃśayaḥ ca na prameya pakṣakaḥ kiṃtu prameya tva pakṣakaḥ bhinna viṣayakaḥ prameya tva pakṣake ca astitva sādhyasya anvaya vyatireki tvam tathā ca ghaṭaḥ prameyaḥ na vā iti saṃśayaḥ mṛgyate sa ca na asti eva 
[068,ix_068,x]	atha pakṣaḥ sādhyavān na vā pakṣe sādhyam asti na vā iti saṃśayau samāna viṣayakau eva tat asya aḥ ti asmin iti matupaḥ vidhānāt iti ced na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva bhedena artha bhedāt mā evam yaḥ eva hi saṃśayaḥ pakṣe sādhya siddhi virodhī saḥ eva anumāna aṅgam āvaśyaka tvāt lāghavāt ca na tu samāna viṣayaka tvam api tatra tantram gauravāt prameya tvam ghaṭa niṣṭhā bhāva pratiyogi na vā iti saṃśayaḥ ca ghaṭaḥ prameyaḥ iti sādhya siddhi virodhī bhavati eva yat vā saṃśaya yogya tā eva anumāna aṅgam saṃśayaḥ ca tadānīm vināśāt na ca sā api sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ prameya tva abhāva asiddhau tad pramāṇa asiddhaḥ tad abhāvā siddhiḥ iti vācyam pakṣa niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tva jñānasya iva sādhya sādhaka tvena tadā abhāvasya eva yogyatā tvāt prameya tvam atyanta abhāva pratiyogī iti bhrāmyataḥ saṃśayaḥ iti anye 
[068,xi]	nanu eka rūpa vikalam idam katham gamakam tattve vā vyatireka vikala vat rūpa antara vikalam api gamakam syāt iti ced na anvaya vyatireka vyāptyoḥ anyatara niścayena anum iti anubhavāt yugapad ubhaya vyāpti upasthitau vinigamana abhāvena ubhayoḥ api prayojaka tve vyatireka upāsanā vyatirekaḥ ca vipakṣa vṛtti tva śaṅkā nivṛtti dvārā vyatireka vyāptau upayujyate atra tu vipakṣa abhāvena śaṅkā eva na udeti 
[069,i]	kevala vyatirekī tu asat sapakṣaḥ yatra vyatireka sahacāreṇa vyāpti grahaḥ nanu vyatireki na anumānam vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā jñānasya tad hetu tvāt atra ca vyatireka sahacārāt tatra vyāptiḥ anvayasya na pakṣa dharma tā na ca vyāpta pakṣa dharma tvam sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam dvayam anumiti prayojakam iti vācyam ananugamāt na ca anyatara tvam tathā eka pramāṇa pariśeṣa āpatteḥ na ca tṛṇa araṇi maṇi nyāyena anumiti viśeṣe tad kāraṇa tvam iti vācyam vyatireki sādhye anumiti tva asiddheḥ ubhaya siddha kḷpta tad kāraṇasya abhāvāt na ca sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam eva anumiti prayojakam iti vācyam gauravāt kevala anvayinī abhāvāt ca 
[069,ii]	atha sādhya abhāva vyāpaka bhāva pratiyogi tvena sādhya vyāpya tvam eva anumīyate evam vyatireka vyāptyā anvaya vyāptim anumāya yatra anumitiḥ saḥ eva vyatirekī iti ucyate iti tat na anvaya vyāpteḥ gamaka tve vyatireka vyāpti upanyāsasya artha antara tā āpatteḥ anvaya vyāpti anukūla tayā ca tad upanyāse anvaya vyāptim anupanyasya tad upanyāsasya aprāpta kāla tvāt iti 
[069,iii]	ucyate nirupādhi vyatireka sahacāreṇa anvavyāptiḥ eva gṛhyate pratiyogi anuyogi bhāvasya niyāmāka tvāt anvaya vyatireki vat na ca evam vyāpti grahaḥ eva pṛthivī itara bhinna iti bhāsitam niyata sāmānādhikaraṇya rūpa tvāt vyāpteḥ iti ced satyam gandhavat tva avacchedena itara bhedasya sādhya tvāt atas eva ācāryaḥ pakṣa tāvat chedake na hetu tvam anumene pṛthivī tvam itara bheda vyāpyam iti pratītau api sarvā pṛthivī itara bhinnā iti pṛthivī viśeṣyaka buddheḥ vyatireki sādhya tvāt ca 
[069,iv_069,v]	yat vā vyatireka vyāpteḥ eva anvayena gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpaka sādhana abhāva abhāvena sādhanena pakṣe sādhya abhāva abhāvasya sādhyasya sādhanāt vyāpaka abhāvena vyāpya abhāva avaśyam bhāvāt atha evam na sā anumitiḥ kḷpta tad hetu liṅga parāmarśa abhāvāt anyathā ananugamaḥ iti ced na anumiti mātre vyāpti jñānasya prayojaka tvāt na ca evam atiprasaṅgaḥ anumiti sāmānya sāmagryām satyām api anumiti virahāt anum iti anutpatteḥ viśeṣa sāmagrī sāpekṣāyāḥ eva sāmānya sāmagryāḥ janakatvāt anvayi vyatireki viśeṣa dvaya sāmagrī ca na asti eva 
[069,vi]	nanu pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ bhidyate pṛthivī tvāt iti vyatirekiṇi sādhyam asiddham tathā ca na vyatireki nirūpaṇam na vā pakṣa tvam na vā liṅga janī a sādhya viśiṣṭa tad jñānam teṣām sādhya jñāna janya tvāt atha sādhyam prasiddham tadā yatra prasiddham tatra hetoḥ avagame anvayitvam anavagame asādhāraṇyam kiñca itara bhedaḥ na svarūpam adhikaraṇa pratiyoginoḥ pṛthivī jala ādyoḥ anumānāt prāk eva siddheḥ na api vaidharmyam jala ādi niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogim atvam tat hi pṛthivī tva ādikam tat ca siddham eva na ca jala ādi niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyegi tvena pṛthivī tvam na siddham iti vācyam jala ādau pṛthivī tva atyanta abhāva graha daśāyām pṛthivī tve api tad pratiyogi tva grahāt anyonya abhāvaḥ tu bhedaḥ yadi api sādhyam sambhavati vaidharmya jñāna sādhya tvāt anyonya abhāva grahasya tathā api jala ādi pratiyogikānyonya abhāvasya aprasiddhiḥ na ca jala ādi pratyekānyonya abhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ asādha araṇya prasaṅgāt 
[069,vii]	atha pṛthivī tejaḥ bhinnā na vā iti saṃśayena tejaḥ bhinna tve avagate pṛthivī tejaḥ bhinnā satī jala ādi dvādaśa bhinnā na vā iti saṃśaye tejaḥ bhinna tve sati jala ādi dvādaśa bhinna tvam prasiddham tat eva sādhyam eka viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭe viśeṣaṇa antara buddheḥ eva viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñāna tvāt evañca saṃśaya prasiddham sādhyam ādāya vyatireka ādi nirūpaṇam yat vā pṛthivī jala ādi bhinnā na vā iti pratyekam trayodaśa saṃśaya viṣayāṇām trayodaśa anyonya abhāvānām samudāyaḥ pṛthivyām avagataḥ vyatireka ādi nirupakaḥ na ca evam pṛthivyām eva sādhya prasiddheḥ vyatireki vaiyarthyam sādhya niścaya artha vyatireki pravṛtteḥ na ca asādha araṇyam samudita anyonya abhāvānām sādhya tve sa pakṣa abhāvāt iti ced na sādhya niścaye hi sādhya vyatireka niścayaḥ bhavati eva sādhya sandehe tad vyatireka saṃśayasya vajra lepa tvāt tathā ca saṃśaya rūpā sādhya siddhiḥ iti śiṣya bandhanam etena pṛthivī jala ādibhyaḥ bhinnā iti vipratipatti rūpa vādi vākyāt ākāṅkṣa ādi mataḥ apūrva artha pratipādakāt sādhya prasiddhiḥ iti parāḥ tam vākyāt eva pṛthivyām sādhya siddheḥ vyatireki vaiyarthyāt 
[069,viii_069,ix^1]	na ca tad buddhau vādi vākya janya tvena apramāṇi asaṃśayāt niścaye api saṃśayaḥ iti tad niścaya artham vyatirekī iti vācyam tarhi saṃśaya prasiddham sādhyam tasya ca na vyatireka niścayāka tvam iti ukta tvāt sva artha anumāne tad abhāvāt ca ucyate ghaṭa ādau eva itara sakala bhedasya pratyakṣatas prasiddhiḥ ghaṭaḥ na jalādiḥ iti pratīteḥ nanu ayam anyonya abhāvaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ atīndriya pratiyogika abhāva tvāt paramāṇu saṃsarga abhāva vat yogyā anupalabdheḥ abhāva grāhaka tvāt nayana unmīlana anantaram stambhaḥ piśācaḥ na bhavati iti pratiteḥ bādhaka balena vāyuḥ vātī iti valliṅga graha upakṣīṇa tvāt iti ced na yaḥ hi ānupalambhaḥ adhikaraṇe pratiyogimattva virodhī saḥ abhāvam grāhayati na tu yogyā anupalabdhi mātram anyathā vāyau rūpa abhāva pratīti vat jala paramāṇau pṛthivī tva abhāva graha prasaṅgāt adhikaraṇe pratiyogi satvañca tarkitam yadi hi stambhaḥ piśācaḥ syāt stambha vat upalabhyeta na piśāca anupalambhaḥ syāt na ca pṛthivī jalāt bhidyate jala āvṛtti dharmavat tvāt tejaḥ vat 
[069,ix^2]	evam anyebhyaḥ api bheda siddhau dvādaśabhinna iti viśeṣaṇam dattvā samavāya bheda sādhanāt anvayinaḥ eva pṛthivyām trayāt aśa bheda siddhiḥ iti kim vyatirekiṇa iti vācyam jala ādi bhinnā satī samavāyibhinnā iti buddhau api trayodaśa bhinna iti buddheḥ vyatireki sādhya tvāt na ca ghaṭasya api pakṣa tvāt aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam sarvā pṛthivī itara bhinna iti uddeśya pratīteḥ abhāvāt pakṣa tāvacchedaka nānātve hi tat atas eva anitye vāc manase iti atra anityā vāc iti buddheḥ uddeśyāyāḥ siddha tvāt aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam anyathā anumāna mātra ucchedāt pakṣasya siddhasya eva sādhya tvāt na ca ghaṭaḥ katham pakṣaḥ sādhya niścayena saṃśaya siṣā dhayiṣayoḥ abhāvāt iti vācyam sarvā pṛthivī itara bhinnā na vā iti saṃśayasya tad prakāraka siṣā dhayiṣāyāḥ ca sāmānyatas ghaṭa viṣaya tvāt ghaṭa tvena viśeṣa darśanam siddhiḥ vā atas tena rupeṇa saṃśaya siṣā dhayiṣe na staḥ pṛthiva tvena tu bhavataḥ eva dhūmavān vahnimān iti dhūmava tvena vahni niścayepi parvate vahni saṃśaya vat 
[070,i]	yat vā sarva tvena rūpeṇa na pakṣatā sarvatra avipratipatteḥ ghaṭa ādi eka deśe itara bhedasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt tathā ca eka deśe vipratipattau sāmānye itara bheda sādhane artha antaram kintu sāmānyena pṛthivī tvena yāvat eva vipratipatti viṣayaḥ tāvatām eva pakṣatā viśeṣyān anugamāt tarhi pṛthivī itara bhinnā pṛthivī tvāt ghaṭa vat iti anvayinā eva itara bhedasya siddha tvāt kim vyatirekiṇā ghaṭa sādhāraṇa pakṣa tve api abheda anumāna vat pakṣasya api dṛṣṭānta tva avirodhāt pakṣa anyatvam hi tatra atantram kintu sādhyavat tayā niścita tvam prayojakam na ca pṛthivī tva agrahe pūrvam gṛhītam yatra sādhyam paścāt smaryate tatra hetu sādhya sāmānā adhikaraṇyā grahāt vyatireki avatāraḥ iti vācyam hetoḥ eva pakṣātāvacchedaka tvena ghaṭe pṛthivī tva graha daśāyām itara bheda sāmānādhikaraṇya graha avaśyaṃbhāvāt iti ced satyam 
[070,ii_070,iii]	anvayi tulya tayā vyatirekiṇaḥ api sāmarthyāt anvaya apratisandhāna daśāyām vyatireki upanyāsasya aparyanuyojya tvāt tat uktam āstām tāvat ayam suhṛd upadeśaḥ kevala vyatireki lakṣaṇam tāvat nirvyūḍham athavā jala ādīnām trayodaśa anyonya abhāvāḥ trayodaśasu prasiddhāḥ pṛthivyām sādhyante atas eva ākāśe vyatirekiṇāḥ jala ādi milita pratiyogika anyonya abhāva apratītau api trayodaśa anyonya abhāvāḥ sādhyāḥ iti na anvayitvā sādhāraṇye 
[070,iv]	yat vā jalam tejaḥ prabhṛti dvādaśa bhinna pratiyogikān yonya abhāva vat dravya tvāt tejaḥ vat iti anumānāt trayodaśa bhinnasya sāmānyatas siddhau pṛthivyām trayodaśa bhinna tvam sādhyam na ca anvayitvam asādhāraṇyam vā pakṣāt anyatra sādhya aprasiddheḥ vastu gatyā pṛthivyām eva sādhya siddheḥ kim vyatirekiṇa iti ced na pṛthivī trayodaśabhinna iti vyatirekiṇam vinā apratīteḥ nanu evam pṛthivī jala ādi trayodaśa bhinna pratiyogikānyonya abhāvavatī dravya tvāt iti pṛthivī bhinna tad bhinna ādi siddhiḥ syāt iti ced na aprayojaka tvāt prakṛte ca anubhūyamāna jala ādi vaidharmyasya pṛthivī tva śabda āśraya tva ādeḥ atiriktam vinā anupapatteḥ 
[070,v]	nanu itara bhedaḥ yadi anyonya abhāvaḥ tadā bhāvāt bhedaḥ na siddhyet abhāvasya abhāva antara abhāvāt yadi ca tena samam svarūpa bhedaḥ eva sādhyaḥ tadā ananugamāt anumāna apravṛttiḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā na bhavati iti abādhita pratīti balāt abhāvasya api anyonya abhāvaḥ asti iti kecid tat na apasiddhāntāt anatiprasakta adhikaraṇa svarūpa mātreṇa eva abhāva prati iti upapattau ca adhika abhāve māna abhāvāt ca iti ced na itara abhāva anyonya abhāvasya sādhya tvāt na ca evam abhāvāt aviveka tādavasthyam tena samam svarūpa bhedasya anvayinā vyatirekiṇā vā sādhya tvāt 
[070,vi]	anye tu pṛthivī tva bhinna dharma atyanta abhāvaḥ eva sādhyaḥ jala tva ādi pratiyogikāḥ tāvantaḥ atyanta abhāvāḥ vā tad tad asādhāraṇa tad tad dharma atyanta abhāva yogaḥ vā ete ca abhāvāḥ jala tvam na ghaṭa ādau ghaṭa ādi jala atyanta abhāva vat iti pratyakṣa ādeḥ kvacid tad tad vaidharmyāt eva prasiddhāḥ iti na aprasiddhiḥ tāvatam abhāvānām vaiśiṣṭyam na prasiddham iti ced kim etāvatā na hi tāvat vaiśiṣṭyam atra sādhyate kim tu jala tva ādīnām yāvantaḥ abhāvāḥ iha sādhyāḥ te ca tatra tatra prasiddhāḥ eva tāvat vaiśiṣṭya dhīḥ tu phalam anyathā siddha sādhanāt militānām api sādhya tve na aprasiddhiḥ kiñcid eka dharma avacchedaḥ hi bala ādi vat melakā arthaḥ sa na na asiddhaḥ na ca hetoḥ asādhāraṇyam tāvat abhāva yogī hi atra sa pakṣaḥ bhavati na tu tad eka deśa katipaya abhāvavān sādhya tāyāḥ tāvatya paryāpteḥ yat vā jala tva atyanta abhāvaḥ tejaḥ tvātya abhāva adhikaraṇa vṛttiḥ atyanta abhāva tvāt ghaṭa tva atyanta abhāva vat evam atyanta abhāva antara sāmānādhikaraṇyam api tatra sādhyam iti kva aprasiddhiḥ 
[070,vii_070,viii]	kim ca itare tāvat prasiddhāḥ eva te ca bheda pratiyoginaḥ meya tvāt iti itara bhedaḥ api sugrahaḥ eva nanu pṛthivī na itara bhedavatī guru tva ādibhyaḥ jala vat iti pratirodhaḥ iti ced na itara bheda niṣedhaḥ hi itara abhedaḥ na tu tejaḥ prabhṛti abhedaḥ jalaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vaikalyāt caturdaśa abhedānām ca ekatra virodhena asambhavāt caturdaśa bhedānām ca ekatra vṛttau na virodhaḥ 
[070,ix]	yat tu sādhya prasiddhau pṛthivī itara bhinnā tad sādhya adhikaraṇa pṛthivī anyatara tvāt tad adhikaraṇa vat pṛthivyām tad sādhyam anvayinaḥ eva setsyati iti tat na anyatara tvasya aliṅga tvāt iti ukta tvāt liṅga tve vā jala ādau api tad siddhi prasaṅgāt evam tarhi pṛthivī jalam pṛthivī tvāt yat na jalam tat na pṛthivī yathā tejaḥ iti sat pratipakṣaḥ astu iti ced na ajalasya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratyakṣatas eva pṛthivī tva niścaye vyatireka vyabhicārāt asya nyūna tvāt tad anavadhāraṇe tu sat pratipakṣa tvam iṣṭam eva 
[070,x^1]	nanu jīvat śarīram sa ātmakam prāṇa ādimattvāt icchā ādikā aryavat tvāt vā iti vyatirekiṇi sādhya aprasiddhau katham vyatireka ādi nirūpaṇam nerāmyam ca na ghaṭasya pratyakṣa vedyam tasya tatra asāmarthyāt na anumāna gamyam nairātmya apratītau anvayinaḥ abhāvāt sa ātmaka tva pratītim vinā vyatirekiṇaḥ anupapatteḥ atha icchā samavāyi kāraṇa janyā kāryatvāt tat ca samavāyi kāraṇam pṛthivī ādi aṣṭa dravya bhinnam pṛthivī ādi tve bādhaka sattvāt iti pṛthivī ādi bhinna ātma siddhau tat vatvam jīvat śarīre sādhyate iti ced yadi sa ātmaka tvam ātma saṃyogavat tvam tadā ghaṭa ādau tat asti iti tatas hetu vyāvṛttau asādha araṇyam jñāna samāna adhikaraṇa jñāna kāraṇībhūta saṃyoga āśraya kārya tvam 
[070,x^2]	sa ātmaka tvam śarīra ātma saṃyogasya jñāna kāraṇa tvāt ātma manasoḥ tathā ātve api akārya tvāt iti ced na śarīrāt anyatra asiddheḥ tatra prasiddhau siddha sādhanāt icchāyāḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga avacchedaka tvasya abhāvaḥ ghaṭa ādau dṛṣṭaḥ tad vyatirekaḥ śarīre sādhyate iti ced na icchāyāḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga vat chedaka tvasya śarīraḥ eva prasiddheḥ siddha sādhanāt anyathā asiddhi vyatireka ādya nirūpaṇāt aprasiddha sādhya saṃsargam iva sādhyam aprasiddham sādhayati vyatirekī iti ced na vyatireka ādya nirūpaṇāt asādhāraṇa dharmeṇa apratīta padārtha anumāne ghaṭa tva ādinā api sva icchā kalpi taḍittha ādi anumāna prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[070,xi_071,i]	ucyate icchā samavāyi karaṇa siddhau icchā tvam saṃyoga samavāyi kāraṇaka vṛtti nitya indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇa vṛtti guṇa tva sākṣāt vyāpya jāti tvāt śabda tva vat sa ca asamavāyi kāraṇam saṃyogaḥ kiñcid avacchinnaḥ saṃyoga tvāt ātma saṃyoga mātrasya icchā janaka tve sa ātmaka tvam śarīre sādhyate yat vā ātmani icchādhāra tā mahat saṃyoga avacchedyāḥ janya vibhu viśeṣa guṇa ādhāra tā tvāt vāyu ādi saṃyoga avacchedya śabda ādhāra tva vat iti sāmānyatas siddham icchā dhāra tā ghaṭaka icchā samavāyi kāraṇa dravya saṃyogava tvam sa ātmaka tvam atas eva jñāna samāna adhikaraṇa jñāna kāraṇībhūta saṃyoga āśraya kārya tvam vā sa ātmaka tvam sva śarīre prāṇa ādimattvasya icchā ādimattvasya ca ceṣṭā avayava upacaya ādi vyāpya tva grahāt ghaṭa ādau ceṣṭā ādi viraheṇa prāṇa ādimattva icchā ādimattva viraha anumānam icchā ādi virahāt icchā ādi prayojaka icchā ādya āghāra tā ghaṭaka icchā ādya samavāyi kāraṇa saṃyāga viraha anumānam kārya abhāvavati kāraṇa abhāva niyamāt 
[071,ii_071,iii]	na ca sa ātmaka tvam śarīra vṛtti śarīre bādhaka abhāvāt śarīra tva vat iti anvayinā eva sādhya siddheḥ kim vyatirekiṇa iti vācyam śarīram sa ātmakam iti śarīra viśeṣyaka buddheḥ vyatirekiṇam vinā anupapatteḥ upāya antarasya upāya antarāt ūṣaka tvāt ca yat vā ceṣṭā saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇikā saṃskāra janya kriyā tvat iti ceṣṭāyāḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga siddhau prayatna vat ātma saṃyogaḥ evam paryavasyati prayatna anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt evam ceṣṭāyāḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga āśraya tve sati śarīra tvam sa ātmaka tvam jīvat śarīre sādhyam ceṣṭāvat tvāt iti hetuḥ ceṣṭā virahaḥ ca ghaṭa ādau pratyakṣa siddhaḥ ceṣṭā virahāt tad asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga virahaḥ api sugrahaḥ 
[071,iv_071,v]	yat vā jīvat śarīram tad avayavaḥ vā ātma bhinna tve sati ātma viśeṣa guṇa kāraṇa bhogān ādhikaraṇa āvṛtti saṃyoga vat prāṇa anyatve sati jñāna kāraṇībhūta prāṇa saṃyogavat tvāt yat na evam tat na evam yathā ghaṭaḥ ātma prāṇa saṃyogaḥ prāṇa manassaṃyogaḥ vā śarīra prāṇa saṃyogena eva anyathā siddhaḥ na kāraṇam bhoga ādhāra tvam bhoga samavāyi kāraṇa atirikta vṛtti sakala bhoga adhikaraṇa vṛtti tvāt prameya tva ādi vat iti tārkikī rītiḥ 
[071,vi]	kim ca saṃśaya upasthita sādhyasya vyatireka nirūpaṇam na yogyā anupalambhāt sādhya niścayam vinā yogyā anupalambha abhāvāt na api vyāpaka abhāvāt sādhya niścayam vinā tad vyāpaka tva niścaya abhāvāt na ca yadi icchā aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya āśritā na syāt aṣṭān āśritā satī dravya āśritā na syāt rūpavat iti sādhya viparyaya koṭau pratikūla tarka saha kṛtaḥ sādhya saṃśayaḥ eva niścaya kāryam karoti atas eva etādṛśa saṃśaya upasthita kalpitaṅittha ādi sādhanam api apāstam tad viparyaye pratikūla tarka abhāvāt iti vācyam sādhya niścayam vinā sādhya vyatireka niśraya tad mūla tarkān avatārāt anyathā aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya vṛtti tva nirūpaṇe tarka udayaḥ tarka udaye ca tad saha kṛta sādhya saṃśayasya sādhya vyatireka niścāyaka tvam iti 
[071,vii]	ucyate icchā āśraya dravya siddhau pṛthivī ādāvi chādhāra tā abhāve tat drayam pṛthivī ādi aṣṭa dravya bhinnam aṣṭa dravya āvṛtti dharmavat tvāt pṛthivī ādi tve bādhaka sattvāt vā iti aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya siddhau icchāyām aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravyavat tvam aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya vṛtti tvam vā sādhyate sādhya prasiddhi dravya tve icchā viśeṣya kāṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya āvṛtti tva pratīteḥ vyatireki sādhya tvāt 
[071,viii^1]	tathā api icchā aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya āśritāḥ aṣṭa dravyām āśrita tve sati dravya āśrita tvāt aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya tva vat iti sādhya prasiddhyā eva dṛṣṭānta prasiddheḥ anvayī hetuḥ syāt iti ced na anvaya vyāptyapratisandhāne vyatireka vyāpti pratisandhāna daśāyām vyatireki sambhavāt na ca dravya tva ādeḥ sa pakṣāt vyāvṛttau asādha araṇyam tat hi sādhya tad abhāva ubhaya sādhaka tvena sat pratipakṣa utthāpaka tayā doṣa āvaham prakṛte ca na hetoḥ sādhya abhāva sādhaka tvam vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt sādhya sādhaka tve tat sattvāt ca atas eva yāvat ekatra anukūla tarkaḥ na avatarati tāvat eva daśa aviśeṣe asādhāraṇyam doṣaḥ iti uktam suvarṇa taijasa tva sādhaka vyatirekiṇi śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda tvāt iti ādau api tathā atha aṣṭa dravya ādhāra tva bādha anantaram icchā ādau guṇa tvāt eva aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya vṛtti tvam sidhyati pakṣa dharma tā balāt prasiddha viśeṣa bādhe sāmānya jñānasya tad itara viśeṣa viṣaya tva niyamāt atas eva asarva viṣaya aniti a jñāna bādha anantaram kṣiti ādau kāryatvena jñāna janya tvam sidhyat nitya sarva viṣaya tvam jñānasya ādāya eva sidhyati iti ced 
[071,viii^2]	na bādhā anantaram aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya viṣaya api anumitiḥ dravya āśrita tva prakārikā syāt anumiteḥ vyāpaka tāvacchedaka mātra prakāraka tva niyamāt na tu aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya vṛtti tva prakārikā tasya pūrvam apratīta tvena prakāra tva asambhavāt iti tad prakārikā anumitiḥ vyatirekiṇā eva anādi ananta t vi aṇukādi yāvat pakṣīkaraṇe anādyana tantā vat upādana gocara aparokṣa jñāna tvam eva nitya sarva viṣayaka tvam etad anya nitya sarva viṣaya tvam vyatirekiṇaḥ eva sidhyati pakṣa dharma tā balena api vyāpaka tāvacchedaka prakāreṇa sādhya siddhiḥ bhavati na tu sādhya gata viśeṣa prakārikā atiprasaṅgāt 
[071,ix_071,xi]	nanu aṣṭa dravya anāśrita icchā dravya āśritā iti yadi sādhyate tadā aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravya āśrita tvam antareṇa pratijñā arthaḥ eva na upapadyate satyam evam api aṣṭa dravya an āśrita icchāyām dravya āśrita tvam sidhyatu tasya aṣṭa dravya atirekyam kutas sidhyet atha sāmānya avyabhicāram ādāya māna antara upanītam tat tad anya tvam upajīvya aṣṭa dravya ani adravya vṛtti tā eva icchā ādeḥ paricchidyate jñāna antara upasthāpita viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa jñānasya surabhi candanam ityādau darśanāt iti ced na māna antarāt niyamena anupasthiteḥ ye ca id chā āśraye pṛthivī ādi bhinna tvam na jānanti icchāyāḥ ca pṛthivī ādi anāśrita tvam na jānanti teṣām api anumānāt iti api āhuḥ 
[071,xii]	atha vyatirekī na anumānam sarvatra prameya tva ādinā sat pratipakṣa grasta tvāt iti ced na vipakṣa bādhakena vyatirekiṇaḥ balavat tvāt anye tu vyatirekiṇya bhāvaḥ eva sādhyaḥ sa ca aprasiddhaḥ eva sidhyati yasya abhāvasya vyāpakaḥ hetu abhāvaḥ gṛhītaḥ tasya abhāvaḥ pakṣe vyāpaka bhāva rūpeṇa hetunā sidhyati vyāpaka abhāvavat tayā jñāte vyāpya abhāva jñāna avaśyam bhāvāt tathā hi pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ bhidyate pṛthivī tvāt iti atra itarasya jala ādeḥ vyāpakaḥ pṛthivī tva abhāvaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti pṛthivī tva abhāva abhāva rūpeṇa pṛthivī tvena pṛthivyām itara anyonya abhāvaḥ aprasiddhaḥ eva sidhyati pratiyegi jñānasya vṛtta tvāt pratyakṣeṇa bhū tale ghaṭa abhāva vat 
[071,xiii]	evam anyatra api avyāpya vṛtti icchāyāḥ sva āśraya tve siddhe sva āśraye yaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ tad avacchedakam ghaṭa ādi sarvam tad avacchedena icchā anupalbhāt tathā ca icchā ati anta abhāva āśraya tāvacchedaka tva rūpasya na īrātmyasya ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādi mattva abhāvaḥ vyāpakaḥ gṛhīta iti jīvat śarīre prāṇa ādimattvena icchā ati anta abhāva āśraya tva avacchedaka tvasya abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka tvam sādhyate 
[072,i_072,ii]	evam prāmāṇyasādhyaka vyatirekiṇī api vyadhikara prakāra avacchinna tvasya vyāpakaḥ samartha pravṛtti janaka tva abhāvaḥ apramāyām gṛhītaḥ atas vivāda adhyāsita anubhave samartha pravṛtti jaka tvena vyadhikaraṇa prakāra vat chinna tvasya abhāvaḥ sidhyati vyadhikaraṇa prakāra avacchinna tvam eva pramātvam nanu sādhya aprasiddhau katham sādhya viśiṣṭa jñanam viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyatvā dvi śiṣṭa jñānasya iti ced na pakṣe sādhya anumiti sāmagrī sattvāt pakṣa viśeṣaṇakaḥ sādhya viśeṣyakaḥ eva pratyayaḥ jāyate bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti abhāva viśeṣyaka pratyaya vat 
[072,iii_072,v]	tathā api sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva abhāva rūpa hetumat tayā pakṣa jñānam vyatirekiṇi gamakataupayikam na ca sādhya prasiddhim vinā etādṛśa pratisandhānam sambhavati na ca vastu gatyāḥ yaḥ sādhya abhāvaḥ tad vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi mattayā jñānam mṛgyate iti vācyam vyatirekya bhāsā anupapatteḥ iti ced na yaḥ abhāvaḥ yasya bhāvasya vyāpaka tvena gṛhītaḥ tad abhāva abhāvena tasya vyāpyasya abhāvaḥ pakṣe sādhyate iti anugatān ati prasaktasya gamakataupayika tvāt ayam ca vyatireki prakāraḥ sva arthaḥ eva param prati sādhya aprasiddhyā pratijña ādi asambhavāt iti sarvam samañjasam 
[072,vi]	vyatireki anumāna siddhau arthāpattiḥ na māna antaram tena eva tad artha siddheḥ syāt etat jyotiśśāstrāt tad kathita liṅgāt vā devadattasya śata varṣa jīvi tvam avagatam caramam śata varṣa jīvī gṛhaḥ eva iti niyame pratyakṣeṇa avagate paścāt yogyā anupalabdhā niścitaḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ jīvana niyama grāhaka pramāṇayoḥ bala abalā nirūpaṇāt bahis sattva kalpanam vinā niyama dvaya viṣayakam saṃśayam janayitvā jīvati na vā iti saṃśayam āpādya jīvana saṃśaya apanuttaye jīvana upapādakam bahis sattvam kalpayati iti yathā ukta sāmagrī anantaram bahis asti iti pratīteḥ tatra anvaya vyatirekābhyām saṃśaya dvārāḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ tad utpādita niyama dvaya viṣayaka saṃśayaḥ vā kāraṇam jīvana saṃśayaḥ eva vā karaṇe savyāpāraka tva aniyamāt pramāṇyoḥ virodha jñānam tat āhita saṃśaya dvārā karaṇam iti kaścid tadā jīvitvasya liṅga viśeṣaṇasya sandigdha tvena anumāna asambhavāt arthāpattiḥ māna antaram 
[072,vii]	nanu saṃśayasya kalpaka tve sthāṇu puruṣa saṃśayāt api tad eka koṭi nirvāha kalpanā pattiḥ na ca pramita saṃśayaḥ kalpana aṅgam jīvanasya tadānīm pramita tve saṃśaya abhāva prasaṅgāt jīvitva niścaye anumānadeva bahissattva niścayāt ca kadācid pramita tve ca prāc pramita puruṣa tvasya antarā tad saṃśaye kalpanā syāt kim ca jīvana saṃśayasya mṛte api dṛṣṭa tvāt na vyabhicāreṇa bahis sattva gamaka tvam iti ced 
[072,viii]	na yathā ukta sāmagrī prabhava saṃśayasya kalpana aṅga tvāt atas eva mṛta janiṣyamāṇayoḥ gṛha abhāva niścayaḥ na yathā ukta saṃśayam āpādayati iti na bahissattva kalpakaḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ ca yogyā anupalabdhi niścitaḥ na saṃśayaḥ iti atha jīvanam iyam agrāhaka pramāṇayoḥ yadi ca tulya bala tvam avagatam kva tarhi bahis sattva kalpanā viśeṣa darśana virahāt kalpane vā pramita jīvana nirvāhaka bahis sattva vat gṛha niyama nirvāhaka maraṇasya api ucita tvena tad kalpanā api syāt jīvana maraṇayoḥ saṃśaya aviśeṣāt atha tayoḥ ekam balīyaḥ aparama balam tadā ekena aparasya bādhaḥ eva iti na saṃśayaḥ 
[072,ix]	tasmāt yatra śata varṣa jīvi tvam avadhāritam gṛha abhāvaḥ ca niścitaḥ tatra bahis sattva kalpanam na tu jīvana saṃśaye evam ca devadattaḥ bahis san jīvitve sati gṛha niṣṭha atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvāt iti vyatirekiṇā bahisattva jñānena arthāpattyā liṅga viśeṣaṇa jīvitva saṃśaye bahis sattva kalpanā ca na asti eva kim ca gṛha abhāva niścayaḥ prāmāṇa dvaya viṣaya saṃśayam janayitvā jīvana saṃśayam āpādya bahissattvam kalpayati iti na yuktam na hi yatas eva yat saṃśayaḥ saḥ eva tat niścayāya prabhavati atiprasaṅgāt mā evam 
[072,x]	yathā ukta sāmagrī janita saṃśayavān evam tarkayati yogyā anupalabdhi gṛhītaḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ iti tat niścayaḥ su dṛḍhaḥ iti jīvana niyama grāhakayoḥ ekam bādhyam viruddhayoḥ apramāṇa tvāt tat iha maraṇam kalpayitvā jīvana grāhakam bādhyatām no vā bahis satvam kalpayitvā gṛha niyama grāhakam tatra bahis sattva kalpane gṛha niyama grāhaka mātra bādhā maraṇa kalpane tu śata varṣa jīvī devadattaḥ śata varṣa jīvaḥ gṛhaḥ eva iti niyama dvayasya api bādhā syāt tat āha jīvana bādhe tad niyama bādhasya āvaśyaka tvāt iti 
[072,xi]	kim ca adya jīvati śvas jīviṣyati ityādi bahutara kṣaṇa lava muhūrta ādi samayoṇa adhiniyatam jīvanam upalabdham iti tad bādhe bahutara vyāpti bādhaḥ devadatta tad avayava gaha sattvi āptiḥ ca alpā tathā abhāva svarūpa maraṇa apekṣayā bahissattvasya bhāvasya laghu tvāt yadi ca gṛhān yonya abhāva āśraya bahis padārtha vṛtti saṃyoga āśraya tvam bahis asattvam iti tad apekṣayā maraṇam eva laghu tathā api maraṇa apekṣayā jīvana mātram laghu iti tat eva kalpayitum arham tatas arthāpatti kalpitam jīvi tvam upajīvya anumānāt api bahis sattva jñānam bhaviṣyati iti etāvat tarka saha kṛtaḥ yathā uktapta āsām agrī prabhavaḥ saṃśayaḥ bahissattvam kalpayati 
[072,xii_073,i]	na ca vācyam tarkāṇām viparyaya aparyanasāyi tve ābhāsa tvam tad paryavasāne ca tat eva anumānam etat tarka sahāyam bahissattvam anumāyayiṣyati iti yatas lāghava gaurava tarkaṇām viparyaya aparyavasāyinām eva pramāṇa sahakāri tvam atas eva pratyakṣa śabdāt avapi saha kārī saḥ na ca tasyām daśāyām eva pramāṇa antaram asti tatas arthāpatti sahakāri tvam tarkasya 
[073,ii]	nanu sva kāraṇa adhīna svabhāva viśeṣāt tarka anugṛhīta yathā ukta saṃśayasya yadi bahis satva pramāpaka tvam tadā mṛte gṛhasthite vā tādṛśa saṃśayāt yatra bahis sattva kalpanā sā api pramā syāt iti ced na yathā hi pramāpakasya indriyasya doṣeṇa pramāśāk ti tirodhānāt aindriya bhramaḥ tathā yathā ukta saṃśayasya api doṣeṇa pramā śak titirodhānāt agraha kva bhrama saṃbhavāt parokṣa jñānānām janaka jñāna avibhrāma tve yathārtha tva niyamaḥ iti ced satyam pravṛttepi jīvana gṛha abhāva grāhaka pramāṇāyoḥ anyatara ābhāsa tvena ābhāsa tva saṃbhavāt yat vā doṣa abhāva saha kṛtasya yathā ukta saṃśayasya bahissatva pramāpaka tvam iti 
[073,iii]	ucyate anayoḥ ekam bādhyam viruddha artha grāhaka tvāt iti sāmānyatas dṛṣṭāt eva tarka saha kṛtāt gṛha niyama grāhaka bādhe liṅga viśeṣeṇa jīvitva niścaye anumānāt bahissattva siddhiḥ tathā hi jīvana pramāṇa bādhe gṛha niyama pramāṇa utthāpita liṅgena maraṇa anumānāt pramāṇa tva abhimatayoḥ dvayoḥ api bādhā syāt gṛha niyama grāhaka māna bādhe ca niṣparipanthi jīvana pramāṇāt liṅga viśeṣaṇa jīvitva niścaye bādhyam iti jāyamāna anumitiḥ paramparā maraṇa jñāpakam viṣayīkaroti na tu bahis sattva paramparā sādhakam jīvana pramāṇam tathā ca sāmānyatas dṛṣṭāt eva gṛha niyama grāhaka bādhe jīvana pramāṇāt liṅga viśeṣaṇa jīvi tva niścaye anumānāt eva bahissattva jñānam iti kim artha āpattyā 
[073,iv]	nanu bahis sattva jñānam vinā jīvī gṛha eva iti asya brahmaṇā api bādhitum aśakyatvāt prathamam bahis sattva jñānam na tu gṛha niyama grāhaka bādha anantaram tat yena niṣparipanthi jīvana grāhakāt jīvi tva niścaye anumānam syāt na prāthamika bahis sattva jñānam arthāpattim vinā na ca gṛha niyama grāhiṇi tulya bale jāgarūke katham artha āpattyā api bahis sattva jñānam iti vācyam tarka sahakāreṇa arthāpatteḥ balavat tvāt bahis sattva jñānam utpādya gṛha niyama grāhaka māna bādhāt iti ced 
[073,v]	na tarka sahakāreṇa sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya balavat tvena gṛha niyama grāhaka bādha sambhavāt tasmāt yathā ukta saṃśaya daśāyām jīvana bādhe tat niyama bādhasya āvaśyaka tvāt iti tarka anantaram eva bahis sattva jñānam iti avivādam tatra kalpanīya pramāṇa bādhe yathā ukta saṃśaye tarkasya na sahakāri tvam gauravāt kim tu niyama grāhaka bādha dvārā bahis satva paramparā sādhake sāmānyatodṛṣṭe lāghavāt na ca sāmānyatodṛṣṭa avatāraḥ eva atra na asti iti vācyam anirdhirita eka bādha prāptau pratyeka bādha anukūla kalpanāyām vinigamakaḥ tarkaḥ bhavati na ca eka bādha prāptiḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭam vinā 
[073,vi_073,vii]	kim ca virodha jñāna anantaram ekam apramāṇam iti yadi dhīḥ na asti tadā prāmāṇya saṃśayaḥ na syāt na syāt ca jīvana saṃśayaḥ dvayoḥ api jīvana maraṇa niścāyaka tvāt atha ekam anayoḥ apramāṇam iti jñānam janayitvā sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya mā aparya vasita tvāt tat janita niyama dvaya saṃśaya ahita jīvana saṃśaya anantaram tarka avatāre bahis asti iti jñānam jāyamānam saṃśayasya kāraṇa tvam vyavasthāpayati iti ced 
[073,viii]	na yat eva hi viruddha artha grāhaka tvam tarkam vinākṛtam anirdhāritekā prāmāṇya anumitim ajījanat tat eva tarka saha kṛtam punar anusandhīyamānam gṛha niyama grāhaka pramāṇam iti anumitim bahis sattva jñāna anukūlām janayati sahakāri vaicitryeṇa ekasya api vicitra phala janaka tvāt na ca jīvana saṃśaya anantaram tad anusandhānam asiddham gṛha niyama grāhakasya jīvana grāhaka tva viruddha artha grāhaka tva anusandhānam vinā bahis sattva kalpane api abādha prasaṅgāt 
[073,ix]	atha yadi paryavasannam api pramāṇam punar anusandhīyamānam sahakāri viśeṣāt phala antara janakam tadā icchā dravya āśritā kāryatvāt iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭa dravya āśrita tva anumitau paścāt aṣṭa dravya vṛtti tva bādhe vyatirekiṇāḥ ātma siddhiḥ iti vijyete aṣṭadṛvya vṛtti tva bādha saha kṛtāt sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt eva punar anusandhīyamānāt tad siddheḥ iti ced 
[073,x]	na anumiteḥ vyāpaka tā vacchedaka prakāraka tva niyamena tad prakāraka buddheḥ vyatireki sādhya tvāt vyatirekiṇaḥ api anyatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇena upāya antarasya adoṣāt ca api ca devattaḥ jīvana maraṇa anyatara pratiyogi prāṇi tvāt madvat iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭam lāghava sahakāreṇa jīvana pratīyogi tvam viṣayīkaroti tathā ca liṅga viśeṣaṇā niścayāt anumānāt eva bahissattva siddhiḥ 
[073,xi]	atha lāghava sācivyāt sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya api viśeṣa viṣaya tvāt niyama grāhaka pramāṇa utthāpita liṅgaka maraṇa anumānena jīvana grāhakasya iva asya api sat pratipakṣa tvam ekena api bhūyasām api pratibandha sambhavāt na ca tarkāt samā anyata udṛṣṭasya balavat tvam vyāpti pakṣa dharmate hi balam tat ca tulyam eva jñātam lāghava ākhya tarkasya viśeṣa mātra paryavasāyaka tvena vyāpti grāhaka tvasya tulya tvāt iti ced 
[073,xii]	tarhi pakṣa dharma tā balāt viśeṣa siddhiḥ kvāpi na syāt sarvatra sāmānya mukha pravṛtta pramāṇasya viśeṣa paryana sāne anya sādharmyeṇa sat pratipakṣa sambhavāt aprayojaka tvāt na viparīta sādhanam iti tulyam niyama grāhakasya aprayojaka tvāt jīvana grāhakasya tu sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya jyotiśśāstrāt yathārtha tvam eva vipakṣa bādhakam vyāpti grāhakam asti 
[073,xiii]	tasmāt sāmānya mukha pravṛttasya sahakāri viśeṣāt viśeṣa parasya anumānasya tad viśeṣa vilakṣaṇa grāhaka pramāṇena sat pratipakṣa tvam na ca pramāṇa virādhena asya tarkaḥ na sahakārī iti vācyam tarkān avatāre viśeṣa paratva abhāvena avirodhāt tad avatāre tad adhika bala tvāt eva anyathā tarkān avatāre sat pratipakṣasya tad avatāre api tattvam na nivartate 
[073,xiv]	kim ca evam artha āpattau api tad virodhena na saha kārī syāt yat uktam maraṇa kalpane śata varṣa avacchinna jīvī gṛhe eva iti asya api bādhaḥ iti tatra viśiṣṭa bādhaḥ na viśeṣya bādhāt maraṇe api jīvī gṛha eva iti asya viśeṣaṇasya ābādhāt kintu viśeṣaṇa bādhāt sa ca śata varṣiṇī vitva bādhaḥ eva viśeṣaṇa abhāva āyattaḥ viśiṣṭa bhāvaḥ api asti iti ced na viśeṣyavati viśiṣṭābhāvasya kevala viśeṣaṇa abhāva ātmaka tvāt viśiṣṭasya atiriktasya anabhyupagamāt 
[074,i]	anye tu śata varṣa jīvī devadattaḥ jīvī gṛhaḥ eva gṛhe na asti iti pramāṇeṣu dvayoḥ avirodhe api tṛtīyam ādāya virodha jñānam asti tatra jīvī gṛhe eva iti apramāṇa ghaṭita pramāṇa dvaya virodha jñāna janita apramāṇi asaṃśaya āhita jīvana saṃśayāt pramāṇayoḥ avirodha upapādaka pramāṇa virodhi bahis satvam kalpyate yathā ukta saṃśayasya ayam eva svābhāvaḥ yat vastu gatyāḥ apramāṇam tat virodhi kalpayati virādha ghaṭakasya vastu gatyā apramāṇa tvam eva vinigamaka tvam iti tad tuccham apramāṇasya api pramāṇa tvena jñānāt tarka ādibhiḥ viśeṣa darśanam vinā yathā ukta saṃśaya anantaram bahis asti iti jñānam asiddham atas na phala balena tathā arthāpatti kalpanam kim ca mṛte gṛhasthite bahis sthite tādṛśa saṃśayāt eva bahissattvam gṛha sattvam maraṇam ca kalpyeta kasyacid kvacid vastu gatyāḥ apramāṇa tvāt arthāpatti ābhāsaḥ ca evam na syāt 
[074,ii]	syāt etat mā bhūt saṃśayaḥ karaṇam artha āpattau anupapattiḥ tu syāt tathā hi jīvī devadattaḥ gṛhe na asti iti jñāne sati bahissattvam vinā jīvataḥ gṛha asattvam anupapannam iti jñāna anantaram bahis asti iti dhīḥ asti tatra anvaya vyatirekābhyām anupapatti jñānam karaṇam na ca devadattaḥ bahis asti vidyamāna tve sati gṛha asattvāt ghaṭa vat iti anumānāt vidyamāna tve sati yatra yat na asti tad anya deśe tat asti yathā gṛhe eva koṇe asan aham madhye tiṣṭhāmi iti vyāpti prabhāva anumānāt vā bahissattva siddheḥ kim arthāpattyā iti vācyam hetu sādhyayoḥ sahacāra ajñāna daśāyām anupapatti jñāne api bahis sattva jñānāt sāmānyatas vyāptiḥ ca anumāne upasaṃhatum aśakyayā iti tad anya deśa siddhiḥ arthāpattyā eva 
[074,iii]	nanu jīvinaḥ gṛha sattvam anupapannam kim devadatta bahis asattvam vinā uta bahissattva mātram vinā na ādyaḥ prathamam devadatta bahissattva pratītau tena vinā idam anupapannam iti jñāna abhāvāt pratītau vā kim artha āpattyā arthāpattitaḥ eva tad pratītau anyonya āśrayaḥ tat uktam yatas anya tvam tasiddheḥ agre tad asiddheḥ iti na antyaḥ anyadīya bahissattva jñānam vinā anupapatti abhāvāt bahis sattva mātra siddhau api devadatta bahissatvau āsiddheḥ iti ced 
[074,iv]	na sāmānyena hi vinā anupapatti jñānam kāraṇam sāmānāni ākāreṇa viśeṣa jñānam phalam tathā hi jīvataḥ bahi sassattvam vinā gṛha asattvam anupapannam iti jñānam yasya gṛha asattvam anupapannam tatra bahisattvam kalpayati na anyatra devadattaḥ ca tathā iti siddhe devadatte bahissattvam kalpyate iti devadatta bahissattvam paryavasyati na tu tena rupeṇa kalpanā na vā tena vinā anupapatti jñānam kāraṇam yathā vahni mātra vyāptāt dhūmāt parvate vahni siddhiḥ na tu parvayatīya tvena eva dhūmāt tad siddhiḥ tena rupeṇa vyāpaka tva āgrāhāt 
[074,v_074,vi]	atha upādaka abhāvavatī upapādya abhāva aniyamaḥ anupapattiḥ na tva bhāva mātram ati prasaṅgāt evam ca vyatireka vyāptimataḥ upapādyāt vyatireki anumāna mudrayā eva sādhya siddheḥ kim artha āpattyā tathā hi devadattaḥ bahis san jīvitve sati gṛha asattvāt yat na evam tat na evam yathā mṛtaḥ gaha sthitaḥ vā na ca anya vyāptyai anyasya gamaka tve ati prasaṅgaḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvasya niyāmaka tvāt na ca artha āpattau svarupasatī vyāptiḥ liṅgam na anumānaḥ iti vācyam anupapatteḥ jñānam vinā kalpanā anudayāt artha atti ābhāsān avakāśāt ca 
[074,vii_074,viii]	mā evam atra hi vyatireka vyāptiḥ anvayasya pakṣa dharma tvam iti vyāpti dhījanyam api bahis sattva jñānam na anumitiḥ tasyām vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā jñāna janya tā niyamāt na ca sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvena pakṣa dharmasya jñānam anumiti prayojakam iha api ati iti vācyam kevala anvayini tad asambhavāt tad apekṣayā sādhya vyāpya tva jñānasya laghu tvāt ca atha vyatireka sahacārāt hetoḥ eva vyāpti dṛś dṛśyate evam ca anvayasya vyatirekasya ubhayasya vā sahacārāt vyāpti graha traividhye anumāna traividhyam atas eva dhūmaḥ daśa aviśeṣe anvayī vyatirekī anya vyatirekī ca iti ced 
[074,ix]	astu tāvat evam tathā api jīvi devadatta abhāvaḥ gṛhe vartamānaḥ na bahissattve liṅgam devadattā vṛtti tvāt bahis sattva gṛha niṣṭhā bhāvayoḥ vyadhikaraṇa tvena niyata sāmāna adhikaraṇyarupa vyāpti abhāvāt ca upari savitā bhūmeḥ ālokavat tvāt iti atra bhūmeḥ upari saṃnihita savitṛka tvena anumānāt na api gṛha niṣṭha abhāva pratiyogi tvam tad pratiyegi tvasya devadatta dharma tayā tad asaṃnikarṣe pratyakṣeṇa jñātum aśakyatvāt atas eva viśeṣya asaṃnikarṣāt tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśaḥ api na pratyakṣeṇa na ca vyatireka vyāpti gṛha niṣṭhā bhāvayoḥ jñānam sahakārya āsādya manasā eva na janyate iti vācyam sahakāriṇaḥ eva māna antara tva prasaṅgāt 
[074,x]	atha vyāpti jñāna anantaram smaryamāṇa dhūmāt katham anumitiḥ ukta nyāyena tatra api liṅga parāmarśa abhāvāt iti ced na kathaṃcid katham tarhi vahni jñānam pakṣa dharma dhūma smṛti sahitāt dhūmaḥ vahnim vinā na asti iti anupapatti jñānāt iti gṛhāṇa atas eva dṛśyamānaḥ dhūmaḥ vahnim vinā anupānnaḥ iti yadā jñāyate tadā arthāpattiḥ eva yadā tu anupapati jñānam vinā vyāpya tvena pratisandhīyate tadā anumānam tvayā api tatra trividha anumāna svīkārāt vyatireka vyāptim upajīvya jīvi devadatta gṛha abhāvaḥ bahis satvam kalpayati 
[074,xi]	ucyate devadattā saṃnikarṣe api tasya gṛha niṣṭha abhāva pratiyogi tvam pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate tathā hi gṛhe devadattasya abhāvaḥ iti pratyakṣam devadattam ṣaṣṭhī artham ca abhāva sambandham pratiyogi tva lakṣaṇam gocarayati sambandha jñānasya saṃbandhi dvaya viṣaya tvāt pratiyoginā samam abhāvasya saṃbandha antara abhāvāt gṛha niṣṭha abhāva pratiyogi tve ca pratyakṣa upasthite smṛta vyāpti vaiśiṣṭyam api pratyakṣeṇa su graham na ca devadatta viśeṣyakam bahissattva vyāpya gṛha niṣṭhā bhāva pratiyogi tva jñānam na asti iti vācyam pakṣa vṛtti liṅga parāmarśa mātrasya anumiti janaka tvāt adhikasya gaurava parāhata tvāt 
[075,i_075,ii]	atha vā anita prasakta sahakāri vaśāt manasā eva smṛta devadatta viśeṣyakaḥ tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśaḥ yathā ca na sahakāri māna antaram tathā upapāditam adhastāt nanu mayūraḥ parvata itare na nṛtyati nṛtyati ca iti jñāna anantaram parvate nṛtyati iti jñānam asti na ca vyatirekiṇaḥ tat sambhavati parvata nṛtya aprasiddhau tena vinā anupapatti pratisandhānam api na iti katham arthāpattiḥ api iti vācyam adhikaraṇam vinā anupapadyamānam nṛtyam prasiddha adhikaraṇa bādha saha kṛtam prasiddhā itaram adhikaraṇam kalpayati iti ced 
[075,iii_075,iv]	na mayūra nṛtyam sādhikaraṇam nṛtya tvāt iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭam prasiddha adhiraṇa bādha sahakṛtam prasiddhā itaram parvatam adhikaraṇam ādāya nṛtya jñānam janayati yat vā parvata itare na nṛtyati iti śabdena nṛtya abhāva bodha anantaram mayūraḥ nṛtyati iti śabdāt jāyamānam jñānam parvata nṛtyam gocarayati prasiddha viśeṣa bādha saha kṛta sāmānya jñāna janaka pramāṇasya prasiddha itaram parvatam adhikaraṇa viśeṣam ādāya jñāna janaka tva niyamāt atas eva anitya jñāna ābādhanantaram kṣiti ādau jñāna janya tvam siddhyat nitya tvam ādāya siddhi ati iti ācāryāḥ 
[075,v_075,vi]	yat vā mayūra nṛtyam parvata adhikaraṇakam parvata itarān adhikaraṇa tve sati sādhikaraṇa tvāt parvata tva vat iti anvayavī atirekī athavā yaḥ sambhāvita tad tadirāvṛttiḥ san tad atirikta vṛttiḥ na bhavati sa tad vṛttiḥ bhavati iti sāmānyena yat tad artha antarbhāveṇa vyāptyā nṛtyasya parvata vṛtti tvam siddhyati evam pīnaḥ devadattaḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti atra api aprasiddha rātri bhojana sādhya pīna tva jñānam rātri bhojanam ādāya siddhyati 
[075,vii]	atha yathā abhojī pīnaḥ iti atra ayogya tā jñānam tathā pīnaḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti atra api divā bhojanasya bādhāt yogyatā ghaṭaka rātri bhojanasya pratīteḥ atas yogyatā ghaṭaka upasthitim vinā anvayam alabhamānam idam vākyam yogyatā ghaṭaka rātri bhojana upapādakam rātrau bhuṅaktaḥ iti vākyam kalpayitvā tena saha anvaya bodham janayati na ca evam lāghavāt rātri bhojanam eva kalpayitum yuktam śābdī hi ākāṅakṣā śabdena eva prapūryate iti nyāyena śabda upasthāpitam ādāya śabdasya anvaya bodha janaka tvāt evam ca śrūyamāṇa śabdasya anvaya bodhaka tvam yogyatā ghaṭaka upasthāpakena śabdena vinā anupapadyamānam tam kalpayitvā yatra anvaya bodham janayati tatra śruta arthāpattiḥ 
[075,viii]	dvāram ityādau pidhā ihi iti śabda kalpanam śruta artha āpattiḥ eva śabdaḥ ca yadi api śrūyamāṇaḥ bādhitaḥ tathā api abhiprāya sthaḥ kalpyate yathā guru mate svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti atra sākṣāt sādhana tā ābādhe paramparā ghaṭakasya anupasthityā paraṃpara asā dhana tā jñāna virahaḥ yogya tā jñāna abhāvāt prasiddha pada sā māna adhikaraṇyā anupapattiḥ iti yogyatā jñānasya paramparā sādhana tā ghaṭakam apūrvam liṅa ādi vācyam kalpayati tatas svarga sādhanam yāgaḥ iti jñānam jāyate anyathā apūrvam api vācya na syāt iti 
[075,ix]	ucyate bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ anvaya virodhi rūpa virahaḥ vā yogyatā atas divā abhojane rātri bhojanā pratītau api bhojana sādhya pīna tvāt divā na bhuṅkte iti śabdāt hīḥ utpadyate na prati iti anupapattiḥ kim tu pratīta anupapattyā rātri bhojanam kalpyate atas eva apūrvam api na vācyam iti vakṣyate tasmāt na arthāpattiḥ anumānāt atiricyata
[075,x]	tat ca anumānam para artham nyāya sādhyam iti nyāyaḥ tad avayavāḥ ca pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni nirūpyante tatra na samasta rūpa upapanna liṅga pratipādaka vākyam nyāyaḥ atra eva vākye ati vyāpteḥ kiṃtu anumiti caram akāraṇa liṅga parāmarśa prayoja ka śābda jñāna janaka vākyam nyāyaḥ pratijña ādi pañca vākya eraka vākya tayā sva artha viśiṣṭa jñānam janyate tena ca viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭyā avagāhimāna antaram utthāpyate tena ca caram aparāmarśaḥ utpādyate iti nyāya janya śābda jñānasya parāmarśa prayojaka tā 
[075,xi_075,xii]	anumiti caram akāraṇa liṅga parāmarśa prayoja ka śābda jñāna jana kaśābda jñāna janaka vākya tvam avayava tvam atas eva vahni vyāpya dhūma vān ayam iti vākye tad avayave ca na nyāya tad avayava lakṣaṇa ativyāptiḥ tena parāmarśasya tad avayavena parāmarśa janakasya jananāt yat tu saṃkṣepataḥ parāmarśa prayojaka vākya tvena viśeṣa abhāvāt saḥ api nyāya eva iti tat na kathā āyāmākāṅkṣā krameṇa abhidhānam iti prathamam viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭye ākāṅkṣā na asti iti tad abhidhāne nigrahāt iti vakṣyate anyathā cakṣuḥ ādeḥ api parāmarśa janakatayā nyāyatva āpattiḥ ākāṅkṣā virahaḥ tulyaḥ eva 
[075,xiii_075,xiv]	anye tu pañca avayava vākyāt vijātīyam eva śābda jñānam utpadyate iti tat hī janaka vākya tvam nyāya tvam evam pratijñā ādi avayavāt api pratyekam vijātīyam śābda jñānam iti tad tat hījana ka śābda tvam eva tat tat lakṣaṇam iti tat na jñāna viśeṣa janaka tvam tad tat jñāna janaka tvam vā nyāye pratijñā ādau ca anati prasaktam anugata rūpam antareṇa dūrni rūpam iti tad svīkāre tasya eva lakṣaṇa tvāt anyathā jāti saṃkara prasaṅgaḥ 
[075,xv_076,i]	tatra pratijñā na sādhya nirdeśaḥ sādhya pade ati vyāpteḥ kim tu uddeśya anumiti hetu liṅga parāmarśa prayojaka vākya artha jñāna janaka tve sati uddeśya anumiti anyūnāna tirikta viṣaya kaśa abda jñāna janakam vākyam anyūnāna atirikta padam vihāya liṅga aviṣayaka tvam vā jñāna viśeṣaṇam tena udāharaṇa ādi vyudāsaḥ nigamanam ca na parāmarśa hetuḥ abādhita asat pratipakṣa tva jñāna janaka tvāt hetu abhidhāna prayojaka jijñāsā janaka vākya tvam vā liṅga aviṣaya kaliṅgi viṣaya ka jñāna janaka nyāya avayava vākya tvam vā itara avayavānām liṅga viṣaya ka jñāna janaka tvāt 
[076,ii_076,iii]	pratijñātvam jātiḥ anyūna anati prasakta tāntrika vyavahārāt iti kecid tat na devadatta prabhava tva ādinā jāti saṃkara prasaṅgāt pratijñā janyam vijātīyam jñānam vyavahārāt iti tad janakam pratijñā iti api na tad janaka tvam janakatva jñānam vā na anugata rūpam antareṇa sambhavati iti uktasya anusaraṇīya tvāt etena śabdaḥ anityaḥ iti liṅgi dhī para vākya janya jñāna vṛtti kṛtaka tvā diti ādi vākya janya jñāna āvṛtti jāti yogi jñāna janaka vākyam pratijñā iti nirastam 
[076,iv]	nanu pratijñā na sādhana aṅgam vipratipatteḥ pakṣa parigrahe tatra pramāṇa ākāṅkṣāyām hetu abhidhānasya prāthamyāt iti ced na vipratipatti agre samaya bandha anantaram śabda anitya tvam sādhaya iti madhyasthasya vādinaḥ vā ākāṅkṣāyām śabda anitya tvam sādhyam na ca sādhya nirdeśam vinā hetu vākyam niṣpratiyogikam anvayam bodhayitum īṣṭe na ca vādi vākye anupasthitam api yogyatayā anveti atiprasaṅgāt na ca vipratipattitaḥ sādhya upasthitiḥ tasyāḥ prativādi vipratipattyā pramāṇa ādi vyavasthayā ca antarita tvāt para vipratipattim samaya bandham ca vinā sthāpanāyāḥ abhāvāt vipratipatti vākyasya pakṣa parigraheṇa paryavasita tayā nirākāṅkṣa tvāt ca āvṛttau tu sā eva pratijñā na ca avayava antarāt hetu anvaya yogyā sādhya upasthitiḥ na api avayava antareṇa ākṣepāt sādhya anvaye tad abhidhānam tad abhidhāne ca sādhya anvayaḥ iti anyonya āśrayāt tasmāt prati iti anupapattyā pratīta anupapattyā vā na iha ākṣepaḥ 
[076,v]	anye tu śabda anitya tve pramāṇam vada iti yadi madhyasthasya anuyogaḥ tathā api pramāṇa mātre na ākāṅkṣā kiṃtu viśiṣṭe viśiṣṭam tu viśeṣaṇam sādhyam anabhidhāya na śakya abhidhānam na ca vastutas yat sādhyam tatra pramāṇam vada iti madhyastha niyogaḥ vādi dvaya madhye tad asambhavāt tasmāt sādhya abhidhānam vinā na hetoḥ ākāṅakṣāḥ na vā anvaya bodhaka tvam iti pratijñā sādhana aṅgam iti 
[076,vi_076,vii]	sādhya nirdeśa anantaram kutas iti ākāṅkṣāyām sādhana tā vyañjaka vibhaktimat liṅga vacanam eva ucitam anyathā anākāṅkṣita abhidhāne nigraha āpatteḥ loke tathā eva ākāṅkṣā nivṛttiḥ iti vyutpatteḥ iti pratijñā anantaram hetu upanyāsaḥ hetu tvam ca anumitikāraṇī bhūta liṅga parāmarśa prayoja ka śābda jñāna janaka sādhya aviṣaya kaśābda dhī janaka hetu vibhaktimat śabda tvam hetu tva pratipādaka vibhaktimat nyāya avayava tvam vā udāharaṇa prayojaka ākāṅkṣā jana kaśābda jñāna janaka nyāyau ayava tvam vā sādhya aviṣayaka jñāna janaka hetu pañcamī anta anumiti para śabda tvam vā pratijñā vākya dhī janya kāraṇā kāṅkṣā nivartaka jñāna janaka hetu vibhaktimat vākya tvam vā pañcamī anta lākṣaṇika pada vat anumiti para vākya tvam vā hetu padena jñāna lakṣaṇāt anyathā liṅgasya ahetutvena hetu vibhakti arthān anvayāt tathā eva ākāṅkṣā nivṛtteḥ anumiti hetu jñāna kāraṇa dhūmavat tva aditi śabda janya jñāna vṛtti pratijña ādi janya jñāna āvṛtti jāti yogi jñāna janaka vākya tvam hetu tvam iti anye jātim vinā kena rūpeṇa jñānasya anumiti janaka tvam vākya viśeṣa janya tvasya api janya tā avat chedaka rūpa aparicaye durgrahāt iti apare 
[076,viii_076,ix]	anvaya vyāpti abhidhāyaka avayava abhidhāna prayojaka jñāna janaka hetu tva pratipādaka vibhaktimat nyāya avayava tvam anvayihetu tvam etat eva vyatireka vyāpti abhidhāyaka pada prakṣepāt vyatireki hetu tvam anvaya vyatireka udāharaṇa ākāṅkṣā prayojaka tathā bhūta avayava tvam anvaya vyatireki hetu tvam yat vā pakṣa sa pakṣa sataḥ vipakṣa asataḥ hetu vacanam anvaya vyatireki atyanta abhāva apratiyogi sādhya samāna adhikaraṇa pakṣa sa pakṣa sat hetu vacanam kevala anvayi 
[076,x]	yat vā a n u m i t i k ā r a ṇ ī b h ū t a p a r ā marśa prayoja kaśābda jñāna kāraṇa sādhya aviṣaya ka śābda dhī janaka pratīta anvaya sādhya sādhana vācaka hetu vibhaktimat śabda tvam anvayihetu tvam etat eva apratita anvaya sādhya sādhana iti viśeṣaṇāt vyatireki hetu lakṣaṇam kathāyām dhūmāt iti eva prayoktavyam na tu dhūmavat tvāt iti matupaḥ vyartha tvāt 
[076,xi]	sāmānyavat tve sati bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tva āditi a pārthakam vibhakti upasthāpita hetu tvena sāmānyavat tvasya vibhakti antara avaruddhasyānanvayāt iti kecid tat na sati saptam ībalāt sāmānyavat tvasya bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣa tvasya ca sāmānādhikaraṇya upasthitau viśiṣṭe hetutva anvayāt tathā eva vyutpatteḥ na hi ayam arthaḥ asmān na avagamyate iti
[076,xii]	hetau ukte katham asya gamaka tvam iti ākāṅkṣāyām vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayoḥ pradarśana prāptau vyāpteḥ prāthamyāt tad pradarśanāya udāharaṇam tatra anumiti hetu liṅga parāmarśa para vākya janya jñāna janaka vyāpya tva abhimata vat niṣṭha niyata vyāpaka tva abhimata sambandha bodha janaka śabda tvam udāharaṇa tvam sāmānya lakṣaṇe sādhya sādhana sambandha bodhaka tvam sādhya sādhana abhāva sambandha bodhaka tvam ca viśeṣa lakṣaṇa dvayam 
[076,xiii_077,ii]	nyāya avayava dṛṣṭānta vacanam udāharaṇam iti tu na dṛṣṭānta prayogasya sāmayika tvena asārvatrika tvāt yaḥ yaḥ dhūmavān saḥ agrimān iti eva vyāpti pratīteḥ na api prakṛta anumiti hetu liṅga parāmarśa para vākya janya jñāna viṣaya vyāpti upanāyakam vacanam tat upanayā ati vyāpteḥ atas upanaya abhidhāna prayojaka jijñāsā janaka vākyam udāharaṇam etat eva anvaya vyatireka vyāpti viṣaya tva viśeṣitam viśeṣa lakṣaṇa dvayam iti anye 
[077,iii_077,v]	atra ca vyabhicāra vāraṇāya vīpsām āhuḥ yatra ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāt eva vyāptiḥ tatra na vīpsā kevalān vayinī a bheda anumāne ca vīpsāyām api vyabhicāra tādavasthyam iti tu vayam vīpsā ca yat pade na tat pade api virūpa upasthitayoḥ api tad padena parāmarśāt buddhi stha vācaka tvāt iti na vyutpatti virodhaḥ yathā yat yat pāpam pratijahi iti atra idam ca s ā d h y asādhana ubhaya āśraya vikalān upadarśita anvaya viparīta upadarśita anvayān upadarśita vyatireka viparīta upadarśita vyatireka bhedāt ābhāsa rūpam iti 
[077,vi]	udāharaṇa anantaram bhavatu vyāptiḥ tathā api vyāptam kim pakṣe vartate na vā iti ākāṅkṣāyām vyāptasya pakṣa dharma tva pradarśanāya upanayaḥ tatra anumiti kāraṇa tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśa janaka avayava tvam upanaya tvam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam sādhya vyāpya viśiṣṭa pakṣa bodhaka avayava tvam sādhya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogimat pakṣa bodhaka avayava tvam ca viśeṣa lakṣaṇa dvayam 
[077,vii]	udāharaṇa antaḥ eva prayogaḥ iti na vācyam tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśasya vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā avagāhinaḥ avayava antarāt alābhāt tad anabhyupagame api pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ alābhāt na ca hetu vacanāt eva tad avagamaḥ tasya kaḥ hetuḥ iti ākāṅkṣāyām eva pravṛtta tvena hetu svarūpa upasthāpakasya atatparatvāt vādi vākyāt eva ākṣepaḥ iti ced na tad arthasya asiddha tvena anākṣepaka tvāt anyathā pratijñā mātrāt eva sarva ākṣepe avayava antara vilayāt pratipādyānām svatas eva tad avagamaḥ iti ced na teṣām vyutpanna avyutpanna tayā sarvatra tad asambhavāt pratipādakena sva vyāpārasya nirvāhayitum ucita tvāt ca anyathā avayava antare api evam prasaṅgāt 
[077,viii_077,ix]	upanaya anantaram nigamanam tat ca anumiti hetu liṅga parāmarśa prayoja ka śābda jñāna kāraṇa vyāpti pakṣa ta adhī prayukta sādhyadhī janakam vākyam na ca vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayoḥ caturbhiḥ eva avayavaiḥ paryāpteḥ kim tena iti vācyam abādhita asat pratipakṣa tvayoḥ alābhe caturṇām api aparyavasānāt atha abhidhāna bhidheyayoḥ vyāpti pakṣa dharma tāvat liṅga pratipādanāt eva paryavasānena avayava antarāṇām nirākāṅkṣa tvam viparīta śaṅkā nivṛtteḥ api tatas eva lābhāt anyathā nigamanena api tad avāraṇāt na hi tad viśeṣa darśam anādṛtya eva tat nivartakam siddha nirdeśa tayā vārayati iti ced na sva rūpa mātra abhidhānāt sādhya tva anupasthitau tasmāt iti hetu vibhakti ananvaya prasaṅgāt ca iti ced na vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā jñāne api bādhasat pratipakṣa buddheḥ sādhya jñāna anutpatti darśanāt tad abhāva abodhane samīhita anirvāhāt 
[077,x_077,xiii]	vyāpteḥ atha bādha ādi virahasya prayojaka tvam na tu tad vodhasya māna abhāvāt asiddheḥ ca iti kim artham bādha ādi virahaḥ bodhanīyaḥ iti ced na yat avagame sati yat na bhavati tad tad abhāva jñāna sādhyam iti na ca ananvayaḥ tasmāt iti anvaya balāt eva hetu anākāṅikṣa tatva lakṣaṇa siddha tva jñānāt na tu anvayāt pūrvam iha kecid yathā tasmāt iti sarva nāmnā hetoḥ parāmarśaḥ pūrva ukta śeṣa rūpa lābhāya tathā sādhya aṃśasya api tathā iti sarva nāmnā siddha sthalaḥ iva virodhi vāraṇāya yuktaḥ iti āhuḥ 
[077,xiv]	tat na tathā iti svarūpe prakāre sādṛśye vā ādye tathā ca ayam iti prakrāntāt tathā iti hetumān iti arthaḥ syāt tathā ca ananvayaḥ na hi hetumat tvāt eva hetumān iti anvitam na dvitīyaḥ sāmānyena pakṣasya api anvaya vyāptau praveśāt tad prakāra anvayaḥ tatra eva iti ananvayāt atas eva na tṛtīyaḥ api abheda anumāne ca anvayini tasmāt tathā iti sādṛśya abhāvāt bahūnām ca prakrame viśeṣyān anvayāt vādi vākye ca yogyatā anvaye ati prasaṅgāt 
[077,xv]	tasmāt iti atra vibhakti arthān anvayāt eva niyamaḥ tasmāt anityaḥ iti abhidhāne viśiṣya siddha tā avagabhyate pūrvam sādhyatayā uktasya samartha hetu saṃbandhena punar utkīrtanāt anyathā tad vaiyarthyāt saṃśaya prayojana ādayaḥ tu avayava lakṣaṇa abhāvāt eva na avayavāḥ kim tu nyāya aṅga tayā upayujyante iti na ādhikyam kaṇṭaka uddhārasya ca na sārvatrika tvam samaya viśeṣa upayogi tvāt iti 
[078,i]	atha hetvābhāsāḥ tattva nirṇaya vijaya prayojaka tvāt nirūpyante tatra anumiti kāraṇībhūta abhāva pratiyegi yatha artha jñāna viṣaya tvam yat viṣayaka tvena liṅga jñānasya anumiti pratibandhaka tvam jñāyamānam sat anumiti pratibandhakam yat tattvam vā hetvābhāsa tvam daśā viśeṣe hetvoḥ eva asā dhāraṇa sat pratipakṣayoḥ ābhāsa tvāt tad buddheḥ api anumiti pratibandhaka tvam 
[078,ii_078,iii]	yadi api bādhasat pratipakṣayoḥ pratyakṣa śābda jñāna pratibandhaka tvāt na liṅga ābhāsa tvam tathā api jñāyamānasya ābhāsasya atra lakṣaṇam yat vā pratyakṣa ādau bādhena na jñānam pratibadhyate kintu utpanna jñāne aprāmāṇyam jñāyate anumitau tu utpattiḥ eva pratibadhyate te ca savyabhicāra viruddha sat pratipakṣā siddha bādhitāḥ pañca 
[078,iv_078,v]	savyabhicāraḥ api trividhaḥ sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa anupasaṃhāri bhedāt tatra savyabhicāraḥ sādhya tad abhāva prasañjakaḥ iti na tritayasādhāraṇam lakṣaṇam ekasya ubhayam pratyasādhaka tvāt anāpādaka tvāt ca na api ubhaya pakṣa vṛtti tvam ubhaya vyāvṛtta tvam vā tattvam ananugamāt atha sādhya saṃśaya janaka koṭi dvaya upasthāpaka pakṣa dharma tā jñāna viṣaya tve sati hetu abhimataḥ saḥ vipratipattiḥ tu pratyekam na tathā na vā pakṣa vṛttiḥ sādhāraṇam anvayena asādhāraṇam vyatirekeṇa anupasaṃhārī pakṣaḥ eva ubhaya sāhacaryeṇa koṭi dvaya upasthāpakaḥ 
[078,vi]	kevala anvayi sādhyakān upasaṃhārī ayam ghaṭaḥ etat tva āditya sādhāraṇaḥ ca sat hetuḥ eva tat ajñānam doṣaḥ puruṣasya atas eva asādhāraṇa prakaraṇa samayoḥ anitya doṣa tvam anyathā sat hetau bādha ādi jñāne hetvābhāsa ādhikya āpattiḥ na ca prameya tvena abheda anumāne śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda ākāśa anyatara tvāt iti atra ca sādhāraṇe avyāptiḥ tayoḥ sādhya vada vṛtti tvena viruddha tvāt iti ced na etat ajñāne api sādhāraṇi ādi pratyekasya jñānāt udbhāvanāt ca sva para anumiti pratibandhāt udbhāvita etat nirvāha artham sādhāraṇa ādeḥ avaśyā udbhāvya tvena tasya eva doṣa tvāt ca 
[078,vii_078,viii]	etena pakṣa vṛtti tve satya numiti virodhi saṃbandha avyāvṛttiḥ anaikāntikaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣa vṛtti tvam ubhaya vyāvṛtta tvam anupasaṃhāri tvañcā anumiti virodhi tad sambandhaḥ pratyekam asti viruddhaḥ api anena rūpeṇa savyabhicāraḥ eva upādheḥ ca na saṅkaraḥ iti vakṣyate iti nirastam etat ajñāne jñānepivā āvaśyaka pratyeka jñānasya doṣa tvāt asādhaka tā anumitau vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca 
[078,ix_078,xi]	atas eva sādhya avyāpya tve sati sādhya abhāva avyāpya hetvābhāsa tvam sādhya vat mātra vṛtti anyatve sati sādhya abhāvavat mātra vṛtti anya tvam vā iti parāḥ tam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt prathamam hetvābhāsa tva ajñānāt ca gaganam anityam śabda āśraya tvāt ityādi bādha viruddha saṅkīrṇa asādhāraṇa avyāptiḥ iti kaścid na api sa pakṣa vipakṣa gata sarva sapakṣa vipakṣa vyāvṛtta anyatara tvam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt anupasaṃhārya vyāpteḥ ca kiñca pakṣa atirikta sādhyavataḥ sa pakṣa tve prameya tvena abheda sādhane anupasaṃhārye avyāptiḥ pakṣa atirikta sādhyavataḥ aprasiddheḥ sādhyavataḥ sa pakṣa tve vivakṣite aprasiddhiḥ vṛttimataḥ dharmasya sādhya vat vipakṣa anyatara vṛtti tva niyamāt 
[078,xii]	na api pakṣa atirikta sādhya vat mātra vṛtti anyatve sati pakṣa atirikta sādhya abhāvavat mātra vṛtti bhinna tvam anupasaṃhārya vyāpteḥ dhūmāt au ati vyāpteḥ ca tasya pakṣe sādhyavati vṛtteḥ na api pakṣa vṛtti tve viruddha anya tve ca satya numiti aupayika sambandha śūnya tvam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt etena anugatam sarvam eva lakṣaṇam pratyuktam pratyekam eva dūṣaṇa tvāt udbhāvane vādi nivṛtteḥ ca 
[079,i_079,iii]	ucyate ubhaya koṭī upasthāpaka tāvacchedaka rūpavat tvam tattvam tat ca sādhāraṇa tva ādi viruddha anya pakṣa vṛtti t tve sati a numiti virodhi sambandha avyāvṛttiḥ vā tena eva rūpeṇa jñātasya pratibandhaka tvāt parasya tathā eva udbhāvanāt ca lakṣaṇa anurodhena pratyekam eva hetvābhāsa tvam yat vā sādhya vat mātra vṛtti anyatve sati sādhya abhāvavat mātra vṛtti anya tvam tena asādhāraṇasya sādhya tad abhāva upasthāpaka tayā dūṣaka tva pakṣe na avyāptiḥ na ca evam ādhikye vibhāga vyāghātaḥ sva rūpa satānugata rūpeṇa trayāṇām ekīkṛtya mahā ṛṣiṇā vibhāga karaṇāt na ca evam sādhya abhāva jñāpaka tvena bādha prakaraṇa samayoḥ tad ajñāpakatayā anyeṣām upasaṃgrahaḥ kutas na kṛtaḥ iti vācyam svatantra icchasya niyoga paryanuyogān arha tvāt 
[079,iv_079,v]	tatra sādhāraṇa tvam na sādhya abhāva vat gāmi tvam sarvam anityam meya tvāt iti anupasaṃhārye bhūḥ nityāḥ gandhavat tva āditya sādhāraṇe saṃyoga ādi sādhyaka dravya tve ca ati vyāpteḥ atas eva na sādhya vat tad anya vṛtti tvam na api niścita sādhya vat tad anya vṛtti tvam sādhya vadanya vṛtti tvasya dūṣaka tvena śeṣa vaiyarthyāt 
[079,vi_079,vii]	atas eva amukena ayam anaikāntikaḥ iti eva udbhāvyate tatas eva vādi nivṛtteḥ ca na tu sa pakṣa gata tvam api anupasaṃhāryaḥ vyāvartyaḥ anyathā tasya etat viśeṣa tva āpattiḥ iti ced tyaja tarhi tam adhikam klapte antarbhāvāt na api sa pakṣa vipakṣa gata tvam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt viruddhaḥ vyāvartya iti ced na vipakṣa gāmi tvasya eva dūṣaka tve tasya api etat antar bhāvāt 
[079,viii_079,ix]	atha pakṣāni asādhya vat tad anya vṛtti tvam sādhāraṇa tvam tena sarvam anityam meya tvāt iti anupasaṃhārye na ati prasaṅgaḥ na ca vyartha viśeṣaṇa tā ghaṭaḥ anityaḥ ghaṭa ākāśa ubhaya vṛtti dvitva āśraya tvāt iti anupasaṃhāryasya viruddhasya anaikāntika bhinnasya vyavacchedya tvāt iti ced na dūṣaka tā prayojaka rūpa bhedam antareṇa bhedasya eva anupapatteḥ sādhya vat vṛtti tve sati sarva sādhya vat anya vṛtti tvam iti api na vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt eka vyaktika sādhye tad abhāvāt ca etena hetvābhāsa antara vyavacchedakam viśeṣaṇam vyartham iti 
[079,x]	ucyate vipakṣa vṛtti tvam sādhāraṇa tvam tanmātrasya dūṣaka tvāt viruddhasya api tattva jñāne vipakṣa vṛtti tā jñāna daśāyām sādhāraṇa tvam anyathā tasya hetvābhāsa antara tā āpatteḥ upādheḥ asaṅkaraḥ eva sarvam anityam meya tvāt iti anupasaṃhārī śabdaḥ nityaḥ śabda tvāt bhūḥ nityāḥ gandhavat tva āditya sādhāraṇaḥ ca vastu gatyā sādhya abhāvavat vṛtti tvena sādhāraṇaḥ api pakṣatādaśāyām udbhāvayitum na śakyate iti ubhayoḥ bhedena upanyāsaḥ 
[079,xi]	sarva sapakṣa vipakṣa vyāvṛttaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ nanu sa pakṣa tvam na sādhya vat mātrat tvam vipakṣa āvṛtteḥ vṛttimataḥ sādhya vat vṛtti tva niyamāt na api pakṣa atirikta sādhyavat tvam śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda tvāt ityādeḥ vyāptidhīdaśāyām api asādhāraṇa tā āpatteḥ na ceṣṭāpattiḥ bādha pratirodhau vinā vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayā jñātāt anumiti niyamāt iti ced na sarva niścita sādhya vat vipa kṣa vyāvṛtta tvasya tattvāt 
[079,xii]	śabdatva anitya tva vyāpti grahe sati śabde sādhya niścayāt na ati vyāptiḥ na ca ghaṭaḥ ayam etat tvāt iti sat hetau ati vyāptiḥ sādhya sandeha daśāyām tasya hetvābhāsa tvāt yadi api bhūḥ nityāḥ gandhavat tvāt ityādiḥ vastutas sādhāraṇaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ śabda tvāt iti viruddhaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda tvāt ityādiḥ sat hetuḥ eva vyāpti ajñānasya puruṣa doṣa tvāt iti udāharaṇa abhāvāt asādhāraṇaḥ na pṛthak tathā api pakṣatā daśāyām sādhya tad abhāva aniścayena tasya doṣa tvam anyathā pakṣatva bhaṅga prasaṅgāt 
[080,i]	atha sarva sapakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ eva doṣaḥ na vipakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ api tasyāḥ anuguṇa tvāt pratyuta vipakṣa vyāvṛt tattvena vyatirekitayā para sādhya sādhakam eva upanyastam syāt na ca saṃśāyaka tayā doṣa tvam tat ca ubhaya vyāvṛtta tva jñānāt iti vācyam vyāpti grāhakam sahacāra jñānam tad abhāva dvāra eva sa pakṣa vyāvṛtti mātrasya doṣa tvāt 
[080,ii]	kiñca śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda tvāt iti uktvā nivṛtte tāvat na idam udbhāvyam nyūna tvena eva vādi nigrahāt tad udbhāvane vādi nivṛtteḥ ca na ca nyūna tve tat upajīvyam asādha araṇya vyatirekeṇa api tad udbhāvanāt na ca vyatireki prayoge tad upanyāsaḥ vyāpti pakṣa dharmatayoḥ apratikṣepe akiñcitkara tvāt sva artha anumāne ca sarva sapakṣa vyāvṛttiḥ eva doṣaḥ iti uktam iti 
[080,iii]	ucyate śabda tvam sādhyavataḥ tad abhāvavataḥ ca nivṛtta tvena jñātam arthāt vyatirekitayā vā pakṣe sādhyam tad abhāvan ca sādhayet aviśeṣāt anyathā pakṣa vṛtti tva anupapattiḥ iti sādhya tad abhāva utthāpakatayā sva artha anumāne asādhāraṇaḥ doṣaḥ sat pratipakṣe dvau hetū tathā atra tu ekaḥ eva iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ asādhāraṇena vyatireki prayoge parasya sarva sapakṣa vyāvṛtta tva mātram udbhāvyam sādhya abhāva utthāpaka tvāt na tu vipakṣa vyāvṛtta tvam api pratikūla tvāt vyartha tvāt ca 
[080,iv]	yat vā vipakṣa vyāvṛtta tayā sādhyam iva sa pakṣa vyāvṛtta tayā sādhya abhāvam api sādhayet iti dṛṣṭānta tayā pratibanditayā vā tad udbhāvanam api lakṣaṇantu sarva sapakṣa vyāvṛtta tvam na tu vipakṣa vyāvṛtta tvam api vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt viruddham api anena upādhinā asādhāraṇam eva anyathā etat avagame viruddha tva ajñāne hetvābhāsa antara tā āpatteḥ 
[080,v]	anupasaṃhāraḥ na asat sa pakṣa vipakṣaḥ siddhi asiddhi virodhāt na api kevala anvayi dharma avacchinna pakṣakaḥ kevala anvayi sādhyakasya sat hetu tvāt vyatireki sādhyakasya tu sādhya tad abhāva vat gāmi tvena sādhāraṇa tvāt anyathā saṃśaya ahetu tvena anaikāntika tā na syāt sarvam kṣaṇikam sattvāt iti sādhya aprasiddhyā vyāpya tva asiddham apārthakam vā sādhya prasiddhau tu sādhāraṇam eva na ca pakṣāni asādhya vat tad anya vṛtti tvam pakṣa atirikta sādhya abhāva vat vṛtti tvam vā sādhāraṇa tvam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt na ca viruddham viśeṣaṇasya vyāvartyam iti uktam 
[080,vi_080,viii]	na api atyanta abhāva pratiyogi sādhyaka tve sati kevala anvayi dharma avacchinna pakṣaka tvam sarvam abhidheyam meya tvāt iti atra vipratipattyā pakṣa tādaśāyām pakṣe sādhya aniścayena anupasaṃhāriṇī avyāpaka tvāt atha pakṣa atirikte vyāpti graha anukūlā pratīta sahacāraḥ anupasaṃhāryaḥ yadi ca pakṣe vyāpti grahaḥ kathañcid tadā śabda upadarśita vyāptika anumāna vat abheda anumāna vat ca sat hetuḥ eva iti ced na tatra eva sat hetau ati vyāpteḥ sarvasya pakṣa tve pakṣa atirikta aprasiddheḥ asādhāraṇa viruddhayoḥ ati vyāpteḥ ca dūṣaka tāyām vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca na ca dūṣaka tānaikāntika tvena na pratyekam iti vācyam artha gatyā vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt na api vipratipatti viṣaya mātra vṛtti tvam kevala anvayi sādhyake avyāpteḥ sarvasya pakṣa tve mātrā artha abhāvāt iti 
[080,ix_080,x]	ucyate vyāpti graha anukūla eka dharmī upasaṃhāra abhāvaḥ yatra sa hetu abhimataḥ anupasaṃhārī sa ca anvayena vyatirekeṇa vā sarvasya pakṣa tve dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt ghaṭaḥ anityaḥ ghaṭa ākāśa ubhaya vṛtti dvitva āśraya tvāt ityādau sādhya sādhana sāhacarya ajñānāt tasya viruddha tva ajñāna daśāyām anupasaṃhāri tvasya iṣṭa tvāt kevala anvayi dharma avacchinna pakṣakaḥ vā sarvam abhidheyam prameya tvāt iti sat hetau na kevala anvayī pakṣa tāvacchedakaḥ niścita sādhya vat vṛtti tvāt vipratipattyā sādhya aniścaya daśāyām pakṣa tve tad anupasaṃhārī eva vyatireki sādhyake sādhya abhāvavat vṛtti tva ajñāna daśāyām idam dūṣaṇam tad avagame api sādhāraṇa saṅkaraḥ eva evam vyāpya tva asiddheḥ jñāne tad udbhāvane ca ayam vyabhicāra vat upajīvya tvāt adoṣaḥ ghaṭa ākāśa ubhaya vṛtti dvitva āśraya tvañca viruddham eva etena anupasaṃhāri tva pratisandhāne yadi vyāpti grahaḥ tadā anumitiḥ eva tad abhāve vyāpya tva asiddhiḥ eva iti nirastam upajīvya tvāt iti 
[081,i]	viruddhaḥ na sādhya abhāva vyāpyaḥ saṃyoga ādi sādhyake sat hetau ati vyāpteḥ na api sādhya vat niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi vyāpya tvam tattvam idam dravyam guṇavat tvāt ityādau saṃyoga ādi vyāpye ati vyāpteḥ kintu sādhya asamāna adhikaraṇa sādhya abhāva vyāpyaḥ sādhya vat anyonya abhāva vyāpyaḥ vā sādhya abhāva tvam sādhya virodhi tva mātram bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇam tena abhāve sādhye abhāva abhāvasya bhāva tve api na avyāptiḥ abhāva abhāvaḥ abhāva pratiyogi nirūpya tvena bhāva bhinnaḥ eva vā na ca bhāva tvena eva upapattau kim adhikena iti vācyam bādhakam vinā abhāva pratīteḥ pramātvāt anyathā atyanta abhāva anyonya abhāvayoḥ aprasiddhiḥ 
[081,ii]	atha sādhya hetvoḥ virodhe pakṣe sādhya sattve hetu asiddhiḥ hetu sattve sādhya abhāva siddhau bādhaḥ na ca pramāṇa antareṇa sādhya abhāva siddhau bādhaḥ na hetu tvena eva iti vācyam viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyāt iti ced na hetoḥ pakṣe sādhya abhāva bādha anupasthāpane api prathama upasthita virodhasya eva upajīvya tvena doṣa tvāt 
[081,iii]	nanu sādhya abhāva sambandhaḥ vyabhicāraḥ eva doṣaḥ na tu tat niyata tvam api gauravāt asādhaka tve vyartha tvāt ca na ca sādhya asahacaritasya sādhya abhāva sahacaritasya vā gamaka tva bhrama rūpāyām aśaktau viśeṣaḥ asti yena aśakti viśeṣa unnāyaka tayā na vyartha viśeṣaṇa tā na ca anaikāntika sāmānya lakṣaṇe vipakṣa vṛtti tvam na viśeṣaṇam asādhāraṇa ādi avyāpteḥ sādhāraṇantu sa pakṣa vṛtti tva sahitam iti vācyam vipakṣa gāmi tvasya eva sādhāraṇa tvāt adhikasya vyartha tvāt na ca viruddham vyāvartyam vipakṣa gāmi tvena atra eva tad antar bhāvāt 
[081,iv_081,v]	atha anaikāntike vipakṣa sambandhaḥ na dūṣaka tā bījam asādhāraṇa ādi avyāpteḥ na ca tatra anyat eva bījam hetvābhāsa ādhikya āpatteḥ iti ced astu tāvat evam tathā api sādhāraṇe viruddha praveśaḥ vajra lepaḥ eva anye tu viruddha lakṣaṇe na vyartha tvam sādhāraṇasya vyavacchedya tvāt na api asādhaka tā anumitau etasya api vyāpya tvāt nīladhūma ādau ca vyāptiḥ asti eva iti na sva artha anumāne doṣaḥ parasya tu vyartha tvam adhikam na ca viruddha tvāt iti atra śabda ādhikyam iti 
[081,vi]	tat na arthaḥ hi liṅgam na ca vyabhicārauvāraka viśeṣaṇa avacchedena api vyāptiḥ gauravāt iti vakṣyate na ca artha gatyā vyartha tve api viruddha tvāt iti atra udbhāvanā śakyatvam āvaśyaka tad vivecane tad udbhāvanasya śakya tvāt iti hetu dvaya upanyāse ca adhikam prathamena dvitīyasya kṛta kartavya tayā duṣṭa bīja tvāt na ca nīladhūmāt ityādau viśiṣṭa kartavyam anyena kena api kṛtam dhūmavat tvāt iti anena eva kṛtam iti ced na tathā anupanyāsāt anyathā nīlān anvaya āpatteḥ 
[081,vii_081,viii]	apare tu sādhya anavagata sahacāraḥ sādhya abhāva sahacārī viruddhaḥ anyathā pṛthivyām meya tvena itara bheda anumānam na viruddham syāt sādhya abhāva avyāpya tvāt na ca tad sādhāraṇam sa pakṣā sattvāt na ca sādhya sahacāra ajñāna daśāyām sādhāraṇā ativyāptiḥ tadā tasya api viruddha tvāt iti prāhuḥ tat na vipakṣa gāmi tva mātram dūṣaka tā prayojakam iti ukta tvāt atas eva vyabhicaritaḥ vyatirekī anaikāntikaḥ eva na api sādhya abhāva sādhaka tvam tad pramāpaka tvam vā sādhya abhāva sambandha buddhim vinā tad ajñānāt na api sādhya vat anyatva vyāpya tvam vyāpya tva vivecane vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt na api sva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi sādhyaka tvam sādhya abhāvasya hetu vyāpaka tva pratītau hetu sādhya abhāva sambandha bhānasya āvaśyaka tvāt 
[081,ix_081,x]	ucyate sādhya vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam viruddha tvam na ca pratiyoginoḥ ananvaye bhāsā mānaḥ eva tad abhāvayoḥ vyāpti grahaḥ bhinna grāhaka sāmagrīka tvāt anyathā vyatireki vilaya āpatteḥ yat vā vṛttimataḥ sādhya vada vṛtti tvam sādhya vat vṛtti tva anadhikaraṇa tvam sādhya asamāna adhikaraṇa dharma tvam sādhya vat vṛtti tva anadhikaraṇa dharmma tvam vā tattvam na ca vyatireki ati vyāptiḥ tatra sādhya aprasiddhyā tathā jñāna virahāt asādhāraṇe ca saṃkaraḥ eva anena api rūpeṇa tasya doṣa tvāt na ca sādhya vat vṛtti tve sati vṛttimat tva jñānāt sādhya abhāva vat gāmi tva jñānam āvaśyakam tena vinā sādhya vat vṛtti tva ajñānāt iti vācyam upajīvya tvena bhinna tvāt upajīvya tve api sādhyavati na vartate iti jñānam na svatas dūṣakam iti ced na asahacāra jñānasya virodhitayā vyāpti graha pratibandhaka tvāt vyabhicāra ajñāna virodhi tvena vyabhicāra jñāna vat 
[081,xi_081,xii]	nanu viruddhasya sva artha anumāna doṣa tve api para artha anumāne apārthaka tvam ayogya tā jñānena niścitān anvayāt iti ced na ayogya tā jñānasya viruddha tva jñānepa jīvaka tvena tasya eva doṣa tvāt bādhe api evam sa ca ayam vidhi sādhane trividhaḥ sākṣāt sādhya abhāva vyāpya tvāt sādhya vyāpaka abhāva vyāpya tvāt sādhya vyāpaka viruddha upalambhāt yathā dhūmavān ayam yogya dhūmavat tayā anupalabhyamāna tvāt niragnika tvāt jalāśaya tvāt na ca sarvatra sādhya vyāpaka viruddha upalambhaḥ iti na traividhyam etat ajñāne api sādhya abhāva tad vyāpaka abhāva vyāpya tvena api jñātasya doṣa tvāt na ca dhūmavān ayam tat abhāvavat tvāt iti traya adhikam sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva apratiyogi tvam hi vyāpaka tvam tat ca abhede api dhūmavān ayam dhūma abhāvavat tayā upalabhyamāna tvāt tadvat tayā anupalabhyamāna tvāt iti anaikāntikam eva 
[082,i]	niṣedha sādhane api trividhaḥ pratiyogi upalambhāt sādhya vyāpaka abhāva upalambhāt sādhya vyāpaka viruddha upalambhāt yathā niragnikaḥ ayam agnimat tvāt dhūma abhāva śūnya tvāt dhūmavat tvāt sarvaḥ ca ayam viśeṣaṇa dvārā api yathā kṛṣṇa aguru prabhava vahnimānayam kaṭuka asurabhi pāṇḍura dhūmavat tvāt ayañca bādha āśraya asiddha svarūpa asiddha asā dhāraṇa saṅkīrṇaḥ kvacid 
[082,ii_082,iii]	sat pratipakṣa pūrva pakṣaḥ sat pratipakṣa tvam na samāna bala bodhita sādhya viparyaya liṅga tvam paraspara pratibandhena ubhayoḥ abodhaka tvāt balañca na sa pakṣa sattva ādi vyatirekiṇya bhāvāt na api samāna vyāpti pakṣa dharma tāvat tvam virodhena ekatra tad bhaṅga niyamāt na api vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayā jñāta tvam virodhi vyāpti pakṣa dharma viśiṣṭa jñānayoḥ anyatara bhrama tva niyamena nitya tva vyāpta śrāvaṇa tva ādi vaiśiṣṭyā prasiddhyā āropayitum aśakyatvāt na ca sādhya vyāpyasya pakṣa dharma tā pakṣa dharmasya vā sādhya vyāpyatā āropya iti vācyam ekatra tad ubhaya abhāvāt viśiṣṭasya aprasiddhyā tad vaiśiṣṭyasya āropa asambhavāt na api anirdhārita viśeṣeṇa bodhita sādhya viparyayaka tvam ubhayoḥ abodhaka tvāt viśeṣaḥ ca na vyāpti bhaṅga rūpaḥ ekatra tad bhaṅga niyamāt 
[082,iv_082,v]	ucyate sādhya virodhi upasthāpana samartha samāna bala upasthityā pratiruddha kārya liṅga tvam tattvam balañca vyāpti pakṣa dharmate virodhi bodhakāni agamaka taupayika rūpa sampattimat tayā jñāyamānena pratiruddha kārya tvam vā tattvam sthāpanāyāḥ vyāpti pakṣa dharma tvam ubhaya va ādi siddham vādinā tad abhāva anupanyāsāt dvitīyasya tattvam anyatara asiddham iti prathamena dvitīyam bādhitam iti sva artha anumānaḥ eva avaśyam doṣaḥ iti eke 
[082,vi_082,vii]	tat na ekadā nirantarayoḥ vā ubhayoḥ vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayā jñātayoḥ pratipakṣa tvāt yugapad upasthiteḥ kāraṇa vaśena svaparasādhāraṇa tvāt atha vastunaḥ advyātmakattvena vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā bhaṅgaḥ ekatra āvaśyakaḥ iti saḥ eva doṣaḥ na ca tayoḥ virodha bhaṅge api upapatteḥ na vyāpti ādi bhaṅga niyamaḥ iti vācyam avirodhe api anumiti avirodhāt virodhe tu vyāpti ādi bhaṅga niyamāt iti ced na pratiruddha tva jñāna anantaram vyāpti ādi bhaṅga jñānam iti upajīvya tvena vyabhicāra vat asya api doṣa tvāt 
[082,viii]	nanu sādhya tad abhāvayoḥ iva tad vyāpya tvena avadhāritayoḥ virodhāt ekatra na niścayaḥ kintu saṃśayaḥ nirṇaye vā anyatara vyāpti saṃśayaḥ iti vyāpya tva asiddhiḥ iti ced na ubhayoḥ ekatra niścaya anantaram anyatara vyāpti saṃśayaḥ iti upajīvya tvena asya bhinna tvāt dūṣaka tā bījantu sama bala virodhi sāmagrī pratibandhena nirṇaya ājanaka tvam na tu vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā virahaḥ eva sat hetau api sat pratipakṣa tvāt ekatra vyāpti bhaṅga jñāna dvārā vā asya dūṣaka tvam cakṣuḥ ādeḥ ca na anumānena pratirodhaḥ tad upasthitau api phala darśanena tasya adhika bala tvāt
