[082,ix]	nanu evam vādi vākya mātrasya pratirodhaka tvena anumāna mātra ucchedaḥ na ca virodhi vākyasya nyūna bala tve lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ samāna bala tve pratirodhaḥ eva adhika bala tve nara śiraḥ śauca anumāna vat tena bādhaḥ eva iti vācyam agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa daśāyām prativādi vākyena sarva anumāna pratirodha āpatteḥ anumānāt pūrvam paścāt vā anumāna antareṇa tasya nyūna adhika bala tvānirūpaṇāt nirūpaṇe vā anumāna vaiyarthya āpatteḥ 
[082,x_082,xi]	mā evam virodhi vākya mātrasya sama bala tva abhāvāt uktam hi vyāpti pakṣa dharmate balam iti pratyakṣa ādeḥ liṅga bhāvena eva anumiti pratirodhaḥ kathāyām tad upanyāsān arha tvāt yat tu virodhi vyāpya dvayasya asādhāraṇa tvāt saṃśaya janaka tvam dūṣaka tā bījam iti tat na ekaikam hi sat pratipakṣam na tu viśiṣṭam tādṛśañca na saṃśāyakam iti anumiti dvayasya prāmāṇya agrāhaka apravṛttiḥ dūṣaka tā bījam iti anye tat na paraspara pratibandhena anumiteḥ avān utpatteḥ 
[082,xii_083,i]	ratna koṣa kāraḥ tu sat pratipakṣābhyām pratyekam sva sādhya anumitiḥ saṃśaya rūpā janyate viruddha ubhaya jñāna sāmagryāḥ saṃśaya janaka tvāt saṃśaya dvārāḥ asya dūṣaka tvam na ca saṃśaya rūpā na anumitiḥ bādhasya iva virodhi upasthiteḥ anumiti sāmagrauvighaṭaka tvena avaghāraṇāt anyathā bādhe api anumiti āpatteḥ iti vācyam adhika balatayā bādhena pratibandhāt tulya bala tvāt anumitiḥ syāt eva sāmagrī sattvāt sādhya abhāva bodhasya ca tatra pratibandhaka tvam na tu tat bodhakasya cakṣuḥ ādeḥ pratyekam nirṇāyaka tvena avadhāritāt katham saṃśayaḥ iti ced na pratyekāt hi jñānum utpadyamānam arthāt saṃśayaḥ na tu pratyekam saṃśaya janaka tvam iti mene tat na sādhya tad abhāvayoḥ virodhena yathā eka jñānasya apara dhī pratibandhaka tvam tathā sādhya abhāva vyāpyavat tvasya api sādhya virodhi tvāt tat buddheḥ api sādhya dhī pratibandhaka tvāt virodhi jñāna tvasya pratibandhaka tve tantra tvāt 
[083,ii]	nibandhe tu hetvābhāsānām phala dvārakam lakṣaṇam anaikāntikānām anvayāt vyatirekāt vā koṭpī upasthāpaka tayā saṃśayaḥ phalam viruddhasya sādhya viparītasya jñānam apakṣa dharmaḥ api viruddhaḥ anyatra viparīta jñāna samarthaḥ eva bādhe anyatas viparīta jñānam na tu hetu abhimata ādeḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ kārya tvāt iti viruddhe bādha saṅkare api adoṣaḥ asiddhe anaikāntika ādi catuṣṭaya jñānāni aliṅga tva jñānam bādhe pakṣa dharma hetau vyāpti bādhaḥ prakaraṇa same tu na vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā bādhaḥ phalam na api aliḍga tva jñānam vyāpti ādi buddhi sattvāt na api viparīta buddhiḥ sva sādhya viparītena aniyamāt na api saṃśayaḥ pratyekam koṭi dvayān upanayāt kintu katham atra tattva nirṇayaḥ iti jijñāsā phalam 
[083,iii_083,iv]	tathā ca prakṛta sādhya hetvoḥ kim tattvam iti jijñāsā janikā vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā upasthitiḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ na hi anupasthite pratipakṣe ekasmāt jijñāsā kintu nirṇayaḥ eva atha jñātum icchā jijñāsā sā ca jñāna iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt saṃśayāt vā iti katham tena vinā virodhi sādhana jñāna mātrāt iti ced na asati prati pakṣe na jijñāsā sati tu sā iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām prakaraṇa samasya api jijñāsa janaka tvāt na ca anaikāntika ativyāptiḥ tatra hi saṃśaya dvārā sādhye jijñāsā atra tu hetu samīcīnatvaḥ iti 
[083,v]	nanu parāmarśayoḥ eka dā anutpādāt katham pratirodhaḥ krama utpannayoḥ ekadā satvāt iti ced na eka anantaram apara hetu vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā jñānābhyām agrima vyāpti viśiṣṭa jñāna utpatti kāle pūrva parāmarśa nāśāt na ca ubhaya hetu vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā jñānānām paraspara pratibandhāt parāmarśa utpādaḥ iti vācyam vyāpti ādi jñāna catuṣṭayasya yaugapadya abhāvāt 
[083,vi_083,vii]	yat tu vyāpti dvaya saṃskāra udbodhaka hetu dvaya jñānayoḥ paraspara pratibandhāt na ubhaya vyāpti smṛtiḥ iti dūṣaka tā bījam iti tat na vyāpti smṛtim vinā sat pratipakṣa abhāvāt vādibhyām vyāpti udbhāvanāt ca iti mā evam hetu dvaya samūha ālambanāt yugapad ubhaya vyāpti smṛtau ubhaya parāmarśa rūpam jñānam utpadyate atas ekadā viruddha kārya dvaya karaṇāt na ekam api kāryam utpadyate tādṛśa parāmarśaḥ ca sva artha anumāne pratyakṣa āditas parasya tu vādi upanyasta nyāya utthāpita pramāṇa avatārāt 
[083,viii]	asya ca kevala anvayinī api sambhavaḥ ghaṭaḥ abhidheyaḥ prameya tvāt iti atra abhidheya tvam ghaṭa niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi jāti anya tve sati ghaṭa mātra vṛtti anya dharma tvāt ghaṭa anyonya abhāva vat paṭa rūpavat ca ghaṭa niṣṭhā atyanta abhāvaḥ abhidheya tva pratiyogikaḥ ghaṭa vṛtti nitya abhāva tvāt ghaṭa niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva vat iti viśeṣa adarśana daśāyām na ca pakṣa aikyam api tantram virodhasya eva dūṣaka tve adhikasya vyartha tvāt iti 
[083,ix]	asiddhiḥ tu na vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā virahaḥ pratyekam ananugamāt atha pratyeka abhāve anugataḥ vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ asiddhiḥ yadi api viśiṣṭasya anya tve pratyeka abhāvaḥ eva saḥ iti ananugamaḥ tathā api viśeṣaṇa avacchinna pratiyogi kaḥ viśeṣya abhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha abhāvaḥ vā viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ anugataḥ iti ced na viśiṣṭa abhāva ajñāne api vyāpti ādi pratyeka abhāva jñāne udbhāvane ca anumiti pratibandhaḥ vādi nivattiḥ ca iti tad pratyeka abhāva avyāptiḥ anyathā teṣām hetvābhāsa antara tā āpatteḥ na ca viśiṣṭa abhāva dhī dvārā pratyeka abhāvaḥ doṣaḥ na tu svatas iti vācyam pratyeka abhāvasya svatas eva doṣa tva sambhavāt 
[083,x]	vastutas viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ doṣaḥ eva na pratyekasya samartha tve tena eva anyathā siddheḥ vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt pratyeka abhāvam ajñātvā na viśiṣṭa abhāva jñānam iti upajīvya tvāt viśiṣṭa abhāva anudbhāvane api pratyeka udbhāvane vādi nivṛtteḥ ca atas eva vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā viśiṣṭa jñāna viṣaya abhāva tvam pratyeka abhāva anugatam asiddha tvam vyabhicāra ādau asiddha tve api upajīvya tvena prāthamyāt tad udbhāvane vādi nivṛtteḥ ca sa svatas eva dūṣakaḥ tatra vyāpti siddhi artham upādhau tu udbhāvite vipratipadyate api tasya durūha tvāt vyabhicāreṇa eva tad anvayāt ca 
[083,xi_083,xiii]	yadi ca vyabhicāra ādikam ajñā tvā api asiddhi buddhiḥ tathā api upadheya saṅkare api upādheḥ asaṅkaraḥ eva iti nirastam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt eva etena vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā anyatara abhāvaḥ asiddhiḥ iti pratyuktam anyataratva ajñāne api pratyeka abhāvasya doṣa tvāt vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca yat tu vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā pramiti virahaḥ āśraya asiddhyā anugataḥ asiddhiḥ tad pramiti sattve tatra anumiti pramiti āpatteḥ iti tat api vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt tad ajñāne api pratyeka jñānasya doṣa tvāt ca nirastam 
[084,i]	vastutas tu prakṛta hetu vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā vaiśiṣṭyasya tad pramiteḥ ca aprasiddhyā tad abhāvaḥ jñātum udbhāvayituñcā śakyaḥ eva yat kiñci dvyāpti pakṣa dharma tā viśiṣṭa pramiti virahaḥ sat hetu sādhāraṇaḥ sva pramiti virahaḥ yat kiñcit pramiti virahaḥ vā sat hetau api sakala tad pramiti virahaḥ dūrni rūpaḥ vyātya bhāvāt eva tad grahe saḥ eva doṣaḥ upajīvya tvāt yadi ca pramiti virahaḥ svarūpa sannā iva doṣaḥ kāraṇa abhāva tvāt tadā vyāpti ādi bhramāt anumitiḥ na syāt na syāt ca hetvābhāsa tā jñāna garbha tallakṣaṇa abhāvāt 
[084,ii_084,iii]	etena vyāpti pramiti pakṣa dharma tā pramiti viraha anyatara tvam asiddhiḥ anyatara tvat ca tad anya anya tvam tena ubhaya virahe api na avyāptiḥ iti nirastam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt eva syāt etat vyāpti pakṣa dharma tābhyām niścayaḥ siddhiḥ tad abhāvaḥ asiddhiḥ atas eva avyāpte apakṣa dharme ca tadāropa rūpā siddhiḥ iti anumitiḥ na tu vyāpta pakṣa dharmāt api tat aniścaye na ca evam hetoḥ api ābhāsa tvam tad ābhāsasya api hetu tvam syāt daśā viśeṣe iṣṭa tvāt sā iyam svarūpa satī dūṣikā kāraṇa abhāva tvāt na ca vyāpti ādi pratyeka niścaya abhāvaḥ eva dūṣakaḥ āvaśyaka tvāt iti vācyam viśiṣṭa niścayasya hetu tve tad abhāvasya kārya anutpādaka tvāt iti 
[084,iv]	mā evam evam savyabhicāra ādeḥ api atra eva antarbhāva prasaṅgāt asiddheḥ svarūpa satyāḥ eva doṣa tve sva jñāna artham vyabhicāra ādi anudbhāvanāt yadi ca tasmāt siddhiḥ na upapadyate iti tasya upajīvya tvam tad āśrayā siddhi ādi jñānāt siddhiḥ na iti saḥ eva pṛthak doṣaḥ syāt asiddhiḥ ca jñātā parasya udbhāvyā iti sva jñāna artham udbhāvitā siddhi nirvāha arthañcā āśrayā siddhi jñānam āvaśyakam kathañca hetu tad ābhāsa vivekaḥ siddhau dvayoḥ api hetu tvāt asiddhau tad ābhāsa tvāt vyabhicāra ādeḥ sat hetau siddhim akhaṇḍayataḥ ca hetvābhāsa tva abhāvāt 
[084,v]	atha suṣuptau jāgare api vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā sattve tat aniścaye anumiti anutpādaḥ hetvābhāsa prayojyaḥ savyabhicāra ādau tathā avadhāraṇa āditya siddhiḥ ajñātā api hetvābhāsaḥ na ca evam hetvābhāsa ādhikyam kḷpta antarbhāvaḥ vā tena rūpeṇa vyāpti asiddhi ādeḥ eva saṃgrahāt iti ced na evam savyabhicāra ādiḥ api asiddhiḥ syāt iti ukta tvāt upajīvanāt bhede āśraya asiddhi ādiḥ api pṛthak syāt suṣapti ādau anumiti abhāvaḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya anutpādaḥ hi na pratibandhaka tvāt kintu kāraṇa abhāvāt api asati api pratibandhake vahni abhāvena dāha an utpatteḥ 
[084,vi_084,viii]	atha anum iti anutpādaḥ hetvābhāsa pratyuktaḥ eva iti ced tarhi anumitau manaḥ yoga ādiḥ api na hetuḥ hetvābhāsāt eva anumiti anutpāde tad vyatirekeṇa anumiti anutpāda abhāvāt siddheḥ eva tad hetu tve carama kāraṇam eva hetuḥ syāt anye tu gamakataupayika pratidvandvi vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā viraha tad niyatayoḥ anyatara tvam hetvābhāsa tvam tatra adhika samāna balau bādha pratirodhau pratidvandvinau vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā virahaḥ ca asiddhiḥ tat niyatau ca savyabhicāra viruddhau na ca anayoḥ api asiddhi antarbhāvaḥ vyāpti viraha niyata tvena jñātayoḥ svātantryeṇa eva dūṣaka tvāt bhrame viśeṣa darśanasya eva iti tat na atra api vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā virahaḥ eva asiddhiḥ paryavasyati tatra ca uktam eva anyatara tvañca na lakṣaṇam vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt hetvābhāsa antara bahiṣkṛtasya vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā niścaya virodhinaḥ rūpasya vivakṣita tvāt tat ca āśraya asiddhi ādikam eva iti 
[084,ix]	ucyate āśraya asiddhiḥ svarūpa asiddhiḥ vyāpya tva asiddhiḥ ca pratyekam eva doṣaḥ pratyekasya jñānāt udbhāvanāt ca anumiti pratibandhāt na tu viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ parāmarśa viṣaya abhāvaḥ vā vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt tasya jñānam udbhāvanam vinā api anumiti pratibandhāt anubhava siddham hi lakṣaṇam na tu lakṣaṇa anurodhena anubhava kalpanā parāmarśa viṣaya abhāva tvena anugatena trayāṇām asiddha tvena saṃgrahaḥ mahā ṛṣiṇā kṛtaḥ iti na vibhāga virodhaḥ hetvābhāsa ādhikyam vā 
[084,x]	atas eva ye vyāpti viraha pakṣa dharma tā viraha rūpāḥ te asiddhi bheda madhyam adhyāsate tad anye ca yathāyatham vyabhicāra ādayaḥ iti siddhānta pravādaḥ api na ca evam sākṣāt pratibandhaka tvena bādha pratirodhayoḥ vyāpti viraha liṅga tvena savyabhicāra viruddhayoḥ api saṅgrahe vibhāga vyāghātaḥ svatantra abhiprāyasya niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt anyathā śāstre paribhāṣā ucchet āpatteḥ savyabhicāra ādeḥ api evam rūpa sattve api upajīvya tvena pṛthaktvam upadheya saṅkare api upādheḥ asaṅkarāt 
[084,xi_084,xii]	nanu āśraya aprasiddhyā katham āśrayā siddhiḥ udbhāvyā na ca śaśīyatayā gavi śrṛḍganiṣedha vat vyoma kamalam iti vācyam śaśaśrṛṅga niṣedhaḥ na gavīti ukta tvāt iti ced vyoma kamalam iti niścitān anvaya tvena apārthakam āśraya viśeṣaṇā siddhyā ca āśraya asiddhiḥ asaṅkīrṇā vyāpti virahaḥ ca vyartha viśeṣaṇa ādau tad uktam ekāma siddhim pariharataḥ dvitīya āpatteḥ iti 
[085,i_085,ii]	upādhiḥ tu na vyāpti virahaḥ vahni vyāpaka dhūma avyāpaka dharmasya aprasiddhyā dhūme tad viraha asiddheḥ kintu yāvat sva vyabhicāri vyabhicāri sādhya sāmāna adhikarapyam anaupādhika tvam vyāptiḥ sādhya vyāpaka sādhana avyāpakaḥ ca dharma antaram na tu tad virahaḥ api tu tat niyataḥ na ca evam upajīvya tvena upādhiḥ hetvābhāsa antaram upajīvya tve api svatas adūṣaka tvena tad artham para mukha vīkṣaka tvāt na hi sādhya vyāpaka avyāpya tvam anumiti virodhi kintu vyabhicāra unnayanena sva vyatirekeṇa sat pratipakṣa tayā vā tat āha upādhau avaśyam vyabhicāraḥ upādheḥ eva vyabhicāra śaṅkā iti aprayojakān yathā siddhau sa upādhī na asiddhau pratikūla tarka anukūla tarka abhāvau upajīvya tve sati svatas dūṣakau api na hetvābhāsau sva rūpa satoreva pratibandhaka tvāt iti uktam 
[085,iii_085,iv]	bādhaḥ na sādhya abhāva vat pakṣaka tvam pakṣa vṛtti abhāva pratiyogi sādhyaka tvam vā pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñāna mātrasya pramātu a jñānam vinā adhika bala tva ajñānena bādhā bhāvāt iti vakṣyate atas eva sādhya abhāva vat pakṣa vṛtti tvam api na asiddhi saṅkīrṇa bādha avyāpteḥ ca kintu sādhya abhāvavat tva pramā viṣaya pakṣaka tvam pramita sādhya abhāva vat pakṣaka tvam pakṣa niṣṭha pramāviṣayatva prakāra abhāva pratiyogi sādhyaka tvam vā iti vivakṣita vivekena sādhya abhāva ādi pramā eva doṣaḥ sā ca pramātvena jñātā na svarūpa satī hetvābhāsa tvāt pramātu ajñānam vinā adhika bala tva abhāvena adoṣa tvāt apramāyām api pramātu a jñāne anumiti pratibandhāt ca 
[085,v]	atha sādhya abhāvavati pakṣe hetoḥ sattva jñāne vyabhicāraḥ tad ajñāne asiddhiḥ saṃśaya yogya tva abhāvena pakṣa tva abhāvāt āśrayā siddhiḥ ca na ca pakṣa bhinne vyabhicāraḥ doṣaḥ vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt sarva upasaṃhāra pravṛtta vyāpteḥ sādhya abhāvavati sādhanam iti avagamāt eva bhaṅgāt na ca evam sandigdha sādhya dṛṣṭānte sandigdha anaikāntika vat pakṣe vyabhicāra saṃśayāt anumāna mātra ucchedaḥ iti pakṣe sādhya sandehaḥ anumāna aṅgam iti vyāptasya pakṣa dharma tā jñānāt anum iti utpādena saṃśaya nivṛtteḥ anyathā viśeṣa darśanasya saṃśaya virodhitā bhajyeta na ca pakṣe sādhya abhāvam pratītya vyabhicāra jñānam iti upajīvya tvāt bādhaḥ pṛthak pakṣe sādhya abhāva pratītiḥ eva hi sādhya abhāva hetvoḥ sambandha ullekhinī iti eka vitti vedya tvena na upajīvya tvam anyathā bādha daśāyām pakṣe hetoḥ ajñāna da siddhiḥ eva 
[085,vi]	na ca udbhāvita vyabhicāra nirvāhāya bādha udbhāvanam āvaśyakam iti upajīvya tvam vyabhicāra udbhāvane param kathantān āvaśyaka tvāt tattve vā tat nirvāhyam eva dūṣaṇam kḷpta tvāt vahniḥ uṣṇaḥ kṛtakaḥ iti udbhāvanāt vahniḥ uṣṇaḥ iti udbhāvane lāghavam iti bādhaḥ pṛthak iti kaścid tat na pakṣe sādhya abhāva pramā sva artha anumāne yadi na doṣaḥ tadā pratyapi na syāt aviśeṣāt iti tad udbhāvanasya dūra nirasta tvāt 
[085,vii]	atha upanīta kāñcana maya tva viśiṣṭa vahni anumiteḥ sat liṅga janyāyāḥ ābhāsattvam hetvābhāsa adhīnam na ca anumiteḥ pūrvam tatra vyabhicāra jñānam viśiṣṭasya aprasiddhyā tad abhāvasya ajñānāt atas eva pakṣa asiddhiḥ api na atas kāñcana maya vahni abhāva rūpāt bādhāt anumāna ābhāsa tvam vyadhikaraṇa prakāra avacchinna pratiyogikaḥ ca atra abhāvaḥ iti ced na vastutas vyabhicārasya api tatra sattvāt jñānañca tasya bādhasi eva anum iti anantaram eva kiñca vahnau kāñcana maya tvasya anumitau eva bhāne kāñcana maya vahnimān itya numitiḥ na syāt viśiṣṭasya pūrvam ajñānāt vahnau liṅgasya asiddheḥ vyabhicārāt ca na ca anumiteḥ viṣaya abhāva adhīna pramātvam kintu hetvābhāsa adhīnam yasya hi jñānam anumiti pratibandhakam sa hetvābhāsaḥ na ca sādhya abhāvaḥ jñātaḥ pratibandhakaḥ iti na saḥ hetvābhāsaḥ 
[085,viii]	vastutas tu upanītasya anumitau bhāne māna abhāvaḥ pratyabhijñā ādau ca pratīti balena tad kalpanam anyathā pūrva upasthita sakala padārtha bhāne yathārtha anum iti ucchedaḥ api caivam para artha anumāne api upanīta bhāne bādhitaḥ arthaḥ upanītaḥ ayam mama bhātaḥ iti udbhāvanāt eva vijayeta vādī uddeśya anumiteḥ apratibandhāt na tatra bādhaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced tulyam sva artha anumāne api atas eva yatra sāmānyatas dṛṣṭa anumānam eva itara bādha sahāyam viśeṣa anumāpakam tatra bādhakānām ābhāsa tve tat prayuktam sāmānyasya adṛṣṭā api ābhāsa tvam iti bādhasyāsāṅkaryāt na ca yadi viśeṣa vipratipattau sāmānya pratijñā tadā artha antaram sāmānya vipratipattau tu na itaratra bādhaka apekṣā iti vācyam sva artha anumānaḥ eva evam bādhā saṅkarasya ukta tvāt iti a pāstam anumityapratibandhena tatra bādhasya adoṣa tvāt 
[085,ix]	nanu pakṣe sādhya abhāva graha vat sādhya abhāva vyāpya grahaḥ api dūṣakaḥ virodhi tvā aviśeṣāt tathā ca sādhya abhāva sambandhaḥ vyabhicāraḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpya sāmānādhikaraṇyam bādhaḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpyañca vahni tva ādikam eva iti ced na pakṣe hi sādhya abhāve jñāyamāne jñāte vā yadi sādhya abhāva vyāpya sāmāna adhikaraṇya buddhiḥ tadā vyabhicāraḥ eva 
[085,x]	atha pakṣe sādhya abhāva buddhim vinā eva sā tarhi hetu sādhya abhāva vyāpyayoḥ agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣayoḥ sat pratipakṣa tvam atha tulya balena sat pratipakṣaḥ adhika balena bādhaḥ iti ced na gamakataupayika rūpa sākalyam hi balam tat ca dvayoḥ jñātam iti katham na sat pratipakṣa tvam gamaka tā bahis bhū tañca na balam atha sādhya abhāva vyāpya buddheḥ anyathā siddha tvam balam tadā tatas sādhanavati pakṣe sādhya abhāva anumitau anaikāntika tvam eva pakṣe sādhya abhāva graha vat iti yat uktam tat api asiddham tasya doṣa tva anabhyupagamāt anyathā hetvābhāsa antara tā āpattiḥ 
[085,xi]	atha hetutaḥ sādhya siddhi sambhā vanāyām vyabhicāra asiddheḥ bādhena hetoḥ asādhaka tve siddhe vyabhicāra siddhiḥ iti upajīvya tvāt bādhaḥ pṛthak anyathā hetoḥ asādhaka tve siddhe sādhya siddhi sambhāvanā virahāt vyabhicāra buddhiḥ tasya añca satyām hetoḥ asādhaka tva dhīḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ iti ced na sādhya siddhi unmukha hetu jñānasya pramita sādhya abhāva sahacarita hetu viṣaya tvena vyabhicāra jñāna tayā adūṣaka tvāt tathā api vyabhicāre sādhya abhāva pramā tantram tām vinā tad abhāvāt iti sā eva doṣaḥ iti ced satyam kintu sādhya abhāva pramā vyabhicāra jñāna tvena dūṣikā kḷpta tvāt na tu svatantrā atas eva pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñāna tvena pratibandhaka tvam na tu sādhya abhāva samāna adhikaraṇa sādhana jñāna tvena iti pratyuktam tasya laghu tve api akḷpta tvāt 
[086,i]	atha pratyakṣa ādau pramā mātram prati svātantryeṇa bādhaḥ doṣa tvena kḷptaḥ iti anumitau api saḥ eva doṣaḥ iti ced na tarhi hetvābhāsaḥ anumiti asādhāraṇa doṣasya tatvāt manaḥ yoga abhava vat svarūpa satas eva pratibandhaka tvāt hetu tva abhimatā vṛtti tvena asādhaka tā āliṅga tva abhāvāt ca bādhita pakṣaka tvam liṅgam iti ced na anyatra tathā dūṣaka tva akalpanāt 
[086,ii]	ucyate pakṣe sādhya abhāva niścayaḥ sādhya abhāva jñāna pramātu a niścayāt jñāna mātrāt artha niścaye prāmāṇya graha vaiyarthyam bhrama tvena jñātāt artha niścaya prasaṅgaḥ ca tathā ca upajīvya tvena adhika bala tvena vā pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñānasya pramātu a niścaye savyabhicāraḥ na anyathā iti ubhayathā api sādhya abhāva niścaya adhīna vyabhicāra jñānāt pūrvam jñātam sādhya abhāva jñāna pramātvam eva doṣaḥ upajīvya tvāt 
[086,iii]	yadi ca pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñānasya pramātva niścayaḥ na anumiti virodhī tadā vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayā hetu jñānam viśeṣa darśana tvena pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñānam paribhūya sādhyam sādhayet eva parvate dhūmaḥ iva vahnim na ca sādhya abhāva buddhiḥ eva agṛhyamāṇa viśeṣā sat pratipakṣa vat pratibandhika iti vācyam rajate na idam rajatam iti jñāne api viśeṣa darśanena rajata tvasya śaṅkhe pīta tva jñāne śukla tvasya ca anumānāt vādi vākyena pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñānāt anumāna uccheda prasaḍgāt ca atha pakṣe sādhya abhāva pramā eva sādhya abhāva hetu viṣayāḥ vyabhicāra jñāna tvena doṣaḥ na tu tasyāḥ pramātu ajñānam api iti ced tarhi pramāyāḥ apramātu a jñāne bhrānta anumitiḥ na syāt na syāt ca pakṣe sādhya abhāva jñāna pramātu a bhramāt anumiti pratibandhaḥ 
[086,iv]	nanūpa jīvya tve api atra sādhya abhāva pramā iti jñānam na svatas dūṣakam kḷpta tvāt pakṣe sādhya abhāva niścayam kurvat vyabhicāra jñāna dvārā iti ced na atra sādhya abhāva pramā iti jñānāt niyamataḥ sādhya jñāna anudayāt tasya eva pratibandhaka tvāt śabda ādau tathā darśanāt sādhya abhāva pramā viṣaya vṛtti tvasya hetu vṛtti tvāt asādhaka tvena sādhya abhāva pramāyā hetvābhāsa tvam sādhāraṇye api jñāyamānam sat yat anumitim pratibadhnāti tasya eva hetvābhāsa tvam na ca sādhya abhāva pramātrā iti niścaya daśāyām pakṣe sādhya abhāva hetvoḥ jñānāt vyabhicāraḥ iti vācyam pramātu ajñānasya sādhya abhāva niścaya hetu tvena tad daśāyām tad abhāvāt pakṣa dharma tā balena prasiddham bādhāt na sidhyati iti bādhaḥ pṛthak prasiddhā abhāvavati pakṣe vyabhicārāt na tad siddhiḥ iti ced tarhi asat prasiddhā abhāvavati sa pakṣe vyabhicārāt tam api na sādhayet tad ajñānāt tad sādhane anumitiḥ apramā syāt 
[086,v]	atha pakṣa vṛtteḥ anyaḥ eva dhūma ādiḥ sa pakṣe tarhi go tva pṛthivī tva dravya tva ādeḥ aprasiddha sāsnā ādi anumānam na syāt sāsnādi pratyeka vyabhicārāt yadi ca sādhya tāvacchedaka sāsnā tva ādi sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogitākā abhāvavati na go tva ādikam iti na vyabhicāraḥ tarhi dhūme api evam vyabhicāra abhāvāt sādhya tāvacchedakena prakāreṇa aprasiddham iva prasiddham api sādhyam dhūma go tva ādikam sādhayet yadi bādhaḥ na doṣaḥ iti vayam sādhya abhāvavat mātra sahacāraḥ na vyabhicāraḥ sādhya prāgabhāva dhvaṃsa vat vṛtti tvena vyabhicāritayā pṛthivī tva ādinā gandha ādeḥ dravya tva ādinā guṇasya anumāna bhaṅga prasaṅgāt kintu sādhya atyanta abhāva vat gāmi tvam evañca sva prāgabhāva dhvaṃsā avacchinna tad āśraye tad pratiyogi sādhane pakṣe vyabhicāraḥ na iti bādhaḥ dūṣaṇam 
[086,vi^1]	atha avacchedye siddha sādhanam avacchedake hetu asiddhiḥ viśiṣṭañca na anyat iti ced tarhi prāc abhāva dhvaṃsa pratiyoginoḥ eka vṛtti tvena eka samayatā api syāt atha yat samayā avacchedena tatra prāc abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ vā na tad samaya avacchedena pratiyogi iti ced tarhi tad avacchedena pratiyogi sādhane na siddha sādhanam kintu bādhaḥ eva anyathā bhāva atyanta abhāvayoḥ api avyāpya vṛtti tva bhaṅgaḥ eka vṛtti tvāt avacchedaka bhedena vṛttiḥ iha api tulyā tatra deśa bhedaḥ avacchedakaḥ atra tu samaya bhedaḥ iti asiddheḥ api bādhaḥ eva upajīvyaḥ na ca evam upajīvya tvāt bādhavat siddha sādhanam api pṛthak upajīvyatvepi svatas adūṣaka tvāt na hi sādhya jñānam tat buddhi virodhi 
[086,vi^2]	dhārāvāhika jñāna udayāt na api anumiti virodhi anumitsayā pratyakṣa siddhe api anumāna darśanāt tad uktam pratyakṣa dṛṣṭam api anumānena bubhutsante tarkarasikāḥ iti śravaṇa anantaram manana darśanāt ca tasmāt siddhi mātra arthinaḥ siddhau na tad icchā siddhi viśeṣa arthinaḥ sā asti iti tasya anumitiḥ eva evañca siṣā dhayiṣita vighaṭana dvārā siddha sādhanam dūṣaṇam na tu svatas 
[086,vii]	nanu abhāva dhīḥ api na bhāva dhī pratibandhikā na idam rajatam iti bhrama anantaram rajata niścayāt naca abhāva pramā tathā api itaḥ śaṅkhaḥ iti pramāpayataḥ eva pītaḥ ayam iti bhrama darśanāt iti ced na virodhi jñānam hi pratibandhakam pratyakṣa bhramasya pratyakṣa pramā virodhinī sā ca śaṅkha ādau doṣāt na asti eva anumitau tu abhāva pramā mātram eva virodhi iti katham abhāva pramāyām bhāva anumitiḥ iti 
[086,viii]	sa ca ayam daśavidhaḥ dharma grāhaka māna bādhitam ghaṭaḥ avyāpakaḥ sattvāt iti pratyakṣeṇa paramāṇavaḥ sa avayavāḥ mūrta tvāt iti anumānena meruḥ pāṣāṇa mayaḥ parvata tvāt iti suvarṇa maya tva bodhaka āgamena sādhya pratiyogi grāhaka bādhitam vahniḥ anuṣṇaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti pratyakṣeṇa śabdaḥ aśrāvaṇaḥ guṇa tvāt iti anumānena gavaya tvam gavaya pada apravṛtti nimittam jāti tvāt iti upamānena sādhya grāhaka bādhitam śuci nara śiraḥ kapālam prāṇi aṅga tvāt iti atra āgamena hetu grāhaka bādhitam jala anilau uṣṇau pṛthivītas viparīta sparśava tvāt tejaḥ vat iti pratyakṣeṇa manaḥ vibhu jñāna sama vāyi ādhāra tvāt iti anumānena rājasūyam brāhmaṇa kartavyam svarga sādhana tvāt agniṣṭoma vat iti rājasūya kartavyatā bodhaka āgamena iti 
[087,i]	atha hetvābhāsānām asādhaka tā sādhaka tvena sat uttara tvam jāti ādīnāñcāsādhaka tā sādha araṇyena parāsādhaka tā sādhaka tayā sva vyāghātaka tvāt asat uttarattvam atha viruddha tva ādi jñānāt eva sva artha anumitiḥ iva para artha anumiteḥ api pratibandhe kim asādhaka tā anumānena yat vacasi vādi ukta dūṣaṇa avagatiḥ sa nigṛhītaḥ iti samaya bandhena kathā pravṛttau dūṣaṇa mātram udbhāvyam anyathārtha antara tvāt iti ced na dvayam
[087,ii]	hi uddeśyam para artha anumiti pratibandhaḥ sthāpanāyāḥ asādhaka tā sādhanatvañca tatra ādyam dūṣaṇa mātra jñānāt eva dvitīyantu liṅga tva jñāpanāt pratibandhaka tva vadanena api rūpeṇa dūṣaka tva sambhavaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa vā asādhaka tā sādhanam nanu evam pañca avaya prayoga apekṣā syāt anyathā nyūna tā āpattiḥ iti ced na dūṣaṇasya asādhaka tā vyāpya tvam aṅgīkṛtya kathā iti tad pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ eva udbhāvya tvāt anyathā adhika tva āpatteḥ 
[087,iii]	nanu evam kṛtaka tvena anitya tva anumāne api vyāptiḥ na abhidheyā ubhaya siddha tvāt iti ced na kathāyām samaya viṣaya tayā dūṣaṇe tu asādhaka tā vyāpti upasthiteḥ āvaśyaka tvāt anyathā kathakatva virodhāt nanu evam kṛtaka tvena anumāne tad vyāptim anaṅgīkṛtya api kathā sambhavāt yaḥ tu kathā ārambhe bādhasya asādhaka tva vyāptim na aṅgīkaroti tam prati tad dūṣaka tvam prasādhya pañca avayava prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ eva 
[087,iv]	yat tu dūṣaṇe pakṣa dharma tā mātram udbhāvyam tatra yatra vādinoḥ tathā samayaḥ anyatra tu pañcau ava prayogaḥ eva iti tat na kathā sampradāya virodhāt atha asādhaka tvam na pakṣe sādhya pratyaya ājanaka tvam tena api tattvena ajñāna daśāyām pakṣe sādhya bhrama jananāt kadācid ajanaka tvam sat hetau api nanu etat kāle sādhya viśiṣṭa pakṣa jñāna ajanakam tat na hi dūṣaṇa tva jñāna daśāyām pakṣe bhrama rūpā api anumitiḥ sādhya viśiṣṭa pakṣa jñānañca hatu tvena jñāna daśāyām prasiddham iti ced na sat hetau asat pratipakṣa tāt aśa ayam api pūrva kāle sādhya viśiṣṭa pakṣa jñāna ajanaka tvam asti iti asādhaka tā prasaṅgāt 
[087,v]	atha pakṣe sādhya bhrama janaka tvam tat bādha viruddhayoḥ api tattva ajñāna daśāyām bhrama janaka tvāt iti ced na sat hetau sat pratipakṣe asādhāraṇe ca tattvena jñāna daśāyām sādhya bhrama janaka tvāt ajñāne sādhya pramājanaka tvāt na api vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā anyatara rāhityam sat pratipakṣa asā dhāraṇa sadhetoḥ a bhāvāt daśā viśeṣe tasya doṣa tvāt sādhya aprasiddhau prakṛta sādhya vyāptya prasiddheḥ ca na api anaikāntika ādi anyam atvam yat kiñcid anaikāntika tvasya ati vyāpteḥ prakṛta sādhya anaikāntika tvasya aprasiddha tvena kevala anvayi sādhane aprasiddheḥ aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanāt sādhya aviśeṣāt ca 
[087,vi]	yat tu etad kālīna etat pakṣīyatva avacchinna pratiyogika etad sādhya pramākaraṇa tva abhāvaḥ tad takāla tad tad pakṣa viṣaya sādhya tva abhimata anitya tva ādi pramā janaka tva abhāvaḥ vā asādhaka tvam na ca pratiyogi aprasiddhiḥ etad kālīnaitpakṣīyatva tad tad kāla tad tad pakṣa viṣaya tvayoḥ vyadhikaraṇayoḥ eva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka tvāt iti tat na sat hetoḥ sat pratipakṣatva ajñāna daśāyām api tādṛśa pramāyāma karaṇa bhāvena asādhaka tā āpatteḥ na api tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśasya apramā tvam tat viruddha ādau parāmarśa abhāvāt sat hetau sat pratipakṣe asādhāraṇe ca tat pramātvāt ca na api anumiti hetu bhūta abhāva pratiyogi jñāna viṣaya tvam tat sat hetau api kadācid vyabhicāritu a sat pratipakṣa tva jñānasya anumiti pratibandhaka tvāt 
[087,vii]	atha anumiti pratibandhaka pramāviṣaya tvam asādhaka tvam sat hetau vyabhicāra ādi bhramaḥ pratibandhakaḥ anumiti pratibandhaka tvañca vyabhicāra ādi pramāyāḥ tṛtīya liṅga parāmarśa vighaṭana dvārā tulya balatayā viṣaya tayā vā iti ced na sat pratipakṣayoḥ viruddhayoḥ vāstava tulya bala tva abhāvena tat bhramasya pratibandhaka tvāt na ca tulya balatayā jñāyamānena bodhita sādhya viparyaka tva jñānam pratibandhakam tat ca pramā eva iti vācyam tulya bala tā jñānam eva hi pratibandhakam na tu jñāyamāna tva jñānam gauravāt asiddheḥ ca na ca sat pratipakṣe anyatara aṅga vaikalya pramā eva pratibandhika iti vācyam anyatara tvam tat atad vṛtti na ca tad atad vṛtti sāmāna adhikaraṇyena jñāyamānasya doṣa tvam dharma mātrasya vyabhicāra jñānāt anum iti uccheda āpatteḥ anyatara aṅga vaikalya jñāna upajīvyasya tulya bala tva jñānasya eva pratibandhaka tvāt ca anyathā vyāpya tva asiddhi antarbhāva āpatteḥ 
[087,viii]	atha anaikāntika ādi jñānasya tad tad anumiti pratibandhaka tvam asādhaka tvam tathā hi idam anaikāntika ādi jñānam etat sādhyavat tayā etat puruṣasya etad kālīna etat pakṣaka anumiti pratibandhakam etat anaikāntika ādi jñāna tvāt etad anya tat jñāna vat iti ced na etat sādhya vat tayā etat pakṣaka anumiteḥ kadācid liṅga bhramāt prasiddhau api etat kālīna etat puruṣasya tādṛśa anumiti aprasiddheḥ na api samīcīn asādhya viśiṣṭa pakṣa viṣaya anumiti ajanaka tvam bādha viruddha asiddheṣu sādhya an adhikaraṇe pakṣe satyasādhya pratītya prasiddheḥ vahnimati bāṣpe dhūma bhramāt vahni anumiteḥ satya tvāt ca na ca anyaḥ eva vahniḥ tatra bhāsate māna abhāvāt tad vahneḥ pratyabhijñānāt eka vyaktike tad asambhavāt ca na ca sa anumitiḥ liṅga viṣaya tvena bhramaḥ anumitau liṅga bhāne māna abhāvāt 
[087,ix]	kiñca bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā ubhayathā api prameyam iti satya anumitau bhāva tva abhāva tvavati prameya tva jñāne ekatra tayoḥ abhāvāt asatya anumitiḥ syāt na ca anyatara tvam liṅgam tad vyāptim aviduṣaḥ api anumiteḥ vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca atha sādhya vyāpya tvam eva tatra tantram tatra ca bādhaḥ na asti iti ced tarhi kūṭa liṅgāt anumitau vahni vyāpyavat tvam eva tantram vahni vyāpyañca kiñcid tatra asti eva atha kūṭa liṅge vahni vyāpya abheda pratīyate vahnau kūṭa liṅga vyāpakā bhedaḥ api anyathā kūṭasya eva vahni vyāpyatva apratīteḥ evañca kūṭa liṅga vyāpakaḥ vahni tvena bhāsate iti vahni anumitiḥ asatyā eva iti ced 
[087,x_087,xi]	na vahni vyāpya āloke dhūma āropāt yatra anumitiḥ tatra asiddhi bhede asatya tva abhāva āpatteḥ āloka vyāpake dhūma vyāpaka abhedāt atha liṅgam anumiti viṣayaḥ niyamataḥ pakṣa dharma tā jñāna viṣaya tvāt vyāpti jñāna viṣaya tvāt niyamena anumiti hetu viśeṣaṇa dhī viṣaya tvāt ca parvata tva vat sādhya vat ca kiñca eka viśeṣaṇava tvena jñāte viśeṣaṇa antara dhī sāmagrī tatra eva viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭyā anumitiḥ iti dhūma viśiṣṭaḥ eva vahni vaiśiṣṭya anumitiḥ iti nanu anumitau vyāpaka tva bhāne anumiti avicchedaḥ na ca phalībhūta jñāna nyūna viṣayasya eva parāmarśasya anumiti hetu tvam gauravāt viṣaya antara sañcārāt na anumitiḥ iti api na parāmarśasya carama kāraṇa tvāt pratyakṣa ādi sāmagrītaḥ balavat tvāt ca iti ced na siddha sādhanena vicchedāt 
[088,i]	yadi api evam liṅga aṃśe apramātve api sādhya pramātvāt katham tasya asādhaka tvam tathā api ukta sādhaka tvam asti eva iti ced astu tāvat evam tathā api daivāt tatra dhūma sattve katham taṃdeśe api asatya tā atas eva ārdra indhana prabhavaḥ vahniḥ dhūma vyāpakaḥ na anyaḥ na ca vahni tvena vyāpaka tvāt anyaḥ api tathā tena vinā api dhūma sattvāt evam bāṣpe dhūma bhramāt dhūma vyāpakaḥ vahniḥ bhāsate sa ca tatra na asti eva iti na sa anumitiḥ satyā iti nirastam daivāt dhūma sattve satya tvāt iti 
[088,ii]	ucyate sva jñāna daśāyām pakṣe sādhya pratyaya ājanaka tvam asādhaka tvam tathā hi viruddha tva ādi jñānadaśāvartī idam pakṣe sādhya pratyaya ajanakam viruddha ādi tvāt pakṣa viśeṣaṇa mahimnā tad haśāyām pakṣe sādhya pratyaya ājanaka tvam siddhyati bādhita ādau api liṅga tva bhramāt pakṣe sādhya pratyaya janaka tvam iti na pratiyogi aprasiddhyā sādhya aprasiddhiḥ yat vā anumiti pratibandhaka tāvacchedaka rūpavat tvam asādhaka tvam tathā ahi idānīm idam anumiti pratibandhaka tāvacchedaka rūpa vat anaikāntika ādi tvāt jñāna vat anumiti pratibandhaka tāvaccheda kañca rūpam jñāne viṣaya tayā anaikāntika ādi tvam eva na ca sādhya aviśeṣaḥ upādhi viśeṣasya anumeya tvāt toya tvena pipāsā upaśamana samartha tāvacchedaka rūpa ratva anumāna vat 
[088,iii]	anye tu anaikāntika bādhita viruddheṣu avyāpya tvam vyāpya tva asiddhe anaikāntika tvam svarūpa asiddha sat pratipakṣa asā dhāraṇeṣu daśa aviśeṣe anumiti pratibandhaka jñāna viṣaya tvam asādhaka tvam na ca evam anaikāntikaḥ asādhakaḥ iti saha prayoga anupapattiḥ tatra avyāpya tvasya asādhaka śabda artha tvāt asādhaka tānanugamepi ca hetvābhāsa tvam anugatam eva yasya jñānam anumiti pratibandhakam tasya hetvābhāsa tvāt iti 
[088,iv]	evam anumāne nirūpite tasmāt jagat nirmātṛ puruṣa dhaureya siddhiḥ kṣiti ādau kāryatvena ghaṭa vat sa kartṛkatva anumānāt nanu kṣiti ādi pratyekam na pakṣaḥ tasya sva śabda ūna abhidhātum aśakyatvāt na api militam eka rūpa abhāvāt atas eva sa kartṛka tvāsa kartṛka tva vicāra ambhaka saṃśaya viṣayaḥ tathābhūta vivāda viṣayaḥ vā na pakṣaḥ eka rūpa abhāvena tayoḥ tāvat grahītum aśakyatvāt vādinoḥ niścita tvena saṃśaya abhāvāt na ca vādya numānayoḥ tulya bala tvena madhyasthasya saṃśayaḥ anumānābhyām tasya saṃśayaḥ madhyastha praśna anantarañcā anumānam iti anyonya āśrayāt ghaṭe api kadācid tayoḥ sambhavāt pratyekam saṃśaye vivāda āspada tvena anumāne artha antara tā āpatteḥ ca 
[088,v^1]	na ca śarīra apekṣeṇa kartrā yat na kṛtam śarīra janyam janyam vā pakṣaḥ janyā ātma viśeṣa guṇa śabda phūtkāra sarga ādyaka ālīna veda ghaṭa ādi lipya ādi sampradāyānām īśvara mātra kartṛkāṇām asaṃgrahāt asiddheḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvārā śarīriṇopi kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvāt na api janya kṛtya janyam janyam ubhaya siddha kṛti janyāni ajanyam vā pakṣaḥ kṣiti ādīnām adṛṣṭa dvārā janya kṛti janya tvāt na api adṛṣṭa janaka kṛtya janyam janya kṛti sākṣāt ajanyam vā janyam pakṣaḥ īśvara kṛteḥ adṛṣṭa janaka tvena kṣiti ādau tad abhāvāt ghaṭa ādau api evam pakṣa tvena aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanāt na ca kṣitiḥ eva pakṣaḥ 
[088,v^2]	aṅkureṇa sandigdha anaikāntika tvāt na ca niścita vipakṣe hetu sandehāt saḥ iti vācyam hetau sādhya abhāva vat gāmi tva saṃśayasya dūṣaka tvāt sa ca sādhya abhāvavati hetu sandehāt hetumati sādhya abhāva san dehāt vā ubhayathā api doṣaḥ na ca evam pakṣe api tat syāt anumāna mātra ucchedaka tvena itaratra tasya dūṣaka tvāt aṅkure hetoḥ aniścayena sandigdha anaikāntikam tad niścaye ca sādhya sandehavati sādhya anumitiḥ eva pakṣa vat sāmagrī sattvāt atas eva aṅkuraḥ pakṣa samaḥ iti ced 
[088,vi]	na tasya apakṣa tvena hetoḥ pakṣa dharma tā viraheṇa sthāpana anumāna aviṣaya tvāt tadā tasya api pakṣa tve pratijñā antara āpattiḥ anumāna antara adhīna tad sādhyānum iti anantarañca pakṣe anumitau itaretara āśrayāt na ekam api anumānam syāt tatra api kṣiti ādau sandigdhānaikāntāt kṣiteḥ vivāda viṣaya tve aṅkure prathamam sādhya sādhane artha antarāt ca kiñca evam ekaika upādāna abhijña siddhau api na īśvara siddhiḥ na api sarga ādyakālīnam dvi aṇukam pakṣaḥ paramprati sarga ādi asiddheḥ 
[088,vii]	kiñca sa kartṛka tvam na tāvat kṛtimat sahabhāvaḥ kṛti mat janya tvam vā asmad ādinā siddha sādhanāt upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛti mat janya tvam tat iti ced na upādāna gocara tvam yadi yat kiñcit upādāna gocara tvam tadā asmad ādinā artha antara tvam jñāna ādi janya tvam api vivakṣitam na ca ghaṭa upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna ādīnām janakatvam sambhavati vyabhicārāt iti ced na kṣiti janaka adṛṣṭa janaka jñāna ādīnām upādāna aviṣaya tva niyamena adṛṣṭa dvārā taiḥ eva siddha sādhanāt na ca sākṣāt tat janya tvam vivakṣitam tat hi na kṛti janyā janya tve sati kṛti janya tvam sva janaka kṛtya vyavahita uttarakṣaṇa varti tvam vā ghaṭa dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikalatā āpatteḥ ghaṭa ādau kulāla ādi kartṛka tva abhāva prasaṅgāt ca na ca śarīra kriyāḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti vācyam ghaṭena anaikāntika tvāt ceṣṭā tvasya upādhi tvāt ca 
[088,viii]	na api kṣiti ādi upādāna gocara tvam vivakṣitam aprasiddheḥ na ca upādāna śabdasya sambandhi śabda tvena ghaṭa kṣiti ādi pada samabhivyavahāre tad tad upādāna bodhaka tvam caitraḥ mātṛ bhaktaḥ maitra vat iti vācyam śābde hi bodhe tathā na ca atra śabdaḥ pramāṇam vādinoḥ anāpta tvāt anumāne tu anugatena vyāpaka tva grahe tena rūpeṇa vyāpaka siddhiḥ tat ca upādāna tvam eva iti katham na artha antaram kiñca evam ghaṭa ādau api tad tad upādāna tvena eva upasthityā sāmānyena rūpeṇa kutra api anupasthiteḥ vyāptiḥ eva na gṛhyeta api ca sāmānya lakṣaṇayā jñāna lakṣaṇayā yoga ja dharma rūpayā pratyāsattyā upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛtimatā asmāt ādinā siddha sādhanam teṣām kṣiti avyavahita pūrva samaya asattve api tadvatas sattvāt adṛṣṭa dvārā teṣām api janakatva sambhavāt jñāna ādi sākṣāt janya tvasya ca nirasta tvāt 
[088,ix]	atha yoga ja dharma ajanya sa vikalpakā janya sāmānya lakṣaṇā pratyāsattyajanya janyā upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛti mada janyam janyam pakṣaḥ yoga ja dharma ājanya sa vikalpakājanya sāmānya lakṣaṇā pratti āsattya janya upādāna gocara jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛtimat janyam iti sādhyam yat vā anāgata gocara sākṣātkāra janaka pratyāsatti ajanya janya jñāna ādi mada janyam janyam anāta gocara sākṣātkāra janaka pratyāsattya janya upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna ādi majjanyam iti sādhyam jñāna avyavahita uttara samaya varti i chātada vyavahita uttara samaya varti kṛtīnām janaka tvam vivakṣitam na tu jñāna ādīnām yaugapadyam paurvāparyam vā atas na sādhya aprasiddhiḥ na vā kṣiti ādau bādhaḥ iti 
[089,i]	mā evam yoga ja dharma sāmānya jñāna rūpa pratyāsattīnām anāgata gocara sākṣātkārasya tad janaka pratyāsattīnāñca parasya aprasiddha tayā tad ajanyasya sākṣātkārasya aprasiddha tvena pakṣa sādhyayoḥ viśeṣaṇā siddhyā param pratyāśraya asiddheḥ sādhya aprasiddheḥ ca tad siddhau vā pakṣe tad ajanya tva asiddheḥ kṣiti janaka adṛṣṭa janaka kṛti cikīrṣā sākṣātkārāṇām yoga ja dharma ādyajanyānām adṛṣṭa dvārā kṣiti janaka tvena siddha sādhanāt na ca tādṛśa sākṣāt janya tvam vivakṣitam ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭānte tad asambhavāt dṛṣṭānte ghaṭa ādau janaka iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya anumiti tvena janya sa vikalpa kavyāpti graha janya tvena sādhya aprasiddheḥ ca 
[089,ii]	nanu vyāpti balena sādhyam sidhyati vyāptiḥ ca yatra yatra kārya tvam tatra tad upādāna abhijña janya tvam iti rūpā na tu yat yat kāryam tad tad kiñcid upādāna abhijña janyam iti evañca yatra yatra kārya tvam tatra tad upādāna abhijña janya tvam iti viśiṣya vyāptyā kṣiti ādau kārya tvam kṣiti ādi upādāna abhijña janya tvam eva sādhayati atas na siddha sādhanam iti ced na ghaṭe paṭe ca kāryatvasya vyāpti grahaḥ kim pratyekam ghaṭa upādāna abhijña janya tvena tad tad upādāna abhijña janya tvena upādāna abhijña janya tvena vā ādye ghaṭa upādāna abhijña janya tva ādau kāryatvasya vyabhicāraḥ eva 
[089,iii_089,iv]	dvitīye tu ananugata tad tad śabda abhidheya ghaṭa ādi upādāna gata anugata rūpa abhāvāt katham vyāpaka tā grahaḥ tad tad śabdasya svabhāvāt samabhivyāhṛta para tayā na ayam doṣaḥ iti ced na anumāne śabda svabhāva upanyāsasya aprayojaka tvāt atas eva idānīm devadattaḥ bahis asti vidyamāna tve sati gṛha asattvāt vidyamāna tve sati yaḥ yadā yatra na asti sa tadā tad atirikte deśe asti yathā aham eva bahis asan gṛha madhye tiṣṭhāmi iti atra pakṣa dṛṣṭānta sādhāraṇayatva tattvayoḥ anugatayoḥ abhāvāt na anvayī kintu vyatirekī iti uktam tṛtīye siddha sādhanam eva atha sarga ādyakālīnat vi aṇukam jñāna icchā ākṛti samāna kālīna sāmagrī janyam kāryatvāt ghaṭa vat adṛṣṭa sāmagrī janya tve adṛṣṭa tva āpattiḥ iti ced na paramprati sarga ādi asiddheḥ jñāna ādīnām siddhau api dvi aṇukā janaka tvāt udāsīna siddha aprayojaka tvāt ca 
[089,v]	etena sarga ādyakālīnam dvi aṇukam dvi aṇukā samavāyi kāraṇa samāna kālīna kṛti janyam iti nirastam dvi aṇukā samavāyikāraṇa samāna kālīna kṛti tvena gaurava aprayojaka tva abhyām ajanaka tvāt kiñca kārya tvam na tāvat yoga upasthita kṛti arha tvam asiddheḥ na api pūrva kāla asattve sati uttara kāla sambandhi tvam tad tad pūrva kāla tvasya ananugata tvāt sakala pūrva kālasya aprasiddheḥ na api kādācid ka tvam prāc abhāvena anaikāntika tvāt na api prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvam dhvaṃsena anaikāntika tvāt na api sattve sati tattvam sattā jāteḥ paramprati asiddheḥ svarūpa sattvasya ca dhvaṃse api sattvāt 
[089,vi]	yat tu ayam ghaṭaḥ etad ghaṭa janaka aniti ajñāna cikīrṣā ākṛti atirikta jñāna ādi janyaḥ kāryatvāt paṭa vat ityādi tat na vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvena aprayojaka tvāt anyathā ayam ghaṭaḥ etad ghaṭa janakān iti ādṛṣṭa atirikta adṛṣṭa janyaḥ kārya tvāt apara ghaṭa vat etad sukha duḥkha sākṣātkārau etat janaka anitya sukha dukha atirikta sukha duḥkha sādhyau sukha duḥkha sākṣātkāra tvāt ityādinā nitya dharma adharma sukha duḥkha āśrayasya api siddhi prasaṅgāt ayam ghaṭaḥ sva janaka anitya jñāna ādi atirikta jñānāt yajanyaḥ ghaṭa tvāt apara ghaṭa vat ityādinā sat pratipakṣāt ca 
[089,vii]	kecid tu dṛśyate tāvat abhimata viṣaya grāhiṇī indriye manaḥ niveśayataḥ puṃsaḥ manaḥ kriyā anukūlaḥ yatnaḥ tathā ca sarga ādyakālīna śarīra janya jñāna dhvaṃsā anādhāra kāla ādhāra jñāna janaka ātma manaḥ yoga janikā manaḥ kriyā tad manaḥ gocara prayatna anādhāra tad manaḥ gocara prayatna tad vyāpya itara sakala kāraṇa ādhāra kāla anantara kāla anādhāra ādya sattākā tat manaḥ kriyā tvāt sammata tanmanaḥ kriyāvat arthāt prayatna ādhāra kāla anantara kāla ādhārā sā kriyā sidhyati iti āhuḥ tat na sarga ādi akāle jñāna jana kamanaḥ saṃyoga janaka kriyāyām māna abhāvaḥ pūrva kriyayā eva saṃyoga sambhavāt īśvara vādinām tad manaḥ gocara prayatna an ādhāraḥ kālaḥ aprasiddhaḥ eva kriyā tvasya eva hetu tve vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvañca kiñca evam prayatna anādhāra kāla anantara kāla anādhāra tvam arthāt tad siddhau māna antarāt īśvara siddhau artha antara tvam iti 
[089,viii]	atra ucyate adṛṣṭa dvāra kopa ādāna gocara janya kṛtya janyāni samavetāni janyāni adṛṣṭa prāc abhāva vyāpya prāc abhāva apratiyogi upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛtimat janyāni sva janaka adṛṣṭa uttara upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛti mat janyāni vā aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā prayatna viṣayī bhavat upādānāni vā samaveta tve sati prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvāt yat evam tat evam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca etāni tasmāt tathā ukta pakṣe kasyacid anantarbhāve api tat ādāya tathā eva niruktasya pakṣatu a nirdeśe samūha ālambana rūpā eva anumitiḥ utpadyate na ca janya kṛtya janya tvam tāvat ananugateṣu eka rūpa abhāvena grahītum aśakyam iti vācyam janya kṛtya janya tvam hi janya kṛti janyā anya tvam iti anya tvena rūpeṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇayā tāvatām upasthiteḥ 
[089,ix]	na ca janya tva viśeṣaṇa vyāvatrtyā aprasiddhiḥ prameyaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti vat avyāvartaka tve api tad uparakta buddheḥ uddeśya tvena tasya uparañjaka tvāt uktāni āma tvam eva sa kartṛka tvam atas eva ghaṭa bhoktā na ghaṭa kartā iti vyavahriyate evañca śabda phūtkāra ādīnām pakṣatā eva jñāna icchā ādīnām api pakṣa tvāt na sandigdha anaikāntika tā upādānasya siddha tve api upādeyasya asiddhatvena tadvat tayā tatra api cikīrṣā yat vā pakṣe hetau ca na samavetat tvam viśeṣaṇam tena dhvaṃsaḥ api pakṣaḥ sādhye ca upādāna padam kāraṇa mātra param anupādeyam eva vā janya icchā kṛtya janya tvañca pakṣe vivakṣitam tena kṛti dhvaṃsasya kṛti janya tve api icchā janya tva abhāvāt pakṣa tvam kṣitiḥ eva vā pakṣaḥ na ca aṅkure sandigdha anaikāntika tvam pakṣapakṣa samanairapekṣyeṇa ghaṭa ādau niścita vyāpteḥ liṅgasya tayoḥ darśanena ubhayatra anumiti avirodhāt na tu anumityoḥ anyaḥ anya apekṣa tvam yena anyonya āśrayaḥ syāt 
[089,x]	pratijñāyāḥ aviṣaya tvāt tatra pakṣa sama vyapadeśaḥ na ca aṅkurasya pakṣa tvena anirdeśāt tatra na pakṣa dharma tā jñānam iti vācyam siṣā dhayiṣā viraha saha kṛta sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvavati liṅga jñānasya anumiti mātra kāraṇa tvāt tat ca kṣitau pañca avayavena aṅkure svatas eva iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ yadi ca kṣitau hetu niścaya daśāyām aṅkurasya hetumat tayā na niścayaḥ tadā kva sandigdha anaikāntika tvam 
[090,i]	atha pakṣa same sādhya abhāva sāmānādhikaraṇya saṃśayāt hetau vyāpti grahaḥ eva na utpadyate utpannaḥ api vā bādhyate iti ced tarhi mahān ase api dhūme vyāpti grahaḥ na syāt bhūtaḥ api vā bādhyate sandigdha vahnika parvatā parvata dhūmavatām eka dharma abhāvena apakṣa tvāt tasmāt sādhya sandehavati hetu niścayaḥ na doṣaḥ kintu guṇaḥ eva anyathā anumāna mātram ucchidyeta pakṣāt anyatra tat dūṣaṇam iti yat uktam tatra pakṣa anyatvam siṣā dhayiṣita sādhya anya tvam yadi tadā anapekṣita anumitiḥ na syāt 
[090,ii]	atha sandigdha sādhya anya tvam sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāva viṣaya anya tvam vā vivakṣitam tadā aṅkure api tat na asti atha pratijñā viṣaya anyatvam tadā sva artha anum iti ucchedaḥ niyata viṣaya jñāna ajanya tvena pakṣa viśeṣaṇāt sarva viṣaya jñāna siddhiḥ sādhye ca jñāna icchā prayatnānām viśeṣaṇa tvena viśiṣṭa sādhana tvam vivakṣitam tena na tad upalakṣita kṣetrajñena artha antaram sāmānyatas api sādhya nirddeśe pakṣa dharma tā balena abhimata viśeṣa siddhiḥ ca 
[090,iii]	nanu ādya sādhya dvaye ghaṭa ādi upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā kṛtīnām eva janaka tvam āyātu iti artha antaram na ca teṣām vyabhicārāt kṣiti ādau na kāraṇa tvam iti vācyam anādau pravāhe kasyacid kadācid kṣiti dvi aṇuka ādi pūrvam ghaṭa ādi upādāna gocara jñāna ādi sattvāt na ca sarga ādyakālīnasya api pakṣa tvāt tatra īśvara siddhiḥ paramprati tat asiddheḥ iti ced na jñāna ādīnām trayāṇām sva viṣaya samaveta kāryam pratyeva janakatvā avadhāraṇena etat anumānasya tad aviṣaya tvāt atas eva anya upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna ādyajanya tvena pakṣa viśeṣaṇam api na yuktam tṛtīya sādhye tu na artha antaram kṣiti ādeḥ ghaṭa ādi upādāna asamaveta tvāt 
[090,iv]	nanu sāmānya lakṣaṇa ādi pratyāsattyā kṣiti ādi upādāna gocaram yat pratyakṣam tat janya tvam eva astu tathā ca īśvare na pratyakṣam na vā icchā prayatnau tayoḥ samāna adhikaraṇa jñāna aviṣaye asattvāt na ca tādṛśa pratyāsattya janya tvam pratyakṣa viśeṣaṇam paramprati asiddheḥ iti ced na dravya tvena jñāna lakṣaṇayā vā kapāla gocara pratyakṣe api ghaṭa ādau akartṛka tvāt kṣiti ādau sa kartṛka tva nirvāhakam jñānam sidhya t vilakṣaṇam eva sidhyati na ca avayava vibhāga dvārā kṣiti ādiṣu jala kṣepāt samudra ādiṣu hasta kṣepāt paramāṇu dvaya saṃyoge ca dvaṇukeṣu asmad ādi kartṛka tvāt aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam iti vācyam tatra hi kṣiti nāśe asmad ādīnām kartṛ tvam na tu khaṇḍa kṣitau avasthita saṃyogebhyaḥ eva tad upapatteḥ sakala tad upādāna gocara jñāna icchā kṛtīnām abhāvāt ca atas eva dvayaṇuke api na kartṛ tvam jala kṣepāt adhika parimāṇaka samudra ādeḥ sa pakṣa tvam eva ghaṭasya iva 
[090,v]	nanu ghaṭe sādhya vikala tvam anvaya vyatirekābhyām jñāna ādeḥ eva janakatvāt na tu tad āśrayasya dharmi grāhakasya anvaya vyatirekasya vā grāhakasya abhāvāt na ca ghaṭaḥ ātma janyaḥ utpattimat tvāt jñāna vat iti vācyam ātma samaveta tvasya upādhi tvāt ghaṭaḥ ākāśa janyaḥ utpattimat tvāt śabda vat iti vat aprayojaka tvāt ca iti ced mā evam prayatna vat ātma saṃyogaḥ ceṣṭā dvārā ghaṭa hetuḥ atas prayatna vat ātmā api hetuḥ na ca ātma saṃyoge sati api prayatnam vinā na ceṣṭā iti prayatnaḥ eva tad kāraṇam asamavāyi kāraṇam vinā kārya anutpatteḥ na ca ātma saṃyogasya kāraṇa tve api saṃyoge paricāyaka mātram ātmā iti vācyam saṃyoga mātrasya akāraṇa tvena saṃyogi viśeṣitasya hetu tvāt 
[090,vi_090,vii]	ātma saṃyoga vyatireka prayukta kriyā vyatirekasya asiddheḥ na ātma saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam iti ced na yā kriyā vyadhikaraṇayadīya guṇa janyā sā tad saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇikā yathā sparśavat vega dravya saṃyoga jā kriyā iti vyāptyā tad siddheḥ na ca kriyāyāḥ mūrta mātra samavetā samavāyikāraṇaka tva niyamaḥ iti vācyam kārya mātra abhiprāyeṇa jñāna ādau vyabhicārāt viśiṣya aprayojaka tvāt asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga āśrayasya tad kārya janaka tva niyamāt ca anye tu anukūla kṛti samavāyi tvam kartṛ tvam na tu janaka tve sati gauravāt kartari kāraka vyapadeśaḥ ca abhiyuktānām sa viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena kṛti paryavasat naḥ eva evam jñāna icchā ākṛti janya tvam eva sādhyam tad āśraya tvam eva īśvarasya kartṛ tvam 
[090,viii]	atha ghaṭe kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam cikīrṣā dvārāḥ hetuḥ tat ca pratyakṣam cikīrṣā viṣaye anāgate indriya āsannikarṣāt kintu anumiti rūpam tathā ca sādhya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya aprasiddhiḥ vā doṣaḥ iti ced na siddha vṛtti asiddha viṣayā hi kṛtiḥ siddha viṣaya pratyakṣe sati sambhavati na hi mṛd avayavānām saṃsthāna viśeṣe kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā anumitau api avayavasya pratyakṣeṇa upasthitim vinā pravṛttiḥ atas eva yāge śabdāt tad upajī viliṅgāt vā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tve avagate api haviḥ ādīnām pratyakṣeṇa anupasthitau na pravṛttiḥ na ca upādāna pratyakṣam pravartaka jñāna upakṣīṇam apratyakṣe paramāṇau tad kriyāyām iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāne api pravṛtti abhāvāt pravṛtti viṣayasya mṛdaṅga ādeḥ pratyakṣa tvāt na śabda phūtkāra ādinā vyabhicāraḥ 
[090,ix]	na ca abhimata grāhaka indriya saṃyoga artham manasi prayatna janya kriyā darśanāt cavī abhicāraḥ adṛṣṭa saha kṛta tvac indriyeṇa hi manaḥ vaha nāḍīnām upalambhena tad gocara prayatnāt nāḍī kriyā tatas sparśavat vegavat nāḍyā nodanāt manasi kriyā na tu prayatnāt atas eva jala ādi abhyavahāra mala utsarga hetu nāḍī nām anādi abhyāsa vāsanā vaśāt adṛṣṭa saha kṛta tvac indriyeṇa upalambhāt tad gocara prayatnaḥ 
[090,x]	nanu evam ghaṭa ādau anumiti janya tva darśanāt īśvare anumitiḥ api siddhyat yathā ca pratyakṣasya indriya janya tve api nityam tat īśvare tathā anumiteḥ liṅga janya tvepi sā tatra nityā eva anityena anādi dvi aṇuka ādi ajananāt iti ced na sukha duḥkha abhāva ādi sādhana tā anumiteḥ hi hetu tvam ghaṭa ādau gṛhītam na ca bhagavati śarīra adṛṣṭa abhāvena sukham asti atas na kṣiti ādau tasya tathā anumitiḥ yathārthā sambhavati na ca tādṛśa anumiteḥ anumiti antarasya vā anumiti tvena ghaṭa ādau pravṛtti viṣaya pratyakṣa vat hetu tvam gṛhītam iti na īśvare anumitiḥ 
[090,xi]	nanu dveṣa janya kṛti sādhye cikīrṣā virahāt vyabhicāraḥ tad dṛṣṭāntena kṣiti ādau dveṣa sādhya tvāt īśvare dveṣaḥ api bhavet dveṣavataḥ saṃsāri tvena bhagavataḥ api tathā tu āpattiḥ iticed na na hi sarpa ādi dveṣāt eva tad nāśa anukūla vyāpāre kṛtiḥ utpattum arhati prayojanam antareṇa prekṣāvatām duḥkha eka phale kṛteḥ anutpatteḥ kintu duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsam tad sādhya duḥkha anutpādam vā phalam uddiśya tad sādhana tā jñānāt tathā ceṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt tatra icchā asti eva iti sā eva kṛti kāraṇam kḷpta tvāt dveṣaḥ tu paramparayā tad upakṣīṇaḥ kutas tarhi dveṣa siddhiḥ śatrum dveṣmi iti abādhita pratyayāt na ca adṛśyasya kartṛḥ anupalabdhi bādhaḥ anupalabdhi mātrasya bādhaka tve atīndriya ucchedāt yogyā anupalabdheḥ ca asiddheḥ paramātmanaḥ ayogya tva niyamāt śaśa śrṛṅga pratibandyā ca na adṛśya mātra nirāsaḥ paramāṇa ādi svīkārāt 
[091,i]	na api ayogya kartṛ nirāsaḥ ceṣṭayā jñāna ādimataḥ paramātmanaḥ anumānāt paramprati tasya ayogya tvāt na api śrṛṅge paśutva vat aprayojakam kartuḥ kārya mātre kāraṇatva avadhāraṇāt pratibandi mātrasya ca adūṣaṇa tvāt śaśe paśu tvena ayogya śrṛḍga siddhiḥ kutas na iti ced na artha antara tvāt vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvena vyāpti asiddheḥ śrṛṅga tvasya yogya saṃsthāna viśeṣa vyaḍga tvena ayogyasya virodhena śaṅkitum aśakyatvāt śaśe śrṛṅgasya atyanta abhāvaḥ iti sarveṣām abādhita pratyakṣa bādhita tvāt ca 
[091,ii^1]	atha kṛti kāryayoḥ na anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpti grahaḥ tvad mate vyāpaka kṛteḥ sattve tad deśe samaye vā kṛti mātra vyatireka anirūpaṇāt nitya kṛteḥ anvayaḥ api na gṛhītaḥ vahni mātra vyatirekaḥ asti gṛhyate ca iti na ca evam ākāśa ātmanoḥ aprasiddhiḥ samavāyi mātrasya vyatireka anirūpaṇena kāryam samavāyi kāraṇa janyam iti vyāpteḥ asiddheḥ iti vācyam samavāyi kāraṇa tva grahe hi tad saṃsarga abhāvaḥ aprayojakaḥ nimitta mātra sādhāraṇa tvāt kintu yat samavāyi tatra kāryam yat na samavāyi tatra na iti anyaḥ anya abhāvam ādāya kāryam samavāyi janyam iti vyāpti graha sambhavāt 
[091,ii^2]	samavāyi tvena tayoḥ anyaḥ anya abhāvaḥ asti gṛhyate ca yat vā bhāva kāryam samavetam iti vyāptyā tayoḥ siddhiḥ iti yathā hi yat yat vahneḥ anvaye dhūmaḥ gṛhītaḥ tad tad vyatireke dhūma mātra vyatireka grahāt vahni dhūma mātrayoḥ vyāpti grahaḥ na tu parvatīya vahneḥ anvaya vyatireka grahāt na ca anya anvaya vyatirekābhyām anya vyāpti grahe atiprasaḍgaḥ iti vācyam yat viśeṣayoḥ anvaya vyatireka grahaḥ tad sāmānyayoḥ bādhakam vinā vyāpti grahāt sa ca vahni dhūma vyāpti grahaḥ utpadyamānaḥ sakala dhūma gocaraḥ dhūma tva puraskāreṇa prasiddha dhūma gocaraḥ eva vā bhavati tathā iha api kṛti viśeṣa kārya viśeṣayoḥ anvaya vyatireka grahaḥ bādhakam antareṇa kṛti kārya mātrayoḥ vyāpti grahe upāyaḥ na tu pakṣa dharma tā bala labhya viśeṣa anvaya vyatireka grahaḥ anumāna mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt 
[091,iii_091,v]	etena kāryatvasya vipakṣa vṛtti hataye sambhāvyate atīndriyaḥ kartā ced vyatireka siddhi vidhurā vyāptiḥ katham sidhyati dṛśyaḥ atha vyatireka siddhi manasā kartā samāśrīyate tad tyāge api tadā tṛṇa ādikam iti vyaktam vipakṣa īkṣaṇam iti nirastam nanu yadi kartṛ mātra vyāpti grahāt adṛśya kartṛ siddhiḥ tadā vahni mātra vyāpta dhūmāt adṛśya jāṭharīya vahni siddhiḥ api syāt na syāt adṛśya vahneḥ dhūmān utpatteḥ dṛśyasya eva tatra hetu tvāt nanu jñāna icchā prayatna traya vyatirekāt na kārya vyatirekaḥ kintu ekaika vyatirekāt tathā ca vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvena viśiṣṭa vyatirekaḥ na hetu vyatireka vyāpya iti na hetoḥ viśiṣṭa siddhiḥ sādhya avyāpaka abhāva pratiyoginaḥ eva sādhya gamaka tvāt iti ced na yatas ekaika vyatirekāt kārya vyatirekaḥ atas eva kārya tva ādeḥ ekaikam sidhyat trayam api sidhyati ārthaḥ tu samājaḥ 
[091,vi]	syāt etat aśarīraḥ nitya jñāna ādimān sarvajñaḥ kartā pakṣe vivakṣitaḥ ghaṭa ādau ca kāryatvasya tad viparīta kartṛ saha cāra darśanāt viśeṣa viruddha tvam iti ced na hetoḥ vivakṣita sādhya viparīta sahacāra mātrasya adūṣaka tvāt anyathā anumāna mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt na ca anitya jñāna asarvajña śarīra kartṛ tvena samam kāryatvasya vyāptiḥ asti yena viparīta sādhane viruddha tvam syāt tādṛśa vyāptiḥ ca tvayā mayā vā na aṅgīkriyate aṅkura ādau yogyā anupalambhena śarīra kartṛkatva abhāvāt 
[091,vii]	atha yathā darśana bala pravṛtta vyāptyā anitya jñāna ādimān kartā upaneyaḥ pakṣa dharma tayā ca nitya jñāna ādimān tathā copaneya viśeṣayoḥ virodhena vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayoḥ virodhāt paraspara sahakāritā virahān na anumānam viśeṣa virodhāt iti ced na anitya jñāna ādi kartṛ janya tvena vyāpti agrahāt jñāna ādimatkartṛ janya tva vyāpteḥ ca pakṣa dharma tā bala labhya viśeṣa avirodhāt kevalāyāḥ vyāpteḥ pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ ca pṛthak upanāyaka tva abhāvāt ca eka vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tathā ca nirapekṣa tādaśāyām viśeṣa anupasthānāt eva na virodha jñānam sa apekṣatā daśa āyāntu saha upalambhāt eva virodha pratiyoginoḥ siddhi asiddhibhyām virodha jñāna abhāvāt ca liṅga viśeṣeṇa sādhya viśeṣeṇa virodhe ca viśeṣa virodhaḥ yathā candana prabhava vahnimānayam asurabhi dhūmavat tvāt iti 
[091,viii]	nanu jñāna tva nitya tvayoḥ kartṛ tva aśarīri tvayoḥ ca paraspara viruddha tvena eka dharmya samāveśāt katham nitya jñāna ādi kartṛ siddhiḥ iti ced na upasaṃhāra sthānasya abhāvāt tathā hi īśvare tad buddhau ca aśarīra tva kartṛ tve buddhi tva nitya tve ca upasaṃhriyamāṇe viruddhe na tu sva āśraya sthite ubhaya uccheda prasaṅgāt na ca īśvaraḥ tad buddhiḥ vā upasthitā upasthitau vā dharma grāhaka mānena tayoḥ virodha apahārāt anupasthite ca tad dvaye virodha jñānam akiñcatkaram eva asmad ādi buddhau vyoma ādau kuvinde mukta ātmani ca upasthite virodha upasaṃhārāt buddhi tva nitya tvayoḥ kartṛ tva aśarīra tvayoḥ anadhigame api īśvare aśarīra kartṛ tva nitya jñāna ādi siddhiḥ apratyūha eva atas eva nitya tva avayavatyoḥ virodha jñānam akiñcitkaram eva iti paramāṇu siddhiḥ īśvara tad buddhi ādi kantarkitam iti ced na tarkasya prasañjanasya saṃśayasya ca ajñāte asambhavāt 
[091,ix_091,x]	syāt etat ghaṭa ādau kṛti sādhya tā hasta ādi vyāpāra dvārā eva gṛhītā na tu sākṣāt na ca pitāputrayoḥ eka ghaṭa sādhana tvam iva prayatna hasta ādi vyāpārayoḥ sākṣāt sādhana tvam vācyam iti vācyam ghaṭa artham hasta vyāpāra vat kulāla samīpa sthasya hasta ādi vyāpāra śūnyasya tad ghaṭa kartṛ tva āpatteḥ na ca hasta ādi vyāpāravat tā aśarīrasya sambhavati anyādṛśī ca kṛti sādhyatā na dṛṣṭā śarīra tad vyāpārau ca aṅkure bādhitau iti kartuḥ api bādhaḥ eva anyathā tvad anumānāt eva kṣetrajñaḥ eva kartā anumīyate buddhi ādimat para ātmanaḥ yogyā anupalabdhi bādha abhāvāt śarīra vyāpāra dvārā eva kṣetrajñasya hetu tvāt śarīra vyāpārasya ca aṅkure bādhāt sa bādhitaḥ iti ced tarhi kartṛ mātrasya api tad dvārā eva ceṣṭa itara kārye kartṛ tva ādhāraṇat tad bādhe kartṛ mātra bādhaḥ api evañca kṛti sādhya tve śarīra vyāpāra janya tvam prayojakam iti saḥ eva upādhiḥ evam jñāna icchayoḥ api icchā ākṛti dvārā janaka tvam iti katham dvāram vinā kṣiti ādau janakatvam iti 
[092,i]	ucyate janya mātre hasta ādi vyāpāra janaka kṛti tvena na janaka tvam ceṣṭāyām kṛtyā ādau ca vyabhicārāt kintu ghaṭa ādau ca tathā janaka tvam iti janya mātre kṛti mātrasya janakatva virodhi viśeṣayoḥ janya janaka bhāve bādhakam vinā sāmānyayoḥ api tathā abhāva niyamāt na hi viśeṣe viśeṣa prayojaka tvena sāmānya prayojaka tva virodhaḥ ceṣṭa itara kārye śarīra vyāpāra dvārā eva kṛteḥ hetu tvāt tena vinā kṣiti ādau na kṛti sādhya tvam iti ced na ceṣṭa itara kārya mātre śarīra vyāpāra janaka kṛti tvena na janaka tvam kṣiti ādau vyabhicārāt kintu tad viśeṣa ghaṭa ādau iti ukta tvāt 
[092,ii]	na ca evam āma vāta jaḍīkṛta kalevarasya prayatnāt eva ghaṭotpattiḥ syāt hasta ādi vyāpāram vinā eva kṛrteḥ hetu tvāt iti vācyam ghaṭe kṛti vat hasta ādi vyāpārasya api hetu tvāt yat uktam kṣetrajñaḥ eva kutas na anumīyate iti tatra hasta ādi vyāpāra kṛtimān yadi kṣetrajñaḥ abhimataḥ tadā hasta ādi vyāpāra kṛtimān kṣetrajñaḥ abhimataḥ tadā hasta ādi vyāpārasya aṅkure yogyā anupalabdhi bādhāt 
[092,iii]	atha hasta ādi vyāpāra rahita kṛtimān abhimataḥ tat om iti ucyate saḥ eva bhagavān īśvaraḥ atas eva sahabhāva nirūpaka tve niyata pūrva varti tvam kāraṇa tvam samavāyi asamavāyinoḥ tathā tvena nimitte api tathā abhāvāt anyathā pratibandhaka abhāva anantaram pratibandhaka sattva kāle kāryam syāt pratibandhaka abhāvasya pūrvam sattvāt na ca kṛteḥ sahabhāva nirūpaka tvam svatas kārya samaye abhāvāt tathā ca tad paricāyita vyāpāra dvārā tasyāḥ sahabhāva nirupaka tvam atas śarīra vyāpāra dvārā eva kṛteḥ janaka tvam na kevalāyāḥ iti apāstam 
[092,iv]	samavāyi asamavāyi pratibandhaka abhāvānām avinaśyat avastha tvena kāraṇa tvāt tathā eva anvaya vyatirekāt tena teṣām abhāve vinā śa kṣaṇe ca na kāryam anyathā prativyakti kārya sahabhāva nirūpaṇe kāryet patteḥ prāk sahabhāvasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt kāraṇa tva aniścayena kvāpi pravṛttiḥ na syāt iti tad jātīya tvasya avaśya vācya tve vinaśyat avastham katham saha bhāvena api vyavacchedyam atas sva rūpa yogya tā rūpā kāraṇa tā tatra api kārya abhāvaḥ tu sahakāri virahāt anyathā nimittānām pratyekam kārya sahabhāva nirūpaka tvena janaka tve gauravam prāgabhāvasya pratiyogi ajanaka tva prasaṅgāt ca anyathā utpannaḥ api ghaṭaḥ punar utpadyeta sāmagrī sattvāt 
[092,v_092,vi]	na ca saḥ eva tatra pratibandhakaḥ abhāva antarasya tatra akāraṇa tvena kāraṇībhūta abhāva pratiyogi tva rūpasya pratibandhaka tvasya prāgabhāva kāraṇa tvaḥ eva viśrāmāt na ca ekā sāmagrī ekadā ekam eva kāryam janayati svabhāvāt iti vācyam sāmagrī tat virahasya kārya tad abhāva prayojaka tvena sāmagryām satyām kāryasya tad abhāve kārya abhāvasya vajralepāyita tvāt 
[092,vii]	syāt etat kartā śarīryeva jñānam anityam eva buddhiḥ icchā dvāra eva icchā kṛti dvārā eva hetuḥ iti ādi prāthamika vyāpti pratyakṣa virodhāt na aśarīra nitya jñāna ādi kartṛ siddhiḥ atas eva śarīram anityam eva iti niyamāt na kartṛ tvena nitya atīndriya śarīra siddhiḥ īśvare na ca aprayojaka tvam nirupādhi tvena śaṅkā kalaṅkān avatārāt kāryatva sa kartṛka tvayoḥ api yadi nirupādhi tvam asti tadā api tulya bala tvena sat pratipakṣāt tad pratibandhoḥ tu na ca kārya tvam pakṣa dharma tā balāt balīyaḥ kartā śarīryā iva ityādau tu tat na asti iti vācyam jñānam anityam iti vyāpteḥ eva kṣiti ādau jñāna janya tva virodhi tvāt 
[092,viii_092,x]	evam kāryam jñāna janyam jñānam anityam eva iti anayoḥ virodhaḥ eva avirodhe tu dvayam api syāt tathā ca kṣiti ādau śarīrarya nitya jñāna paryavasāne virodhaḥ eva syāt kiñca jñānam anityam eva ityādau nitya jñāna ādeḥ aprasiddheḥ tad avyāvartaka tayā na upādhi tva niścayaḥ tad saṃśayaḥ vā kāryatva sa kartṛka tva vyāpti graha daśāyām śarīra vyāpāra avi abhicārāt upādheḥ niścayaḥ saṃśayaḥ vā asti iti tat na jñānam anityam eva ityādi vyāpteḥ asiddheḥ vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvena aprayojaka tvāt nirupādhi sahacāra darśana vyabhicāra adarśanāt eva vyāpti grahaḥ nirupādhi tvena vā vipakṣe bādhakam iti ced na avayavaḥ mahān eva tejaḥ udbhūta rūpam eva ityādi vyāpti grahāt parama aṇu nayana ādeḥ asiddhi prasaṅgāt 
[092,xi]	atha dravya cākṣuṣe aneka dravyavat tvasya sākṣātkāre viṣaya indri sannikarṣasya hetu tvāt tad mūlaka vipakṣa bādhakena paramāṇu ādi sādhakasya balavat tvāt paramāṇu ādi siddhau virodhi vyāpteḥ bādhaḥ na tu vaiparītyam vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvena tasya abalavat tvāt iti manyase tarhi jñāna ādi kārya kāraṇa bhāva avadhāraṇāt tad mūlaka vipakṣa bādhakena niṣkalaṅka vyāpti grahāt pakṣa dharma tā graha sahitān nitya jñāna ādi siddhau vyabhicārāt na vyāptiḥ anyathā sādhyam pakṣa atiriktaḥ eva ityādi nirupādhi sahacārāt vyāpti grahe sakala anumāna ucchedaḥ 
[092,xii]	vayantu brūmaḥ pakṣa dharma tā balāt nityam jñānam siddhyat buddhiḥ anityaiḥ eva iti vyāpti pratyakṣeṇa na pratibadhyate asmadā api buddhi viṣayaka tvena bhinna viṣayaka tvāt eka viṣaya virodhi jñānasya eva pratibandhaka tvāt nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ eka jātīye dravye avirodhāt buddhi mātre anitya tva avagamāt katham tad viśeṣe nitya tva buddhiḥ iti ced na buddhi mātrasya īśvarāni īśvara buddhi paratve virodhāt vyabhicārāt ca asmad ādi buddhi paratve ca bhinna viṣaya tvena apratibandhaka tvāt buddhi tvam nitya āvṛttyā iva iti avagatam atas katham tatra nitya vṛtti tva avagamaḥ iti ced na ubhaya siddha nitya avṛtti tva avagame api atirikta nitya vṛtti tva avagatau virodha abhāvāt buddhi tvam anitya tva vyāpyam avagatam na anitya tva abhāvavati jñātavyam iti ced na anitya tva vyāpya tvam anitya mātra vṛtti tvam tatra ca uktam eva etena kartā śarīryā iva ityādi api jñānam pratibandhakam iti nirastam 
[092,xiii_092,xiv]	nanu kartṛ janya tve janya tvam na avacchedakam kintu ghaṭa tva ādikam eva tena eva rūpeṇa anvaya vyatireka grahāt āvaśyaka tvāt ca ananugatam api janya tā avacchedakam vahni janyatāyām dhūma tva ādi vat atha ghaṭa tva ādi vat janya tvam avacchedakam na hi viśeṣaḥ asti iti sāmānyam aprayojakam tathā ca vahni janya tve dhūma viśeṣaḥ prayojyaḥ asti iti na dhūma sāmānyam agnim gamayet tasmāt yat viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad sāmānyayoḥ api bādhakam vinā tathā tva niyamaḥ iti ced na 
[093,i_093,ii]	tatra bādhaka abhāvāt atra ca jñānam anityam eva ityādi prāthamika bahu vyāptau bādhāt tulya tve vā vyāpti saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvāt na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva mūlaka tvena kāryatva sakṛrtṛka tva vyāptiḥ balīyasi iti vācyam virodhi pratyakṣeṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya eva asiddheḥ etena dhūma ādau vahni janya tāvacchedakam anugatam na sambhavati iha tu janya tvam anugatam asti atas bādhakam vinā na mucyate iti nirastam jñānam anityam eva ityādi sahacāra avasāyasya bādhakam vinā pakṣa dharma vyāpti paryavasāyi tvena bādhaka tvāt iti 
[093,iii]	mā evam nirupādhi tvena sahacāra avasāyasya sādhakam bādha kañca vinā sādhāraṇyena vyāpti saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvāt anyathā sādhyam pakṣa atirikte eva sukham duḥkha sambhinnam eva ityādi vyāpti grahasya kārya kāraṇa bhāva grāhaka bādhaka tve tad saṃśaya ādhāyaka tve vā kāryāt kāraṇa anumāna ucchede nirīham jagat jāyeta tasmāt yat viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad sāmānyayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ balavatā bādhakena apanīyate na ca atra tat asti virodhi vyāpti sādhakasya vipakṣa bādhakasya abhāvāt 
[093,iv]	navyāḥ tu kāryam kartṛ janyam iti vyāptitaḥ aśarīra nitya jñāna kartaka rtrupasthitau jñānam anityam eva iti anena virodha pratisandhānam na tu tām vinā pratiyogi anupasthitau virodha anirūpaṇāt tathā ca upajīvya bādhāt jñānam anityam eva iti vyāpti jñānam akiñcitkaram eva atas eva pakṣa dharma tā vinākṛtam virodhi vyāpti jñānam na hetvābhāsa tayā uktam virodha pratiyogi siddhi asiddhi parāhata tvāt iti 
[093,v]	syāt etat astu śarīra janya tvam upādhiḥ na ca pakṣa itara tva vat pakṣa mātra vyāvartaka viśeṣaṇavat tvāt sādhana viśeṣita tvāt sādhana tulya yogakṣema tvena sādhya vyāpaka tva aniścayāt ca na upādhi tvam iti vācyam ceṣṭa itara kāryeṣu śarīra vyāpāra dvārā eva kartuḥ kāraṇa tvāt śarīra saha kṛtasya eva sva kārye kāraṇa tvāt ca na hi śarīra vinākṛtaḥ kartā śarīra kriyām ceṣṭām ghaṭa ādikam vā janayati na ca yat saha kṛtam yat janakam tena vinā tad janakam atas arthāt śarīra janyam eva kartṛ janyam iti sādhya vyāpaka tva niścayāt pakṣa itara tva ādau ca vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvāt na sādhya vyāpaka tā niścayaḥ iti teṣām anupādhi tve bījam atas eva bādha unnītam vahni itara tvam vahnimat tvena dhūmavat tve sādhye ārdra indhana prabhava vahnimat tvam rasavat tvena gandhavat tve sādhye pṛthivī tvam upādhiḥ vipakṣa bādhakaiḥ teṣām sādhya vyāpaka tva niścayāt 
[093,vi_093,vii]	na ca sādhana viśeṣita tvam api janya tvam hi prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvam śarīra janya tvañca śarīra kāraṇava tvam anyā nirakteḥ itara pada samabhivyāhāreṇa janya padāditara kāraṇakasya eva pratīteḥ tad arthaka tva kalpanāt iti vidhau vakṣyate atas eva śarīra kartṛka tvam upādhiḥ śarīra saha kṛtasya eva kartuḥ kāraṇa tvāt vyāpyam vyāpaka koṭau aniveśyataḥ eva pramāṇasya vyāpti grāhaka tvāt śarīra kartṛka tva sa kartṛka tvayoḥ na vyāpti grahaḥ iti ced na viśiṣṭa aviśaṣṭa bhedena vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva avirodhāt atas eva janya tvena kāraṇa janya tvam anumīyate iti 
[093,viii]	mā evam kartuḥ hi śarīra sahakāritā kim ghaṭa ādau kartavye kārya mātre vā sva kārye vā ādye kartā śarīram vinā ghaṭa ādikam na karoti iti kim āyātam kartuḥ kārya mātra karaṇe dvitīye ca kārya mātram kartṛ janyam iti na tvayā svīkriyate svīkāre vā śarīra ajanyam api kāryam kartṛ janyam iti sādhya avyāpaka tvam tṛtīye tu sva janya tvam na sva janya tāvacchedakam ātma āśrayāt tathā api yaca sa kartṛka tvam asti tatra śarīra janya tvam āvaśyakam iti tasya sādhya vyāpaka tvam tulya yogakṣema tvena hetu vyāpya tā saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvena sandigdha upādhi tvam vā iti ced na 
[093,ix]	lāghavena bādhakam vinā kartṛ janya tve sati janya tvam avacchedakam na tu śarīra janya tvam gauravāt tathā ca śarīra janya tvam na sa kartṛka tva vyāpakam ghaṭa ādau tvā arthaḥ samājaḥ ghaṭa tvena śarīra janya tu a niyamāt na tu vyāpka tva prayuktaḥ māna abhāvāt śarīra janya tvam na sa kartṛka tva vyāpakam tad vyāpya jala tva avyāpaka tvāt nitya tva vat iti bādhakāt hasta ādinā pi kartṛ tva nirvāheṇa śarīrasya aprayojaka tvāt sākṣāt prayatna adhiṣṭeya janya tvasya sādhana vyāpaka tvāt ca śarīra kartṛka tvam api na upādhiḥ janya mātre kartuḥ śarīra sahakāritā virahāt 
[093,x_093,xi]	atha yad viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad sāmānyayoḥ api bādhakam vinā tathā niyamaḥ iti tvayā niraṭaṅki tathā ca kartṛ viśeṣa śarīra janya viśeṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamāt kartṛ mātra śarīra janya mātrayoḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ tathā ca śarīra janya tvam kartṛ janya tāvat śejakam iti bhavati upādhiḥ na ca evam ghaṭa tva vat śarīra janya tvam sa kartṛkatva vyāpyam na tu vyāpakam api iti vācyam ubhaya siddha sakala sa kartṛka vṛtti tvena sādhya vyāpaka tā nirṇayāt janya tve api sa kartṛkatva vyāpya tva grāhakam asti iti ced tarhi ubhayatra vyāpti grāhaka sāmye vinigamaka abhāvāt vyāpti saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvena sandigdha upādhiḥ vyāpya tva asiddhiḥ vā hetu vyāpya tā saṃśaya ādhāyakaḥ eva hi sandigdha upādhiḥ sa ca sādhya vyāpaka tve sādhana avyāpka tve vā ubhayatra vā saṃśayāt 
[093,xii]	na ca vācyam śarīra janya tvasa kartṛka tvayoḥ anvaya vyatireka jñāne janya tvasa kartṛka tvayoḥ tat grahaḥ āvaśyakaḥ iti lāghavāt tayoḥ eva vyāpti grahaḥ na tu upādhi sādhyayoḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ anvayavyatiḥ eka jñānañca śarīra janya tvānavagame api bhavati iti vinigamakam iti yatas na kartṛ mātra janyam ācayoḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpti grahaḥ kartṛ mātrasya vyatireka abhāvāt kintu viśeṣayoḥ anvaya vyatirekeṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvena vā sāmānyayoḥ tathā tva grahaḥ tau ca tulyau eva iti ced 
[093,xiii]	ucyate astu tāvat ghaṭa tva vat janya tva śarīra janya tvayoḥ api kartṛ janya tāvat chedaka tvena sa kartṛkatva vyāpya tvam grāhaka taulyāt vinigamana abhāvāt virodha abhāvāt ca sa kartṛka tva vyāpakatvantu śarīra janya tvasya kutas ghaṭa tva vat avyāpakasya api janya tā avat chedaka tvāt ubhaya siddha sakartṛke anvaya vyatirekābhyām śarīra janya tvasi avyāpaka tva grahaḥ iti ced na śarīra janya tva vinivedya tvena tulya nyāyena ca prathamam kartṛ janya tve janya tvam avacchedakam kḷptam iti tad virodhena śarīra janya tu asya sa kṛrtṛka tva vyāpaka tvān avagamāt atas eva na sandigdha upādhi tvam 
[094,i_094,ii]	nanu ghaṭa ādau śarīra janya tve kartṛ janya tvam anugatam avacchedakam bādhaka abhāvāt na ca lāghavāt ghaṭa tva ādikam eva tathā kartṛ janya tve api janya tvasya ātathā tva āpatteḥ evam śarīra janya tvasya vyāpyam sa kṛrtaka tvam vahneḥ dhūmā eva iti bhavati upādhiḥ kiñca kartṛ janya tve janya tvam śarīra janya tve vā sa kartṛka tvam avacchedakam iti saṃśaye api na hetoḥ sādhya vyāpya tva niścayaḥ iti ced tarhi ghaṭa ādau kartṛ janya tve gṛhīte tasya śarīra janya tva avacchedaka tvam grahītavyam ghaṭe ca ghaṭa tva vat janya tvam api bādhakam vinā kartṛ janya tāvacśedakam gṛhītam atas janya mātre kartṛ janya tvāt na śarīra janya tve tad avacchedaka tvam prathama gṛhīta upajīvya virodhāt atas eva na tasya hetau vyāpti saṃśaya ādhāyaka tvam api 
[094,iii]	etena anaṇu tva kṣiti avayava vṛtti anyatva ādayaḥ upādhi tvena nirastāḥ janya tvasya sādhya vyāpya tvena teṣām sādhya avyāpaka tvāt tathā api kṣiti ādikam na kartṛ janyam śarīra ajanya tvāt gagana vat iti sat pratipakṣaḥ astu iti ced na asya prasiddha kartṛ janya tva abhāva viṣayaka tvāt apratīta pratiyogikasya abhāvasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt sthāpana anumānañca pakṣa dharma tā balāt prasiddha kartṛ bhinna kartṛka tva sādhakam atas bhinna viṣayaka tvāt na pratibadhya pratibandhaka bhāvaḥ atas eva tad vyāpaka rahita tva ādikam abhāva sādhakam bādhakam apāstam tasya prasiddha abhāva viṣayaka tvena aprasiddha abhāva viṣayaka tvāt vyakti sādhakasya ca viśeṣataḥ aprasiddha vyakti sādhaka tva niyamāt anyathā anumāna vaiyarthyāt 
[094,iv]	kartṛ janya tvam anugatam ghaṭa ādau prasiddham yat sādhyam tad abhāvaḥ mayā sādhyate iti ced kartṛ janya tvam anugatam api pakṣa dharma tā balena aprasiddham kartāram adāya paryavasyati tad abhāvaḥ tu prasiddhasya kartuḥ abhāvam ādāya siddhyati na aprasiddhasya anugatasya api kartṛ janya tvasya tad abhāvasya ca kartṛ vyakti ghaṭita tvāt anyathā vyakti tad abhāva asiddhi prasaṅgāt na ca evam sat pratipakṣa uccheda prasaḍgaḥ tasya go tva ādi eka bhāva abhāva sādhaka viṣaya tvāt 
[094,v]	etena jñāna tvam na nitya vṛtti jñāna mātra vṛtti jāti tvāt smṛti tva vat jñānam na nitya guṇa vṛtti guṇa tva vyāpya jāti yogi cetana viśeṣa guṇa tvāt sukha vat ātmā na nitya viśeṣa guṇa ādhāra vṛtti dravya tva apara jātimān vibhu tvāt gagana vat iti ādi apāstam prasiddhe nitye vyoma ādau prasiddhāyāḥ ca rūpa tva jala tva ādi jāteḥ vyatireka viṣaya tvāt aprayojaka tvāt ca 
[094,vi]	kiñca kṣiti ādau śarīra ajanya tvam asiddham adṛṣṭa dvārā tad janya tvāt na ca adṛṣṭa advāraka janya jñāna ajanya tvam hetuḥ jñāne janya tva viśeṣaṇasya avyāvartaka tvena vyartha tvāt na ca sthāpanāyām pakṣa viśeṣaṇe api ayam doṣaḥ prameyaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti vat tad uparakta buddheḥ uddeśya tvāt api ca śarīrājanya tve vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam lāghavena ajanya tvasya eva vyāpta tvāt na ca niṣprayojana viśeṣaṇavat tvam asiddham vyāpti graha upayukta viśeṣaṇa vat pakṣa dharma tā aupayika viśeṣaṇasya api sa prayojana tvāt vyabhicāra vārakasya api sārthaka tve anumiti prayojaka tvasya eva bīja tvāt vyabhicāra vāraka viśeṣaṇavati ā iva vyāpti grahaḥ iti ced na nirviśeṣaṇe api go tva ādau vyāpti grahāt tatra api vyakti viśiṣṭe vyāpti grahaḥ iti ced na svatas vyāvṛtta go tvasya vyabhicārāt anyathā anyonya āśrayāt api ca vyabhicāra vāraka viśeṣaṇavati ā iva vyāpti grahaḥ iti aprayojakam sahacāra darśana ādi sattve tad abhāvena vyāpti graha avilambāt vyabhicārauvāraka viśeṣaṇa śūnyaḥ eva vyāpti grahaḥ iti ced na prameya tvena jñāyamāne dhūme vyāpti grahāt 
[094,vii]	atha tatra upātta vyabhicārāvāraka viśeṣaṇa śūnya tvam vivakṣitam na ca tatra prameya tvam viśeṣaṇam upāttam iti ced na virodhāt na hi tatra upāttam tena śūnyañca iti sambhavati yat viṣayaka tvena parāmarśaḥ kāraṇam anumitau tad liṣ gam prakṛte ca vyabhicārāt anyathā siddheḥ ca na viśeṣaṇa viṣayaka tvena tattvam iti ced na dhūmasya avyāpya tva āpatteḥ vyabhicārāt tad viṣaya tvena anumiti akāraṇa tvāt atha ekam avacchedakam aparatra vyāptiḥ yat vā lāghavena vyāsa jya vṛttiḥ ekā eva vyāptiḥ iti viśiṣṭa vyāpti arthaḥ tatra viśeṣya tāvacchedakasya vyāpti anavacchedaka tvena viśeṣaṇasya tad avacchedaka tvam iti niyamāt eka vṛtti tva bādhe sati eva vyāsajya vṛtti tvam iti vyāpteḥ ca na śarīra janya tva abhāve nīladhūma ādau ca vyāptiḥ iti viśeṣa mātre sā tathā ca svarūpa asiddhiḥ tad vāraṇa artham viśeṣaṇa abhidhāne vyāpya tva asiddhiḥ iti ced na avyabhicārasya anaupādhika tvasya vā viśiṣṭe nīladhūma ādau sattvena tad vyatireka sādhane bādhāt na ca viśeṣya tvam upādhiḥ sādhana vyāpaka tvāt 
[094,viii]	kañca saurabha viśeṣa vat dhūma rahitam idam candana prabhava vahni rahita tvāt nirdhūmaḥ ayam ārdra indhana prabhava vahni rahita tvāt iti ādau api kāraṇa viśeṣa abhāvena kārya viśeṣa abhāva anumānam na syāt vahnirahita tva ādi kañca upādhiḥ bhavet vyatirekiṇī aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravyān āśrita tvañca hetu abhāva vyāpyam na syāt dravya an āśrita tvasya eva vyāpya tvāt rūpa ādiṣu madhye gandhasya eva vyañcaka tvāt ityādau tvayā api asiddhi vāraka viśeṣaṇa svīkārāt ca api ca gauraveṇa viśiṣṭasya vyāpaka tā api na syāt tathā ca sthāpana anumāne upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna cikīrṣā ākṛti mat janyatā dhūmena ārdra indhana prabhava vahniḥ ghaṭa tvena śarīra janya tva ādikam na anumīyeta 
[094,ix]	yat tu janyā anyaḥ anya abhāva apekṣayā śarīra janyā anyonya abhāvasya alpa tvāt teṣām eva vyāpya tvam iti viparītam eva lāghavam iti tat na virodha abhāvena bahūnām alpasya ca vyāpya tvāt snehe śīta sparśavatu a jala tvayoḥ gandha abhāve apṛthivī tva pṛthivī tva abhāvayoḥ iva anyathā nīladhūmasya eva vyāpya tve dhūma mātrasya avyāpya tva prasaḍgaḥ kiñca tu ad naye vahni anyonya abhāva apekṣayā janya tva atyanta abhāvasya eva vyāpya tā syāt eka tvāt prameya tva ādi ananta dharma viśiṣṭasya vyāptau api prayojana abhāvāt na anumāne tad upanyāsaḥ 
[094,x]	atha lāghavena janya tvasya śīghra upasthitika tayā janyatā bhāva tvena śīghram vyāpti grahaḥ na tu śarīra janyā bhāva tvena vilambita pratītika tvāt yatra viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya anyatara abhāvavati sādhyam tatra viśiṣṭa abhāvasya api vyāptiḥ iti ced na evam sati utpattimat tve sati sattva ādikam anitya tva sa kartṛka tva vyāpya tayā na gṛhyeta śīghra upasthitika tayā ghaṭa tva ādeḥ eva tathātvāt yadi ca sāmānya viśeṣa abhāvāt virodha abhāvena ubhayasya api vyāpya tā tadā śarīra ajanya tva janya tva abhāvayoḥ api tulyam kiñca śarīra janya tvam viśiṣṭa tad abhāvam api viśinaṣṭi na tu sākṣāt tathā ca śarīra janya tva abhāvaḥ akhaṇḍaḥ eva hetuḥ atas na vyartha viśeṣaṇa tā na ca atra viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ viśeṣya abhāvaḥ eva kṣiti ādau ajanyata āpatteḥ atas eva sthāpanāyām śarīra janya tvam upādhiḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpya abhāva pratiyogi tvena sādhya vyāpaka tva niyamāt vyartha viśeṣaṇe adhikam nigraha sthānam iti ced na hetu dvaya upanyāse hi adhikam iha tu viśiṣṭam ekam eva hetuḥ iti viruddha sthale uktam iti 
[094,xi]	ucyate nīladhūma ādau vyāptiḥ asti eva anyathā viśeṣāṇām avyāpya tve nirāśrayā vyāptiḥ syāt nīla tvam api na vyāpya tāvacchedakam gauravāt kintu dhūma tvam eva daṇḍa tvena kāraṇa tve rūpam iva dhūma tvañca na nīlimni kintu tad āśraye dhūmaḥ iti na nīladhūmasya hetu tvam nīladhūme nīlasya viśeṣaṇa tve tad viśiṣṭe na dhūma tvam upalakṣaṇa tve ca dhūmāt eva anumitiḥ kiñca vyāpya tāvacchedakasya eva hetu tāvat chedaka tvam iti na nīladhūma tvam tathā na ca evam dhūma tvasya avacchedaka tve api sāmagrī sattvāt nīladhūmāt anum iti utpattau hetvābhāsa tvam na syāt anumiti pratibandhakasya tattvāt iti vācyam tad abhāve api nīla dhūma prayukta sādhya vat pratyayasya bhrama tvena tad kāraṇa tvasya ābhāsa tva sambhavāt iti diś evam śarīra janya tve api na śarīram avacchedakam gauravāt yena viśeṣaṇena vinā vyāptiḥ na gṛhyate tasya eva vyāpya tāvacchedaka tva niyamāt 
[095,i]	atas eva gandhasya eva vyañjaka tvāt iti atra aprasiddha tvena rūpa ādiṣu madhye iti viśeṣaṇam vinā vyāptiḥ grahītum na śakyate iti asiddhivārakam api viśeṣaṇam sārthakam eva surabhi dhūma viśeṣa ādau ca candana prabhava agni ādeḥ kāraṇa tvāt kāraṇa abhāvasya kārya abhāva prayojaka tayā vyāpya tva niścayaḥ vyāpake ca na vyartha viśeṣaṇa tā viśiṣṭasya kāraṇa tvena vyāpaka tvāt pariśeṣa vyatirekiṇi vipakṣa bādhakena ananya gatika tayā viśiṣṭasya vyāpaka tvāt viśiṣṭa abhāvasya hetu abhāva vyāpya tvam yatra ca vipakṣa bādhakam na asti tatra viśiṣṭasya vyāpaka tā api na yathā kāryasyat vi kartṛka tvena api śarīra janya tva abhāvaḥ akhaṇḍaḥ hetuḥ 
[095,ii^1]	yadi hi śarīra janya tvam sa kṛrtṛkatva prayojakam syāt tadā tad abhāva prayuktaḥ sa kartṛka tva abhāvaḥ iti tasya sādhya vyāpyatā syāt na ca evam kintu janya tvam lāghavāt tathā tathā aca ajanya tvam eva upādhiḥ sādhya vyāpya abhāvaḥ sādhya abhāva vyāpakaḥ iti niyamena tasya sādhya vyāpaka tā niścayāt sa kartṛka tva śarīra janya tvayoḥ vyāpti abhāvena tad abhāvayoḥ api vyāpti abhāvaḥ iti vyāpya tva asiddha tvāt ca atas eva śarīra janya tva abhāvasya akartṛka tva vyāpya tvāt tad abhāvayoḥ api vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ iti nirastam śarīra janya tvasya sa kartṛkatva aprayojaka tvāt na ca akartṛka tvam pūrva sādhana vyatireka tvena na upādhiḥ 
[095,ii^2]	sat pratipakṣa uccheda prasaṅgāt iti vācyam sthāpanāyāḥ yatra ābhāsa tvam tatra viśeṣa adarśana daśāyām sat pratipakṣe pūrva sādhana vyatirekasya sādhya avyāpaka tvena anupādhika tvāt yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ guṇa tvāt iti atra śabdaḥ nityaḥ vyoma eka guṇa tvāt iti anena sat pratipakṣe guṇa tva abhāvaḥ na upādhiḥ jala paramāṇu rūpe sādhya avyāpaka tvāt na ca evam anaikāntika tvam eva tatra udbhāvyam sat pratipakṣam upekṣya tasya udbhāvanā anarha tvāt kiñca prāc abhāva pratiyogi tve sati samaveta tvasya tad pratiyogi tve sati sattvasya sattve sati utpattimat tvasya vā hetu tve eṣām anyatama vyatirekaḥ upādhiḥ iti na pūrva sādhana vyatirekaḥ atas eva ajanya tvasya na upādhi tvam dhvaṃse sādhya avyāpaka tvāt iti na doṣaḥ 
[095,iii]	anye tu yat niṣṭhā yat nirūpitā ca vyāptiḥ yena viśeṣaṇena vinā na gṛhyate tatra viśiṣṭam vyāpya tāvacchedakam akartṛka tva nirūpita abhāva niṣṭha vyāptau ca śarīram vinā eva pratiyogi tayā janya tvam avacchedakam kḷptam iti na śarīra janya tvam avacchedakam dhūme nīladhūma tvam iva ati gauraveṇa śarīra janya tvam apratiyogi tayā ca janya tvam na avacchedakam iti vyāpya tāvacchedaka abhāvāt na śarīra janya tva abhāvaḥ akartṛka tva vyāpyaḥ vyabhicāra abhāvāt tathā iti ced na kṣiti ādau eva vyabhicārāt anyathā kṣiti ādikam na adṛṣṭa hetukam śarīra janya tva abhāvāt ityādi api syāt 
[095,iv_095,v]	nanu astu tāvat aśarīra nitya jñāna ādi kartṛ anumitiḥ tathā api sa anumitiḥ ayathārthā aśarīre kartṛ tva jñāna tvāt jñāna icchā prayatneṣu nitya jñāna tvāt śarīrājanye sa kartṛka tva jñāna tvāt ghaṭaḥ kartā ghaṭa jñāna ādikam nityam vyoma sa kartṛkam iti jñāna vat iti sādhyam na ca upajīvya bādhaḥ anumitiḥ hi upajīvyā nanu astu tat yathārtha tvam api iti ced na kartṛ kāryayoḥ niru pādhi kārya kāraṇa abhāvena etasya aprayojaka tvāt anyathā parvate vahni anumitiḥ ayathārthāḥ ubhaya siddha vahnimat bhinne vahni jñāna tvāt ityādinā sakala anvaya vyatireki u chedaḥ 
[095,vi]	kiñca anumiteḥ ayātha arthyam anena jñāpyam na tu kāryam tathā ca doṣāt utpannasya anena jñāpane tatra ayam eva doṣaḥ doṣa antaram vā na ādyaḥ anyonya āśrayāt utpanne tasmin jñāpanam jñāpakāt eva ca tasmāt doṣāt tad utpattiḥ iti na antyaḥ asiddheḥ tarka apariśuddhiḥ tu na dūṣaṇam yadi īśvaraḥ kartā syāt śarīri syāt iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavān syāt prayojanavān syāt anitya jñānavān syāt kṣiti ādi yadi sa kartṛkam syāt śarīri kartṛkam syāt ityādi tarkāṇām viparyaye āśraya asiddhi vyartha viśeṣaṇa tva ādinā viparyaya aparyavasānena ābhāsa tvāt 
[095,vii]	nanu kṣiti ādau eka kartṛ siddhiḥ kutas eka kartṛka tvena vyāpti abhāvāt na ca lāghavāt tasya apramāṇa tvāt sa kartṛka tva pramāṇāt eva lāghava saha kṛtāt tad siddhiḥ iti ced na tāvat anumiti mātre lāghavam sahakāri vyabhicārāt māna abhāvāt ca na hi liḍga parāmarśe sati tad vilambena anumiti bilambaḥ yena tad sahakāri syāt na api laghu anumitau anyaḥ anya āśrayāt na api vyakti anumitau dhūmena vahnyā anumitau eka dvi hasta ādi saṃśaya abhāva āpatteḥ sādhaka abhāvena nānātva asiddhau kartṛ siddheḥ eva eka kartṛ siddhiḥ iti ced na eka tva sādhaka abhāvena ekatva asiddhau kartṛ siddhiḥ eva nānātva siddhiḥ iti asya api suvacana tvāt 
[095,viii]	atha yam artham anālambamāna anumitiḥ pakṣe na sādhya saṃsargam viṣayīkaroti sa pakṣa dharma tā balāt sidhyati na tu adhikam api tathā ca dvitīyam kartāram aviṣayīkurvati api kartāram viṣayīkaroti eva iti na dvitīyam avagāhate ekaḥ tu kartā sidhyati tad aviṣaya tve kartṛ viṣaya tā eva na syāt eka viṣaya tva abhāve nānā viṣaya tvasya api abhāvāt tad ghaṭita tvāt tasya iti ced evam tarhi kartṛ ekatvam api na viṣayaḥ syāt eka tva viṣaya tvam vinā api kartṛ viṣaya tva sambhavāt vastu gatyā ekaḥ sidhyati na tvaketvena iti ced na eka tva asiddhyā vastu gatyā ekaḥ iti jñātum aśakyatvāt tathā ca īśvare ekatva aneka tvayoḥ nitya saṃśayaḥ iti 
[095,ix]	ucyate yatra pramāṇe laghu guru viṣaya tā sambhavati tatra lādhava sahakāritā kāraṇa tā kārya tā vyāpya tā ādi grāhake pratyakṣe pravṛtti nimitta grāhake upamāne śabda śakti grāhaka anumāne tathāvidha pramāṇa mātre ca sakala tāntrikaiḥ sahakāri tva kalpanāt evam lāghavam eva gauravam iti jñāna anantaram bādhakam vinā laghūnām eva kāraṇa tva kārya tva vyāpya tva pravṛtti nimitta tva śabda śakya tvānām jñāna darśanāt tatra api lāghavān ādare śabda śakya tva ādi saṃśaye tad mūlaka vyavahāra ucchedaḥ vinigamaka abhāvāt saḥ ayam vicāram ārabhate lāghavañca tad aṅgam na aṅgīkurute iti mahat sāhasam
