[095,x]	nanu evam vastu gatyā nānā kartṛkeṣu ghaṭeṣu ghaṭa tvena kulāla kartṛka tva anumāne api bādhakānavatāradaśāyām lāghavāt eka kartṛ siddhiḥ syāt na ceṣṭāpattiḥ anumiti anantaram nānātva ekatve saṃśayāt iti ced na tatra api lāghavena kartṛ ā aikyam eva siddhyati tat sandehaḥ tu jñāna prāmāṇya saṃśayāt iti paścāt nānā kartṛka tva sādhaka pramāṇāt eva eka kartṛka tā anumānam tatra bādhyate na ca evam kṣiti ādi kartari api prāmāṇya saṃśayāt eka tva aneka tva saṃśayaḥ durucchedaḥ eka tve bādhakasya abhāvena prāmāṇya niścayāt na ca eka tva sādhaka abhāvaḥ eva bādhakaḥ anumiteḥ eva lāghava sahakāreṇa eka tva sādhaka tvāt 
[096,i]	anye tu kṣitikartā aṅkura kartra bhinnaḥ aśarīra kartṛ tvāt aṅkura kartṛ vat iti abheda anumānāt eka kartṛ siddhiḥ na ca kṣitikartā aṅkura kartṛ bhinnaḥ aṅkura akartṛ tvāt kulāla vat iti sat pratipakṣaḥ anitya jñānānām āśraya tvasya upādhika tvāt iti āhuḥ atra api aprayojaka tve bheda abhedayoḥ gaurava lāghave eva śaraṇam tathā api katham nitya sarva viṣaya jñāna siddhiḥ pakṣa dharma tā balāt iti ced vyāpaka tayā avagatasya pakṣa sambandha mātram pakṣa dharmāt hetoḥ sidhyati tathā ca pakṣe tad upādāna gocara jñāna mātram sidhyet na tu nitya sarva viṣaya jñānam tena rūpeṇa vyāpaka tva āgrahāt na ca yena vinā anupapattiḥ saḥ api viṣayaḥ vyatireki vilaya āpatteḥ 
[096,ii]	tatra prāñcaḥ yam artham anālambamāna anumitiḥ pakṣe sādhya sambandham na viṣayīkaroti sa pakṣa dharma tā balāt sidhyati iti anupapatti mūlakaḥ anvayī pratīta anupapattyā ca vyatirekī tad iha ana ādi dvi aṇuka ādi kārya pravāhasya pakṣa tve tad upādānasya anādi jñāna gocara tvam vinā na upādāna gocara jñāna janya tvam anādi kārya pravāhasya anumitiḥ ālambate anāditā eva ca nityatā sarva muktau api tat sattvam anādi bhāva tvāt pakṣa tad upādāna viṣaya tā eva ca sarva viṣaya tā lāghavāt tu tāvat viṣaya kamana ādi ekam eva jñānam sidhyati na tu nitya aniti ajñānāni iti 
[096,iii_096,v]	navyāḥ tu anitya jñāna ajanya tvena pakṣa viśeṣaṇāt jñānam sidhyat nityam eva sidhyati anitye bādhāt iti vācaspati miśrāḥ tu lāghavāt eka jñāna siddhau utpattim ataḥ anādi kārya pravāham pratyajanaka tvāt pariśeṣaṇa nitya jñāna ādi siddhiḥ niyata viṣaya tā ca jñānasya kāraṇa adhīnā kāraṇañca nitya jñānāt nivartamānam niyata viṣaya tām ādāya nivartate iti sarva viṣaya tva siddhiḥ iti ṣaṣ padārthī pratipādaka veda kartṛ tvena īśvarasya ṣaṭpadārthī gocara sākṣātkāra tvena vā sārvajñyam ghaṭa ākāśa saṃyoga ādikam prati īśvarasya kartṛ tvāt ghaṭa ādi gocaram api jñānam siddham iti kecid 
[096,vi]	nanu ghaṭa ādīnām katham īśvara kartṛka tvam bhavati ghaṭaḥ īśvarakartṛkaḥ kāryatvāt kṣiti vat iti anumānāt iti ced na ghaṭasya dvi kartṛka tayā tad dṛṣṭāntena kṣiti ādeḥ api dvi kartṛka tā āpatteḥ tathā ca ghaṭa vat kṣitiḥ kṣiti vat ghaṭaḥ iti īśvara ānantyam kārye kartṛ tvena kāraṇa tā na tu dvi kartṛka tvena iti ced tarhi na īśvara kartṛka tvena kāraṇa tā kintu kartṛ tvena iti mā evam jñāna ādīnām nitya tvena sarva viṣaya tā ghaṭa ādi upādāna viṣaya tvam api iti katham na teṣām ghaṭa ādi kāraṇa tā kulāla ādi jñāna tulya tvāt 
[096,vii]	tad āhuḥ ācāryāḥ paramāṇu adṛṣṭa adhiṣṭhātṛ siddhau jñāna ādīnām nitya tvena sarva viṣaya tve vema ādi adhiṣṭhānasya api nyāya prāpta tvāt na tu tad adhiṣṭhāna artham eva īśvara siddhiḥ iti aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ mattaḥ sarvam pravartate iti ādi āgamāt ca ayam arthaḥ adhyavaseyaḥ atha īśvarasya sarvajña tve sarva viṣaya bhrānteḥ jñāne īśvaraḥ api bhrāntaḥ syāt bhramasya iva tasya api bhrama viṣaya viṣayaka tvāt iti ced na rajata tva prakāraka jñānavān ayam iti jñānam na bhramaḥ abhrāntasya tathātvāt idam rajatam iti jñāne rajata tvam prakāraḥ tena sa bhramaḥ īśvara jñāne ca rajata tva prakāraka tvam prakāraḥ iti sa na bhramaḥ atas eva asmad ādiḥ api bhrānti jñaḥ na bhrāntaḥ iti 
[096,viii]	syāt etat prayojanam vinā katham īśvaraḥ pravartate sukhasya abhāvāt adharma abhāvena nirduḥkha tvāt karuṇayā pravartate iti ced tarhi para sukha duḥkha prahāṇe prayojane tathā ca svargiṇam eva sṛjet na nārakiṇam dharma adharma paratantra tvāt tad anurūpam phalam prāpayati iti ced tarhi āvaśyaka tvāt karma nimittam eva jagat vaicitryam astu kim īśvareṇa anapekṣita kīṭa ādi jñānavatā karma nirapekṣa tve ca ekadā eva sadā ca sarga pralayau syātām jñāna ādīnām nitya tvāt kiñca tat prayatnasya karuṇā janya tvena śarīra ādi janya tva āpattau saṃsārita āpattiḥ iti 
[096,ix]	na īśvara anabhyupagame vicārasya āśraya asiddha tvāt tam abhyupagamya pṛcchasi ced tat ākarṇaya jagataḥ eva tad icchā viṣaya tvena sva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sattvāt vastutas tu kṣiti ādi tad tad asādhāraṇa kramikā dṛṣṭa ādi sāmagrī samavahitāḥ īśvara jñāna ādayaḥ yadā bhavanti tadā kṣiti ādikam karoti iti vyavahāraḥ sarga pralayāsa ādhāraṇa kramikā dṛṣṭa ādi sāmagrī samavahita tvam eva tad icchāyāḥ cikīṣā sañji hīrṣā tve na ca evam kim tad jñāna ādinā iti vācyam kṣiti ādīnām kāryatvena jñāna janya tayā nitya jñāna ādīnām api janaka tvāt sukha ādi śabdayoḥ ātma ākāśa ādi vat 
[096,x]	nanu aśarīrāt katham veda ghaṭa ādi śabda vyavahāra sampradāyaḥ ucyate sarga ādau adṛṣṭa upagṛhīta bhūta bhedāt mīna śarīra utpattau adṛṣṭa vat ātma saṃyogāt adṛṣṭa saha kṛta prayatna vat īśvara saṃyogāt vā sakala veda artha gocara jñānāt vivakṣā sahitān mīna kalevara kaṇṭha tālu ādi kriyā tad janya saṃyogāt veda utpattiḥ evam kulāla ādi śarīra avacchedena adṛṣṭa saha kṛta prayatna vat īśvara saṃyogāt tad buddhi icchā sahitāt ceṣṭā utpattau sakala ghaṭa ānukūla vyāpārāt ghaṭa utpattiḥ evam prayojya prayojaka jñānāya vyāpāra abhimata śarīra avacchedenā api adṛṣṭa sahakṛta īśvara jñāna icchā prayatnāt eva vāc vyavahāraḥ tatas tad darśī bālaḥ vyutpadyate saḥ ayam bhūta āveśa nyāyaḥ 
[096,xi_096,xii]	yat tu yathā lipya ādinā mauni ślokaḥ anumāya paṭhyate tathā sarga antara utpannatatva jñānavatā bhoga artham sarga ādau utpannena manu ādinā sarvajña īśvara abhiprāya sthaḥ vedaḥ sākṣātkṛtyā anūdyate tatas agrima sampradāyaḥ saḥ eva ca kāya vyūham kṛtvā ghaṭa ādi vāc vyavahāram pravartayati iti matam tat na pratisarga ādi ananta sarvajña kalpanāyām gauravāt teṣām eva kṣiti ādi kartṛ tva sambhavena īśvarān anumānāt ca etena sarga ādau sarga antara siddha yoginaḥ eva kṣitikartāraḥ santu iti parāḥ tam sarga ādau ananta sarvajña siddhiḥ ca kim pramāṇa antarāt kṣiti ādi kartṛ grāhakāt vā na ādyaḥ tad asambhavāt na antyaḥ anādi dvi aṇuka ādi kārya pravāhasya sa kartṛkatva anumānāt lāghava sahakṛtāt ekasya eva sarvajñasya siddheḥ 
[097,i]	atha īśvara jñāna mūlaka śabda śākti grahe prayojya vyāpāra anumita ghaṭa jñāne ghaṭa śabdasya kāraṇa tva grahaḥ bhramaḥ syāt tadīya jñānasya nitya tvāt tathā ca tad janya ghaṭa śabda śakti grahasya bhrama tve sa kala śābda jñānam bhramaḥ syāt bhrama paramparā mūlaka tvāt anitya sarvajña mūla ka śābda grahe ca na ayam doṣaḥ iti ced na vyāpāra anumitam idam ghaṭa jñānam ghaṭa pada janyam iti jñānasya śabda śakti graha kāraṇasya bhramatve api ghaṭa padam ghaṭa śaktam iti jñānasya yathārtha tvāt viṣaya ābādhāt na ca bhrama mūla tvena asya bhrama tvam anumeyam tad aṃśe vyadhikaraṇa prakāra abhāvena bādhāt bādhita viṣaya tvasya upādhi tvāt ca atas eva ghaṭam ānaya iti śabda anantaram sūtra sañcāra adhiṣṭhita dāru putrakasya ghaṭa ānayana vyavahāra darśanāt bālaḥ ghaṭa pade vyutpadyate tad mūla kaśābda jñānam api na bhramaḥ tasya api bhrama tve prayojya vyavahārāt idānīm vyutpattiḥ na syāt kim ayam prayojyaḥ cetana vyavahārāt vyutpannaḥ acetana vyavahārāt vā iti saṃśayasya vajra lepāya māna tvāt iti 
[097,ii_097,v]	viśvatas cakṣuḥ uta viśvatomukhaḥ viśvatas hastaḥ uta viśvataspād sam bāhubhyām dhamati sam patatraiḥ rdyāvā bhūmī janayan devaḥ ekaḥ ityādi śrutayaḥ uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ lokatrayam āviśya vibhatrti avyayaḥ īśvaraḥ ityādi smṛtayaḥ ca bahvyaḥ māna tvena anusandheyāḥ 
[097,vi]	syāt etat īśvara vat kāryeṇa eva śaktiḥ api anumīyate tathā hi yādṛśāt eva kara tala anala saṃyogāt dāhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśāt eva pratibandhake sati na jāyate atas yad abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ tat abhyupeyam vahni ādau tena vinā tad abhāva āyatta dāha abhāva anupapatteḥ iti vyatireka mukhena śakti siddhiḥ na ca adṛṣṭa vaiguṇyam dṛṣṭa sāt guṇye tad abhāvāt tasya tad artha tvāt anyathā dṛḍha daṇḍa nunnam api cakram na bhrāmyet 
[097,vii^1]	atha adṛṣṭa vilambāt api vilambaḥ yathā vandhyā strī samprayoge paramāṇu karmaṇi adhyayana tulya tve api ekatra phala abhāve ca iti ced na adṛṣṭa vilambaḥ hi na tad nāśān utpādau maṇi apasāraṇa anantaram dāha abhāva prasaḍgāt kiñca niyamataḥ maṇi sadbhāve kārya abhāvaḥ tad abhāve kāryam iti dṛṣṭa tvāt maṇi a ādi abhāvaḥ eva kāraṇam anyathā kadācimnaṇya ādi abhāve api tad abhāvāt kāryam na syāt vandhyā samprayoge tu dṛṣṭa vyabhicārāt adṛṣṭa vilambāt eva vilambaḥ adṛṣṭañca kvacid sākṣāt janakam anyathā paramparayā hetuḥ api na syāt na ca sama prajñayoḥ samañca nirantaram abhyastayoḥ ekaḥ pragalbhaḥ na aparaḥ iti dṛśyate na ca sarva utpattimatām adṛṣṭam nimitta kāraṇam agamyā gamana ādi sādhye sukhe vyabhicārāt tat hi na adharmāt sukha vat na api dharmāt tena hi agamyā gamanam utpādya 
[097,vii^2]	sukham utpādanīyam tathā ca agamya āgamana kāraṇa tvena na sa dharmaḥ śyena apūrvavat niṣiddha phalaka tvena anarthaka tvāt dāha pratikūlā dṛṣṭāt eva dāha abhāvaḥ iti ced na tasya uttejaka abhāva saha kṛta maṇya janya tve tatra ādāha arthinaḥ apravṛtti prasaṅgāt tat janya tve api tad utpādakāt eva dāha abhāvaḥ iti kim adṛṣṭena a prathama upasthita tvāt upajīvya tvāt ca pratibandhaka abhāva hetu tvasya tena abhyupagamāt adṛṣṭa utpattau śauca ācamana ādeḥ sādhāraṇasya atra api anvayaḥ syāt aśuceḥ eva tad utpattau śauce sati tad abhāva āpatteḥ pratipakṣa sannidhāpaka adṛṣṭasya eva pratibandhaka tve sati maṇya prayoge api dāha anāpattiḥ agrima kāle eva sannidhi darśanena tad asiddhi abhāvāt 
[097,viii]	astu tarhi uttejaka abhāva saha kṛta pratibandhaka abhāvasya anvaya vyatirekābhyām hetu tvam evam kevala uttejaka sadbhāve ubhaya sattve ubhaya abhāve ca viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ anugataḥ hetuḥ tat ca maṇi a ādi abhāva tvena na tu pratibandhaka abhāva tvena iti na anyonya āśrayaḥ atas eva pratibandhaka tva abhimata maṇya ādīnām abhāvakūṭaḥ eva kāraṇam tena maṇi sadbhāve mantra ādi abhāve ca na kāryam anatirikta abhāva vādi mate ca vyavahāra artham tad sthāna abhiṣiktasya hetu tvam na ca abhāvaḥ na kāraṇam bhāvavat tad grāhaka taulyāt dṛṣṭañca kuḍya saṃyoga abhāvasya gatau anupalambhasya abhāva vijñāne vihita akaraṇasya pratyavāye nirdoṣa tvasya veda prāmāṇye janakatvam iti prāñcaḥ 
[097,ix_097,x]	mā evam viśiṣṭam hi na artha antaram yena tad abhāvaḥ anugataḥ syāt kintu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandhāḥ iti teṣām pratyeka abhāvasya hetu tve kvacid viśeṣya maṇya bhāvaḥ kvacid uttejakā bhāva rūpa viśeṣaṇa abhāvaḥ kvacid ubhayaḥ kāraṇam iti vyabhicāreṇa na ekam api hetuḥ syāt syāt etat pratiyogi bheda ādi vat pratiyogi ta avacchedaka viśeṣaṇa bhedāt api abhāvaḥ bhidyate anyathā pṛthivī ādi traya pratyeka rūpa abhāve avagate api vāyau rūpa saṃśayaḥ na syāt evañca yathā kevala daṇḍa sadbhāve daṇḍa puruṣa sadbhāve dvaya abhāve ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya ubhaya viraha prayuktaḥ kevala puruṣa abhāvaḥ abādhita anugata vyavahāra balāt pratīti siddhaḥ tathā viśeṣyasya pratibandhakasya abhāve viśeṣaṇasya uttejaka abhāvasya abhāve ubhaya abhāve ca kevala pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa ubhaya abhāva vyāpakaḥ anugataḥ eva dāha akāraṇam astu 
[097,xi_098,i]	atha viśeṣaṇa ādi abhāvaiḥ eva kevala puruṣa ādi abhāva vyavahāraḥ eka śaktimat tvāt iti ced na anugata vyavahārasya anugata jñāna sādhya tvāt śakteḥ ca atīndriya tvāt atha uttejaka prayoga kāle maṇeḥ kaḥ abhāvaḥ na tāvat prāk pradhvaṃsa abhāvau tayoḥ pratiyogi asamāna kāla tvāt na ca śyāmaḥ ayam āsīt iti atra yathā śyāma dhvaṃsa prayuktaḥ śyāma ghaṭa tvena pakva ghaṭasya dhvaṃsaḥ eva na tu ghaṭa tvena tathā uttejaka abhāva dhvaṃsa prayuktaḥ uttejaka abhāvavat tvena maṇeḥ dhvaṃsaḥ eva iti vācyam dhvaṃsasya ananta tvena uttejaka apanaye api dāha prasaṅgāt na api atyanta abhāvaḥ tasya kādācid ka tva abhāvāt iti ced na yathā daṇḍa upanaya apanaya daśāyām kevala puruṣa abhāvaḥ utpāda vināśavān anyathā abādhita kevala puruṣa abhāva tad abhāva vyavahārayoḥ upapādayitum aśakyatvāt tathā uttejaka upanaya apanaya śṛṅkhalāyām pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ api tathā eva svīkaraṇīyaḥ tulya nyāya tvāt 
[098,ii]	yadi ca saṃsarga abhāva traya vaidharmyāt tatra na antarbhavati tadā turīyaḥ eva saṃsarga abhāvoḥ tu na hi kḷpta viśeṣa bādhe sāmānya bādhaḥ viśeṣa antaram ādāya api tasya sambhavāt anyathā kḷptānādi saṃsarga abhāva ādi vaidharmyeṇa dhvaṃsaḥ api na sidhyet vyavahārānyatha anupapattiḥ ca tulyā eva saḥ ayam asmākam sagotra kalahaḥ na tu śaktivādaḥ astu vā dhvaṃsaḥ eva asau saṃsarga abhāva vibhāge janyā bhāva tvena dhvaṃsasya vibhajanāt na ca evam vināśi tvena prāc abhāvaḥ eva saḥ paribhāṣāyāḥ aparyanuyojya tvāt yat vā atyanta abhāvaḥ eva asau tasya nitya tve api kādācid kā pratīti kārya anudayau pratyāsattikādācitka tvāt pratyāsattiḥ ca viśeṣaṇa abhāvaḥ viśeṣya abhāvaḥ ca tadā eva viśiṣṭa atyanta abhāva satvāt iti 
[098,iii]	tat na yadi hi atīta viśeṣaṇa avacchedena vidyamānasya eva viśeṣyasya dhvaṃsaḥ syāt tadā kṣaṇa rūpa atīta viśeṣaṇā avacchinna tvena pratikṣaṇam ghaṭasya vināśaḥ syāt iti kṣaṇa bhaṅga āpattiḥ kiñca vidyamānasya vinaṣṭa tvena apratīteḥ śikhā vinaṣṭā puruṣaḥ na vinaṣṭa iti viparīta ābādhita pratyayāt ca na viśeṣaṇa abhāve api viśeṣya dhvaṃsaḥ śyāmaḥ ayam āsīt kevalaḥ ayam āsīt puruṣaḥ iti ādau sa viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena viśeṣyavati śyāma kaivalya ādi dhvaṃsaḥ eva pratīyate dhvaṃsasya dhvaṃsa anupapatteḥ ca na vidyamānasya dhvaṃsaḥ 
[098,iv]	etena uttejaka sadbhāve sati uttejaka abhāva viśiṣṭa maṇeḥ utpanna dhvaṃsasya uttejaka apanaya samaye dhvaṃsaḥ jātaḥ adhvastaḥ ca dhvaṃsaḥ kāraṇam iti na viphalaḥ uttejaka apanayaḥ iti apāstam vidyamāna dhvaṃsasya ca dhvaṃsa abhāvāt na ca dhvaṃsa anyaḥ saṃsarga abhāvaḥ viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ iti vācyam utpanna abhāvasya vinaṣṭa pratīti hetu tayā tatas api vidyamānasya vinaṣṭa tva pratyaya āpatteḥ na api viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ tathā hi saḥ eva kvacid viśeṣaṇa abhāva sahitaḥ kvacid viśeṣya abhāva sahitaḥ dāha kāraṇam iti ananugamaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvayoḥ pratyāsatti tva avacchedaka anugata dharma abhāvāt 
[098,v_098,vi]	atha viśiṣṭa virodhi tvam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvayoḥ anugatam tad avacchedakam asti tayoḥ sattvaḥ eva viśiṣṭa atyanta abhāva sattvāt iti ced tarhi viśiṣṭa virodhi tvena anugatena tayoḥ eva hi viśiṣṭa abhāva tvena dāha vyavahāra ādau janakatvam astu kṛtam tad upajīvina atirikta viśiṣṭa abhāvena atha uttejaka kāle vidyamāna atyanta abhāva anuvṛttau api uttejaka apanayane uttejaka abhāva vyaktiḥ yā jātā tad avacchinna maṇeḥ abhāvaḥ na tatra iti tadā na kārya audayaḥ tad tad uttejaka abhāvānām ananugata tvena anugata viśiṣṭa abhāva vyavahāra anupapatteḥ uttejaka abhāva tvena anugame ati prasaḍgaḥ eva 
[098,vii_098,viii]	atha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvayoḥ viśiṣṭa viredhi tvam anugata kāraṇa tāvacchedakam yatra tad anyatara abhāvaḥ tatra na viśiṣṭam yatra viśiṣṭam tatra na tayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti saha anavasthāna niyamasya virodhasya anubhava siddha tvāt iti ced na saha anavasthāna niyamaḥ na paraspara viraha rūpa tayā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvasya pratyekam viśiṣṭa abhāva tayā tad pratyeka abhāva abhāvasya viśiṣṭa tva āpatteḥ tathā ca viśeṣya viśeṣaṇayoḥ pratyekam viśiṣṭa tva āpattiḥ tad abhāvasya tattvāt na ca ubhaya abhāva abhāvaḥ ubhayam viśiṣṭam evam hi abhāva dvayam viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ na tu pratyeka abhāva rūpaḥ iti pratyeka abhāvāt viśiṣṭa abhāva vyavahāraḥ na syāt nā api paraspara viraha vyāpya tvam tat ākṣepaka tvam vā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvasya viśiṣṭa abhāva tvena tat avyāpya tvāt tad anākṣepaka tvāt ca abhede tayoḥ abhāvāt 
[098,ix]	etena anyat api viśiṣṭa vyavahāra virodhi tva ādinā anugata tvam apāstam kena api anugatena rūpeṇa viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvasya viśiṣṭa abhāva tve pratyeka abhāva abhāvasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya anyatara mātrasya viśiṣṭa tva āpatteḥ tad abhāva abhāvasya tattvāt iti ukta tvāt tasmāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya abhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇa avacchinna viśeṣya abhāvaḥ na viśiṣṭa abhāvaḥ iti 
[098,x]	atra ucyate viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ sambandhāt viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ iti tayoḥ sambandha abhāvāt viśiṣṭa abhāva vyavahāraḥ iti ghaṭa tadabhāva vyavahārau iva ghaṭa sattva asattvābhyām na hi tayoḥ asambandhe viśiṣṭa vyavahāraḥ na vā tad abhāve sati na viśiṣṭa abhāva vyavahāraḥ yasya yatra yaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ eva tatra tasya vaiśiṣṭyam sa ca sambandha abhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇa abhāvāt viśeṣya abhāvāt ubhaya abhāvāt sarvatra aviśiṣṭaḥ ekaḥ teṣām vyāpakaḥ anugata viśiṣṭa abhāva vyahāra ādi kāraṇam iha daṇḍī puruṣaḥ na asti iti atra tathā darśanāt atas eva daṇḍa mātra sadbhāve daṇḍa puruṣa sadbhāve ubhaya abhāve ca kaivalya puruṣayoḥ sambandha abhāvaḥ sarvatra asti iti anugataḥ kevala puruṣa abhāva vyavahāraḥ evañca pratibandhaka uttejaka abhāvayoḥ sambandha abhāvaḥ dāha kāraṇam sa ca pratibandhaka abhāve pratibandhaka uttejaka sadbhāve ubhaya abhāve ca asti sarvatra pratibandhaka uttejaka abhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ na asti iti pratīteḥ 
[098,xi^1]	nanu evam yatra pratibandhaka uttejaka abhāvau tatra api dāhaḥ syāt adhikaraṇa bhāvayoḥ atirikta sambandha abhāvāt iti ced na tad abhāvaḥ api svarūpa sambandhasya abhāvāt sarvatra svarūpa sambandhāt eva adhikaraṇa abhāvayoḥ vaiśiṣṭya pratīteḥ tathā api pratibandhaka uttejaka abhāvau eva svarūpa sambandhaḥ tayoḥ abhāvaḥ ca pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ utteja kañca dāha kāraṇam tathā ca ubhaya abhāve uttejakā satve param dāhaḥ syāt uttejakavati pratibandhake dāhaḥ na syāt iti ced na adhikaraṇa abhāvau eva svarūpa sambandhaḥ tayoḥ ghaṭa vat bhū tala cattu arīya tada bhāvayoḥ api svarūpa sattve ghaṭavati ghaṭa abhāva vyavahāra āpatteḥ kintu upa śliṣṭa svabhāva tvam tat ca sambandha antaram vinā viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana yogya tvam na ca ghaṭa vat bhū tala catvarīya tadabhāvayoḥ viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana yogya tvam asti 
[098,xi^2]	ghaṭavati kadāpi ghaṭa abhāva pratyaya an udayāt tat iha api pratibandhaka uttejaka abhāvayoḥ viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana yogya tvam svarūpa sambandhaḥ anyathā uttejakavati pratibandhake catvarīya uttejaka abhāva viśiṣṭa pratyaya āpatteḥ tādṛśa svarūpa sambandha abhāvaḥ ca pratibandhaka abhāve pratibandhaka uttejaka sadbhāve ubhaya abhāve ca aviśiṣṭaḥ eva yat vā adaṇḍa puruṣasya abhāve daṇḍī puruṣaḥ na pratiyogī tasya adaṇḍa tva abhāvāt kintu tad anyaḥ tasya abhāvaḥ daṇḍi sadbhāve api daṇḍa mātra sattve ubhaya asattve ca aviśiṣṭaḥ iti tasmāt kevala puruṣa abhāva vyavahāraḥ anugataḥ 
[099,i_099,ii]	tat uktam na hi daṇḍini satya daṇḍānām anyeṣām na abhāvaḥ kintu daṇḍa abhāvasya eva iti yuktam anyathā tatra anyeṣām iti padasya vyartha tā āpatteḥ tathā kevala pratibandhaka abhāve uttejaka saha kṛtaḥ pratibandhakaḥ na pratiyogī tasya kevala tva abhāvāt kintu tad anyaḥ tad anyasya ca kevala pratibandhakasya abhāve uttejaka sahita pratibandhaka sattve uttejaka mātra sattve ubhaya asattve vā viśiṣṭaḥ eva iti na ananugamaḥ uttejaka apanaye ca kevala pratibandhakaḥ asti iti na tad abhāvaḥ iti dāhaḥ na bhavati iti 
[099,iii]	nanu na pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ kāraṇam eka daṇḍa anvaye ghaṭa utpatti vat pratibandhaka sattve api pratibandhaka antara abhāve api kārya anudayāt na hi yāvat kāraṇa tāvacchedaka avacchinnam tāvat anvaye api kāryam iti ced na pratibandhaka abhāva tvena na kāraṇa tvam anyaḥ anya āśrayāt kintu maṇi ādi abhāva tvena iti ukta tvāt tattve api vā ghaṭe daṇḍa salila ādi vat pratibandhaka abhāvakūṭasya dāha hetu tvāt yat vā pratibandhaka tva avacchinna pratiyogikaḥ eva abhāvaḥ kāraṇam sa ca yāvat viśeṣa abhāva niyataḥ iti na pratibandhaka sattve apara pratibandhaka abhāve api kārya udayaḥ pratibandhakasya ca saṃsarga abhāvaḥ hetuḥ tena tad sattve tad anyaḥ anya abhāve api na kāryam anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyāpti kāraṇa tvayoḥ grahe saṃsarga abhāvasya tvayā api hetu tva aṅgīkārāt anyathā sāmagrī vyāpakayoḥ sattve tad anyonya abhāve kārya vyāpya abhāva āpattau kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāve vyāghātāt 
[099,iv]	kiñca tava api pratibandhaka abhāve śaktiḥ asti iti tad sattve tad anyaḥ anya abhāvam ādāya śakti sattva prasaḍgaḥ na ca sa durvacaḥ na vā prāc abhāva ādi tvena ananugama vyabhicārau pratiyogi adhikaraṇayoḥ saṃsargam āropya yaḥ niṣedhaḥ sa saṃsarga abhāvaḥ bhū talam ghaṭa saṃsargaḥ na iti atra bhū tale ghaṭa saṃsargasya saṃsargaḥ na āropyate kintu tādātmyam 
[099,v]	vayantu brūmaḥ yatra pratiyoginam adhikaraṇe samāropya niṣedha avagamaḥ sa saṃrgā bhāvaḥ yatra ca adhikaraṇe pratiyogita avacchedakam āropya niṣedha avagamaḥ saḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ bhū talam na ghaṭaḥ iti atra bhū talasya ghaṭa tva avagamāt ghaṭa tvam eva ca ghaṭa tādātmyam āropasya hetu tve kim mānam iti ced mā bhūt tāvat anyat na idam iha na idam idam iti abādhita vilakṣaṇa vyavahārasya eva tatra māna tvāt iti 
[099,vi]	nanu pratibandhaka atyanta abhāvaḥ na hetuḥ tasmin sati api kārya abhāvāt na hi kara ādau maṇi ati anta abhāvaḥ tad saṃyoga atyanta abhāvaḥ vā maṇeḥ sva avayava vṛtti tvāt saṃyogasya ca avyāpya vṛtti tvāt atas eva na tad prāgabhāva pradhvaṃsau hetū tayoḥ kara ādau avṛtteḥ guṇa karma ādeḥ ca pratibadhya tva anāpatteḥ ca tasya janya dharmān āśraya tvena tatra tayoḥ abhāvāt na ca anyaḥ saṃsarga abhāvaḥ asti iti ced na saṃsarga avacchinna pratiyogikasya abhāva viśeṣasya sati pratibandhake abhāvāt sa ca samaya viśeṣa avacchedena saṃsargi tayā atyanta abhāvaḥ eva tathā eva anvaya vyatireka avadhāraṇāt 
[099,vii]	atha evam pradhvaṃsa prāgabhāva sthale samaya viśeṣa avacchinna atyanta abhāvena eva upapattau na tayoḥ siddhiḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ hi avyāpya vṛttiḥ tasya ca ekatra bhāva abhāve kvacid deśaḥ avacchedakaḥ kvacid kāle iti ced na tatra vidyamāna tā virodhi tvena eva kapāle na ghaṭaḥ iti pratīti vailakṣaṇyāt na tu evam bhū tale ghaṭa abhāva pratītiḥ 
[099,viii_099,ix]	anye tu bhaviṣyati ghaṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti vilakṣaṇa pratītyoḥ atyanta abhāvena ekena samarthayitum aśakyatvāt anyaḥ eva ayam saṃsarga abhāvaḥ iti api āhuḥ etena viśeṣaṇa abhāva viśeṣya abhāva tad ubhaya abhāva ghaṭitam sāmagrī trayam eva astu hetuḥ dāhe ca jāti traya kalpanam iti pratyuktam anugata hetu sattvāt dāha vaijātyasya yogyā anupalambha bādhita tvāt ca vyakti yogya tayā eva jāti yogya tvena yogye ayogya jāti abhāvāt 
[099,x]	nanu praharam mā daha ityādau sa avadhi mantra pāṭhe mantra vināśe dāhaḥ syāt na ca saṅkalpa viṣaya kāla viśeṣaḥ eva tatra pratibandhakaḥ saṅkalpa nāśe samayasya svatas aviśeṣāt na ca uddeśya tvam eva tatra viśeṣaḥ tasya vināśāt na ca uddeśya dhvaṃsaḥ api hetuḥ tasya yāmāt ūrdhvam api sattvāt na ca mantra pāṭha janitam adṛṣṭam eva tatra pratibandhakam tad kāla dāhā prāpti kapāla nāśya tvena na agre dāha apratibandhaḥ iti vācyam pratibandhaka mantra pāṭhasya aniṣiddha tvena avihita tvena ca adṛṣṭa ajanaka tvāt tad ācārasya vigīta tvena śruti ādi ananumāpaka tvāt iti ced 
[099,xi]	mā evam uddeśya tva jñāna āhita saṃskāra viṣaya kālasya pratibandhaka tvāt nanu pratibandham akurvata apratibandhaka tvena śaktim ana pakapakurvatām mantra ādīnām na pratibandhaka tvam atas śakti siddhiḥ na ca kārya anutpādaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ tad janaka tvam eva pratibandhaka tvam iti vācyam kārya anutpādaḥ hi tatra na tad prāc abhāvaḥ na vā tad uttara kāla sambandhaḥ tasya mantra ādyajanya tvāt iti ced na mantra ādīnām apratibandhaka tvāt tad prayoktāraḥ tu pratibandhakāḥ te ca kiñcitkarā eva mantra ādau ca kārye kāraṇa upacārāt svārthika kan pratyayāt vā tathā vyapadeśaḥ pratibandhaḥ ca sāmagrī virahaḥ mantra ādi abhāva ghaṭita sāmagrī virahaḥ ca mantra ādiḥ eva tad abhāva abhāvasya tattvāt 
[099,xii]	navyāḥ tu na pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ kāraṇam na vā śaktiḥ kintu tad tad kālīna dāha viśeṣam prati tad tad kāla pratibandha itara vahneḥ kāraṇa tvam iti pratibandhaka abhāvaḥ kāraṇa tāvacchedakaḥ na tu kāraṇam daṇḍa tva vat ākāśa ādau tu eka vyaktike na yathā kāraṇa tvam kvacid pratibandhe api anyatra śabda utpatteḥ kintu bherī ādeḥ tathā kāraṇa tvam iti tad pratibandhe na śabda utpattiḥ iti āhuḥ 
[099,xiii]	tat na vahni pratibandhaka abhāvayoḥ anvaya vyatireka taulyena ubhayasya api kāraṇa tvāt na tu ekam eva avacchedakam vinigamaka abhāvāt kiñca yasmin sati api yad abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ tasya kāraṇa tvam āyāti na tu tad avacchedaka tvam na hi kārya ayoga vyavacchedaḥ kāraṇa tvam kintu niyata pūrva sattvam tat ca sahakāri viraha prayukta kārya abhāve api akṣatam anyathā cakra sahita daṇḍa tvena kāraṇa tve saha kāri ucchedaḥ yasya yat dharmam avagamyā eva niyata pūrva sattvam agamyate tasya tad avacchedakam daṇḍa tvam iva sahakārī tu na tathā 
[100,i_100,ii]	nanu mā bhūt arthāpattiḥ śaktau mānam anumānantu syāt tathā hi sthiraḥ avayavī janaka daśā viśiṣṭaḥ vahniḥ ajana ka daśā vyāvṛtta bhāva bhūta dharmavān janaka tvāt kuṇṭha kuṭhārāt tīkṣṇa kuṭhāra vat dāhya asaṃyukta vahneḥ dāhya asaṃyukta vahni vat ca pratibandhaka sattve saṃyoga ādeḥ ajanaka daśa āvarti tvena tad atiriktā atīndriya bhāva bhūta dharma siddhiḥ yadi api śakteḥ bhāva hetu janya tvena na ajanaka daśā vyāvṛtta tvam tathā api ukta viśiṣṭāyāḥ tathā tvam yat vā dharme atīndriya tvam viśeṣaṇam na ca dṛṣṭānta siddhiḥ tulya ādhāra tve api loha viśeṣa ghaṭita kuṭhāre vilakṣaṇa chidā kriyā rūpa kārya balāt ati indriya tīkṣaṇa tva siddhiḥ 
[100,iii]	athavā tathābhūtaḥ eva vahniḥ kārya anukūlā atīndriyāt viṣṭha dharma samavāyī janaka tvāt ātma vat atīndriya tvañca yadi api na sākṣātkāra aviṣaya tvam anitya sākṣātkāra aviṣaya tvam yoga ja dharma ādyajanya sā akṣātkāra aviṣaya tvam vā param svam vā pratyasiddheḥ saṃyoga ādi pañcaka janya jñāna aviṣaya tvam aindriyakāṇām api tathā api saṃyoga ādi anyatara pratyāsati janya sākṣātkāra aviṣa tvam ubhayava ādi siddham anyataratvañca tat anya anya tvam na ca abhāva atīndriya tvam tasya asiddheḥ na ca vahnau sthiti sthāpake na artha antaram tatra tad abhāvāt kriyāyāḥ vegena adṛṣṭa vat ātma saṃyogena vega utpatteḥ na ca ātma tvam nitya tvam vā upādhiḥ sparśa eka tva ādimati dvi aṇuke sādhya avyāpaka tvāt 
[100,iv_100,v]	yat vā piṇḍībhūtaḥ vahniḥ dāha anukūlāt viṣṭhā ati indriya bhāva bhūta dharmavān dāha janaka tvāt ātma vat na ca ātma tvam upādhiḥ adṛṣṭa tvasya dāha anukūla tvena adṛṣṭe sādhya avyāpaka tvāt athavā kara vahni saṃyogaḥ kārya anukūlā atīndriya dharma samavāyī janaka tvāt ātma vat dvi aṇuka vat ca na ca ātma tvam dravya tvam vā upādhiḥ dvi aṇuka eka tva sparśa ādau sādhya avyāpaka tvāt yat vā pratibandhaka daśāyām pratyakṣa sakala dāha hetu samavahitaḥ dāha ajanakaḥ vahniḥ janaka daśā vṛtti kārya anukūla bhāva bhūta dharma śūnyaḥ ajanaka tvāt kuṇṭha kuṭhāra vat yat vā tathābhūtaḥ vahniḥ dāha janaka daśā vṛtti dāha anukūla bhāva bhūta dharma śūnyaḥ dāha ajanaka tvāt dāhyā saṃyukta vahni vat anukūla tvañca kārya abhāva prayojaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam kāraṇa tad avacchedaka sādhāraṇam dṛḍha daṇḍa tvena kāraṇa tve dṛḍha tva abhāvāt api kārya abhāva darśanāt iti 
[100,vi]	ucyate sādhyam vinā api ubhaya siddha pratibandhaka abhāvāt eva janakatvā ādi hetu sambhavāt vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvena anumānānām aprayojaka tvam yadica sahacāra darśana vyabhicāra adarśana upādhi anupalambha mātrāt eva vyāpti grahaḥ tadā śakti siddhi anantaram tena eva hetunā sādhye śakti atirikta tva prakṣepeṇa śa dvitīya ādi tādṛśa dharmam vinā api prathama anumita śaktyā eva janakatvā ādi upapatteḥ na tādṛśa ananta dharma siddhiḥ iti ced hanta evam śaktim vinā api tad artha siddheḥ kim śaktyā yat hi īśvara anantya vat na śakti ānantyam iti uktam tad abodhāt kārya mātre hi kartṛ tvena kāraṇa tvam na tu īśvara tvena dvi kartṛka tva ādinā vā gauravāt ghaṭe tvā arthaḥ samājaḥ 
[100,vii]	evam ajanakadaśā vyāvṛta tvena eva prayojaka tvam na tu bhāva bhūta tvena iti gauravāt api ca bhāva kārya mātrasya samavāyi kāraṇa janya tvena śakteḥ api tathā tvāt śakti anukūlā śaktiḥ aparā samavāyi kāraṇe mantavyā evam sā api samavāyi kāraṇa janyā iti tad anukūla śakti svīkāre śakti anavasthā kiñca prathama anumāne ajanaka tvam na svarūpa ayogya tvam vahnau kuṭhāre ca tad abhāvāt kintu kārya anupadhānam 
[100,viii]	tathā ca tad anupadhāna daśā ayam api vahnau śaktiḥ kuṭhāre taikṣṇyam iti bādhaḥ dṛṣṭānta asiddhiḥ ca loha viśeṣāṇām eva sa atiśayāt chidājanaka tvam iti na ati indriya taikṣṇya siddhiḥ agrima caturṣu bahis indriya apratyakṣa tvam upādhiḥ tulya yogakṣema tve api sandigdha upādhi tvena dūṣaka tvāt api ca janakatvasya kevala anvayitvena vyatireka aprasiddhyā na anvayavyatirekī na ca janakatva abhāvasya śaktau eva prasiddhiḥ anyonya āśrayāt na ca guru vacana paramparātaḥ eva vākya artha tayā tad siddhiḥ tu ad naye siddhārthasya apramāṇa tvāt na ca parārdha saṅkhyāyām sādhya janaka tva vyatirekayoḥ prasiddhiḥ apratyakṣāyāḥ śabda eka vedyāyāḥ tasyāḥ pratyakṣeṇa sādhya hetu vyatirekayoḥ grahītum aśakyatvāt 
[100,ix_100,x^1]	etena paṇḍā pūrve api tad siddhiḥ apāstā syāt etat tṛṇa araṇi maṇīnām vahnau kāraṇa tvāt eka śaktima tvam upeyam eka jātīya kārye eka jātīya kāraṇa tva niyamāt vahni avāntara jātīye teṣām pratyekam kāraṇa tvam iti ced na vahni jātīyasya akasmika tā āpatteḥ kāraṇa gata eka rūpam apahāya kārya gata bahutara rūpa kalpane gauravāt tṛṇa araṇi maṇi prabhava vahniṣu avāntara jāteḥ anupalambha bādhi tvāt ca yatra ca tad tad indhana prayojyam pradīpa dāru dahana ādau vaijātyam anubhūyate tatra kāraṇeṣu eka śaktimat tvam api na asti kiñca gomaya vṛścika prabhava vṛścika ādiṣu vaijātya kalpane tad prabhava vṛścikeṣu api vaijātyam kalpyam evam tad prabhava tad prabhaveṣu api iti vaijātya ānantyam 
[100,x^2]	vijātīya kāraṇānām vijātīya kārya janaka tva niyamāt na ca tayoḥ na ekaḥ vṛścikaḥ buddhi vyapadeśayoḥ aviśeṣāt yadi vijātīyeṣu eka kārya śakti samavāyāt na kārya viśeṣāt kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ tad abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ kvāpi anumīyeta tad abhāve api tad jātīya śaktim ataḥ anyasmāt api tad utpatti sambhavāt iti ced vahni vṛścika ādau evam etat nirūpita niyata vahni ādi kāraṇaka dhūma ādau kutas na tad anumānam anyathā kārya vaijātye api tṛṇasya vahni viśeṣaḥ iva vahni tvena dhūma viśeṣaḥ eva kāraṇa tvam na tu dhūma mātre tṛṇa ādi prabhava tva graha anantaram vahni avāntara jāti graha vat vahni tadajanya janya tva jñāna anantaram dhūmāvāntara jāti grahaḥ bhaviṣyati iti api āśaṅkyeta bādhakam vinā dhūma tvena vahnikārya tā iti ced tarhi bādhakam vinā dhūmam prati bahni tvena kāraṇa tā iti api tulyam 
[100,xi_100,xii]	yat tu tṛṇa tvena kāraṇa tva c rahasya upajīvya tvāt tat rakṣā artham vahnau jāti viśeṣaḥ eva kalpyate iti tat na vahni tvena kāryatva grahāt tad rakṣā artham tṛṇa ādau śakti kalpanā aucityāt yathā ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām tṛṇa phūtkārayoḥ paraspara sahakāri tvam tathā eva tad śaktyoḥ api paraspara sahakāri tvena vahni anukūla tvam tathā eva kārya darśanāt evam tṛṇa araṇi maṇi phūtkāra nirmantha nataraṇi kiraṇānām vahni anukūla śaktima tvena kāraṇa tve api phūtkāreṇa tṛṇāt eva nirmanthanena āraṇeḥ eva pratiphalita taraṇi kiraṇaiḥ maṇeḥ eva agni utpattiḥ na tu maṇi phūtkāra ādibhyaḥ maṇi phūtkāra śaktyoḥ paraspara sahakāri tva virahāt yat tu tṛṇa phūtkāra ādi stoma traye viśiṣṭe śaktiḥ iti tat na tṛṇa tvena gṛhīta kāraṇa tā bhaṅga prasaṅgāt iti 
[101,i]	ucyate tṛṇa raṇimaṇi phūtkāra ādi vyaktīnām ānantyena prativyakti bhāva hetu janita ananta śakti svīkāre gauravam tāvat ananta vyakti janya ananta vahni vyaktiṣu jāti kalpane lāghavam iti tat eva kalpyate na ca jātau yogyā anupalabdhi bādhaḥ gomaya vṛścika prabhava vṛścikayoḥ īṣat nīlatva kapila tva vyaṅgya vaijātyasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt tṛṇa janya nānā vahni vyaktiṣu tṛṇa janya tva jñāna anantaram maṇi janya vyāvṛtta anugata buddhiḥ asti jāti viṣayā tṛṇa janya tvena upādhinā sā iti ced na bādhakam vinā anugata buddheḥ tat vyaṅgya jāti viṣaya tva niyamāt na ca gomaya vṛścika prabhava vṛścika paramparāyām ananugata jātyāpattiḥ gomaya janya vṛścika prabhava vṛścikeṣu vṛścika prabhava tu ajāteḥ sattvāt vahni mātre ca dāha sparśavān avayavaḥ tad saṃyogaḥ pavana ādiḥ ca kāraṇāni na ca tṛṇa ādikam vinā api tad utpatti prasaḍgaḥ viśeṣa sāmagrīm ādāya eva sāmānya sāmagryāḥ janakatvāt 
[101,ii]	nanu tṛṇa araṇi maṇīnām vahnau kāraṇa tva grahe śakti vaijātyayoḥ anyatara kalpanam tad grahaḥ ca na anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyabhicārāt atha araṇi maṇī abhāvavati stoma viśeṣe tṛṇam vinā vahni vyatirekaḥ tṛṇa anvaye vahniḥ iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām tatra eva stome tad itarasakala hetu samavadhāne tṛṇa anvaye avaśyam vahniḥ iti niyata anvayena rāsabha ādi vyāvṛttena tṛṇa ādi kāraṇa tā grahaḥ iti ced na tṛṇam vinā api vahniḥ iti jñāne sati vahni niyata pūrva varti tvasya kāraṇa tvasya grahītum aśakyatvāt tṛṇājanye vahnau maṇeḥ kāraṇa tva grahaḥ iti ced na vyabhicāreṇa vahnau tṛṇa janya tva agrahe tad ajanya tvasya api agrahāt vahni mātrasya eva tad ajanya tvāt ca na ca maṇyajanya tvena tṛṇa janya tva grahaḥ anyaḥ anya āśrayāt 
[101,iii_101,iv]	yat tu yatra kāraṇa tā grāhakam na asti tatra vyabhicāraḥ tad graha paripanthi iti tat na abādhita niyata pūrva varti tva abhāva grahe tad grahasya asambhavāt abhāva pramāyām bhāva jñāna anudayāt iti ucyate ukta grāhakaiḥ vahni niṣṭha kārya tā nirūpita kāraṇa tāvacchedaka rūpavat tvam tṛṇasya tṛṇa niṣṭha kāraṇa tā nirūpita kārya tāvacchedaka rūpavat tvam vahneḥ vā akārya akāraṇa vyāvṛttam rūpam paricchidyate na tu tṛṇa tvena kāraṇa tvam vahni tvena kārya tvam vā tat ca ubhayathā api sambhavati vahni tvena kārya tayā tad anukūla śaktima tvena ca tṛṇa ādīnām kāraṇa tayā vahni tva avāntara jāti viśeṣeṇa kārya tayā vā tatra vinigamakam uktam eva 
[101,v_101,vi]	atha tṛṇa araṇi maṇīnām abhāva traye na kāryam abhāva traya abhāve kāryam iti anvaya vyatireka abhyām abhāva traya abhāva tvena tṛṇa ādīnām kāraṇa tvam iti na vyabhicāraḥ abhāva abhāvasya bhāva paryavasanna tvāt iti ced abhāva traya abhāvaḥ kim tṛṇa ādi pratyeka vyāpakaḥ anyaḥ eva uta tṛṇa ādi pratyekam eva ādye abhāvasya kāraṇa tvam iti kim āyātam tṛṇa ādi kāraṇa tve dvitīye tṛṇasya na araṇi maṇya bhāva abhāva tvam tad ubhaya tva āpatteḥ etena abhāva traye na kāryam tad abhāve kāryam iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām tṛṇa ādi pratyekasya kāraṇa tva grahaḥ iti parāḥ tam 
[101,vii]	syāt etat mā bhūt sahaja śaktiḥ ādheya śaktiḥ tu syāt eva tathā hi vrīhīn prokṣati iti atra kāla antara kārya anukūlaḥ atīndriyaḥ atiśayaḥ prokṣaṇa janyaḥ asti iti ubhaya vādi siddham sa vrīhi samavetaḥ na vā iti saṃśaye vrīhi niṣṭhaḥ eva vācyaḥ katham anyathā prokṣitānām eva teṣām kāla antare avaghāta ādau viniyogaḥ na ca mantra ādi saha kṛta tvam eva vrīhiṣu viśeṣaḥ teṣām cira dhvasta tvāt 
[101,viii]	nanu katham prokṣitasya eva avaghāta ādau anyaḥ vrīhīn avahanti iti śruteḥ tad mātra anvaye api upapatteḥ atha vrīhibhiḥ yajeta vrīhīn prokṣati vrīhīn avahanti puroḍāśaiḥ yajeta iti atra yathā puroḍāśe prakṛti apekṣāyām avahata vrīhīṇām avayava anuvṛtti dvāra anvayaḥ prokṣaṇe ca yāga artham upātta vrīhiṇām tathā avaghāte vrīhi ākāṅkṣāyām prokṣitānām eva anvayaḥ bādhakam vinā śabdānām sannihita viśeṣa paratva niyamāt vyakti vacanānām sannihita viśeṣa paratvam iti nyāyāt anyathā prakaraṇa ādi sannihita tyāge tad anya sannidhi kalpane gauravam iti ced 
[101,ix]	na tarhi ekasya dvayam yatra prokṣaṇam tatra avaghātaḥ na tu prokṣaṇa viśiṣṭe yatra rūpam tatra rasaḥ iti vat tathā ca prokṣaṇasya śabdena kāla antara kārya janakatvā bodhāt katham tat nirvāha artham atiśaya kalpanam prokṣitāḥ vrīhayaḥ avaghātāya kalpante iti vākya śeṣāt prokṣaṇa viśiṣṭasya avaghāte kāraṇa avabodhaḥ iti ced astu tāvat evam tathā api prokṣitāḥ iti atra bhūte kta anuśāsanāt atīta prokṣaṇe vrīhau avaghāta anvayaḥ tathā ca avaghāte prokṣaṇa dhvaṃsaḥ kāraṇam na tu prokṣaṇam iti ced 
[101,x]	mā evam prokṣaṇam avaghāta janakam pramāṇataḥ tad artham upādīyamāna tvāt avaghāte vrīhi vat na ca asiddhiḥ aprokṣite avaghāta abhāvat avaśyam avaghāta artham prokṣaṇa upādānāt na ca vyāpāram vinā tathā sambhavati na ca prokṣaṇa dhvaṃsaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ pratiyoginaḥ ahetutva āpātāt anyathā yāga ādau api tathā syāt phalasya ca niyata samaya utpattika tvam apūrvavat svabhāvāt eva bhaviṣyati na ca prokṣitāḥ vrīhayaḥ tathā niranvaya dhvasta tvena upalakṣaṇasya ahetutvāt kurūṇām kṣetram iti atra tu kuru jñānasya itara vyāvṛtta kṣetrajña vyavahāra janaka tvam na tu kuroḥ anyathā yāga upalakṣitaḥ yajvā eva svargam phaliṣyati kim apūrveṇa na ca devadatta ādi a śarīram devadatta viśeṣaṇa guṇa janyam janya tve sati tad bhoga sādhana tvāt tat nirmata sragvat iti tad siddhiḥ janma antarīyaiḥ adṛṣṭa janaka tva abhimataiḥ jñāna icchā prayatnaiḥ siddha sādhanāt 
[101,xi]	tasmāt prokṣaṇa ādayaḥ bhāva bhūtam atiśayam janayantaḥ eva kāla antara bhāvi kārya janakāḥ pramāṇataḥ tad artham upādīyamāna tvāt roga cikitsā vat sa ca atiśayaḥ lāghavāt phala samāna adhikaraṇaḥ iti vrīhi niṣṭhaḥ eva tena tad samavahita tvam vrīheḥ sākṣāt sambandhāt puruṣa niṣṭhatvena ca vrīhīṇām sākṣāt sambandha abhāvāt paramparā sambandhe gauravāt na sākṣāt vrīhi samavahita tvam syāt kiñca yaḥ yat gata phala arthi tayā kriyate sa bādhakam vinā tad gatam eva tat anukūlam atiśayam janayati roga cikitsā vat atha prokṣaṇam puruṣa samaveta atiśaya janakam kāla antara bhāvi kārya janaka tve sati vihita tvāt yāga vat anyathā vidhi virodhāt iti ced na kṛṣi cikitsā ādinā vyabhicārāt aprayojaka tvāt ca tena vinā api vidhi sambhavāt sa ca prativrīhi nānā eva na ca evam eka vrīhi nāśe phalān udayaḥ tāvat saṃskāraṇām abhāvāt iti vācyam saṃskāra tvena prayojaka tve kiñcid samavadhāne api daṇḍa ādi vat kārya sambhavāt 
[102,i_102,ii]	astu vā sakala vrīhi niṣṭhaḥ ekaḥ eva na ca eka vrīhi nāśe tad nāśāpattiḥ kiñcid āśraya nāśasya vṛkṣa ādau ivakārya nāśaka tvāt iti ucyate atiśaya grāhaka mānāt lāghava sahakṛtāt saḥ ekaḥ eva sidhyati na nānā puruṣa niṣṭhaḥ ca tathā hi prokṣaṇam apūrva janakam dṛṣṭa dvāra abhāve sati kāla antara bhāvi kārya janakatayā vihita tvāt yāga tad aṅga vat kṛṣi ādau dṛṣṭa dvāra sambhavāt na vyabhicāraḥ na vā aprayojaka tvam yāgadāna homa ādi tad aṅgānām apūrva janaka tve dṛṣṭa dvāra abhāvesati kāla antara bhāvi kārya janakatayā vihita tvasya eva prayojaka tvāt anyasya ananugamāt na ca yaḥ yat gata phala arthi tayā kriyate sa bādhakam vinā tad gatam eva tat anukūlam phalam janayati iti niyamaḥ śatru vadham uddiśya pravartite śyena yāga ādau vyabhicārāt vipakṣe bādhaka abhāvāt ca na ca yat uddeśena yat kriyate na tat tatra bhāvi kāryā anukūlā atiśaya janakam iti vyāptiḥ haviḥ tyāga ādibhiḥ vyabhicārāt 
[102,iii]	nanu prokṣita vrīhiṇā adṛṣṭasya janita tvāt barhiṣaḥ iva na tasya punar upayoga antaram syāt viniyukta viniyoga virodhāt upayoge vā tad jātīya antaram api upādīyeta aviśeṣāt na vrīhīn avahanti iti atra ukta nyāyena prokṣitasya eva vrīheḥ anvayāt vidheḥ durlaṅghya tvāt yathā barhiḥ tṛṇāti barhiṣi haviḥ āsādayati iti atra yat vā vicitrāḥ saṃskārāḥ kecid uddeśya sahakāriṇaḥ eva agrima kārya kāriṇaḥ yathā abhicāra saṃskāraḥ yam deham uddiśya prayuktaḥ tad apekṣaḥ eva tad sambaddhasya eva duḥkham janayati tathā prokṣaṇa saṃskārāḥ api uddeśya vrīhi saha kṛtāḥ eva agrim a kārya kartāraḥ yathā kārīri janita saṃskāra ādhāra puruṣa saṃyogāt jalam ucām a dṛṣṭa samavadhānam tathā prokṣaṇa janyā dṛṣṭa vat ātma saṃyogāt vrīhīṇām uttara kriyā viśeṣāḥ kartṛ karma sādhana vaiguṇyāt phala abhāvaḥ tulyaḥ eva āgāmika tvāt cāṇḍāla ādi sparśasya āhavanīya ādi saṃskāra nāśaka tva śruteḥ vyadhikaraṇasya api apūrva nāśaka tvam dharma nāśe karma nāśa apāra gamana vat niṣiddha kīrtana vat ca 
[102,iv]	kiñca prokṣaṇa janyā atiśayaḥ vrīhi niṣṭhaḥ na nānā ātma vṛtteḥ ekasmāt api ukta nyāyena kārya upapatteḥ na api ekaḥ eka dvitra āśraya nāśānām pratyekam ananugamena kārya nāśe āśraya mātra nāśasya janaka tvāt eva vrīhi nāśena tad nāśāt apara prokṣita vrīhīṇām ananvaya āpatteḥ atha vrīhin prokṣatīti īpsitatama dvitīya aśruteḥ kriyā janyā iṣṭa phala bhāgi tvam vrīheḥ eva avagamyate na ca apūrvasya vrīhi vṛtti tvam sākṣāt sambandhasya eva autsargika tvāt iti ced na dhātu artha tāvacchedaka saṃyogena vrīhikarma tā upapatteḥ na ca saṃyoga avacchinnaḥ eva vyāpāra viśeṣaḥ prokṣaṇa arthaḥ tathā ca katham prokṣaṇa eka deśasya prokṣaṇa sādhyatayā anvayaḥ iti vācyam saṃyogasya upalakṣaṇa tvena āpadārtha tvāt anyathā grāmam gacchati ityādau kā gatiḥ kā vā saktūn prokṣati ityādau tatra ādheya śakti abhāvāt 
[102,v]	kiñca ghaṭam sākṣātkaroti ityādau kriyā janya saṃskāra ādīnām ghaṭa vṛtti tvāt saṃskārasya svarūpa sambandhena ghaṭa vṛtti tvam vahnim anuminoti ityādi vat prayoga sādhuḥ eva vā dvitīyā iti yadi tadā prakṛte api tathā astu atha pratimā ādau pratiṣṭhā janyam na yajamāna adṛṣṭam pūjya tve prayojakam bhoga ādinā tad nāśe api pūjya tvāt tad sattve api cāṇḍāla ādi sparśena apūjya tvāt anya dharmam pratyanya dharmasya anupayogāt ca na ca pratiṣṭhā dhvaṃsaḥ tathā tatas eva upajīvya pratiṣṭhā prayojaka tva bhaṅga āpatteḥ ca tasmāt pratiṣṭhā janyāḥ aspṛśya sparśa ādi nāśyā pratimā ādi niṣṭhā śaktiḥ abhyupeyāḥ iti ced pratiṣṭhā vidhinā pratimā ādau devatā sannidhiḥ ahaṅkāra m amakāra rūpaḥ kriyate sva sādṛśya darśinaḥ citra ādau iva jñānasya nāśe api saṃskāra sattvāt aspṛśya sparśa ādinā ca tad nāśaḥ acetana devatā pakṣe ca yathā artha pratiṣṭhita pratyabhijñānasya aspṛśya sparśa ādi viraha saha kṛtasya tathātvam pratiṣṭhitam yūjayet iti vidhi balāt tad tad pratisandhānasya āvaśyaka tvāt iti prāñcaḥ 
[102,vi_102,vii]	navyāḥ tu pratiṣṭhā vidhinā eva tava ādheya śakti vat apūrva antaram janyate tad adṛṣṭa vat ātma saṃyoga aśrasya pūjya tvam aspṛśya sparśena tad nāśe ca apūjya tvam iti āhuḥ vayantu brūmaḥ pratiṣṭhitam pūjayet iti vidhi vākyena pratiṣṭhāyāḥ kāraṇa tvam na bodhyate kintu bhūta arthe kta anuśāsanāt atīta pratiṣṭhāyām pūjya tvam bodhyate tathā ca pratiṣṭhā dhvaṃsaḥ pratiṣṭhākā ālīnaya avada spṛśya sparśa ādi pratiyogikānādi kāla saṃsarga abhāva sahitaḥ pūjya tva prayojakaḥ sa ca prāc abhāvaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ ca kvacid kāminī caraṇa abhighāta dohada ādibhiḥ aśoka puṣpa utkarṣa darśanāt api na ādheya śakti siddhiḥ samaya viśeṣa avacchinna caraṇa dohat ādi saṃyoga dhvaṃsasya eva kāraṇa tvāt caraṇa abhighāta ādi ākṛṣṭa bhāga antara janita vṛkṣāt eva vā tad upapatteḥ kāla antare puṣpa ādi utkarṣāt vṛkṣa avayava upacaya avaśyambhāvena vṛkṣa bheda āvaśyaka tvāt na api tāmra kāṃsi a ādau astu bhasma saṃyoga ādi janya śuddhi rūpā ādheya śaktiḥ tad saṃyoga dhvaṃsasya saṃyoga samāna kālīna aspṛśya sparśa ādi pratiyogikayā vadana ādi saṃsarga abhāva sahitasya śuddhi padārtha tvāt 
[102,viii_102,ix]	bhasma ādi saṃyoga janitaḥ kāṃsya ādi upabhoga kartṛ niṣṭhaḥ saṃskāraḥ eva śuddhiḥ iti anye abhimantrita payaḥ pallava ādau api samaya viśeṣa avacchinna abhimantraṇa dhvaṃsaḥ eva vyathā ādi apanāyakaḥ tad tad mantra devatā sannidhiḥ eva vā kalama bīja ādīnām āparamāṇu anta bhaṅge tatra ca avāntara jāteḥ abhāve niyata kalama jātīya ādi siddhiḥ api paramāṇu pāka ja viśeṣāt eva kārya vṛtti rūpa ādi sajātīyasya pūrvarūpa vijātīyasya paramāṇau pākaja rūpa ādeḥ ubhaya siddha tvāt yathā hi kalama bījam yava ādeḥ jātyā vyāvartate tathā tad paramāṇavaḥ api pākajaiḥ eva evam māgha karṣaṇa ādi janitāt paramāṇu pāka paramparā viśeṣā deva haimantika sasya utpattiḥ 
[102,x]	etena lākṣā rasa avaseka ādayoḥ vyākhyātāḥ nimitta viśeṣa janita pāka jāt tad tad phala viśeṣaḥ yathā hārīta māṃsam harindra anala sādhitam upayogāt sadyas vyāpādayati na anyathā sādhitam ityādi yatra ca toya tejaḥ vāyuṣu na pāka jaḥ viśeṣaḥ tatra udbhavān udbhava drava tva kaṭhina tva ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ tad upanāyaka adṛṣṭa viśeṣāt eva tulā ādau ca adhivāsa ādi pūrvaka tulā ārohaṇa sāmagrī tulyasya satya asatya pratijña tva sahitā prācīna dharma adharma phale tad jaya bhaṅgau janayati yat vā aham niṣpāpaḥ pāpavān vā iti tulā adhirūḍha abhiśasta jñāna viśeṣa sahitā sā tathā 
[102,xi_102,xii]	tat āhuḥ tān tu devāḥ prapaśyanti svaḥ ca eva antara pūruṣaḥ iti atha vā pratijñā aśuddhi aśuddhī apekṣyatayā dharma adharmau janyete tābhyāñca jaya parājayau satya asatya pratijña abhiśasta tulā ārohaṇasya iṣṭā aniṣṭa phala tvena arthataḥ vidhi niṣedhāt abhiśastaḥ satya pratijñaḥ vijaya kāmaḥ tulām ārohet asati apratijñaḥ na tulām arohet iti śruteḥ unnayanāt yat vā tayā devatā sannidhiḥ kriyate tāḥ ca karma anurūpam liṅgam abhivyañcayanti 
[103,i_103,ii]	kaḥ tarhi śakti padārthaḥ kāraṇa tvam tat ca svasva vyāpi a itara sakala sampattau kārya abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam atha vā yatra kārya abhāva vyāpya tā itara abhāva avacchinnā tad kāraṇam bīje aṅkura abhāva vyāpya tā na bīja tvena avacchidyate itara sam avadhāne sati bījāt aṅkura sambhavāt ki yat vā anyāsam avadhāna avacchinna kārya an utpatti vyāpya tvam kāraṇa tvam rāsabha ādeḥ svatas eva kārya abhāva vyāpya tā anyāsam avadhānasya vaiyarthyena anavacchedaka tvāt ananyathā siddha niyata pūrva varti jātīya tvam vā tattvam 
[103,iii]	anyathā asiddha tvañca tridhā yena saha eva yasya yam prati pūrva varti tvam avagamyate yathā ghaṭam prati daṇḍa rūpasya anyam prati pūrva varti tve jñātaḥ eva yam prati yasya pūrva varti tvam avagamyate yathā śabdam prati pūrva varti tve jñātaḥ eva jñānam pratyākāśasya anyatra kḷpta niyata pūrva vartinaḥ eva kārya sambhave tad saha bhūta tvam yathā gandhavati gandha anutpādāt gandham prati tad prāgabhāvasya niyata pūrva varti tva kalpanāt pākaja sthale gandham prati na tu avagamyamāne yatra janyasya pūrva varti tve avagate janakasya pūrva bhāvaḥ avagamyate tatra janyena janakasya anyathā siddhiḥ 
[103,iv_103,vi]	yatra ca janakasya tathātve avagate janyasya pūrva bhāva avagamaḥ tatra tad dvārā tasya janaka tvam eva sati tu jāyate tad jātīyam prati tat ananyathā siddham ananyathā siddha niyata pūrva varti tvam kāraṇa tvam iti anye tat na īśvara tad buddhi ādīnām asaṃgrahāt tad vyatirekasya tad samavadhāna vyatirekasya vā abhāvāt kāryasya anyathā anupapadyamāna tā vyavasthāpya tvam vā ananyathā siddha tvam nanu evam atirikta śaktau sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt nityam saṃśayaḥ na ca sādhaka abhāvasya bādhaka tvam bādhaka abhāvasya api sādhaka tvāt iti ced na sādhaka abhāvena vahnau anyatra siddha 
[103,vii]	parama prayojanam anumānasya apavargaḥ ātmā vai are śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ iti śruteḥ sa ca samāna adhikaraṇa duḥkha prāc abhāva asaha vṛtti duḥkha dhvaṃsaḥ nanu na asau puruṣa arthaḥ atīta duḥkha ghu aṃsasya siddha tvāt anāgata duḥkhasya dhvaṃsayitum aśakyatvāt vartamānasya puruṣa prayatnam vinā eva virodhi guṇa nāśya tvāt atīta duḥkha vat hetu ucchede puruṣa vyāpāraḥ prāyaścitta vat iti ced na tat kim hetu ucchedasya sukha duḥkha abhāva itara tvena svatas apuruṣa artha tvāt anāgatā anutpādam uddiśya kriyamāṇa tvāt ca yathā tatra duḥkha anutpādaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ tathā iha api iti vivakṣitam atha anutpādasya prāc abhāva tvena asādhya tvāt phala antarasya abhāvat ca ananya gatika tayā kaṇṭaka nāśa vat duḥkha sādhana nāśaḥ eva svatas puruṣa arthaḥ tathā iha api iti vā ubhayathā api duḥkha dhvaṃsasyā puruṣa artha tvam eva na ca tayoḥ api puruṣa artha tvam iti vakṣyate 
[103,viii_103,ix]	mā evam duḥkha antara dhvaṃsasya āyatna sādhya tve api tādṛśa duḥkha dhvaṃsasya mithyājñāna uccheda dvārā puruṣa prayatna adhīna tattva jñāna sādhya tvāt tathā hi tattva jñānāt savāsana mithyā jñāna abhāve doṣa an utpattau pravṛti abhāve adṛṣṭa anutpattau janma abhāve tādṛśa duḥkha dhvaṃsaḥ bhavati atha carama duḥkhe utpanne tad dhvaṃsaḥ tad jñānāt eva bhaviṣyati tad anutpāde ca tattva jñānāt api na syāt iti ced na pratiyogi vat tattva jñānasya api tad hetu tvāt tulya vat ubhayoḥ api kāraṇa tvāt tena vinā tad nutpatteḥ atas eva śukasya tattva jñānam utpannam iti tasya tat dhvaṃsaḥ utpannaḥ na asmad ādīnām iti ced anādau saṃsāre tat kutas na utpannam sva kāraṇa abhāvāt iti ced na anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinaḥ tattva jñānāt anyasya anviṣyamāṇasya abhāvāt muktau sa dhvaṃsaḥ asti eva tasmin sati muktiḥ asti eva iti sa mukti utpādaka utpādya iti sarva vādī upagatam muktiḥ sā anyā vā 
[103,x]	nanu evam dhvaṃsa artham duḥkham upādeyam tad anutpādya dhvaṃsa anutpādāt iti ced satyam puruṣa artha heta tvena loke duḥkha tad sādhanayoḥ api upādāna darśanāt anāgata kumbha nāśa artham mudgara ādau pravṛtti darśanāt anāgata duḥkha dhvaṃsa artham api pravṛttiḥ carama duḥkha dhvaṃsaḥ na duḥkha dhvaṃsa tvena uddeśyaḥ ayatna siddha duḥkha antara dhvaṃsa vat apuruṣa artha tvāt iti ced na samāna adhikaraṇa duḥkha prāc abhāva asaha vṛtti duḥkha dhvaṃsa tvena tasya uddeśya tvāt duḥkha asambhinna sukha vat tasya ca puruṣa prayatna sādhya tvam eva iti uktam 
[103,xi_103,xii]	etena duḥkha dhvaṃsa tvam eva mokṣa tvam tad tad ātma yāvat duḥkha dhvaṃsa samvalana daśāyantu tathā vyapadeśaḥ prati puruṣam duḥkha dhvaṃsa stomasya vyakti sthānīya tvāt tejaḥ bhāve samvalite andhatama sapada prayoga vat yathā samvalitaḥ eva dvau iti buddhi vyapadeśau pravṛttiḥ api samvalana artham iti apāstam militānām asādhya tvāt melakasya anatirikta tve ati prasaṅgāt atirikta tve janyasya dhvaṃsa āvṛtteḥ ajanyasya puruṣa artha tva abhāvāt sādhya tayā saṃvalane bhoga avaśyam bhāvāt andhatamasā ādau tathā samvalaḥ eva prayogāt etena saṃskāra ajanaka bhoga viṣaya duḥkha dhvaṃsaḥ saṃskāra ajanaka anubhava dhvaṃsaḥ vā muktiḥ na ca ati vyāptiḥ janakatvasya ajanayati api bhāvāt iti nirastam apuruṣa artha tvāt 
[104,i]	anye tu duḥkha prāc abhāva asaha vṛtti duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsaḥ mokṣaḥ loke ahi kaṇṭaka ādi nāśasya vaidike prāyaścitta ādau pāpa nāśasya ananya gatika tayā duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsa tvena puruṣa artha tvāt atha ahikaṇṭaka ādi pāpam vā nāśyatām tena tat janyam duḥkham na bhavati iti duḥkha anutpādam uddiśya pravṛtteḥ duḥkha anutpādaḥ eva prayojanam na tu duḥkha sādhana abhāvaḥ sukha duḥkha bhāva itara tvāt iti ced na duḥkha anutpādasya prāc abhāva tvena anāditayā asādhya tvāt na ca tad pālanam sādhyam pālanam hi na tad svarūpam tasya asādhya tvāt na uttara samaya sambandhaḥ abhāve sambandhi dvaya atiriktasya tasya aprāmāṇika tvāt anabhyuparamāt ca na api sambandhi dvaya svarūpam sādhyam prāgabhāvasya api asādhya tvāt samaya tad upādhyoḥ ca prayatnam vinā eva siddheḥ 
[104,ii]	atha duḥkhe dveṣāt yathā tad bhāve icchā tathā duḥkha sādhane dveṣāt tad abhāve api icchā tayā tad sādhane pravṛttiḥ iti ced na yat icchayā yat sādhane yasya pravṛttiḥ tasya eva tad prayojana tvam iti duḥkha sādhana abhāvasya eva prayojana tvāt atha cikirṣa ayoni prayatne prayojana jñāna apekṣā tena vinā upāye cikīrṣā virahāt na tu dveṣa yoni yatne aniṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt ahikaṇṭaka ādau dveṣaḥ dveṣāt tad nāśa anukūlaḥ yatnaḥ utpadyate ayam eva hi dveṣa svabhāvaḥ yat pratibandhakam vinā sva viṣaya nāśa anukūlam yatnam utpādayati anyathā prayatna dvaividhya anupapatteḥ atas eva phalam vinā eva utkaṭa krodha andhānām ātma ghāte pravṛttiḥ iti ced na prayojanam anuddiśya dveṣa mātrāt duḥkha eka phalake prekṣāvatām prayatna anutpādāt krodhāndhanām api tātkālikaḥ phala abhimānaḥ asti eva utkaṭa rāga andhānām iva para dāra ādau api pravṛtteḥ iti 
[104,iii]	tat na duḥkham me mā bhūt iti uddiśya prāyaścitta ādau pravṛtteḥ duḥkha anutpādasya eva prayojana tvāt na ca prāc abhāvasya asādhya tvam duḥkha sādhana vighaṭana dvārā tasya api kṛti sādhya tvāt duḥkha sādhana samavadhāna daśāyām kṛtau satyām duḥkha sādhana nāśe satya grima samaye prāc abhāva svarūpam asti tena vinā na asti iti anvaya vyatirekayoḥ tatra sattvāt ghaṭe api kṛtau satyām agri makṣaṇe tat sattvam tayā vinā na iti eva kṛti sādhya tvam na tu prāc asataḥ agri makṣaṇe sattvam utpattiḥ gauravāt kṛtim vinā na yat svarūpam tad kṛti sādhyam tad prāgabhāva svarūpantu na tathā iti ced na kṛti dhvaṃse api ghaṭa sattvena agri makṣaṇe iti āvaśyaka tvāt atas eva yoga vat kṣemasya api anāgata aniṣṭa anutpāda janakasya parīkṣaka pravṛtti viṣaya tvam iti vakṣyate niṣedha apūrva prastāve 
[104,iv]	nanu prāyaścitta nāśya pāpa janya duḥkhasya prāgabhāvaḥ yadi asti tadā duḥkham āvaśyakam tasya pratiyogi janaka tva niyamāt na asti ced tarhi tad abhāvāt eva duḥkha anutpādaḥ iti ubhayathā api prāyaścittam aphalam tasmāt duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsa mukhena prāgabhāvasya sādhyatā iti tatra eva kṛti sādhya tva paryavasānāt duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsaḥ eva puruṣa arthaḥ na tu duḥkha anutpāda arthitayā iti tatra prāgabhāva sattva asattva vicāraḥ vāyasa darśana vicāra vat 
[104,v]	atha tadā api prāgabhāvasya asattve tad abhāvāt pāpam na duḥkha sādhanam iti na tad nāśa artham pravartate tasya sattve ca pāpam ādāya eva tasya duḥkha utpādaka tva niyamāt prāyaścitte sati api gale pādikayā pāpa avasthānam iti na tatas pāpa nāśaḥ iti ced na prāgabhāvasya asattve api duḥkha sādhana jātīya nāśasya puruṣa artha tvāt sattve api pāpa antaram ādāya api tasya duḥkha janaka tva sambhavāt prāyaścittāt pāpa nāśaḥ syāt eva iti prāgabhāva sattva asattva sandehe api prāyaścitta ādau pravṛttiḥ apratyūha eva iti 
[104,vi]	ucyate tatra duḥkha prāc abhāvaḥ asti eva tasya eva duḥkha anutpāda rūpa tvena puruṣa artha tvāt sa ca pāpa nāśa dvārā prāyaścitta sādhyaḥ iti prāgabhāva satvepi na niṣphalam prāyaścittam tena prāc abhāvena duḥkham avaśyam jananīyam iti ced satyam kintu pāpa antaram āsādya na ca evam prāyaścittam aphalam duḥkha anutpādena tasya saphala tvāt na ca duḥkha anutpādasya api duḥkha anutpāda antaram eva phalam tat ca tatra na asti iti aphala tvam svarūpa satas eva tasya puruṣa artha tvāt anavasthānāt ca atas anena pāpena duḥkham me mā bhūt iti vidyamāna pāpa nāśa artham prāyaścitte pravṛttiḥ 
[104,vii]	etena cīrṇa prāyaścitte duḥkha prāgabhāvaḥ na asti eva anyathā tasya pratiyogi nāśya tvena anirmokṣa prasaṅgāt na ca prāyaścitta vaiphalyam na vā bhagavataḥ duḥkha maya karma upadeśaka tvena anāpta tvam tasya pāpa dhvaṃsena eva saphala tvāt prāc abhāva aniścaye api naraka sādhana pāpa niścayāt tad nāśa artham pravṛttiḥ iti apāstam duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsasya svatas apuruṣa artha tvāt pāpa antareṇa tad pratiyogi janane tad nāśāt tasmāt duḥkham me mā bhūt iti uddiśya tad sādhana dhvaṃsa artham pravṛttiḥ iti duḥkha anutpādaḥ eva puruṣa arthaḥ na tu duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsaḥ iti sthitam api ca na tāvat duḥkha maya saṃsāra bīja mithyājñānasya dhvaṃsaḥ muktiḥ tattva jñānāt tad nāśe api śarīra dharma ādi sattva daśāyām mukti prasaṅgāt na api śarīra indriya buddhi ādi tad nidāna dharma adharma dhvaṃsaḥ acīrṇa prāyaścitta karmaṇām bhoga eka nāśya tvena tattva jñāna anāśya tvāt bhoga dvārā tad nāśasya ca apuruṣa artha tvāt iti 
[104,viii]	apare tu duḥkha atyanta abhāvaḥ muktiḥ yadi api para duḥkha atyanta abhāvaḥ svatas siddhaḥ eva sva duḥkha atyanta abhāvaḥ sva ātmani asambhavī ghaṭa ādau ati prasaktaḥ asādhyaḥ ca tathā api duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsaḥ eva sva vṛtti duḥkha atyanta abhāva sambandhaḥ sa ca sādhyaḥ eva na ca evam āvaśyaka tvena saḥ eva muktiḥ tasya svatas apuruṣa artha tvena duḥkha abhāvam uddiśya tatra pravṛtteḥ duḥkhena atyantam vimuktaḥ carati iti atra atyanta abhāva tvena mukti śravaṇāt ca yadi api duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsaḥ na puruṣa arthaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ ca na sādhyaḥ tathā api viśiṣṭasya puruṣa artha tvam viśeṣaṇa sādhya tvena viśiṣṭa sādhyatvañca ahikaṇṭaka ādi nāśasya api tad tad vyakti sādhya duḥkha atyanta abhāvam uddiśya tad sambandha tvena eva sādhyatā iti 
[104,ix]	tat na adharma ādi duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsasya na mukti nirvāhaka tvam iti ukta tvāt kiñca nānāgata sva vṛtti duḥkhasya atyanta abhāva sambandhaḥ sādhyaḥ muktasya anāgata sva vṛtti duḥkhasya anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā amukta tva āpātāt atyanta abhāva sambandha virodhāt ca na api utpannasya sva vṛtti duḥkhasya tad vṛtteḥ tatra atyanta abhāva sambandha virodhāt tad abhāvasya svatas siddha tvāt atīta duḥkha abhāvasya anuddeśya tvāt ca na api parakīya duḥkha atyanta abhāva sambandhaḥ tasya svatas siddha tvāt api ca duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsasya na atyanta abhāva sambandha tve mānam asti duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsā dau asya duḥkhasya atyanta abhāvaḥ iti buddhi vyapadeśau staḥ iti ced na tasya samāna adhikaraṇa duḥkha asamāna kāla duḥkha abhāva viṣaya tvena api upapattau atirikta sambandha aviṣaya tvāt 
[104,x]	etena sarva duḥkha prāc abhāva saṃsarga abhāvaḥ muktiḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ ca na mukta tvam duḥkha sādhana dhvaṃsa viśeṣita etat yoginaḥ mukta padārtha tvāt tathā eva vyavahārāt yoga rūḍhibhyām paṅkaja ādi pada vācya tva vat iti nirastam prāc abhāva saṃsarga abhāvasya svataḥ anuddeśya tvāt pratyuta atyanta abhāvasya asādhya tvena dhvaṃsa rūpa tvena tasya duḥkha rūpa tayā heya tvāt 
[105,i]	prābhākarāḥ tu ātyantika duḥkha prāgabhāvaḥ muktiḥ na ca tasya anādi tvena apuruṣa artha tvam kadācid kṛti anapekṣa tve api pratiyogi janaka adharma nāśa mukhena tasya kṛti sādhya tvāt kṛtī adhīna tattva jñānāt adharma nāśe satya grima samaye duḥkha prāgabhāva svarūpat na asti tayā vinā adharmeṇa duḥkha ājananāt na tad prāgabhāva svarūpam asti iti ghaṭa vat kṛti sādhya tvāt vyavasthāpitañca tvayā prāgabhāvasya kṛti sādhya tva mahikaṇṭaka ādi nāśa prāyaścitta kṣema arthi pravṛtti sthale na ca evam yugapad a dharma dhvaṃsaḥ eva muktiḥ prāgabhāvasya anāditayā vivakṣita vivekena tatra eva kṛti sādhya tva paryavasānāt iti vācyam adharma dhvaṃsasya svatas apuruṣa artha tvāt duḥkha anutpāda hetu tvena eva tasya prayojana tā vācyā sā ca katham asādhya tve prāgabhāvasya syāt iti atas eva duḥkha janma ityādi sūtram api saṃgacchate anyathā mithyājñāna ādi anutpādānām duḥkha anutpāda ahetu tvena asaṅgatam syāt iti āsthiṣatā iti 
[105,ii]	tad atisthavīyaḥ tathā hi astu prāgabhāvasya sādhya tvam tathā api tasya pratiyogi janaka tva niyamāt muktasya api duḥkha utpāda prasaḍgaḥ adharma śarīra ādi sahakāri virahāt na duḥkha utpāda prasaṅgaḥ iti ced tarhi uttara avadhi vidhura tvena anādeḥ atyanta abhāva tva āpattau prāc abhāva tva vyākopaḥ pratiyogi janaka nāśya jātīya tvena tatra prāc abhāva tva vyapadeśaḥ vastutas nityaḥ eva saḥ iti ced na nitya tvena atyanta abhāva rūpa tayā pratiyogi janaka nāśa mukhena tasya asādhya tvāt ca 
[105,iii]	api ca mukteḥ prāgabhāvasya samāna adhikaraṇam bhāvi duḥkham na pratiyogi tasya abhāvāt bhāve vā amukta tva āpātāt na api samāna adhikaraṇam atītam vartamānañca tad prāgabhāvasya vinaṣṭa tvāt na api vyadhikaraṇam anya vṛtti duḥkhasya anyatra atyanta abhāvena prāc abhāvāt tasya pratiyogi samāna deśa tvāt na ca duḥkha mātram pratiyogi sva parāvṛtteḥ duḥkha mātrasya aprāmaṇika tvāt tasya atyanta asataḥ nitya nivṛtta tvena tad nivṛttaye prekṣāvat pravṛtti anupapatteḥ ahikaṇṭaka ādi nāśa prāyaścitta ādi sādhya duḥkha prāgabhāvasya kalañja bhakṣaṇa prāgabhāvasya ca samāna adhikaraṇam eva bhāvi duḥkham bhakṣaṇañca pratiyogi 
[105,iv]	nanu duḥkha abhāvaḥ na puruṣa arthaḥ sukhasya api hāneḥ tulyāyavyaya tvāt na ca bahutara duḥkha anuviddha tayā sukhasya api prekṣā vadheya tvam āvaśyaka tvena duḥkhasya eva heya tvāt sukhasya nirupadhi icchā viṣaya tvāt anyathā duḥkhān anuviddha tayā tathātvena puruṣa artha tva virodhāt iti ced na sukham anuddiśya api duḥkha bhīrūṇām duḥkha hāna artham pravṛtti darśanāt duḥkha abhāvasya svatas eva puruṣa artha tvāt na hi duḥkha abhāva daśāyām sukham asti iti uddiśya duḥkha hāna artham pravartate vaiparītyasya api sambhave sukhasya api apuruṣa artha tva āpatteḥ atas duḥkha abhāva daśāyām sukham na asti iti jñānam na duḥkha abhāva arthi pravṛtti pratibandhakam tasmāt avivekinaḥ sukha mātra lipsavaḥ bahutara duḥkha anuviddham api sukham uddiśya śiraḥ madīyam yadi yāti yātu kṛtvā para dāra ādiṣu pravartamānāḥ varam vṛndāvane ramye ityādi vadantaḥ na atra adhikariṇaḥ 
[105,v_105,vi]	ye ca vivekinaḥ asmin saṃsāra kāntāre kiyanti duḥkha durddināni kiyatī sukha khadyotiketī kupita phaṇi phaṇā maṇḍala chāyā pratimam idam iti manyamānāḥ sukham api hātum icchanti te atra adhikāriṇaḥ na ca bhoga arthi nām apravṛttau puruṣa artha tā hīyate kasyacid apravṛttau api cikitsā ādeḥ puruṣa artha tvāt atha duḥkha abhāvaḥ api na āvedyaḥ puruṣa arthatayā iṣyate na hi mūrchā ādi avastha artham pravṛttaḥ ddaśyate sudhīḥ 
[105,vii]	puruṣa artha tve sukha vat jñāyamāna tva niyamāt na ca muktau jñānam sambhavati iti ced na hi duḥkha abhāvam jānīyām iti uddiśya pravṛttiḥ kintu duḥkham me mā bhūt iti uddiśya iti atas duḥkhasya abhāvaḥ eva puruṣa arthaḥ tasya jñānañca sva kāraṇa adhīnam na tu puruṣa artha tā upayogi sukhī syām iti uddiśya pravartate na tu sukham jānīyam iti sukham eva tathā astu na tu tad avagamaḥ tasya āvaśyaka tvena anyathā siddha tvāt gauravāt ca 
[105,viii^1]	kiñca bahutara duḥkha jarjara kalevarāḥ duḥkha abhāvam uddiśya maraṇe api pravartamānāḥ dṛśyante na ca maraṇe tasya jñānam asti na te vivekinaḥ iti ced na puruṣa artha tve viveka anupayogāt kiñca carama duḥkha anubhave anāgata duḥkha dhvaṃsaḥ api viṣayaḥ tathā ca agri makṣaṇe tad uparamaḥ tad viṣayaka tvañca vinaśyat avastham jñānam asti iti vartamānam api aciram anubhūyate jñāna samaye mukti lakṣaṇasya sattvāt na jñānam mukti virodhi pramāṇantu duḥkha tvam deva datta duḥkha tvam vā sva āśraya asamāna kālīna dhvaṃsa pratiyogi vṛtti kārya mātra vṛtti dharma tvāt santati tvāt vā etat pradīpa vat santati tvañca nānā kālīna kārya mātra vṛtti dharma tvam evam sukha tva ādau api sādhyam tena sakala ucchede mokṣeḥ na ca aprayojaka tvam 
[105,viii^2]	santati ucchede mūla ucchedasya prayojaka tvāt prakṛte ca mithyājñānasya saṃsāra mūlasya śravaṇa ādi krameṇa utpanna tattva jñānāt nivṛttiḥ sambhavati eva ātmā jñātavyaḥ na sa punar āvartate iti śrutiḥ ca pramāṇam rātri satra nyona artha vāda upanīta punarāvṛtteḥ adhikāri viśeṣaṇa tvāt saḥ ātma jñaḥ na punar āvartate na punar śarīrī bhavati iti arthaḥ ātmā vai are śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ iti upakramya duḥkhena atyantam vimuktaḥ carati iti śrutiḥ ca mānam 
[105,ix]	ācāryāḥ tu aśarīram vāvasantam priya apriye na spṛśataḥ iti śrutiḥ tatra pramāṇam vāvasantam iti yaṅluki tena saṃsāritādaśāyām kṣaṇa mātram aśarīra tvena na anyathā siddhiḥ nanu dvandva svarasena milita sukha duḥkha ubhaya niṣedhaḥ pratīyate sa tu nitya vat prāptaḥ eva ekaika niṣedhe ca vākya bheda āpattiḥ na ca muktau pramāṇam iti ced na dvi tvena ekena rūpeṇa upasthitayoḥ pratyekam niṣedha anvaye api vākya bheda abhāvāt dhava khadirau chindhi iti atra pratyekam chidā anvayaḥ iva na hi tatra milita chidā api ca na priya apriya rūpam kiñcitasti iti milita niṣedhaḥ api ekaika anvaye pratyeka abhāve vā bhavet tatra eka anvayasya aśarīre ayogya tvāt pratyeka abhāvaḥ eva paryavasyati atas eva sarva muktiḥ api sarva duḥkha santati pakṣīkaraṇe tad siddheḥ anyathā muktiḥ api na syāt tatra eva vyabhicārāt 
[105,x]	yadi ca ubhaya ātmānaḥ eva kecid tadā tad śaṅkayā mokṣa artham na kaścid pravarteta śama dama bhoga an abhiṣvaṅga ādi mukti cihnena śruti siddhena sandeha nivṛttiḥ iti ced na saṃsāri tvena mukti yogya tvāt na tu tad viśeṣaṇa śama ādimattvena sāmānye bādhake sati eva yogyatāyāḥ viśeṣa niṣṭha tvāt kiñca śama ādayaḥ śrutau sahakāritayā bodhitāḥ na tu yogyatayā tattve api saṃsāri tvena te api sādhanīyāḥ śama ādikam api hi kāryam tatra api saṃsāri tvena eva yogyatā sāmānye bādhaka abhāvāt 
[106,i]	na ca nitya sukha abhivyaktiḥ muktiḥ sā hi na nityā mukta saṃsāriṇoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt na utpādyā tad hetu śarīra ādi abhāvāt jñāna mātre sukha mātre vā tad hetutva avadhāraṇāt na ca saṃsāri daśāyām tad hetuḥ sāmānye bādhaka abhāvāt atas eva svarga ādau śarīra kalpanā kiñca tad janakam na tāvat ātma manaḥ yogaḥ tasya adṛṣṭa ādi nirapekṣasya ajanaka tvāt viṣaya mātrapekṣaṇe tu saṃsāridaśāyām api tad abhivyakti prasaḍgaḥ na api yoga jaḥ dharmaḥ sahakārī tasya utpanna bhāva tvena vināśi tve apavarga nivṛtti āpatteḥ na ca tad janyā abhivyaktiḥ anantā tasyāḥ api atas eva nāśāt 
[106,ii^1]	atha tattva jñānāt savāsana mithyā jñāna nāśe doṣa abhāvena pravṛtti ādi abhāvāt dharma adharmayoḥ anutpāde prācīna dharma adharma kṣayāt duḥkha sādhana śarīra ādi nāśaḥ eva tatra hetuḥ atas eva tasya ānantyena abhivyakti pravāhaḥ api anantaḥ iti ced na śarīram vinā tad anutpatteḥ tasya tad hetu tve māna abhāvāt ca na ca mokṣa arthi pravṛttiḥ eva tatra mānam duḥkha hāna arthitayā api tad utpatteḥ na ca nitye sukhe mānam asti nityam vijñānam ānandam brahmā ānandam brahmaṇaḥ rūpam tat ca mokṣe pratiṣṭhitam ityādi śrutiḥ mānaḥ i atha sukhasya brahma abheda bodhanāt eva ayogya tā anityam sukham vihāya vākya artha tvena nitya sukha siddhiḥ svarga vat na tu nitye sukhe siddhe tad abheda bodhanam 
[106,ii^2]	yena anyonya āśrayaḥ yat vā nityam sukham bodhayitvā tat abhinnam brahma bodhyate na ca vākya bhedaḥ vākya eka vākya tvāt iti ced na ātmanaḥ anubhūyamāna tvena tat abhinnasya nitya sukhasya api anubhava prasaṅgāt sukha mātrasya sva gocara sākṣātkāra janaka tva niyamāt tad ananubhave vā ātmanaḥ api anubhavaḥ na syāt atha ātmā bhinnam nitya sukham anubhūyate eva sukha tvam tu tatra na anubhūyate iti ced na sukha anubhava sām agrāḥ eva sukha tva anubhāvaka tvāt tasmāt ānandam brahma iti matu arthīyāt pratyaya anta tvena andavat tvam bodhyam tena abhedaḥ anyathā napuṃsa kaliṅga tva anupapatteḥ 
[106,iii_106,iv]	etena brahmā dvaita sākṣāt kārāt avidyā nivṛttau vijñāna sukha ātmakaḥ kevalaḥ ātmā apavarge vartate iti vedāntimatam apāstam sva prakāśa sukha ātmaka brahmaṇaḥ nitya tvena mukta saṃsāriṇoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt puruṣa prayatnam vinā tasya sattvāt apuruṣa artha tvāt ca a tridaṇḍinaḥ tu ānanda maya paramātmani jīva ātma layaḥ mokṣaḥ layaḥ ca liṅga śarīra apagamaḥ liṅga śarīrañca ekādaśa indriyāṇi pañca mahābhūtāni sūkṣma mātrayā sambhūya avasthitāni jīva ātmani sukha duḥkha avacchedakāni iti āhuḥ tat na liṅga śarīra dhvaṃsasya svatas duḥkha sādhana abhāva tayā apuruṣa artha tvāt na ca upādhi śarīra nāśe aupādhika jīva nāśaḥ layaḥ sva nāśasya apuruṣa artha tvāt brahmaṇaḥ nitya tvena tat abhinnasya nāśa anupapatteḥ bheda abhedasya ca virodhena abhāvāt 
[106,v]	na api anupaplavā cit santatiḥ apavargaḥ āvaśyaka tvena anupaplavasya duḥkha abhāvasya puruṣa artha tvena cit santateḥ aparuṣa artha tvāt śarīra ādi kāraṇam vinā cit santateḥ anutpādāt ca na hi cittamātram tad sāmagrī śarīra ādi vaiyarthya āpatteḥ na api duḥkha hetu tvena ātmanaḥ hānam eva muktiḥ sukha duḥkha abhāva itara tvena apuruṣa artha tvāt jñāna rūpa ātma hānasya āyatna siddheḥ atirikta hānasya aśakya tvāt 
[106,vi]	yat tu yogā ṛddhi sādhya niratiśaya ānanda mayīm jīvanmuktim uddiśya pravṛtteḥ kāraṇa vaśāt ātyantika duḥkha abhāva rūpām muktim āsādayati iti matam tat na parama mukteḥ apuruṣa artha tva āpatteḥ viraktasya mokṣe adhikārāt sukha uddeśena apravṛtteḥ ca mokṣe ca sarva āśramiṇām adhikāraḥ āśrama catuṣṭayam upakramya saḥ brahma saṃsthaḥ amṛta tvam eti iti śruteḥ saṅkoce kāraṇa abhāvāt ākāṅakṣāyāḥ aviśeṣeṇa anantaryasya aprayojaka tvāt katham tarhi mokṣa śramaḥ caturthaḥ vai yaḥ bhikṣoḥ parikīrtitaḥ iti pravajyām mokṣa āśramam āhuḥ gṛhasthasya ca putra dāra ādi saṅgaḥ durvāraḥ iti asādhāraṇyena tathā upadeśāt tattva jñāna niṣṭhaḥ gṛhasthaḥ api mucyate iti āgamāt ca 
[106,vii]	evam sthite mokṣam upakramya ātmāvāḥ are śrotavyaḥ mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ iti śrutiḥ śrutibhyaḥ ca śarīra ādi bhinnam ātmānam avadhārya śāstreṇa padārthān vivicya tad bodhita upapattibhiḥ tasya sthirīkaraṇa rūpam mananam vidadhāti na ca śabda upapatti janya tattva jñānāt sākṣātkāri saṃsāra bīja savāsanam idhya ajñāna nivṛttiḥ diś moha ādau tathā anupalabdheḥ atas śruti smṛti upadiṣṭa yoga vidhinā cira nirantarā dāra sevita nididhi āsana janya yoga ja dharmāt ātma tattva sākṣātkāram saṃsāra bīja savāsana mithyā jñāna nihanana samartham āsādya doṣa abhāvat pravṛtti ādeḥ abhāve anāgata dharma anutpāde anādi bhava sañcita karmaṇām bhogena kṣayāt apavṛjyate upadeśa mātrāt śarīra bhinna ātmā avagame api anya paratva śaṅkayā saṅkāsūkasya na aśraddhā amala kṣālanam iti mananam āvaśyakam tathā ca mantavyaḥ ca upapattibhiḥ iti śrutiḥ eva upapatti bodhakasya śāstrasya apavarga hetu tvam bodhayati mananasya tad eka sādhya tvāt evañca śama dama brahmacarya ādi upabṛṃhita yāvat nitya naimittika sandhyā upāsana ādi karma sahitāt tattva jñānāt muktiḥ 
[106,viii]	syāt etat jñāna karmaṇoḥ na sama prādhānyena samuccayaḥ karmaṇām svākyāt phala antara artha tvena śruta tvāt mokṣa artha kalpanā virodhāt tattva jñānasya karma nairapekṣyeṇa mukti hetu tva pratīteḥ ca na api aṅga aṅgi bhāvena tathā hi na karma sannipatya upakārakam tattva jñāna śarīrā nirvāhaka tvāt na api prayāja ādi va dārāt upakārakam sva vākyate eva karmaṇām prayojana lābhena phalavat sannidhau aphala tva abhāvāt upapatti viruddhaḥ ca jñāna karma samuccayaḥ kāmya niṣiddhayoḥ tyāgāt na api asaṅkalpita phala vat kāmya karma samuccayaḥ caturtha āśrama virodhāt atas eva na yāvat nitya naimiktaka samuccayaḥ api na api yati āśrama vihitena karmaṇā tattva jñāne sati gṛhasthasya api mukteḥ 
[106,ix_107,i]	jñānam pradhānam na tu karma hīnam karma pradhānam na tu buddhi hīnam tasmāt tayoḥ eva bhavet prasiddhiḥ natu eka pakṣaḥ vihagaḥ prayāti nyāya gata dhanaḥ tattva jñāna niṣṭhaḥ atithi priyaḥ śrāddha kṛt satya vādī ca gṛhasthaḥ api vimucyate iti smṛteḥ na ca ananugatam api sādhanam svarga vat apavarge prakāra bheda abhāvāt na ca apavarga arthi kartavya tayā karmāṇi vihitāni yena tat samuccayaḥ syāt tasmāt sannyasya sarva karmāṇi iti smṛteḥ sarva karma sannyāsaḥ jñāna mātrāt ca mokṣaḥ iti 
[107,ii_107,iv]	mā evam sva sva āśrama vihitena karmaṇā jñānasya sama prādhānyena samuccayāt jñāna karmaṇoḥ tulya tvena mukti artha tva abhidhānāt tathā ca śrīmat bhagavat gītā sve sve karmaṇi abhirataḥ saṃsiddhim labhate naraḥ sva karmaṇa tam abhyarcya siddhim vidanti mānavaḥ śrī viṣṇupurāṇe tasmāt tad prāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ paṇḍitaiḥ naraiḥ tad prāpti hetuḥ vijñānam karma ca uktam mahāmate 
[107,v_107,vii]	hārītaḥ ubhābhyām eva pakṣābhyām yathā khe pakṣiṇām gatiḥ tathā eva jñāna karmabhyām prāpyate brahma śāśvatam śrutiḥ ca satyena labhyaḥ tapasā hi aṣaḥ ātmā samyak jñānena brahmacaryeṇa ca iti etat mulakam eva parijñānāt bhavet muktiḥ etat ālasya lakṣaṇam kāya kleśa bhayāt ca eva karma na icchanti paṇḍitāḥ 
[107,viii_107,xi]	na ca phala antara artha tvena śrutasya karmaṇaḥ phala antara artha tvam anupapannam tathā vākya svarasāt jñāna tulya tā pratīteḥ tad tad phala janaka tve api hi karmaṇam śabdaḥ eva mānam evam anyatra api bhavatu vai ārāt upakāri tayā aṅga aṅgi bhāvena samuccayaḥ sa prayāja ādi vat apūrva dvāra eva yat tu jaḍa bharata upākhyāne na papāṭha guru proktām kṛta upanayanaḥ śrutim na dadarśa ca karmāṇi śāstrāṇi jagṛhe na ca iti tad yogi dharma saṅga tyāga artham jāti smara tvena na śikṣitāni iti evaṃparam vā tat uktam jñeja jātismaraḥ dvijaḥ sarva vijñāna sampannaḥ sarva śāstra artha tattva vid iti 
[107,xii]	atra kecid anutpanna tattva jñānasya jñāna arthinaḥ tad pratibandhaka adharma nivṛtti dvārā prāyaścitta vadārāt upakārakam karma sannipatya upakārakantu tattva jñānam utpanna tattva jñānasya tu antarā labdha vṛṣṭeḥ kārīri samāpti vat ārabdha āśrama paripālanam loka saṃgraha artham yadi api loka saṃgrahaḥ na prayojanam sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana itara tvāt tathā api akaraṇe lokānām na ca vigānāt nintya tvena yat jñānam tad parihāra artham tad karma sādhya duḥkha utpādanena adharma kṣaya arthañca iti 
[107,xiii]	tat na tattva jñānam pratyaṅga tva pakṣe karmaṇām hi apūrva dvārāḥ janaka tvam durita dhvaṃsa kalpanātaḥ laghu tvāt tasmāt yāni karmāṇi upanīta mātra kartavya tvena vihitāni sandhyā upāsana ādīni tāni mokṣa arthibhiḥ api avaśyam kartavyāni tad parityāgasya pratyavāya hetu tvena āśāstrīya tvāt saṅkoce māna abhāvāt niṣiddhāni kāmyāni ca bandha hetu tvāt mukti paripanthīni iti tyajyante dhana mūlāni ca dhana tyāgāt eva tyajyante saḥ ayam saṃnyasya sarva karmāṇi iti asya arthaḥ ayam eva hi sannyāsa padārthaḥ 
[107,xiv_107,xv]	tathā ca gītā kāmyānām karmaṇām nyāsam sannyāsam kavayaḥ vidaḥ niyatasya tu sannyāsaḥ karmaṇaḥ na upapadyate mohāt tasya parityāgaḥ tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ iti tattva jñānam dharma dvārā mukti sādhanam vihita tvena dharma janaka tvāt iti dharmasya eva prādhānyam sa ca dharmaḥ muktyā eva phalena nāśyate iti kecid tat na mithyājñāna nivṛttyā dṛṣṭa dvāreṇa eva upapattau adṛṣṭa kalpanā anavakāśāt anyathā bheṣaja ādiṣu api tathā syāt evañca tatra eva vihita tvasya vyabhicāraḥ 
[107,xvi]	atra vadanti saṃsāra kāraṇa uccheda krameṇa kārya ucchedāt mokṣaḥ evañca tattva jñāna mātrāt eva mithyājñāna ucchedāt apavargaḥ tatra na tasya karma sahakāri tvam mithyājñāna unmūlane karma vinākṛtasya eva tasya diś moha ādau hetu tva avadhāraṇāt karmaṇām apavarga hetu tā śrutiḥ ca tattva jñāna dvārā api upapadyate sākṣāt tasya aśruteḥ tattva jñānavataḥ ca adhikāre nitya akaraṇe api doṣa abhāvena pratyavāya abhāva upapatteḥ anyathā bhoga artham vihita niṣiddha ācaraṇena dharma adharma utpattau mokṣa abhāva prasaṅgaḥ nanu tad tad tīrtha dāna mahā snāna kāśī maraṇa ādi karmaṇām tattva jñāna nairapekṣyeṇa mukti hetu tvam śrūyate tat katham tattva jñānam eva tad hetuḥ na ca teṣām tattva jñānam eva vyāpāraḥ anupadam tattva jñāna anutpādāt adṛṣṭa dvārā tad hetu tvam vācyam tathā cāpa varga kāraṇam eva dṛṣṭam kalpyatām lāghavāt na ca tattva jñāna pratibandhaka adharma nāśaḥ eva teṣām vyāpāraḥ pratibandhaka durita dhvaṃsataḥ apūrvasya laghu tvāt 
[108,i_108,ii^1]	atha tad tad karmaṇām ananugamāt katham muktiḥ anugatā duḥkha dhvaṃse prakāra abhāvāt iti ced na guṇa nāśe samavāyi asamavāyināśa virodhi guṇānām na aśaka tva niyamāt tad tad nāśa viśeṣe tu tat tad hetuḥ iti ced tarhi tad tad duḥkha dhvaṃse tat tad karmaṇām api tathātvam astu tava api tattva jñāne tattpratibandhaka durita dhvaṃse ca ananugatānām eva tad tad karmaṇām janaka tvam mumukṣum uddiśya vihita tvam vā anugatam asti iti ced na jñāna karmaṇoḥ nirapekṣa kāraṇa tā śravaṇat vrīhi yava vat vikalpaḥ eva nirapekṣa eka sādhana avaruddhepara sa ādhana anvayaḥ na vikalpam antareṇa sambhavati ākāṅkṣā virahāt iti nyāyāt sāhitya bodhakam vinā ekam pratyanekasya hetu tā yatra śabdena bodhyate tatra vikalpena anvayaḥ yathā vrīhi yavayoḥ iti vyutpatteḥ vā vastutas tu dṛḍha bhūmi sava āsana mithyā jñāna unmūlanam vinā na mokṣaḥ iti ubhaya siddham tādṛśa mithyā jñāna nāśe ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām tattva jñāna kāraṇa tvam avadhāritam atas na tena vinā saḥ iti tatra api tattva jñānam āvaśyakam yadi api mithyājñāna nāśe virodhi guṇasya eva hetu tvam 
[108,ii^2]	tathā api mithyājñāna prāc abhāva asaha vṛtti mithyā jñāna dhvaṃsasya tad eka sādhya tvam ātmā jñātavyaḥ na sa punar āvartate iti śruteḥ mokṣam prati tattva jñānasya hetu tva avadhāraṇāt tam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate ayanāya iti śrutyā tattva jñānam vinā na mokṣaḥ kintu tasmin sati eva iti pratipādanāt ca anyathā svarga ādau na śarīra ādayaḥ kalpyeran karmaṇām tattva jñāna dvārā api mukti janaka tva sambhavāt pramāṇavataḥ gauravañca na doṣāya karmaṇām tattva jñāna viśeṣaḥ eva janaka tvam atas na tatra ananugamaḥ doṣāya vārāṇasī maraṇasya tattva jñāna phala janaka tvam āgamāt eva avagamyate tattva jñānāt adatta phalāni eva karmāṇi prāyaścittāt iva vinaśyanti ananyathā siddha śabda balāt na ca prāyaścittasya durita utpatti nimittaka tvam pāpa nāśa phala śravaṇāt 
[108,iii_108,v]	atas eva na brahmahatyā ādīnām prāyaścitta duḥkham eva phalam naraka phala śruti virodhāt prāyaścitta vidhi vaiyarthyāt ca duḥkha eka phala tvena tatra apravṛtteḥ na api karma antara adhikāraḥ eva phalam mahāpātaka atirikte anadhikāra abhāvāt anyathā yat kiñcit pāpavataḥ akṛta prāyaścitta tvena anadhikāra āpatteḥ prāṇāntike tad abhāvāt ca śrūyate hi bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe para ātmani iti smṛtiḥ api jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute arjunaḥ iti 
[108,vi]	na abhuktam kṣīyate karma iti atra ca prāyaścitta ādi smṛtitaḥ saṅkocasya āvaśyaka tvena śabda bodhita nāśaka anāśya karma paratvam lāghavāt na tu tat tad anya karma paratvam gauravāt pāpa puṇya kṣaya hetūnām bahutara tvāt jñānasya na aśaka tvam śabda bodhyam iti uktam atha bhasmasāt padasya lākṣaṇika tvena yathā vahneḥ paramparayā bhasma tathā jñānāt karma kṣayaḥ iti arthaḥ tathā ca na abhuktam kṣīyate karma iti smṛtiḥ utsargataḥ bhogena eva kṣayam āha ananyathā siddha prāyaścitta vidhinā sā bādhyate jñāna nāśya tvañca bhoga dvārā api sambhavati iti abādhe sambhavati bādha kalpanā na iti ced na kamaṇaḥ bhoga nāśya tve jñānasya anāśaka tvāt na hi bhogaḥ tattva jñāna vyāpāraḥ tathā aśravaṇāt tena vinā api karmaṇaḥ eva tad upapatteḥ ca karmaṇaḥ bhoga nāśya tve tattva jñāna anupayogāt 
[108,vii]	yat tu na abhuktam iti smṛti virodhena kṣīyante ityādi śruteḥ anyathā varṇanam tat na smṛteḥ pratyakṣa veda bādhita tvena viruddha arthaka vedān anumāpaka tvāt vāmadeva saubhari prabhṛtīnām kāya vyūha śravaṇāt tattva jñānena kāya vyūham utpādya bhoga dvārā karma kṣayaḥ iti ced na tapaḥ prabhāvāt eva tattva jñāna anutpādepi kāya vyūha sambhavāt bhoga janana arthañca karmabhiḥ avaśyam tad tad kāya niṣpādanam iti na tatra tattva jñāna upayogaḥ yaugapadyañca kāyānām tad janaka karma svabhāvāt tapaḥ prabhāvāt vā na ca jñānam bhoga dvārā karma nāśakam iti uktam 
[108,viii]	etena āgamayoḥ paraspara virodhāt anirṇaye vimati padam karma bhoga nāśyam prāyaścitta ādi anāśya tve sati karma tvāt bhukta bhujyamāna karma vat iti anumānāt nirṇayaḥ iti apāstam jñānasya prāyaścitta tulya tvena aprayojaka tvāt śruti bādhita tvāt ca śabda bodhita nāśakānāśya tu asya upādhi tvāt ca akṛta pradhānena kṛta pradhānena ca aṅga apūrveṇa vyabhicārāt ca tasya pradhāna yāga ādi nāśya tvāt na ca tasya api yāgasya iva svarga phalaka tvam iti tat nāśya tvam eva adhikṛta adhikāre api svarga kāmasya adhikārāt anyathā niṣphale apravṛtteḥ iti vācyam svarga phala tve aṅga tva virodhāt pravṛttiḥ ca phalavat yāga arthi tayā tat uktam pradhāne rāgāt aṅge vaidhi iti 
[108,ix]	nanu tāvat eva asya ciram yāvat na vimokṣaḥ atha sampatsyate kaivalyena iti śruteḥ tāvat eva asya utpanna tattva jñānasya ciram vilambaḥ yāvat na utpanna karmaṇaḥ vimokṣaḥ atha sampatsyate kaivalyena iti atra bhogena kṣayayitvā iti śeṣaḥ na ca śeṣe māna abhāvaḥ sati api vijñāne karma avasthāne kḷpta sāmarthyasya bhogasya eva na aśaka tvena ākṣepaka tvāt iti ced na tattva jñāne sati tattva jñāna daśāyām na mokṣaḥ kintu tad agri makṣaṇaḥ iti ārtha tvena api upapatteḥ 
[108,x]	yat tu akṛta pradhānaṅga apūrva abhiprāyam etat jñāna agriḥ sarva karmāṇi ityādi teṣām kāryāṇām nāśaka antara abhāvāt iti tat na pradhāna arthi tayā kḷptānām tad abhāve tad sāmagrya siddheḥ tad sattve api sarva karma padasya karma antara parigrāhakasya saṅkoce māna abhāvāt yat api bhasmasātkaraṇa ādinā phalājanaka tvam ucte tatu ajñānāt kṛtam api vihitam karma na phalāya iti tathā ca śrutiḥ tat yathā puṣkara palāśena apaḥ śliṣyante ityādi tat api na na hi bhasmasāt karaṇam kṣayaḥ ca anutpattiḥ ucyate na ca lakṣaṇā mukhye bādhaka abhāvāt 
[108,xi]	ucyate karmaṇaḥ bhoga nāśya tve api jñānasya karma nāśaka tvam bhogasya tattva jñāna vyāpāra tvāt na ca bhoga mātrasya eva karma nāśe sāmarthyāt tattva jñāna vyabhicāraḥ karma prāgabhāva asaha vṛtti karma nāśe yugapad karma bhoge vā avi abhicārāt atas eva anumānena āgama bādhā prayojaka tvena ca śruti vākya śeṣe māna abhāvaḥ utpanna tattva jñānasya apavarga vilamba upapādana artham ukta rītyā bhogasya eva ākṣepāt iti tat asya apavargasya parama puruṣa arthasya śruti siddham kāraṇam anumānam iti viviktam iti 
[109,i]	atha upamānam nirūpyate tatra sādṛśya pramākaraṇam upamānam iti kecid sādṛśyañca padārtha antaram tathā hi sādṛśya vyavahārāt abādhitāt asti sādṛśyam tat ca na pratipadārtham ekam sarvasya sarva sadṛśa tva āpatteḥ su sadṛśa manda sadṛśa vyavahārasya tat ekatve anupapatteḥ ca na ca vyañjaka bhūyaḥ sāmānya alpa tva bhūyaḥ tvābhyām tat dhīḥ iti vācyam bahubhiḥ alpaiḥ ca vyajyamāna ghaṭa ādau hrāsa vṛddhyoḥ adarśanāt vyañjaka abhimatāt eva vyavahāra siddhau atirikta asiddheḥ ca na api saṃyoga vat vyāsa jya vṛtti anekam go tva upalakṣita sādṛśya āśraya tvāt gavaya vat goḥ api su sadṛśa tva prasaṅgāt gorasat nikarṣe saṃyoga vat apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt ca pratyakṣa tve vā gavaya nirūpita sādṛśyasya eka vitti vedya tvena goniṣṭhatayā cākṣuṣa tva prasaṅgaḥ kintu pratyāśrayam bhinnam na ca ekaikasya vyabhicārāt anugata rūpa abhāvāt ca anugata pratyayaḥ sādṛśya pada vyutpattiḥ ca na syāt iti vācyam anugata ākāra vitti vedya sādṛśya tva sāmānyāt sapta padārtha atirikta tvāt vā jāti vat antya viśeṣa vat ca sva lakṣaṇāt vā tayoḥ upapatteḥ 
[109,ii]	tat ca na dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā guṇa karma vṛtti tvāt na ca sadṛśa āśraya tvāt eva tatra vyavahāraḥ āśraya vaisādṛśye api tatra tad pratīteḥ atas eva na āśraya sādṛśya asaṃsarga āgrahāt saḥ bādhaka abhāvāt aviśeṣeṇa vaiparītya sambhavāt ca na api sāmānyam tat hi na sarva vṛtti ekam anabhyupagamāt su sadṛśa manda sadṛśa vyavahāra anupapatteḥ ca 
[109,iii_109,iv]	atha vijātīya tve sati a vayava guṇa karma vṛtti bhūyas sāmānyam tat atas eva dūra sthe pratiyogini bhūyaḥ sāmānya ajñānāt na tathā sādṛśya pratyayaḥ vanam prāsādāḥ iti vat bahu tvasya samudāya tvasya vaikalya tvāt ekam sādṛśyam iti dhī prayogau anyathā vana ādi api artha antaram syāt sāmānyasya bahutva alpa tvābhyām su sadṛśa manda sadṛśa vyavahāraḥ tat ucyate sāmānyāni eva bhūyāṃsi guṇa avayava karmaṇām bhinna pradhāna sāmāni a vyaktam sādṛśyam iṣyate iti 
[109,v]	na sājātye api aravinda dvaya vat sajātīya avayava ādi śūnye guṇa ādau jātau ca sadṛśa pratyayāt visadṛśayoḥ karabha rāsa bhayoḥ tat sattvāt ca na api dharmi antare dharmi antara vṛtti dharma bāhulyam asādhāraṇa dharma śūnya tve sati tad gata bhūyas dharmavat tvam vā sva niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi dharma samāna adhikaraṇa bhūyas dharmavat tvam vā tri catur pañca ādi bhedena bhūyas tvasyānanugamāt na ca kapiñjala vat tritva paryavasannam visadṛśayoḥ api hasti maśakayoḥ sādṛśya prasaṅgāt tat uktam
