[122,i^1]	atha śabdaḥ utpadyate utkarṣava tve sati apakarṣava tvāt mādhurya vat atas eva anitya tvam iti ced na tāra tva manda tvayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣayoḥ gakāre pūrva nyāyena asiddheḥ siddhau vā jāti saṅgara bhayena utkarṣa apakarṣayoḥ jātyoḥ rasa tva śabda tva vyāpyayoḥ nānātvena rasa śabda sādha araṇya abhāvāt atas eva sajātīya sākṣātkāra pratibandhaka tāvat chedaka sāmānyam utkaṣaḥ tad pratibadhya sākṣātkāra viṣaya tāvacchedaka sāmānyam apakarṣaḥ iti sādhāraṇaḥ hetuḥ apāstaḥ tāra tvādeḥ gakāra jāti tva asiddheḥ sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpaka mūrta guṇa tvasya aśrautra tvasya ca upādhi tvāt aprayojaka tvāt ca na hi kāraṇa adhīnaḥ eva utkarṣaḥ apakarṣaḥ ca parama mahati paramāṇau ca parimāṇe pratyekam satvāt na ca ubhayasya ekatra satvam kāraṇa prayojyam ekaika vat dvayoḥ api pratyekam eka tvāt syāt etat śrotra vyāpāra anantaram idānīm śruta pūrvaḥ gakāraḥ na asti vinaṣṭaḥ kolāhalaḥ iti pratīteḥ pratyakṣam eva śabda anitya tvam vināśi bhāva tvena utpattimat tva anumānāt vā 
[122,i^2]	pratyakṣa pratiyogika abhāva tvena hi pratyakṣa tvam dhvaṃsasya ghaṭa dhvaṃsa vat na tu vināśa grahe pratiyogi samavāyi pratyakṣaṃtvam tantram dharmma abhāvasya pratyakṣa tva āpatteḥ tad indriya agrahye api pratiyogi samavāyini gandha rasa abhāvayoḥ grahaṇāt ca na ca pratiyogi yogya tvasya tantra tve vāyu sparśa dhvaṃsaḥ api pratyakṣaḥ syāt iti vācyam āśraya nāśa janyasya tasya grāhaka indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt kiñca yasya satvam yatra anupalabdhi virodhi tasya abhāvaḥ tatra gṛhyate iti yogyā anupalabdha arthaḥ atas evam pṛthivī tva abhāvaḥ jalīya paramāṇau na pratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ca vāyau rupabhāvaḥ asti ca tathā śabde tasya tatve samavadhāne ca pratīti prasaṅgāt niradhikaraṇa abhāva pratītiḥ na asti iti ced 
[122,i^3]	na iha idānīm śabdaḥ na asti iti pratīteḥ tasmāt yatra adhikaraṇe deśe samaye vā pratiyogi atra vartate tatra tad abhāvaḥ nirūpyate atas eva sadbhyām abhāvaḥ nirūpyate iti uktam śabda abhāvasya ca svatas eva indriya sannikṛṣṭa tvāt na āśraye sannikarṣa apekṣā indriya viśeṣaṇa tayā na abhāva grahaṇām iti ced na ayogya tvasya upādhi tvāt anyathā guṇasya saṃyukta samavāyena grahaṇa darśanāt na samavāyena śabda grahaḥ syāt iti 
[122,ii]	mā evam atas eva hi śabdasya vyañjaka virahāt anupalabdhi mātram na tu dhvaṃsaḥ tad tadya apya itara sakala tad upalambhaka samavadhāne tad anupalabdhi rūpa yogyā anupalabdheḥ abhāvāt pratiyogi upalambhaka vyañcaka vāyoḥ abhāvāt vinaṣṭa pratīḥ api tvac indriya upanīta vyañcaka vāyu sparśa dhvaṃsa upādhikā eva vāyuḥ na utpādakaḥ kintu vyañcakaḥ iti atra kim vinigamakam iti ced na idānīm śruta pūrvaḥ gakāraḥ na asti vinaṣṭaḥ kolāhala eti prati iti anantaram punar śravaṇe śruta pūrvaḥ ayam gakāraḥ punar saḥ eva ayam kolāhalaḥ iti pratyabhijñānam eva ghaṭa dhvaṃsa pratīti anantarañca saḥ eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti na pratyabhijñānam iti tatra vinaṣṭa pratīti a adhvaṃsaḥ eva sidhyati atas eva tāra tva tāratara tva manda tva manda tara tva pratītīnām bhrama tva kalpanāt daram pratyabhijñāna mātrasya bhramatva kalpanam iti apāstam etāsu satīṣu api abheda pratyabhijñānāt 
[122,iii^1]	syāt etat śabdaḥ prayatna sādhyaḥ tad anabhivyaṅgya tve sati tad anantaram upalabhyamāna tvāt paṭa vat abhivyañjaka tvam hi indriya sambandha pratibandha kāpanāyaka tvāt indriya sannidhāpaka tvāt vā kuhya utsāraṇena iva paṭa ādīnām tat ubhayam api śabde na sambhavati nitya samaveta tvena āvaraṇa apanayana sannidha apanayoḥ abhāvāt na api śrotra saṃskārāt indriya saṃskārasya unmīlana āloka ādeḥ sakṛt indriya sambandha yogya sarva artha upalabdhi anukūla saṃskāra janaka tvam dṛṣṭam tadvat vāyuḥ api sakṛt eva sarva śabda upalabdhi anukūlam śrotre saṃskāram ādadhyāt tathā ca sarva śabda upalabdhiḥ syāt tat uktam sakṛñca saṃskṛtam śrotram sarva śabdān prakāśayet ghaṭayā unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na hi na budhyate atha anvaya vyatirekābhyām kārye pratiniyata janaka janya tva vat śabde api pratiniyata vyañcaka vyaṅya tvam iti ced 
[122,iii^2]	na varṇāḥ hi na pratiniyata vyañcaka vyaṅyāḥ eka avacchedena samāna deśa tve sati samāna indriya grāhya tvāt ghaṭa eka tva parimāṇa vat na ca avayava saṃyoga bahutva vyañcaka avyaṅyena avayavinā utpala tva vyañcaka dīpa avyaṅyena tad nīlimnā ghaṭa vṛtti pṛthakta avyañcaka avyaṅyena ekatvena vā vyabhicāraḥ avayava saṃyogā avayavinoḥ nīla tva utpala tvayoḥ ca avyāpya vyāpya vṛttinoḥ utpala tvasya ca adhika vṛtti tvena eka avacchedena vṛtti abhāvāt bahu tva pṛthaktva vyañcaka vyaṅya tvañca avayavi eka tvayoḥ iti na paraspara vyabhicāri vyañcaka vyaṅya tvam atas eva nīlā balākā iti atra rūpa parimāṇayoḥ arddha nikhāta vaṃśa saṅkhyā parimāṇayoḥ vā na vyabhicāraḥ iti mā evam varṇāḥ pratiniyata vyañcaka vyaṅkhyāḥ āśrayeṇa saha samāna indriya agrāhya tvāt gandha vat iti āpātataḥ sat pratipakṣa tvāt 
[122,iv]	vastutas tu ananyathā asidva pratyabhijñāna balena abheda siddhau pratiniyata vyañcaka vyaṅgya tva sādhakasya eva balavat tvam śabdasya śabda janaka tvañca śabda nāśaka tvam vīcī taraṅga nyāyena utpatti kalpa nañca kalpanam eva śabdasya śabde ajanaka tvāt anāśaka tvāñca antyādya śabda vat etena sāmānyavat tve sati asma bahid ādiḥ indriya ja pratyakṣa tvāt iti apāstam pratyabhijñāna bādhāt śabda tva gatvādeḥ asiddheḥ ca tasmāt śabdaḥ nityaḥ vyoma eka guṇa tvāt tad parimāṇa vat śrotra grāhya tvāt śabda tva vat viśeṣa guṇa antara asamāna adhikaraṇa eka vṛtti guṇa tvāt samaya parimāṇa vat pṛthivī itara nitya bhūta viśeṣa guṇa tvāt apākaja tve sati nitya eka samaveta tvāt jala paramāṇu rūpavat avyāsa jya vṛtti tve sati anātma vibhu guṇa tvāt kāla parimāṇa vat vipakṣe bādha kañca pratyabhijñānam eva iti 
[122,v^1]	atra ucyate gakāra ādi vyakta yona ekaikāḥ asti ca śuka sārikā manuṣya prabhaveṣu strīpuṃsa tad viśeṣa prabhaveṣu ca gakāra ādiṣu sphuṭatara vailakṣaṇyāt svarūpa tobheda prathā ikṣu kṣīra ādi mādhurya vat na ca iyam aupādhikī bheda pratītiḥ na hi vidita kuṅkumasya kuṅkuma aruṇā taruṇī iti vat strīpuṃsa prabha tvamānubhavikam upādhiḥ indriya āsannikarṣeṇa strīpuṃsā ādi bhedam aviduṣaḥ api śabda bheda pratyayāt yatas anumāpayanti śuka śabdaḥ ayam strī śabdaḥ ayam ityādi anyathā anyonya āśrayāt tad prabhava tve jñāte bheda pratyayaḥ tasmāt ca tad anumānam iti na ca kṛpāṇa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt kṛpāṇe mukha dīrgha tva vat aupapattikam aupa adhika tvam 
[122,v^2]	anya anuvidhāna abhāvāt atha vyañjaka vāyoḥ eva vailakṣaṇyam śuka ādi gakāra gata tvena bhāsate vāyoḥ upalabdhiḥ tena eva rūpeṇa iti ced na gakāra gata tve bādhaka abhāvāt na ca abheda pratyabhijñānam bādhakam na hi yaḥ eva śuka śabdaḥ saḥ eva strī śabdaḥ iti pratyabhijñānam anyathā teṣu bheda jñāna abhāvena vaktṛ viśeṣa anumānam na syāt na ca abhivyañjaka vāyoḥ eva vailakṣaṇyam śuka ādi anumāpakam tasya gakāra āvṛtti tvāt tatra ca ārope anumiteḥ bhrānta tva āpātāt tasmāt yathā kṛṣṇā gauḥ śuktāḥ gauḥ iti bhede bhāsamāne gakāra anugata pratītiḥ go tvam ālambate tathā śuka ādi gakāreṣu bheda ibha asamāne ayam gakāraḥ abhayam api gakāraḥ iti buddhiḥ ga tvam ālambate iti pratyabhijñā ca bheda prathā ca upapadyate 
[122,vi^1]	kiñca gatvā ādikam yadi na jātiḥ tadā kolāhala pratyayaḥ na syāt tathā hi nagara ādau bahubhiḥ varṇānām ekadā uccāraṇe dūra sthena anabhivyaktta gakāra ādi varṇa vibhāgam kolāhala mātram śrūyate na ca tatra varṇāni asya dhvani rūpasya śabdasya śrutiḥ sambhavati tad abhivyañcaka bherī tāṅana ādeḥ abhāvāt na ca varṇa abhivyañcakāḥ eva dhvani vyañjakāḥ sannidhāne api śrūyamāṇe varṇe tad śravaṇa prasaṅgāt na ca varṇa abhivyañja vāyubhiḥ eva dūre dhvani mātram abhivyajyate kavyañjakasya gavyañjanaḥ iva varṇa vyañjakasya dhvani vyañjane asāmarthyāt tad samartha śaṅkha ādeḥ abhāvāt ca na ca tatra śabda tvam eva pratīyate na śabdaḥ vyakti agrahe jātya grahāt na ca abhivyañjaka uvāyuḥ eva kolāhala tvena pratīyate 
[122,vi^2]	śabda tvena pratyayāt sannidhau api tathā pratyaya prasaṅgāt ca gakāra ādi grahe api teṣām paraspara bheda agrahāt kolāhala dhīḥ iti ced na teṣu vaidharmya abhāvāt tad abhāve anyobhāvasya abhāvasya abhāvāt svarūpa grahaṇāt samīpe vahu gakāreṣu bheda abhāvena tad agrahe kolāhala dhī prasaṅgat ca aneka varṇa uccāraṇasya tad hetu tve dūre api tat apratyaya āpatte tasmāt avaśyam gatvā ādi jāti rūpeyāḥ yat agrahe gakāra ādi grahe api kolāhala buddhi vyapadeśau asti ca śabdasya kaḥ api ca jāti viśeṣaḥ śrotra grāhyaḥ yasmāt prācī a ādi diś deśa viśiṣṭa śaṅkha prabhava tvam anumīyate avyapadesya tve api ikṣu kṣīra ādi mādhuryyauvāntara vat tat sattvāt anyathā diś deśa viśiṣṭa śaṅkha ādīnām grahe śrotrasya asāmarthāt tad pratītiḥ na syāt eva tathā api gatvā ādinā para apara bhāva anupapattyā śuka ādi gakāra ādiṣu na jāti viśeṣāḥ iti ced 
[122,vi^3]	śukakakāra ādiṣu katva ādi vyāpyāḥ nānā jātiḥ bhinnā tayā pratyekam śuka kakāra ādiṣu śuka ādi prabhava tvam anumāya tad vyavahāraḥ na tu śuka kakāra ādiṣu ekā jātiḥ asti śuka prabhava tva ādi anumāpikā tahi avahāra kārikā vā gatvā ādinā saṅkara prasaṅgāt gatvantu na nānā ananugata tvena tatas anugata vyavahāra anupapatteḥ atas eva tāra tvam api gatvā ādi vyāpyam nānā na tu ga tvam tad niścaye api gatvasan dehaḥ ca vyāpya tāvacchedaka rūpā niścayāt na ca anugata vyavahāra anupapattiḥ sajātīya mākṣātkāra pratibandhaka tāvat chedaka tvena anugatena nānā tāra tveṣu anugata vyavahāra sambhavāt tad ajñāne vyavahāra asiddheḥ tāra tva manda tve na jātī sa pratiyogika tvāt iti ced na 
[122,vi^4]	tāra tva tāratara tva ādayaḥ utkarṣa agi rūpāḥ jāti viśeṣāḥ eva te ca āśraye gṛhyamāṇaḥ eva gṛhyante na tu utkarṣa a adhyapekṣāḥ yathā madhuratara tva ādayaḥ utkarṣa vyavahāram itarasā apekṣāḥ kurvanti tathā manda ādi apekṣayā tāra tva ādi vyavahāram utkarṣaḥ tu jāti rūpāt anyaḥ asambhāvitaḥ eva gakāre tu na evam ananyathā asidvabheda pratyaya balena vaktṛ viśeṣa anumāna balena ca tad siddheḥ gatvaka tva vyāpya tad nānātva svīkārāt tava api vāyu vṛtti tve śuka ādi kakāra gakāra ādi vyañcaka vāyūnām vijātīya tvam vācyam tathā ca kakāra vyañjaka vāyu tu a vyāpyam yadi śuka varṇa abhivyañjaka vāyu tvam tadā śuka gakāra vyañjaka vāyau na syāt atha vyāpakam tadā sarve eva kavyañjaka vāyavaḥ śuka varṇa abhivyañjaka vāyavaḥ syuḥ tasmāt vāyu vṛtti tve api tāsām nānā tvam āvaśyakam 
[123,i]	atha astu strī puṃsā ādi gakāra bhedaḥ tathā api yāvat vaktṛ bhedam anantāḥ eva nityāḥ varṇāḥ pratyabhijñānāt iti ced asti utpāda vināśa pratītau satyām api saḥ eva ayam gakāraḥ iti pratyabhijñā asti hi tad anantaram api utpāda vināśa prathā na ca utpāda pratīti abheda pratyabhijñayoḥ anyatarasya parasparam vihāya anyat bādhakam asti na vā anayoḥ parasparam bādhya bādhaka bhāve vinigamakam yena eka bhrānta tvena avirodhaḥ syāt katham vā bheda ābhāt ajñānayoḥ anyatra avadhāritam paraspara pratibandhaka tvam paribhūya prathamam tayoḥ eka sattve api apara utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti saṅkaṭa praviṣṭa tvena pratyabhijñānam śabda nitya tve pramāṇayitum na śakyate 
[123,ii^1]	nanu evam utpattimat tva ādinā api anitya tva siddhiḥ katham ittham utpāda ādi buddhi pratyabhijñayoḥ api avaśyam viṣaya bhedaḥ eka viṣaya tve virodhena eka anantaram apara anutpatti prasaṅgāt evañca bhede bhāsamāne pratyabhijñāyāḥ sajātīya tvam viṣayaḥ na vyakti abhedaḥ na ca evam varṇaḥ tad janaka kaṇṭha tālu ādi abhidhātā abhāvāt iti vācyam tad jātīya tva pratīteḥ api saḥ ayam iti ākāra darśanāt yathā sā eva iyam gāthā tat eva idam auṣadham bahubhiḥ kṛtam mayā api pratyaham kriyamāṇam asti ityādau na hi tāvat varṇa mātram ānupūrvī jarā rājā nadī dīna ādiṣu tat na anātyāt 
[123,ii^2]	kintu tad uccāraṇa anantaram uccāraṇam tad jñāna anantaram jñānam vā tat ca nānā iti tadvatī gāthā api nānā eva naca abhede bhāsamāne utpāda ādi buddhiḥ eva anyasya utpāda ādikam avagāhate gakāra gata tva pratīteḥ bhrānta tva prasaṅgāt na ceṣṭāpattiḥ abhede bhāsamāne tad viruddha dharmmava tu abhramān udayāt vinigamaka abhāvena ubhayasya api yathārtha tvāt ca kutas tarhi tasyāḥ abhedaḥ viṣayaḥ yatra prathamam na bheda prathā atas eva bheda sattve tad ajñānāt kvicid sā bhrāntā tasmāt yatra bheda pratītiḥ tad itara bādhaka ābādhyā tatra pratyabhijñā eva na bhavati bhavanti vā tad jātīya tvam ālambate na tu bhrāntā viśeṣa darśane bhramān udayāt 
[123,iii^1]	api ca yathā śaṅkha ādi dhvanīnām utpatti vināśa pratyayāt tāra tva ādi viruddha dharma saṃsargāt ca anitya tve sā eveyaṅguḥ jarī iti ādi pratyabhijñā tad jātīya tva viṣayā tathā varṇa pratyabhijñā api anyathā dhvanayaḥ api nityāḥ syuḥ utpatti vināśa tāra tva ādi pratītīnām pratyabhijñāna balena aupādhika tvāt na ca varṇeṣu tāra tvena eva bhāsamānāḥ dhvanayā aupādhayaḥ sambhavanti na tu dhvaniṣu tad jātīyaḥ ayam iti syāt na tu saḥ ayam iti vācyam varṇa uccāraṇa daśāyām api gurjarīta ādi janakānām abhāvāt tasmāt utpatti vināśa tāra tva ādi pratyayasya pratyabhijñānasya ca tulya tve ddayoḥ api nitya tvam anitya tvam vā na ca ubhayoḥ api nitya tvam eva ukta nyāyena pratyabhijñāyāḥ tad jātīya tva viṣaya tvāt kiñca yadi vyaṅgyaḥ śabdaḥ syāt tadā bāhya loka abhāve ghaṭasya iva vyañcaka abhāve śabdasya anupalambhāt tad saṃśayaḥ syāt na tu iha idānīm śabdaḥ na asti iti niścayaḥ tasmāt varṇaḥ na nityaḥ anityaḥ vā satve sati utpattimat tvāt 
[123,iii^2]	asmad ādi bahis indriyaya grāhya tve sati jātimat tvāt asmad ādi pratyakṣa guṇa tvāt vā ātmā eka tva pratyakṣa tva pakṣe pratyakṣa viśeṣa guṇātvāt vyāpaka samaveta pratyakṣa viśeṣa guṇa tvāt anātma pratyakṣa guṇa tvāt avyāpya vṛtti tvāt īśvara jñānañca na tathā tad prayoka kāraṇa abhāvāt bahis indriya vyavasthā hetu guṇa tvāt bhūta pratyakṣa guṇa tvāt utkarṣa apakarṣā śabda pravṛtti nimitta jātimat tvāda ityādi rasa tva ādi vyāpya jāteḥ nānātve api tādṛśa pravṛtti nimitta tvasya sādhāraṇyāt na ca atra sāghana avacchinnasya pakṣa dharmmau avicchannasya vā sādhyasya vyāpakaḥ sparśa vat samaveta tvam upādhiḥ sarvatra varṇa ātmaka śabda pakṣīkaraṇe vyoma guṇeṣu anityeṣu dhvaniṣu sādhya avyāpaka tvāt sparśavat padasya pakṣa mātra vyāvartaka tvena pakṣetara tvāt ca iti yadā ca varṇāḥ eva na nityāḥ tadā kā eva kathā puruṣa vivakṣā dhīna anupūvḥ vyādi viśiṣṭa varṇa samuha rūpāṇām padānām kutas ta śañca tad samūha rūpasya vāvayasya kutas ta māñca tad samūhasya vedasya iti 
[123,iv^1]	tathā api paratantra puruṣa parampara adhīna tayā pravāha āvicchedam eva nitya tvam brūmaḥ iti ced na smṛti ācāra anumitānām śākhānām uccheda darśanāt syāt etat vivāda padam apūrva bodhikā smṛtiḥ smṛti artha anubhava janaka veda mūlāḥ avigīta mahā jana parigṛhīta smṛti tvāt pratyakṣa veda mūlaka smṛti vat veda mūlaka tvañca veda janyā anubhava janya tvam jñāna dvārā jñāyamānasya eva vedasya smṛti hetutayā anumānam kuvindasya iva jñāna ādi vyavahitasya paṭe na tu kāraṇa kāraṇa tā vede sati eva tad pratisandhāne smṛti praṇayanāt veda artha smṛti tā ca prasiddhi siddhā smṛti arthaḥ ca smṛtitaḥ eva upasthitaḥ na ca mṛti artha bodhaka veda anumāne smṛti artha rūpa veda arthasya viṣaya tvāt vedaḥ anuvādakaḥ jñāna antara upanītasya viśeṣaṇa tvena viśiṣṭa buddhi sambhavāt pāka kṛtau mānasa pratyakṣāyām pākasya saṃjñā saṃjñi jñāne saṃjñāyāḥ jñāna yathā artha tve tad anu vyavasāye bhrama viṣayasya iva 
[123,iv^2]	anyathā abhrānta bhrānti jña saṅkara āpattiḥ na tu śabda arthaḥ anumānasya viṣayaḥ tasya asiddha tvena ajanakatayā smṛti avyāpaka tvāt sa ca vedaḥ nityam anumeyaḥ eva anumitāt eva artham avadhāryya smṛti praṇayana sambhavāt nanu āsaṃsāram apaṭhitasya na veda tvam utpattitaḥ abhivyaktitaḥ mauni śloka vat abhiprāyatīva ānupūrvī hīna varṇa mātrasya nirarthaka tvāt jñāna janaka samabhivyāhārasya aneka tve viśeṣān anumānāt ca iti ced na smṛti artha jñāpaka tvena eva jñātasya vedasya smṛti artha anubhāvaka tvāt na hi śābda bodhe niyata pada ānupūrvī hetuḥ vyabhicārāt padasya varṇa viśeṣa ānupūrvī niyame api tad ta varṇa ānupūrvīka pada viśeṣa tvena na hetu tvam hasta kara ādi padānām pratyekam vyabhicārāt kintva vyabhicāri tadartha jñāpaka tvena jñātasya lāghavāt āvaśyaka tvāt ca tad artha jñāpaka tva jñāna artham eva kvacid varṇa krama svara viśeṣāṇām upayogaḥ atas eva varṇa lopa ādau kuśam ānaya iti sakāra sandehe lipau uccāraṇe vā hasta kara sandehe api vākya artha bodhaḥ 
[124,i^1]	nanu kramika padava tvam vākya tvam na ca atra pada kramaḥ anuccāryamāṇatayā uccāraṇa adhīnasya yugapad anumīyamāna tayā buddhi adhīnasya vā tasya abhāvāt iti ced na hi kramika padava tvam vākya tvam gauḥ aśvaḥ iti ādau abhāvāt kintu viśiṣṭa artha para śabda tvam tat ca atra api asti eva atha anuccāryyamāṇasya na vākya tvam na vai artha anubhāvaka tvam iti ced na lipyanumitānām api vākya tvāt artha bodhaka tvāt ca lipi tulyā ca smṛtiḥ kiñca vākyam uccāryate na tu uccāraṇāt vākya tvam anyathā vākyam uccārayeti atra ananvaya āpattiḥ anuccāriti tam auniślokaḥ ca vākyam na syāt uccāraṇa daśā yāñca vākya tve vākyasya asatvam eva syāt ekadā tāvat padānām uccāraṇa abhāvāt na ca kṛta kriyamāṇa kariṣyamāṇa uccāraṇasya vākya tvam 
[124,i^2]	samudāye pratyekasya abhāvāt tasmāt artha viśeṣa jñāpaka tvena eva jñātāt artha viśeṣa dhīḥ atas eva asti vahni liṅgam iti śabdāt pratīte dhūme vahneḥ anumānam na tu tad artha jñāpaka tvena jñātāt padāt artha jñāna mātram syāt na tu saṃsarga dhīḥ ghaṭaḥ karma tvam ānayanam bhāvanā tat dodhakam iti jñāne api ghaṭamānaya iti vākyāt iva anvaya bodha abhāvāt evañcān vaprakāra karmma tva ādi upasthāpaka vibhakti ādimat pada viśeṣasya tad utthāpita ākāṅkṣā ādeḥ ca jñānam vākya artha dhī hetuḥ atas na tarvinā jñāpaka tva mātreṇa jñātāt artha dhīḥ hasta kara ādi sandehe kuśam ānaya ityādau vibhakti ādi jñānāt eva vākya artha anubhavaḥ iti 
[124,ii^1]	mā evam na hi tad tad vibhakti ādimat pada viśeṣa tvena vākya arthathī hetu tvam ananugamāt kintu ghaṭaḥ karmma tvam iti ādi anvaya virodhi padā janya padārtha upasthitiḥ tathā sā ca iha api asti vastutas tu nānā padāt padārtha upasthiti anantaram vākya artha vodhe tathā eva sāmagrī anumita vedāt vākya artha anubhave vilakṣaṇā eva sā smṛti artha jñāpaka tvena eva jñātasya smṛti artha anubhāvaka tvāt dharmma grāhaka pramāṇena tasya tathā eva siddha tvāt tavaśavarasi ā iva aśarīrasya kartṛ tve atas eva varṇapada vibhakti ādi viśeṣa ghaṭita tvena ajñātasya akhaṇḍasya sa khaṇḍasya vā vākya artha anubhāvaka tvāt padārtha sthānīyaḥ tasya vākya arthaḥ tatra
[124,ii^2]	varṇa samūhaḥ padam pada samūhaḥ vākyam iti atra api tatas grahaḥ pramāṇa śabda tva mātreṇa tasya siddheḥ anyathā kḷpta hetum vinā saḥ anubhāvakaḥ ityādau tat asiddhau āśraya asiddhiḥ siddhau vā bādhaḥ tena vinā eva sarva anupapattim paribhūya tad anubhāvaka tvasya dharmma grāhaka māna siddha tvāt atas eva kvacid stuti nindābhyām kalpita vidhi niṣedhaka veda artham adhigatya pravṛtti nivṛttī anyathā vidhi niṣedhakānām nānā prakāraka tvena vibhakti ādi viśeṣa vat padasya anumātum aśakyatvāt na tatas artha dhīḥ syāt tathā api vaktṛ jñāna anumāna anantaram iva anumita anumānāt eva vākya artha siddheḥ laukika vākya vat vedasya anuvādaka tvam syāt iti ced 
[124,ii^3]	na dharmma āgrāhaka mānena smṛti artha jñāpaka tayā jñātāt sambhūta sāmagrīka tvena anupadam eva vākya artha bodha udayāt apekṣaṇīya antara abhāvāt anumānasya vyāpti ādi jñāna apekṣita tvena vilambita tvāt na ca vedasya api yogyatā ādi jñāna apekṣita tayā vilambaḥ tad nirapekṣa bodhakasya eva dharmma grāhaka māna siddha tvāt yogyatā ādi viśiṣṭasya iva anumānāt vā evam maṅgala ācārasya ādigīta riṣṭa ācāra tvena kartavyatām anumāya sā kartavyatā veda bodhitā alaukikā vigīta śiṣṭa ācāra kartavyatā tvāt iti tad vodhaka tvena anumita vedāt kartavyatā adhīḥ tatas pravṛttiḥ 
[124,iii]	nanu saḥ ācāraḥ veda bodhita kartavyatā adhīkaḥ tādṛśa ācāra tvāt iti anumita vedāt natkartati atādhīḥ vibhakti ādikam vinā anumita vedāt tad kartavya tā jñāna abhāvāt maṅgalam ācaret iti evaṃrūpasya ca vedasya na anumānam tathā vyāpti abhāvāt tasmāt tasya kartavyatām anumāya tad bodhaka veda anumānam prathamam kartavyatā jñāne api veda anumānam avinā abhāvāt na ca tatas eva pratyakṣa veda anumānam pratyakṣa tve uccheda anupapatteḥ śākhā antara vat 
[124,iv]	yat tu aṣṭakāḥ kartavyāḥ kāryāḥ aṣṭakāḥ iti evaṃrūpam eva vākyam anumeyam upasthita tvāt evañca tatra eva arthe prati puruṣam anyānyaveda anumānam na doṣāya eka artha aneka pada upasthitau vā aneka vākya anumānam eva iti tat na ācārataḥ veda anumāne maṅgalam ācaret ityādi anyatara upasthitau niyama abhāvāt aneka veda kalpane ca sva anubhava virodhaḥ manu smṛti mūlañca anekam vākyam na āvaśyakam iti katham ādhunikaḥ anekam anuminuyāt na ca smṛti artha bodhakovedaḥ smṛti sadṛśaḥ eva anumeyaḥ niyamataḥ smṛteḥ upasthita tvāt iti vācyam tad artha smṛteḥ api nānā prakāra tvāt tasya ca pradoṣa ādau anuccarita vedasya iva veda tvam śrotra grahāṇa arha tayā ca śabda tvam vākya tvam artha bodhaka tvāt iti etat eva yuktam smṛti ācāreṇa ca anumitaḥ vedaḥ artham bodhayati iti pūrva pūrveṇa anumita vedāt uttarottara smṛti ācārau iti na andha paramparā śabda artha śarakti graha vat svatas pramāṇa mūlaka tvāt tasmāt itya anumeya tvam vedasya na tu ucchedaḥ iti 
[124,v^1]	atra ucyate ucchinna vedāt artham pratītya smṛti ācārayoḥ upapatteḥ na sāmagryantara kalpanam atas eva na āśraya asiddhiḥ bādhaḥ vā smṛti ācāra anumita vedasya asmābhiḥ abhyupagamāt idānīñca smṛteḥ artham prati iti ācārāt ca kartavyatām anumāya pravṛttiḥ na ca evam kim vedena iti vācyam tulya tvāt avinā abhāvāt ca tad kalpanam tulyam tathā ca smṛti ācārayoḥ veda janyā anubhava mūla tva anumānāt eva pakṣa dharmma tā balāt pratyakṣa veda mūlaka tva siddhiḥ anyathā tasya anubhāvaka tva abhāvena mūla tva anupapatteḥ tasmāt smṛti ācāra anumitaḥ vedaḥ pratyakṣaḥ adhyayana viṣayaḥ ca veda tvāt sammata vat 
[124,v^2]	anyadhā sāmagrī antara kalpane gaurava prasaṅgaḥ nanu stuti nindā artha vādena kalpitāt vidhi niṣedhaka vākyāt katham artham avagamya pravṛtti nivṛttī na hi tatra varṇa pada vibhakti vidhi pratyaya krama viśeṣāṇām anumānam sambhavati vyabhicārāt iti ced na stuti nindā vākyābhyām pravṛtti nivṛtti parābhyām pravṛtti nivṛtti hetuḥ arthaḥ eva kalpyate lāghavāt na tu vidhāyaka niṣedhaka vākyam gauravāt ukta doṣāt ca yatra ca artha vādāt eva tad artha vagamaḥ tarati mṛtyum iti ādau tatra na tad kalpanā api atha tasya adhyayana viṣaya tve śākhā antarava tvāt vahubhiḥ medhā vibhiḥ ādhyātmika śakti sampannaiḥ dhiyamāṇa śākhāyāḥ uccheda asambhavaḥ iti ced 
[124,v^3]	na ekasya na sakala śākhā adhyayane śaktiḥ iti ekena iva aparaiḥ api tad anadhyayane śākhā uccheda sambhavāt eka an adhītāyāḥ apara adhyayana viṣaya tva niyame māna abhāvāt śākhā tvasya iva pratyakṣa śākhā tvasya aprayojaka tvāt yadi api veda sahasra śākhā vidaḥ vyāsa ādayaḥ santi eva tathā api adhyayana abhāvaḥ eva śākhā ucchedaḥ nanu śākhā ucchede varṇa pada vākya hāni śaṅkayā pratyakṣa vedāt api vākya artha prayogayoḥ aniścaye vaidika vyavahāra mātram lupteta iti ced na śrūyamāṇa mātrasya eva mahā jana parigṛhīta tvāt tanmātra bodhita aṅga iti kartavya tayā eva śiṣṭaiḥ anuṣṭhīyamāna tvāt ca tad artha niścayāt na ca ucchinna śākhā bodhita iti kartavyatā śaṅkayā ekasmin api karmmaṇi anāśvāsa prasaṅgaḥ nānā śākhā iti kartavyatā āpūraṇīya tvāt tasya iti sāmpratam santi hi tat tad karmmaṇi nānā śākhā bodhita sakala iti kartavyatā bodhanāya enam eva kāla krama bhāvinam ana aśvāsam aśaṅkamānaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ praṇītāḥ mahā jana parigṛhītāḥ smṛtayā eti nānā āśvāsaḥ anyathā ekasya sakala śākhā anavagamāt śākhā antara bodhita iti kartavya tā saṃśayena eka śākhātas na artha niścayaḥ syāt 
[124,vi]	yat tu vibhakti ādimat tad tad papadānām tad samudāyānāñca pratyakṣatu anteṣu api kaścid vedaḥ tatra ayam samudāyaḥ vedaḥ iti aniścayaḥ eva nitya anugeya arthaḥ veda tvam vā tatra anumeyam iti tat na pratyakṣa veda atirikta vākye tad abhiyuktānām mahājanānām veda tva abhāva niścayāt atas eva veda tvam tatra na anumeyam bādhāt viśiṣya pakṣa ajñānāt ca dharma vedanā janaka tvañca veda tvam na anumeyam tad janakatvasya pratyakṣa tvāt na adhyayana viṣaya tvam tad abhāvāt na jātiḥ anabhyupagamāt iti 
[125,i]	syāt etat smṛti ācārayoḥ veda mūla tve tatra uccheda ādi vivādaḥ tat eva tu asiddham tathā hi veda samāna arthā mahājana parigṛhītā ca smṛtiḥ sva artha upasthiti anantaram smṛti artha anubhāvaka veda anumāne liṅgam tathā ca prāthamyāt sādhya prasiddhi artham upajīvya tvāt ca smṛteḥ eva apūrva ādi vākya artha jñānam astu kim vedena tad arthasya smṛtitaḥ eva siddheḥ apūrvasya api śabdeka gamya tvena smṛtitaḥ jñātasya jñāpaka tvena anuvādaka tā āpatteḥ ca sā ca smṛti antarāt iti anādiretra smṛti dhārā vaśyakī anyathā manu smṛteḥ pūrvantavāpi veda anumānam na syāt sarvā ca smṛtiḥ smṛti janya vākya artha pramā janya tvena mahā jana parigṛhīta tvena ca pramāṇam iti na andha paramparā pratyakṣā ca smṛtiḥ smṛti mūlam na anumitāḥ anumita veda vat tasya ananubhāvaka tvāt veda artha smṛtita aprasiddhiḥ tu pratyakṣa veda mūla smṛti sāhacaryeṇa bhramāt pratyakṣa veda ābodhita lobha nyāya mūla smṛtau iva tāntrikāṇām liṅga bhāsa janya veda mūla tva bhramāt vā bhavantī na sambhavat mūla antarāṇām veda mūlaka tvam kalpayati 
[125,ii^1]	atha smṛtiḥ iva tad veda mūlaka tva prasiddhiḥ api mahā jana parigṛhītāḥ evañca sā veda mūla tva nibandhanāḥ avigīta mahā jana parigṛhīta veda mūla tva prasiddhi tvāt pratyakṣa veda mūla smṛtau tad prasiddhi vat evam veda artha tā prasiddhiḥ api anyathā mahā jana parigṛhīta anādare vedasmṛtyoḥ api prāmāṇyam na syāt iti ced na yūpa hasti ādi smṛteḥ tad prasiddhau vyabhicārāt kḷpta lobha āditaḥ eva tad sambhavāt vicārakāṇām vipratipatteḥ ca tatra tad prasiddhau vigānam mahājanānām iti ced na atra api mūla antara sambhavāt vipratipatteḥ ca vigānam eva teṣām atas eva smṛtīnām nyāya mūla tve sambhavati veda mūla tva siddhau api na veda mūla tvam na ca veda mūle ayam iti kṛtvā smṛteḥ mahājana parigrahāt tad mūla tvam veda mūlā iyam iti prathamam jñātum aśakyatvāt śakya tve vā kim anumānena na ca veda mūla tvena prakāreṇa mahā jana parigrahaḥ 
[125,ii^2]	aprasiddheḥ manu ādi smṛti tvena pūrva mahā jana parigraheṇa uttarottareṣām parigrahāt anuṣṭhāna ādi upapatteḥ evam har lāka ādi ācāre api veda liṅgena eva kartavyatā jñāna upapatteḥ kim vedena tad arthasya liṅgāt eva upapatteḥ avigīta alaukika viṣayaka śiṣṭa ācārasya veda mūla tva darśanāt veda anumāne ca avigīta śiṣṭa ācāra tvena bhojana ādi ācāraḥ api veda mūlaḥ syāt vedam vinā api tad kartavyatā ādhī sambhavāt na tad artham veda eti iha api tulyam ācāra kartavyatā anumānayoḥ anādi tvena ācārāṇām kartavyatva anumāna mūlaka tvāt na andha paramparā na ca pūrva anumāna sāpekṣam uttara anumānam iti svatantra pramāṇa mūlaka tva abhāvāt sā vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā sattvena sarveṣām svatantra pramāṇa tvāt na api itara prāmānya adhīnam sarvasya prāmāṇyam iti na nirapekṣa tvam pratyakṣa ādeḥ api tathā tva āpatteḥ 
[125,iii_125,iv]	etena vivāda padam ācāraḥ nirapekṣa pramāṇa mūlakaḥ avigīta mahā jana ācāra tvāt pratyakṣa veda mūla ācāra vat iti nirastam anumānasya nirapekṣa pramāṇa tvāt pramāṇa mūla tvena eva hetoḥ upapatteḥ nirapekṣa tvasya gauraveṇa aprayojaka tvāt ca na ca sa apekṣa tvena na pramāṇa tā vyāpti ādi satvāt anyathā pramāṇe nairapekṣasya vaiyarthāt na ca ācāre veda mūla tva prasiddheḥ tad anumānam asiddheḥ vyabhicārāt anyathā upapatteḥ ca na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigrahāt tathā na hi veda mūlaḥ ayam iti kṛtvā mahājanānām tad parigrahaḥ veda mūla tvasya prathamam jñātum aśakyatvāt śakya tve vā kinumānena na ca veda mūla tvena eva mahājana parigṛhītaḥ ayam ācāraḥ iti jñātvā tatra mahā jana parigrahaḥ gauḥ ivāda siddheḥ ca pūrva mahā jana parigrahāt eva uttarottareṣām parigrahāt anuṣṭhāna upapatteḥ tādṛśa smṛti ācārayoḥ veda mūla tvena vyāpteḥ veda siddhiḥ iti ced na asambhavat mūla antara tvasya upādhi tvāt anyathā lobha nyāya mūla smṛteḥ api veda mūla tva prasaṅgaḥ astu vā smṛti ācārayoḥ anādi tvam na ca ācārāt smṛtiḥ smṛteḥ ācāraḥ iti andha paramparā mūla bhūta pramāṇa abhāvāt iti vācyam smṛti ācārayoḥ ubhayoḥ api pramāṇa tvāt anyathā na tatas veda anumānam api iti 
[125,v]	ucyate pralaye pūrva smṛti ācārayoḥ ucchedāt sarga ādau nitya sarva jñeśvara praṇīta veda mūla tvam smṛti ācārayoḥ anyathā mūla abhāvena andha paramparā prasaṅgaḥ na manu ādīnām atīndriya artha darśi tvam tad upāya śravaṇa ādeḥ tadānīm abhāvāt pūrva sarga siddha sarvajñam anu ādayaḥ eva te iti ced na pramāṇa abhāvāt smṛti ācārayo pramāṇa mūla tvam eva tad kalpakam iti ced na pratisargam teṣām anya anya tva kalpane gaukham iti ekasya eva nitya sarvajñasya kalpanāt na ca smṛtayaḥ eva tad praṇītāḥ tāsām manu ādi kartṛka tvena smṛtau bodhanāt smṛtau eva smṛtīnām veda mūla tva smaraṇāt ca evañca smṛti ācārayoḥ mahājana parigraha dveda mūla tva sādhakam api bhagavati pramāṇam atas eva pratimanvantarañcā eṣā śrutiḥ anyā avidhīyate iti āgamaḥ api evañca pūrvam pratyakṣa mūlau eva smṛti ācārau agre ca kāla krameṇa āyuḥ ārogya bala śraddhā grahaṇa dhāraṇa ādi śakteḥ ahara har apacīyamāna tvāt tad adhyayana vicchedena śākhā ucchedāt smṛti ācārābhyām eva kartavyatām adhigatya prakṛtiḥ 
[125,vi^1]	nanu evam smṛtiḥ aḥ tu veda mūla amaṅgala ādya ācāra rūvīśvarāt eva bhaviṣyati ghaṭa lipya ādi sampradāya vat iti ced na bahu vyāpāra ghaṭitasya tat tad ācārasya guru tvena maṅgalam ācaret ityādi vākyasya eva lāghavena kalpanāt na ca maṅgala ādi pada śakti graha artham ācāraḥ āvaśyakaḥ iti vācyam svarga ādi pada vat vākya arthe tad upapatteḥ atas eva yatra vacana mātrāt para pratipattiḥ tatranācāraḥ parīkṣakāṇām tasya ca veda tvam na īśvara praṇīta tvena śakti grahaṇa artha tad vacane vyabhicārāt kintu tādṛśa ācārasya veda mūla tva niyamāt iti syāt etat pralaye sati evam eva tat saḥ eva tu na asti pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ced na 
[125,vi^2]	kāla kapālāni āvṛtti ghaṭa prāgabhāvaḥ kārya dravya an ādhāra ādhāraḥ kāryya dravyān adhikaraṇa kāryya adhikaraṇa vṛttiḥ vā abhāva tvāt ākāśavatyā anyaḥ bhāva vat iti vṛtta pralaya sādhanāt evam eva ghaṭa dhvaṃsam pakṣīkṛtya āgāmi pralaya sādha jam yat vā ghaṭaḥ kārya dravya an adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt śabda vat yat vā kārya dravya tvam kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa kārya adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyagi vṛtti kārya mātra vṛtti tvāt śabda tva vat yat vā eka kālīnāḥ sarve paramāṇavaḥ samagra upādeya prabandha śūnyāḥ ārambhaka tvāt naṣṭa pavana ārambhaka paramāṇu vat sarvatra pakṣa tā avacchedaka avacchinnam sādhyam pratīyate iti ekakātve śūnyatā labhyate na ca pavana parama aṇūnām api pakṣa tvena aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam 
[125,vi^3]	pakṣa dharmatā bala labhya sādhya apratīteḥ ameda anumāna vat ca pakṣasya dṛṣṭānta tva avirodhaḥ yat vā paramāṇavaḥ kārya dravyān adhikaraṇa vṛtti kāryavantaḥ nitya dravya tvāt ākāśa vat bhū golaka santānaḥ ayam bhū golaka santāna an adhikaraṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogī kāryatvāt ghaṭa vat yat vā etad karma atiriktā nikarmmāṇi etad prativandhaka pratibadhyāni karma tvāt etat karma vat na ca atra vyabhicāra śaṅkā sarveṣām evaṃrūpa tvāt anevambhāve ca svabhāva pradhyavāt anyathā niyame api niyama antara apekṣāyām anavasthiteḥ āgamaḥ api amum eva artham saṃvadati iti kṛtam prasakta anuprasaktyā 
[126,i]	ācāra mūla tvam vedasya pravartaka jñāna janaka tvena bhavati iti pravartaka jñānam nirūpyate tatra abhidhā saṅkalpa apūrva bhāvanā jñānam na pravartakam tasmin sati api apravṛtteḥ asati api pravṛtteḥ ca kāryatva jñānam pravartakam iti guravaḥ tathā hi jñānasya kṛtau janyāyām cikīrṣā atiriktam na kartavyam asti tad sattve kṛti vilambe hetu antara abhāvāt cikīrṣā ca kṛti sādhya tva prakārikā kṛti sādhya kriyā viṣaya icchā pākam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti tad anubhavāt sā ca sva kṛti sādhya tā jñāna sādhyā icchāyāḥ sva prakāraka dhī sādhya tva niyamāt atas eva sva kṛti sādhye pāke pravartete na tu iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyā sva kṛtya sādhye cikirṣā patteḥ sva kṛti asādhya tva jñānam pratibandhakam iti ced na tad abhāva kāraṇa tve gauravāt 
[126,ii]	atha abhāvaḥ ubhaya siddhaḥ kṛti sādhya ta adhīra siddhā iti atas na lāghava avasaraḥ iti ced na yatra śabdāt anumānāt vā daivāt sā tatra lāghava avatārāt icchāyāḥ sva prakāraka jñāna sādhya tva niyamena kṛti sādhya tva jñānasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca janaka jñānam vighaṭayate eva jñānasya pratibandhaka tvāt ca vyāpti jñāna vighaṭana dvārāḥ anumiti pratibandhaka anaikāntika jñāna vat anyathā sva kṛti asādhya tva aniṣṭa sādhanatva upekṣaṇīya tva niṣphala tva jñānam pratibandhakam kriyā jñānam eva pravartakam kalpyeta 
[126,iii]	nanu sanaḥ dhātu artha gocara icchā vāci tvāt lāghavāt ca kṛtau icchā cikīrṣā sā ca vṛṣṭauviva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt iti ced na vahninā sādhayāmi iti vat kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchāyāḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvam anubhūyamānāyāḥ sanantā vācya tvena gauraveṇa ca pratyākhyātum aśakyatvāt kiñca pākam cikīrṣati iti atra prādhānyena pākasya icchā viṣaya tvam anubhūyate na tu kṛteḥ dhātoḥ ca san pratyaya abhidheya icchā prakāra vāci tvam odanam bubhukṣate iti atra bhojana viśeṣyatayā odanasya icchā viṣaya tva anubhavāt iṣṭa sādhana tvena vṛṣṭau iva kṛtauvicchā sambhave api kṛtīcchā na pravartikā kintu sva kṛti sādhya icśā eva ghaṭam jānāti cikīrṣati karoti iti jñāna cikīrṣā kṛtīnām eka viṣaya tva anubhavāt 
[126,iv]	atha yadi kṛtyā sādhayitum icchā sā tadā cikīrṣitasya pākasya anyatas siddhau sā na apagacchet na hi upāya viśeṣa sādhya tvena icchā upāya antara adhīna phala lābhena nivāryate prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsāyāḥ anivṛtteḥ iti ced na sva viṣaya sidva tvasya phala icchā vicchedasya ca upāya icchā virodhi tvāt asti ca tatra pāka odanayoḥ siddha tvam anya odana icchāyām pāka cikīrṣā bhavati eva pratyuta asiddha tvāt kṛtau eva icchā na vicchidyeta yadi kṛti viṣaya siddha tva phala icchā vicchedau na virodhinau prītyā dhana lābhe ca tad adhika dhana icchā na vicchidyate tasya asiddha tvāt tad phala icchāyāḥ ca sattvāt dhana mātra arthitnaḥ ca prītyā dhana lābhe api pratigraheṇa tad lipsā na asti eva dhana mātrasya siddha tvāt kiñcid viśeṣa siddhyā eva hi sāmānya it chā vicchedaḥ anyathā sakala sva viṣaya siddheḥ asambhavena tad vicchedaḥ na syāt eva 
[126,v^1]	vastutas tu kriyā anukūlā kṛtiḥ iṣṭa upāyaḥ iti jñāne kriyāyāḥ kṛti sādhya tvam iṣṭa upāya tvañca bhātam kriyā dvāra eva kṛteḥ iṣṭa sādhana tvāt iti tat bodhāt kṛtau iva kṛti sādhya tvena kriyāyām api sā eva icchā iti cikīrṣāyām kṛti sādhya tva prakāra naiyatyam atas kṛti samāna viṣaya cikīrṣā tvena cikīrṣāyāḥ kṛti kāraṇa tvam na tu kṛti icchā tvena bhinna viṣaya tayā gauravāt tathā api yena rūpeṇa yasya iṣṭa sādhana tvam tena prakāreṇa tatra icchā yathā sva kedāra vṛṣṭi tvena iṣṭa sādhana tvāt tathā eva iti tathā kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya iṣṭā sādhana tvam atas kṛti sādhya tvena tatra icchā bhavati iti 
[126,v^2]	kṛtau kṛti viṣaye vā cikīrṣāyām na vṛṣṭī icchā vilakṣaṇa sāmagryantara kalpanam iti ced bhavet evam yadi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā syāt na ca evam gauravāt kintu pāka tvena sa tu kṛtim vinā na iti anyat etat vahninā sādhayamīti vat kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna devā iti ced tarhi tatra vahni sādhya tā jñāna vat atra api kṛti sādhya tva jñānam kāraṇam āvaśyakam kṛtau ca anubhava siddha cikīrṣā adhīna tvam viśeṣaḥ tena prāṇa pañcaka sañcāre jīvana yoni kṛti sādhye na pravṛtti anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tatra pravṛrteta 
[126,vi]	nanu cikīrṣā adhīna tvasya upalakṣaṇa tve upalakṣya mātra gata anati prasakta dharma abhāvāt kṛti mātrasya ca ati prasaḍgāt tad tad kṛti viśeṣāḥ upalakṣyāḥ tathā ca tad ananugamāt pravṛtti ananugamaḥ viśeṣaṇa tve cikīrṣāyām pravṛttau ca cikīrṣā jñāna kāraṇa tve gauravam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ca kiñca cikīrṣā asādhya avasthāyāḥ kṛteḥ siddha avastha sādhana tva virodhena kṛti sādhya tā pāka ādau na jñāyeta iti ced na asti hi kṛti viśeṣaḥ mānasa pratyakṣa siddhaḥ jīvana yoni prayatna vyāvṛttaḥ cikīrṣā upalakṣyaḥ yatra cikīrṣā kāraṇa tva grahaḥ sa ca tava jāti rūpaḥ mama tu anugata kāṇa upādhi rūpaḥ evañca cikīrṣā adhīna tvena anugatena kṛti viśeṣāṇam upalakṣyāṇām anugata tvam api yathā go tvena taṭa sthena upalakṣitāḥ mahiṣī ādi vyāvṛtta dhāna karma vyakti viśeṣāḥ dhenu padena ucyante na tu go tvam api tathā cikīrṣā api evam jīvana yoni yatna vyāvṛtta kṛti viśeṣāṇām kṛti tvena jñānam kāraṇam iti na ananugamaḥ 
[126,vii]	nanu kṛti sādhye na kṛtiḥ vaśeṣaṇam asattvāt sattve vā kṛtau satyām jñānam jñāne ca kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ na upalakṣaṇam ati prasaḍgāt iti ced na kṛtiḥ hi jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam eva sādhye ca paricāyaka tayā upalakṣaṇam anyathā iṣṭa sādhane api iṣṭam na viśeṣaṇam asattvāt na upalakṣaṇam ati prasaḍgāt liṅga jñāna ādau vā kā gatiḥ 
[126,viii]	nanu evam śrame api cikīrṣā syāt tasya api cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti sādhya tvāt atra vadantiśramaḥ tu bhojana ādi kriyā sādhyaḥ na tad kṛti sādhyaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt kṛteḥ sva dhvaṃsa sākṣātkāra atirikte cikīrṣā viṣaya mātre janakatvāt na hi bhojana cikīrṣā adhīna kṛtyā gamanam sādhyate iti kecid tat na gurutara bhāra uttolane kṛtya sādhye bhramāt pravṛttasya nigaḍa niścala dehasya vā kṛtau satyam uttam uttolana calana kriyā anutpāde api śrama anubhavāt kṛteḥ eva kāraṇa tvāt na tu tad janya kriyāḥ sukhe vyabhicārāt ca na hi sukham kṛti kāraṇa cikīrṣā viṣayaḥ upāya cikīrṣā janyā hi kṛtiḥ na tu sukha cikīrṣā janyā cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam na śrame dveṣa yoni prayatnāt api tad utpatteḥ iti apare tat na śatra badhasya iṣṭa sādhana tvena cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvāt dveṣasya yatna ajanaka tvāt dveṣa siddhiḥ tu śatrum dveṣmi iti anubhava balāt 
[126,ix^1]	yat tu śramaḥ kṛti tvena kṛti sādhyaḥ na cikīrṣā adhīna kṛtivena yadi acikīrṣite api śrame cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti tvena kāraṇa tā syāt tadā cikīrṣitam eva bhojanam kṛtyā sādhyate na acikīrṣitam gamana ādi iti na syāt śrama vat gamane api tad janya tva prasaṅgāt bhojana ādiḥ ca cikīrṣā adhīna kṛti viśeṣāt sa hi kṛti mātram vyabhicarati jīvana yoni kṛteḥ tad anutpādāt yat vā śramaḥ na bhojana kṛti sādhyaḥ kintu tad nirantara utpannāt jīvana yoni prayatnāt eva iti tat na na hi kṛrtivena tat śrama janaka tvam 
[126,ix^2_127,i]	na api kṛtī antarāt eva śrama utpattiḥ jīvana yoni prayatne sati api bhāra udvahna ādi karma kurvataḥ tādṛśa śramān anubhavena tasya śrama ajanaka tvāt tasmāt bhojana ādi vat śrama viśeṣāṇām api bhojana ādi kṛti sādhya tvam ananya gatika tvāt suptasya sveda ādi anumitaḥ śramaḥ tad janyaḥ iti ced na sveda ādeḥ śramāni ahetuka tvāt anyathā jāgare api tad anuvṛttau śrama anuvṛtti prasaṅgāt iti mā evam sva icchā adhīna tvasya kṛti viśeṣaṇa tvāt śramaḥ ca niyamataḥ anya icchā adhīna kṛti sādhyaḥ śrame duḥkha tvena icchā virahāt atas eva anya icchā janya kṛti sādhya tvena śramaḥ na antarīyakaḥ iti ucyate sva cikīrṣa adhīna tvantu na kṛtau viśeṣaṇam gauravāt anye tu kṛti gatam dharma antaram eva uddeśya tvam tad viśiṣṭa kṛti sādhyaḥ ca na śramaḥ acikīrṣita tvāt kintu kṛti mātra sādhyaḥ atas eva kaṣṭam karma iti anubhavaḥ lokānām 
[127,ii_127,iii]	atas eva kaṣṭam karma uti anubhavaḥ lokānām evam cikīrṣāyām mama ekam kṛti sādhya tvam prayojakam tava tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañcā iti ca tuṣṭyam icchā prayojakantu mama sukha tvam duḥkha abhāva tvañcā iti dvayam vṛṣṭi sādhye sukhe hi icchā vṛṣṭim api viṣayīkarī iti na tu iṣṭa sādhana tvena tatra icchā sādhana tvasya icchā virodhi tvāt tava tu trayam viṣa bhakṣaṇe tu kṛti sādhya tve api balavat aniṣṭa sādhana tvena cikīrṣā na asti iti kṛtau cikīrṣā janya tvam viśeṣaṇam iti kaścid tad tuccham evam hi viṣa bhakṣaṇam kṛti sādhyam eva na syāt jīvana yoni kṛteḥ tasya anutpatteḥ iti vyartham viśeṣaṇam syāt etat iṣṭa sādhana tā bhramāt viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhya tvam asti jñāna prayukta tvāt kāryatvasya tathā ca sañjāta bādhaḥ api tatra kāryatva jñānāt pravarteta tathā tṛptaḥ api bhojane 
[127,iv^1]	nanu sva kṛti sādhyata anubhavaḥ tathā anyathā iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇe viṣa bhakṣaṇe api pravarteta na ca iṣṭa sā adhana tā jñānam vedaḥ vā anubhāvakam asti iti ced na vastutas tatra kṛti sādhya tve liṅga antareṇa āpta vākyena vā tad anubhava sambhavāt liṅga ābhāsāt śabda ābhāsāt vā apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca bheda agrahavādinaḥ tatra tava tad anubhava abhāvāt mā evam sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā pratisandhāna janyam hi kārya tā jñānam pravartakam tathā hikāmye puruṣa viśeṣaṇam kāmanā tatas kāmya sādhana tā jñānena yāga pāka ādau kārya tā jñānam nitye ca kāla śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇam tathā ca etat sandhyām aham kṛti sādhya sandhyā vandanaḥ sandhyā samaye śauca ādimattvāt pūrva sandhyāyām aham iva iti kārya tā jñānam śauca ādi sva viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyam tad uktam 
[127,iv^2]	sa ca kārya viśeṣaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaṇa avagataḥ pravṛtti hetuḥ iti saṃjāta bādhasya ca viṣa bhakṣaṇe caitya vandane ca bhramadaśāyām iva na iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam asti yena tad janya kārya tā jñānāt pravarteta tṛptasya ca kāmanā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna abhāvāt na tathā bodhaḥ anye tu ātmanaḥ tu ātmanaḥ jīvitva prasandhāna janyam śrame kṛti sādhya tā jñānam sambhavati iti jīvana vyatirikta tvam sva viśeṣaṇe viśeṣaṇam iti tat na śrame sva icchā dhīna kṛti sādhya tva abhāvāt iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakam kārya tā jñānam pravartakam iti apare tat na nitye tad abhāvāt 
[127,v^1]	nanu viṣa bhakṣaṇa vyāvṛttam iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva kṛti sādhyatā jñāne viṣaya tayā viśeṣaṇam astu sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā jñāna janya tva apekṣayā laghu tvāt kiñca upāya viṣayā cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyāḥ upāya icchā tvāt vṛṣṭī icchāvat bhoga cikīrṣāyām tad abhāvāt aprayojakam iṣṭa sādhana tvam iti ced na tava api sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janya tva abhāvena tatra tasya aprayojaka tvāt kṛti hetu cikīrṣāyām tat prayojakam na ca bhoga cikīrṣā tathā upāya cikīrṣātaḥ eva kṛti sambhavāt iti ced tulyam iti mā evam sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ varodhana ekatra jñātum aśakyatvāt asiddha avasthasya hi sādhya tvam siddha tādaśāyām tad abhāvāt siddha tādaśā yāñca sādhana tvam 
[127,v^2]	asiddha avasthāvataḥ kārya anutpatteḥ tathā ca pāka ādeḥ asiddha tva siddha tva jñāne sādhya tva sādhana tvagrahaḥ na ca ekam ekena ekadā siddham asiddhañcaḥ iti jñāyate na ca svarūpa gata tā sādhya tva sādhanat kayoḥ atas na virodhaḥ iti vācyam yadi hi svarūpa nibandhanam sat ubhayam tadā tad svarūpam sadā eva siddham asiddhañca syāt bhinna nirūpita tve api tayoḥ siddha tva asiddha tve anavagamya ajñānāt tasmāt samaya bheda upādhikaḥ eva tad ubhaya sambandhaḥ pāke idānīm sādhya tvam agre sādhana tvam jñāyate iti ced 
[127,v^3]	na idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt ananugamena vyāpti agrahāt śabdena tathā pratipādayitum aśakyatvāt gauravāt ca na ca kṛtitaḥ siddham iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt cikīrṣā na hi siddham kaścid cikīrṣati kṛteḥ pūrva kṛtitaḥ siddham iti jñāna abhāvāt ca na ca kṛti sādhya tvena pāka ādeḥ iṣṭa sādhana tvāt sādhana tvam api sādhyam na hi kṛti sādhya tvena pākasya odana sādhana tā iti uktam tasmāt kṛta kriyamāṇa vilakṣaṇam kṛtī anantara bhaviṣyattā rūpam kṛti sādhya tvam cikīrṣā prayojakam tādṛśañca sādhana tva virodhi ā iva kiñca sādhana tvasya siddha mātra dharma tvāt sādhana tva jñānam icchā virodhi hi kaścid siddham icchati iti uktam etena vṛṣṭyādāviṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena kḷptam iti nirastam katham tarhi svatas asundare vṛṣṭi ādau icchā tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt iti gṛhāṇa 
[127,vi^1]	anye tu sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhaneṣu icchā prayojakam anugatam uddeśya tvam puruṣa artha pada vedanīyam dharma antaram asti anugata kāryasya anugata kāraṇa niyamya tvāt tat eva duḥkha tad sādhana vyāvṛtam sukha tad sādhana ādau cikīrṣā prayojakam iti na ca duḥkha virodhi tvam eva tathā asti iti vācyam saha anavasthāna niyama virodhasya asambhavāt vadhya ghātaka bhāvasya eka samaye sāmānādhikaraṇya abhāvasya ca yatna ādi sādhāraṇyāt iti tat na tad ajñāne api sukha tva jñānāt icchotpatteḥ na hi sukha tve jñāte dharma antara jñānam vinā na iccha iti tathā tve svatas prayojana hāni āpatteḥ tat eva hi svatas prayojanam yat avagatam sat sva vṛttitayā iṣyate kiñca anugata dharma kalpanā api kāraṇe na ca sukha ādi icchā kāraṇam 
[127,vi^2]	anāgata tvāt kintu tad avagamaḥ tarhi sukha ādi jñāne tat sva rūpa sadeva icchā prayojakam astu iti ced na yathā hi uddeśya tvam sukha jñāna ādiṣu utpadyate anyatara tvāt tṛṇa araṇi maṇinyāyāt vā tathā eva icchā eva jāyatām kṛti sādhya tvañca kṛtau satyām agri makṣaṇe svarūpam na kṛtim vinā kṣema sādhāraṇañca etat kṛti sādhya tvañca na kṛteḥ pūrvam 
[127,vii^1]	nanu kṛtau naṣṭāyām san api dharmaḥ na kāryaḥ tathā ca katham kārye apūrve kāminaḥ anvayaḥ kṣaṇika tvena kriyā tulya tvāt iti ced na yat vṛtti kāmya sādhana tvam tatra kārya tā buddheḥ prayojaka tvāt na tu kārya tā viśiṣṭasya kāmya sādhana tā iti vyāptiḥ nanu pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tā jñānam na pratyakṣeṇa kṛti antaram pāke sati kṛti sādhyatā jñānam tasmin sati kṛtiḥ iti anyonya āśrayāt kṛti sādhyata uttīrṇe cikīrṣā akṛtya uḥ asambhavāt ca iti ced na pākaḥ mad kṛti sādhyaḥ mad kṛtim vinā asattve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tvāt vā mad bhojana vat iti anumānāt sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam 
[127,vii^2]	yasya yat iṣṭa sādhanam yat kṛtim vinā yadā na sambhavati tat tadā tad kṛti sādhyam iti vyāptoḥ asiddhasya iṣṭa sā dhana tva abhāvāt balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvan ca liṅga viśeṣaṇam tena na madhu viṣa saṃmpṛkta anna bhojane vyabhicāraḥ atīta pāke ca kṛti sādhyata uttīrṇe na vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyatas tasya api kṛti sādhya tvāt atīta tā daśā yāñca atīta odana icchā viraheṇa iṣṭa sādhana tva abhāvāt atas eva nidāgha dūna dehaḥ varṣati vāride tīyadāt toya lābha sambhāvanāyām vā saraḥ avagāhane na pravartate iṣṭa santāpa śānti sādhana toya sambandhasya sva kṛtim vinā api siddhi pratisandhānena liṅga abhāvena sva kṛti sādhya tva jñāna abhāvāt yadā ca mata kṛtim vinā na sambhavati iti pratisandhate tadā pravartate 
[128,i_128,ii]	yasya santāpa śānti mātram iṣṭam sa saraḥ avagāhanasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvam eva na pratisandhatte upasthita vṛṣṭitaḥ api tat tad sambhavāt iti kaścid tat na toya sambandha tvena santāpa śanti sādhana tvam tasya ca saraḥ avagāhane api sattvāt anyathā vṛṣṭiḥ api tad sādhanam na syāt saraḥ avagāhanāt api tad siddheḥ kārya sādhana tvañca kṛti sādhya tve na liṅgam pāka ādi vat odana ādeḥ api pravṛtteḥ pūrvam kṛti sādhya tva jñāne hetu abhāvāt 
[128,iii]	nanu evam liṅga jñānam eva pravartakam astu prāthamika tvāt āvaśyaka tvāt ca na ca lāghavāt kṛti sādhya tva jñānam tathā kṛti sādhyata anumitau tadā māna abhāvena yugapad upasthiti abhāvāt pravṛtti sāmagrya anumiti pratibandhāt ca iti ced na liṅga jñāne kṛti sādhya tva aprakāśe tad prakāraka cikīrṣāyām tasya ahetu tvāt atas eva liṅga antara jñānam api na pravṛtakam 
[128,iv^1]	nanu pāka ādiḥ kṛtaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ vā na pakṣa tasya kṛti sādhya tve bādhāt na api anāgataḥ bhāvi pāke māna abhāvena āśraya asiddheḥ pāka tvam bhaviṣyat vṛtti sāmānya tvāt go tva vat iti mānam iti ced na māna abhāvena go tve api tasya aprasiddheḥ pāka mātram pakṣaḥ iti ced na mātrā arthaḥ yadi pāka tvam tadā bādhaḥ liṅgāsiddhiḥ ca sarva pāka paratve ca tasya siddha bhāge bādhaḥ anāgata bhāge ca āśraya asiddhiḥ vartamāna ādi udāsīnaḥ pākaḥ pakṣaḥ pāka sāmānye ca kṛti sādhya tvam na bādhitam iti api na 
[128,iv^2]	siddhasya pakṣa tvam na asiddhasya iti anumiteḥ siddha viṣaya tve bādhāt bhinna viṣaya tve vā siddha viṣaya icchā pravṛtti ādi anutpādaka tvāt ca kṛta kriyamāṇa sādhāraṇa kṛti sādhya tva jñānāt eva asiddha viṣayā cikīrṣā kṛtiḥ ca utpadyate ananya gatika tvena tathā kāraṇa svabhāva kalpanāt iti ced tarhi yādṛśam kṛti sādha tvam cikīrṣāyām prakāraḥ tādṛśam jñāne na asti iti anya prakāraka jñānāt eva cikīrṣā syāt tathā ca liṅga jñānam eva pravṛtti hetuḥ astu prāthamika tvāt yat tu smṛta pāke kṛti sādhya tva asaṃsargā grarhā pravṛttiḥ sa ca asaṃsarga grahaḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā grahāt iti tat na smṛta pākasya siddha tvena tatra kāryatva asaṃsarga grahe anumāna bādhāt smṛta pākasya siddhatvam tadā na gṛhyate iti ced 
[128,iv^3]	tarhi smṛta pākasya siddha tva grahe odana arthī pāke na pravarteta siddhaudanaḥ api pāke tṛptaḥ api bhojane pravarteta tatra siddha tva grahāt tad asaṃsarga grahaḥ iti cat tulyam api ca smṛta pāke kāryatva asaṃsargāt vidyamānā saṃsarga āgrahāt visaṃvādinī pravṛttiḥ syāt kiñca evam siddha pāka jñānāt ajñāte asiddhe pāke icchā pravṛttī syātām iti atra brūmaḥ pāke kṛti sādhya tvam siddhyat siddhe bādhāt anagāta pākam ādāya sidhyati pakṣa tā avacchedaka dharma sāmānādhikaraṇyam sādhyamānasya liṅgena siddhati iti anumāne kḷpta tvāt yathā prasiddha vahni bādhe api vahni mātram na bādhitam iti aprasiddhaḥ api vahniḥ sidhyati 
[128,iv^4]	tathā prasiddha pāke kṛti sādhya tva bādhe api pāka mātre na bādhitam iti aprasiddham pākam ādāya tat sidhyati aprasiddhayoḥ pakṣa sādhyayoḥ siddhau aviśeṣāt tasmāt asiddhasya kvacid siddhe siddhe siddhasya ca kvacid aprasiddhasya ca asiddhe siddhiḥ tena anumā tridhā anyathā kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api pāka ādau kṛti sādhya tvam katham avagamyeta kiñca tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt katham vṛṣṭi ādau icchā siddhatvasya icchā virodhi tvāt anāgatasya jñātum aśakyatvāt atas eva siddha asiddha viṣaya tva nirāsena sukha ādi jñānāt phale api na icchā iti na vṛṣṭyādāviṣṭa sādhana tā api na ca vṛṣṭi ādi sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vṛṣṭi ādau icchā icchāyāḥ siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣaya tva vikalpa grāsāt 
[128,v]	atha sāmānya lakṣaṇa pratyāsattyā vṛṣṭi ādi tvena sukha ādi tvena ca siddha asiddha vṛṣṭi ādi tad phala viṣayakam jñānam utpannam tena siddham virodhinam tyaktvā asiddha viṣaya icchā utpadyate yadi ca sāmānya lakṣaṇam na asti tadā yena rūpeṇa iṣṭa sā adhana tva graha tena rūpeṇa jñāte siddhe vā icchā utpadyate anvaya vyatirekābhyām tādṛśa jñānasya tādṛśa icchā janaka tva avadhāraṇāt sukha icchāyām api evam iti ced tarhi mama api pākatva avacchedena kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt anāgate cikīrṣā tat ca jñānam sakala pāka viṣayam sannikṛṣṭa pāka viṣayam vā iti anyat etat bālasya vyāpti ādi a graheṇa ādyā pravṛttiḥ jīvana adṛṣṭa udbodhita janma antara saṃskāra janyāt stana pānam kāryam iti smaraṇāt tava api iṣṭa sādhana tā smaraṇāt tatra pravṛttiḥ ananya gatika tvāt na ca janma antare api paryanuyogaḥ janma dhārāyāḥ anādi tvāt pratyakṣa anumāna mūlaka tvāt ca na andha paramparā 
[128,vi^1]	vastutas tu śuṣka kaṇṭatayā bālaḥ duḥkham anubhavan virodhitayā sukham smarati tatas sukha tva jñānāt sukha vṛtti kārya tvam sukha vṛtti tayā antaraṅga tvāt na tu stana pānam iṣṭa sādhanam iti smaraṇam sukha āvṛtti tvena bahis aṅga tvāt sukha kārya tvañca stana pāna dvārā janma antara anubhūtam iti kārya tva smaraṇe stana pānam api viṣayaḥ tena stana pāne kāryatva jñānāt eva pravṛttiḥ iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya tadānīm sāmagrya bhāvāt evañca ādya pravṛttau kāryatva jñānam prayojakam kḷptam iti agre api tat eva pravartakam kḷpta tvāt navīnaḥ tu mama idam kṛti sādhyam iti jñānam na pravṛtakam anāgata viṣaye pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ asambhavāt 
[128,vi^2]	kintu yādṛśasya puruṣasya kṛti sādhyam yat dṛṣṭam tādṛśa tvam ātmanaḥ pratisandhāya tatra pravṛtate tathā hi odana kāmasya tad sādhana tā jñānavataḥ ca taṇḍula ādi upakaraṇavataḥ pākaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ aham api ca tādṛśaḥ iti jñānāt iti jñānāt pāke pravartate evañca anya kṛta pāke kṛti sādhya tā jñānam ātmanaḥ pāke kṛti sādhya tva prayojaka viśeṣaṇa vat tva jñānañca pravartakam anyatra api pravṛttiḥ evam eva iti anāditā eva atas eva sañjāta bādhaḥ caitya vandane viṣa bhakṣaṇe ca na pravartate iṣṭa sādhanatā jñānavataḥ hi tat kṛti sādhyam na ca sañjāta bādhaḥ tatra iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānavān evam tṛpti icchāvataḥ api bhojanam kṛti sādhyam tṛptaḥ ca na tṛpti icchāvat tvam ātmani avaiti iti na bhojane pravartate 
[128,vii_128,viii]	ati navīnāḥ tu yādṛśasya ityādau avigīta tvam tad kṛtau viśeṣaṇam āhuḥ sañjāta bādhaḥ tu viṣa bhakṣaṇam caitya vandanañca vigīta kṛti sādhya tvena eva jānāti iti tatra na pravartate vṛtti viṣayaḥ ca sāmānyatas kāla asambhinnaḥ pāka ādiḥ jñāyate pravṛtti mahimnā ca anāgata pāka siddhiḥ cikīrṣā ca kāla asambhinna viṣayā na tu bhāvinam kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti ākārā eva iti 
[128,ix^1]	atra ucyate viṣa bhakṣaṇa divya avṛttam kṛti sādhya tva jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam viṣaya tayā avacchedakam lāghavāt na tu sva viśeṣaṇa vat tā pratisandhāna janya tvam gauravāt na ca siddhāsiddha avasthayoḥ sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ nirviśeṣitayoḥ tayoḥ avirodhāt pākaḥ asiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ siddhaḥ sādhanañca iti anubhavāt tadā sādhya tvam hi tadā sādhana tvasya virodhi niyamataḥ tena eva tasya pratikṣepeṇa saha anavasthāna niyamāt na tu sādhana tvasya anyadā sādhana tvasya vā tayoḥ apratikṣepāt anyadā sādhana tve api sādhana tvam asti eva sāmānya abhāve viśeṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt evantadāḥ asiddha tvasya tadā siddha tvam virodhi 
[128,ix^2]	nayamatas tasya eva pratipakṣepāt na tu siddha tva mātram anyadā api tatra siddha tva abhāva prasaṅgat nirviśeṣitayoḥ virodhe ca siddha tva asiddhatvayoḥ ca anyataradeva pāka ādau syāt na tu samaya bhede api ubhayam na ca tadā kṛti sādhya tve sati tadā iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānam pravartakam atas eva vājapeyena yajeta iti atra yāgasya karaṇa avasthāyām siddha tvena na vājapeyasya sādhya tā ekadā tayoḥ virodhāt iti karma nāmadheya tvam na tu karaṇasya siddha tvena sādhya tva virodhaḥ yāga svarūpe tayoḥ sattvāt 
[129,i^1]	atha viruddhayoḥ avaccheda bhedam ādāya ekatra pratītiḥ syāt na ca kṛti sādhya tva iṣṭa sādhana tvayoḥ samaya bhedam ādāya ekatra pratītiḥ asti tathā liṅga abhāvāt iti ced na sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhasya ukta tvāt evam siddhatvā siddha tvayoḥ bhāva abhāva rūpa tve api na virodhaḥ eka dharma gata tvena māna siddha tvāt tasmāt saṃyoga tadabhāvayoḥ iva yena prakāreṇa yayoḥ virodhaḥ tena tayoḥ eka dharma gata tvam na pratīyate na tu rūpa antareṇa api iti api ca yadi sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ virodhaḥ tadā tava api iṣṭa sādhana tvena kārya sādhana tvena vā kārya tvam na anumīyeta hetu sādhyayoḥ virodhena sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāvena vyāpti asiddheḥ pakṣe sādhya sādhanayoḥ anyatara sattve bādhā siddhyoḥ anyatara prasaṅgāt ca na ca vācyam idānīm mad kṛti sādhya tvam sādhyam agre mad iṣṭa sādhana tvam hetuḥ 
[129,i^2]	daiva ādi anadhīna tve sati yat agre mad iṣṭa sādhanam tat idānīm mad kṛti sādhyam iti vyāptiḥ tathā ca samaya bhedam ādāya sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ avagamaḥ iti idānīm agrima padārthayoḥ nānā tvāt anugata rūpa abhāvena vyāpteḥ agrahāt pāka nyāyena anyatra api tad tad samaya antar bhāvena sādhya tva sādhana tvayoḥ apratītiḥ pratītau vā mama api idānīm kṛti sādhya tve sati agre iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānam pravartakam astu na ca pāke sādhya iṣṭaka tvena kṛti sādhya tvam anumeyam asiddha avasthāvataḥ hi pāka ādiṣṭa anutpatteḥ pākasya siddhatvam avagamya tad sādhya tvam iṣṭasya avagantavyam asiddha tvañcau agamya kṛti sādhya tvam iti siddha tva asiddha tvayoḥ arva rodhaḥ atra api durvāraḥ api ca sva viśeṣaṇa dhī janya kārya tā jñāna abhāvāt sukhe katham cikīrṣā na hi kṛti sādhya tā jñāna mātrāt sā sañcāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādau cikīrṣā prasaṅgāt atha upāya cikīrṣāyām tad kāraṇam icchā kāraṇa sukha tva jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam yadā viṣayaḥ tadā sukhe cikīrṣā no ced icchā mātram iti dvayam eva cikīrṣā hetuḥ iti ced 
[129,i^3]	tarhi icchā hetu jñāne yadā kṛti sādhya tvam bhāsate tadā cikīrṣā no ced icchāmācam iti eva sukha tad upāya cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu lāghavāt sukha tva jñāna vat iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya api icchā kāraṇa tvāt atas eva pāke iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāne kṛti sādhya tvam viṣayaḥ iti tatra cikīrṣā na tu vṛṣṭi ādi jñāne tad viṣaya tvam iti icchā mātram sukha cikīrṣāyām icchā kāraṇa jñāne kṛti sādhya tā viṣayake cikīrṣā janakatva avadhāraṇāt anyathā tatra cikīrṣā anutpatteḥ 
[129,ii^1]	vastu tas tu upāya cikīrṣā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna sādhyāḥ upāya icchā tvāt vṛṣṭi chāv na ca bhoga cikīrṣā vat tena vinā api syāt iti aprayojaka tvam upāya icchāyāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt vṛṣṭeḥ ca svatas asundara tvena icchā anutpatteḥ anugata upāya icchāyām anugatasya prayojaka tve sambhavati bādhakam vinā tyāga ayogāt ca na ca cikīrṣā anya tve sati upāya icchātvam icchā tvam vā tad janya tve prayojakam gauravāt 
[129,ii^2]	sukha icchāyām tad abhāvāt ca evañcopāya cikīrṣāyām iṣṭa sādhana tva jñāne dhruve ati prasaṅga vāraṇa artham kṛti sādhya tva nirvāha arthañca kṛti sādhya tvam api viṣaya tayā avacchedakam astu na tu tad vihāya tanmātram kḷpta kāraṇam vinā kārya anupapatteḥ atas eva stana pāna pravṛttau api upāya it chā kāraṇa tvena gṛhītasya iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānasya api kalpanam dṛṣṭa anurodhi tvāt kalpanāyāḥ nanu sādhana tvam icchā virodhi tasya siddha dharma tvāt vṛṣṭi ādau tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānātā icchā iti ced na nirviśeṣitayoḥ siddha tva asiddha tvayoḥ virodhena icchā sādhana tvayoḥ avirodhāt tadā asiddhatvam tadā siddha tvam ca na icchā sādhana tvayoḥ prayojakam iti tathā na jñāyate eva 
[129,iii]	yat tu tad sādhya iṣṭa jñānāt vṛṣṭi ādau icchā iti tad tuccham asiddha avasthāt vṛṣṭi ādeḥ iṣṭa nityatteḥ tasmāvadvayam siddha tvam avagantavyam icchā anurodhi tvāḥ ca asiddha tvam iti tatra api virodhaḥ eva vṛṣṭau satyām iṣṭa tayā vinā na iti anvaya vyatireka grahasya vṛṣṭi siddhatnam ādāya dṛṣṭi nirūpita iṣṭa sādhyaka tva grāhaka tvāt kiñca cikīrṣā janya kṛti sādhyam maṇḍalīkaraṇam iti artha pratipādakam maṇḍalī kuryāt iti vākyām pramāṇam syāt viṣaya ābādhāt 
[129,iv]	etena navīna matam api apāstam parasya hi kṛti sādhya tva odana kāma nāvat tva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānānām jñānam tathā ātmanaḥ odana kāma nāvat tva iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya jñānam na pravṛtti kāraṇam gauravāt kintu mad kṛti sādhya tve sati mad iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva lāghavāt yathā ca sādhya tva sādhana tvayā urivirodhaḥ anāgatasya pāka ādeḥ kṛti sādhyatā jñānañca tathā upapāditam eva kiñca para kṛti sādhya tvam ajñātvā api sva kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānāt sva kalpita lipya ādau yauvanam kāma udrekāt sambhoga ādau pravṛtteḥ ca tat eva pravartakam 
[129,v]	vastutas tu siddha viṣaya ka kṛti sādhya ta ajñānāt katham kṛtyā sādhayāmi iti icchā siddhe icchā virahāt asiddhasya ajñānāt atha siddha viṣayāt eva kṛti sādhya tā jñānāt asiddha viṣayā kṛti sādhya tvena icchā jñāyate icchāyāḥ asiddha viṣaya tva svabhāva tvāt eka prakāraka tvena jñāna cikīrṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na tu eka viṣaya tve sati gauravāt icchāyāḥ anāgata viṣaya tvāt tasya ca ajñānāt tathā tva darśanāt sukha ādi icchāyām api evam iti ced na asiddha viṣaya icchā anu rodhena anāgata jñāna upāyasya darśita tvāt astu ca evam tathā api kṛti sādhya tā jñāne iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva vyāvartaka m astu sva parakīya iṣṭa sā adhana tā jñāna phala kāmanā jñāna apekṣayā laghu tvāt iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna jñānasya phala kāmanā jñānasya ca hetu tve māna abhāvāt ca 
[129,vi^1]	navyāḥ tu sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñānam eva pravartakam tena sva kṛtya sādhye vṛṣṭi ādau kārīḥ yāñca kṛṣīvalasya na pravṛttiḥ na ca san jāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇe pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ sva kṛti sādhya ta ajñāna viṣaye iṣṭa tvasya svarūpa satas pravṛttau sahakāri tvāt na ca san jāta bādhasya viṣa bhakṣaṇāt ā icchāsti iṣṭa sādhana tvena ajñānāt atīta bhojane api atas eva na pravarteta tṛpteḥ siddha tayā icchā viraheṇa bhojane tad upādhika iṣṭa tva abhāvāt atīta tṛptau icchā na asti iti tad sādhane api iṣṭa tva abhāvāt eva na pravṛttiḥ na ca evam pāke na pravarteta 
[129,vi^2_130,ii]	tasya svarasataḥ iṣṭa tva abhāvāt iti vācyam iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānena tasya api iṣṭa tvāt hanta evam prāthamika tvāt iṣṭa tva artham avaśya apekṣaṇīya tvāt ca kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam eva cikīrṣā kāraṇam astu iti ced na iṣṭa sādhana tva abhāve api bhoge cikīrṣā sattvāt tasyām sva kṛti sādhya tva jñāne sati iṣṭa tvam eva kāraṇam na tu iṣṭa sādhana tvam vyabhicārāt pāka ādau tad anvaya vyatirekau api iṣṭa tva upakṣīṇau evam bhoge api pravartā iti ced na iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api mukti rūpa iṣṭa sādhane sukhe pravarteta iti tulyam sukhe cikīrṣā bhavati eva kṛtiḥ tu na bhavati kṛteḥ siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣaya tva niyamāt iti ced talyam tasmāt sva kṛti sādhya tvam vidhiḥ iṣṭa tvam sahakārī iti mā evam iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānasya upāya icchāyām hetu tva avadhāraṇāt tasyāḥ tad janya tva niyamāt i chāyāḥ sva viṣaya icchā anutpādaka tva niyamāt ca nanu siddhaudanaḥ kutas pāke na pravartate odana mātrasya siddha tvena iṣṭatva abhāvāt atas eva atīta bhojana ādau na pravṛtate atīta tṛṣṇā ādi virahāt 
[130,iii^1]	nanu sāmudrika vida ākhyāte bhāvi yauva rājye bhoga sādhane sva kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tva jñānāt kutas na pravartate bhāvi rājyasya asiddha tvāt pravṛtteḥ siddha viṣaya tva niyamāt rājya upāya aparicayāt ca tad paricaye ca pravartate eva devatā ārādhana ādau iti ced na siddhe cikīrṣā viraheṇa yāga ādau api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt devatā ārādhana ādeḥ api asiddha tvena tatra api apravṛtti prasaṅgāt ca kiñca rājya upāya aparicaye tatra mā pravartiṣṭa sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte rājye pravarti prasaṅge kim āyātam na hi kṛti sādhya iṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāne api tad upāya jñānam tatra pravartakam gauravāt bhinna viṣaya tvāt ca iti ced mā evam yauvane hi tāvat pravartate eva rājye bālye tu rājya upāyam akṛtvā mad kṛtya idānīm rājyam na sidhyati iti sva kṛti a sādhyata ajñānāt eva na pravartate 
[130,iii^2]	yathā taṇḍulam vinā pāke sva kṛti asādhyata ajñānāt rājya upāye tu sva kṛti sādhyeṣṭa sādhana tvena jñāte devatā ārādhana ādau pravartate eva atas eva vrīhi avaghātam akṛtvā puroḍāśaḥ tam akṛtvā yāgaḥ tam akṛtvā apūrvam sādhayitum na śakyate iti kramaśas avaghāta ādau pravartate na yugapad siddha vṛtti asiddha kriyā viṣaya svabhāva tvāt pravṛtteḥ yāga anantarañca na apūrve pravartate kṛti antaram vinā eva yāga kṛtitsta sambhavāt iṣṭa sādhane ceṣṭā utpattinā antarīyaka duḥkha adhika duḥkha ājanaka tvam viśeṣaṇam na tu tad jñāna abhāvaḥ kāraṇam kintu tat eva viṣaya tayā kāraṇa tāvacchedakam lāghavāt tena madhu viṣa sampṛkta anna bhojane na pravṛttiḥ pareṇa api pravṛtti pūrvam liṅga viśeṣaṇa tvena anyathā vā tad jñāna viniyoga svīkārāt evañca alpa āyāsa sādhya ādiṣṭa utpatti sambhave bahu āyāsa sādhye na pravṛttiḥ atas eva śruta svarga phalaka tve api bahu vitta vyaya āyāsa sādhye jyotiṣṭoma ādau phala bhūmā kalpa pate anyathā alpa āyāsa sādhyāt eva svarga siddhi sambhave tatra apravṛttau ananuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam aprāmāṇyam tad vidheḥ syāt 
[130,iv]	balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvañca na viśeṣaṇam bahu vitta vyaya āyāsa sādhya bahutara duḥkhasya api abalavat tvam kvacid alpa duḥkhasya api balavat tvam iti anugatasya tasya abhāvāt na ceṣṭā apekṣayā aniṣṭasya adhika tvam balavat tvam tasya api ukta atiriktasya ananugamāt āstikasya niṣiddha tvena jñāte api pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena naraka sādhana tva jñāna tirodhānāt 
[130,v]	nanu na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti atra vidhi artha niṣedha anupapattiḥ tad bhakṣaṇasya tṛpti rūpa iṣṭa sādhana tvāt na ca asura avidyā ādi vat paryudāsa lakṣaṇayā virodhi aniṣṭa sādhana tva bodhanam nañaḥ asamasta tvāt kriyā saṅgata tvena pratiṣedha vācaka tva vyutpatteḥ ca iti ced na viśeṣyavati viśiṣṭa niṣedhasya sa viśeṣaṇe hi iti nyāyena viśeṣaṇa niṣedha paryavasāyitayā kalañja bhakṣaṇam iṣṭa utpattinā antarīyaka duḥkha atirikta duḥkha sādhanam iti na kalañjam bhakṣayet iti anena bodhanāt iṣṭa sādhana tā vācakasya vidheḥ sāmānyatas niṣedha anupapatteḥ balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhana tva viśeṣa niṣedha tātparyam tathā ca aśakya viśeṣa niṣedha paratvam nañaḥ iti kaścid tat na yathā hi ayogya tayā sa chidram vihāya ghaṭa tvena tad itara anvayaḥ na tu chidra itara tvena yugapad vṛtti dvaya virodhāt tathā atra api balavat aniṣṭa an anubandhi tvena anupasthitau katham tat niṣedhaḥ 
[130,vi]	śyenena abhicaran yajeta iti atra katham vidhi pravṛttiḥ hiṃsāyāḥ balavat aniṣṭa anubandhi tvāt iti ced na tatra kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tvam eva yogyatayā anveti na tu balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi tvam api ayogya tvāt nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca hiṃsāyāḥ balavat aniṣṭa anubandhi tva avagamāt atas eva vihite api śyene vigānāt na tāttvika pravṛttiḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ utkaṭa tvena aniṣṭa anubandhi aṃśasya tiraskārāt kasyacid pravṛttiḥ iti eke 
[130,vii]	anye tu abhicārasya vairi vadha phalaka tvena śruta tvāt badha sādhana tvena śyenaḥ vidhīyate na tu vadha sādhya naraka sādhana tvena narakasya phala tvena aśruteḥ na ca janaka janakasya janakatva niyamaḥ kumbhakāra pitṛ paramparāyāḥ kumbha janakatva āpattaḥ vidhinā eva śyenasya balavat aniṣṭaḥ nanubandhi tva bodhanāñca na ca śyenasya naraka ahetu tve apekṣita vairi vadha hetu tve vā avigānena pravṛttiḥ syāt iti vācyam śyenāt vadhaḥ vadhāt ca avaśyam narakaḥ iti pratisandhānena vigānāt 
[130,viii^1]	nanu śyenaḥ maraṇa phalaka vyāpāra tvena hiṃsā sā ca naraka janikā iti ced na na hi sākṣāt paramparā sā dhāraṇa maraṇa phalaka vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā kūpa ādau vinaṣṭe gavi tad kartuḥ go vadha kartṛ tva āpatteḥ vadhyasya api hantuḥ mṛtyu utpādana dvāreṇa ātma hantṛ tva prasaṅgāt ca na hi anutpādita manyuḥ kaścid kam api vyāpādayati kintu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phala kaḥ vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā yad anantaram maraṇam bhavati eva na ca śyenaḥ tathā kintu khaṅga hanana ādikam eva atha maraṇonukūla vyāpāraḥ maraṇet deśena anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca tathā kūpa ādau ca na maraṇa uddeśena anuṣṭhīyamāna tvam iti ced 
[130,viii^2]	na evam sati gauravāt maraṇān uddeśena kṣipta nārāca adha brāhmaṇe ca hiṃsā na syāt kiñca hinasti dhātu arthe avacchedakam phalam avyavahitam eva maraṇam avyavahita phalakasya eva vyāpārasya dhātu vācya tvāt anyathā paramparāyāḥ viklitti phalaka anna kāma iṣṭa taṇḍula kraya ādau api pacati iti prasaṅgāt evam khaṅga ubhighāta anantaram yatra vilambena maraṇam vraṇa pāka paramparayā vai anne viṣa prayogena vā tatra hantṛ tvam prāyaścitta ādi ca na syāt iti ced na prāyaścitta tulya tā artham hi tatra hantṛvya apadeśaḥ gauṇaḥ vinigama kañca lāghavam eva 
[130,ix]	vastutas tu maraṇa uddeśena kṛtaḥ adṛṣṭāt vārakaḥ tad anukūla vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā śyenaḥ ca adṛṣṭa dvārā maraṇa sādhanam atas na hiṃsā yadi ca adṛṣṭa dvārā api maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā syāt tadā saptamī taila abhyaṅgasya adṛṣṭa dvārā iṣṭa bhāryā vināśa īhetu tvāt abhyaṅga kartuḥ hiṃsaka tva āttiḥ atas eva kūpa ādau gomaraṇe api na vadha kartṛ tvam tat kartuḥ gala lagna anna maraṇe na bhoktuḥ na vā pariveṣayituḥ ātma hantṛ tvam brahma hantṛ tvam vā vraṇa pāka paramparayā vilambena viṣa prayogena ca hantṛ tvam mukhyam eva na tu anuniṣpādi maraṇa phalaka tvam gala lagna anna maraṇe sva hantṛ tva āpatteḥ anya uddeśena kṣipta nārācena hate brāhmaṇe brahma hantṛ tvam na syāt iti ced na iṣṭa āpatteḥ vyāpadeśaḥ tu gauṇaḥ prayogaḥ lakṣaṇayā api samarthayitum śakyate tad pakṣe ati prasaṅgaḥ vārayitum na śakyate iti idam eva vinigamakam atas eva atad uddeśena kṛte api niṣiddhe prāyaścitta arddham uktam 
[130,x]	apare tu anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa sādhanam hiṃsā khaḍga kārasya anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāra dvārāḥ maraṇa sādhana tvam tasya hi nara antara vyāpāraḥ nābhisaṃhitaḥ kintu dhana lābhaḥ iti khaḍga kāraḥ na ghātakaḥ viṣasya anne prakṣepeṇa nara antara vyāpāraḥ bhojanam eva abhisaṃhitaḥ anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya viṣa prayogāt iti hiṃsā eva anne viṣa prayogaḥ iti tat na gala lagna kavalāt i atra maraṇam tatra pariveṣayituḥ ghātaka tā āpātāt anena idam bhoktavyam iti abhisandhāya pariveṣaṇāt bhoktuḥ ātma hantṛ tva āpatteḥ ca anabhisaṃhita nara antara vyāpāram advārīkṛtya maraṇa anukūla anna bhakṣaṇa nuṣṭhānāt atas eva avyavahita prāṇa viyoga phalakaḥ vyāpāraḥ hiṃsā vraṇa pāka paramparayā mṛte tu hantṛ tvam vyāpārasya avyavadhāyaka tvāt iti nirastam 
[131,i^1]	syāt etat na iṣṭa sādhatā vidhiḥ nitye sandhyā upāsana ādau phala abhāvāt atha na asti eva tat nityam yatra artha vāda ādikam vidhi vākye vā na phalam śrutam asti sandhyām upāsate ye tu satatam śaṃsita vratāḥ vidhūta pāpāḥ te yānti brahma lokam sanātanam iti ādi artha vādāt dadyāt aharahar śrāddham pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āvahan ityādi vidhi vākya śravaṇāt ca kṛtvā acintayātu ucyate yatra na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajit nyāyāt svargaḥ phalam iti ced na kāmanā upādhi kārya tvena yāga vat nitya tā bhaṅga prasaṅgāt aharahar śrutyā hi tad kāla jīvi mātra kṛti sādhyam sandhyā vandanam avagatam kāmanā upādhi kārya tve ca yadā phala kāmanā na asti tadā tad samayaḥ eva tad kartavyatā na syāt na hi tad kāle phala kāmanā vaśyambhāvaḥ 
[131,i^2]	pramāṇa abhāvāt kiñca prathama pravṛtta itara nirapekṣā hara har śrutyā jīvi mātrasya adhikāraḥ avagataḥ tathā ca tad sāpekṣa caram apravṛtti arthavāda upanīta phala kāmasya na tatra adhikāraḥ prathama pravṛttā aharahar śruti virodhāt nitye phala śruteḥ artha vādasya ca stutau tātparyam atas eva pratyavāya parihāraḥ api na phalam tad kāmanā upādhi kārya tve nitya tā kṣateḥ kiñca nitye kartavya tā bodhanāt prāk na pratyavāye pramāṇam asti vidheḥ kartavya tvam avagamya kartavyā karaṇe pratyavāya kalpanam vidhiḥ ca phala abhāvena prathamam mūkaḥ eva evañca pratyavāya pramitau vidhi pravṛttiḥ tad pravṛttau ca kartavyā karaṇe pratyavāya kalpanam iti anyonya āśrayaḥ 
[131,ii]	apare tu na vidheḥ kartavya tvam avagamya kartavyā karaṇe pratyavāya kalpanam yena anyonya āśrayaḥ kintu nindā artha vādena prāyaścitta upadeśena ca upāsanasya prakṛti arthasya tāvat vyāpāra svarūpasya abhāvaḥ pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ tathā ca sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ pratyavāya dvārāḥ duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ sandhyā upāsanam duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena phalam prāyaścitte pāpa dhvaṃsa vat iti tad sādhana tvena kṛtiḥ bodhyate vidhinā na ca evam pratyavāya parihāraḥ eva phalam astu iti vācyam parihārasya prāc abhāva rūpa tvena anāditayā asādhya tvāt na ca upāsana ākaraṇam pratyavāya hetuḥ na upāsana abhāvaḥ tathā ca duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena kṛtiriṣṭāḥ na tu upāsanam iti vācyam nindā artha vādasya ubhayatra sattvena ubhayasya api tathā tvāt iti tat na evam api kāmya tve nitya tā kṣati prasaṅgāt kiñca akurvan vihitam karma ityādinā na upāste yaḥ ca paścimām ityādinā ca karaṇa bhāvasya eva pratyavāya hetu tvam bodhyate na tu tad viṣaya abhāvasya anyathā akartuḥ pratyavāyaḥ na anyasya iti katham syāt viṣaya abhāvasya sādhāraṇyāt 
[131,iii_131,iv^1]	vastutas tu kṛti sādhya tve sati iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam pravartṛka tvena niryūḍham na ca kṛtau kṛti sādhya tvam asti iti atas na kiñcid etat navyāḥ tu nitya apūrva prāgabhāvaḥ durita dvārā duḥkha sādhanam tad abhāvaḥ apūrvam duḥkha sādhana abhāva tvena iṣṭam tad sādhana tvena kṛti sādhya tvena ca sandhyā upāsanam vidhīyate iti tat na nindā artha vāda ādinā sandhyā upāsana abhāvaḥ tad akaraṇam vā pratyavāya hetuḥ avagataḥ na tu apūrvā bhāvaḥ prathamam pramāṇa abhāvena tad anupasthiteḥ vidheḥ iṣṭa sādhana tva bodhaka tvāt pariśeṣeṇa apūrvam iṣṭam kalpyate iti ced 
[131,iv^2]	tarhi viśva jit nyāyena svargaḥ eva phalam kalpyatām kāmya tvasya tvayā api svīkārāt kiñca vidhi pravṛttau apūrva jñānam apūrva jñāne ca vidhi pravṛttiḥ iti anyonya āśrayaḥ yāvat nitya naimittika nirvāhasya tad tad āśrama vihita karmaṇām samyak paripālanasya ca brahma loka avāptiḥ phalam śrūyate tathā ca nityasya saphala tvam iti kecid tat na tasya vidheḥ nitya vidhim upajīvya pravṛttiḥ tasya ca phala abhāvena prathamam mūka tvāt anyathā paraspara sāpekṣa tvena anyonya āśrayaḥ tasmāt kārya tā eva vidhiḥ nanu nitye vedāt kārya tā jñāne api prayojana jñānam vinā katham pravṛttiḥ na hi prayojanam anuddiśya mandaḥ api pravartate iti ced na nitye phala bādhena pravṛtti mātre prayojana jñānasya aprayojaka tvāt kāmye api prayojana jñānam na sākṣāt pravartakam upāya aviṣaya tvāt prayojane apravṛtteḥ ca kintiṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna dvārā kārya tā jñāne upakṣīṇam eva katham ayam niścayaḥ nitye iṣṭa sādhana tā jñāna asambhavāt kārya tā ajñānasya vedāt api sambhavāt 
[131,v^1]	nanu niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā prekṣāvatām katham pravṛttiḥ veda adhīna kārya tā jñāna sattvāt saphala pravṛttau api tasya eva tantra tvāt yat tu laukike niṣphale duḥkha eka phale vā na pravartate tat iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅgakasya kārya tā ajñānasya veda adhīnasya vā abhāvāt na ca duḥkha eka phala tva jñānam pravatti pratibandhakam sati kārya tā jñāne tasya pratibandhakatvā darśanāt atha vā kāmye liṅaḥ apūrva vācaka tvāt nitye api liṅā upāsana ādi viṣaya kamapūrvam bodhyate tat ca niṣphalam api svatas eva sukha vat prayojanam nityam abhyarthyam ānañca iti ucyate sarvatra nitye phala śravaṇāt jīvi phala kāmasya samvalita adhikāraḥ yathā uparāge naimittikam snāna śrāddha ādi phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe prāyaścitta ādi śruteḥ ca niyata kartavya tākam 
[131,v^2]	yathā vā ṣoḍaśa śrāddhasya preta tva vimukti kāmanā śruteḥ preta tva vimukti hetu ṣoḍaśa śrāddhe saṅkalpam vidhāya mahājanānām ācārāt kāmya tvam nindā artha vādena akaraṇe pratyavāya śruteḥ avaśya kartavya tvam tathā sandhyā upāsanam api phala śruteḥ kāmyam akaraṇe naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca niyata kartavya tākam yat tu yāge kāmya tve api na niyata kartavya tāka tvam tad akaraṇe prāyaścitta anupadeśāt na ca nitye phala kāmanāyāḥ asambhavaḥ tri kāla kāmyaḥ tava pāṭha vat nitye phala kāmanām ambhavāt yat tu prathama pravṛtta āharaḥ śrutyā tad kāla jīvimācasya adhikāra bodhanāt na phala kāmasya adhikāraḥ iti tat na aharahar śruti artha vādayoḥ prathama gṛhīta eka vākyatā balena tad kāla jīvi phala kāmasya sa āvalita adhikārāt arthavāda upasthita phala anvayam vinā eka vākyatā bhaṅgāt na ca artha vādasya stuti paratva at na eka vākyatā bādhakam vinā sva artha aparityāgāt vidhi vākya upasthite phale vidhi vākya stha phalam ādāya eva aharahar śrutyā kārya tā bodhanāt 
[131,vi_131,vii]	nanu evam tad kāla jīvi kāminaḥ adhikāre yadā phala kāmanā virahaḥ tadā aśuceḥ iva adhikāra abhāvāt niyata kartavyatā na syāt adhikṛta akaraṇe pratyavāyaḥ na tu akaraṇa mātraḥ iti ced na naimittike api tad kāle kasyacid kāmanā virahiṇaḥ aniyata kartavyatā āpatteḥ atha apavāda abhāvena autsargikī phala kāmanā asti eva phala jñānasya sva viṣayaka icchā janaka svabhāva tvāt yasya tu mumukṣa apavādena phala antare kāmanā na asti tasya akaraṇe api na pratyavāyaḥ iti na tat niyata kartavya tāka tvam naimittike tathā nitye api mumukṣayā phala kāmanā bādhena akaraṇe api na pratyavāyaḥ iti tulyam kiñca arthavāda upasthita phala upādhikartavya tve avagate akurvan vihitam karma ityādi vākyāt śauce sati sandhyā vandana akaraṇe nindā artha vādena ca naraka śruteḥ prāyaścitta upadeśāt ca pratyavāyaḥ kalpyate tad phala kāmanā virahe api pratyavāya parihāra artham niyamataḥ pravartate vidhi pravṛtti anantaram pratyavāyasya prāmāṇika tvāt akaraṇet mukhasya karaṇena pratyavāya prāgabhāvasya sādhya tvāt naimittike phala upādhi kartavya tve kāmanā virahe api niyata kartavya tāvat 
[131,viii]	yat tu niṣphale api nitye veda adhīna kārya tā jñānāt pravartate iti tat na duḥkha eka phala tvena jñāyamāne prekṣāvatām kṛteḥ anutpāda niyamāt ayogya tayā nitye kṛti sādhya tvasya bodhayitum aśakyatvāt atas eva sandhyā upāsanam aphalam api kriyate veda bodhita kartavya tāka tvāt iti āśaṅkya guru matam etat na guroḥ matam iti abhiprāyeṇa īpekṣitavān ācāryaḥ 
[131,ix]	yat tu paṇḍa apūrvam svatas eva prayojanam iti uktam tat api na evam tava api kāmya tve nitya tva hāni āpatteḥ kiñca sukham duḥkha abhāvaḥ ca mukhyam prayojanam tad sādhanañca gauṇam nitya apūrvantu teṣu na ekam api paṇḍa apūrva tvāt kāmyāpūrvañca sukha hetuḥ gauṇam prayojanam pravartaka vidhi anurodhena tat api pravartakam kalpyate iti ced na pravartanīyena lokena tasya prayojana tvena ajñānāt guruṇā nitya apūrvam prayojanam uktam iti ucyamāne api na ādaraḥ prekṣāvatām mukti svargau ca alaukikau api sukha duḥkha abhāvasa jātīya tayā prayojane tasmāt evam vadan guruḥ api laghuḥ eva 
[132,i]	tat ayam saṅkṣepaḥ nitye duḥkha eka phala tvena pravṛtti anupapatteḥ phala upādhi kartavya tā tat ca phalam duḥkha sādhana abhāvaḥ pāṇḍa apūrvam vā iti tad icchā pravṛci artham pratyaham upeyā tām vinā pravṛtti anupapatteḥ tathā ca artha vādikam vidhi vākya śru tañca phalam astu kṛtam anyena na ca kāmanā virahe niyata kartavyatā na syāt apūrva ādi icchā virahe api tulya tvāt pratyavāya parihā artham niyamataḥ pravṛttiḥ tulyā eva yatra ca na phala śrutiḥ tatra viśvajit nyāya iti 
[132,ii]	nanu idam iṣṭa sādhanam iti jñānāt etat sādhyam iṣṭam iti jñānāt ca pravṛtti darśanāt prathamasya eva pravartaka tve kim vinigamakam ucyate phala icchāyām sva viṣaya viśeṣyaka jñānasya hetu tvena kḷpta tvāt upāya cikīrṣā api bādhakam vinā tathā vastutas tu kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭa jñānasya pravṛrtaka tve yajeta iti padāt prathamam kṛti sādhyaḥ yāgaḥ iti jñānam tatas kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ iti jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna sādhya tvāt viśiṣṭa jñānasya iti jñāna dvayam tava mama tu yāgaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ iṣṭa sādhanam iti ekam eva jñānam na ca kṛti sādhya tvam yāge bodhayitvā kṛti sādhya yāgasya sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ iti liṅā bodhayitum śakyam api eka sva artha anvayam aparada arthe bodhayitvā tad anvita apara sva artha nvaya bodhaka tvasya pade avyutpatteḥ yajipade ca kṛtyā yāga anvayam bodhayitvā paryavasite punar sva artha anvaya bodhaka tve āvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ 
[132,iii^1]	atha sādhyam iṣṭam yasya iti sādhya iṣṭaka tvam śakyam tathā ca bahu brīhi artha apekṣayā iṣṭasya sādhanam iti ṣaṣṭhī arthasya laghu tvāt tat eva śakyam kiñca tad sādhya tvam na niyamataḥ tat uttara sattvam daṇḍa sādhye ghaṭe vyabhicārāt na api tad avacchinna kṣaṇa uttarakṣaṇaḥ eva sattvam eva kāra vyavacchedya tad anuttara samayasya ākāśe aprasiddheḥ śabdasya tat asādhya tva āpatteḥ atas eva na tad abhāva vyāpaka abhāva pratiyogi tvam rūpe rasa sādhya tva āpatteḥ ca na api tad avadhika uttara tva vyāpya samaya sambandhaḥ uttara tva vyāpya tvam hi uttara tva an adhikaraṇa kāla āvṛtti tvam tat ca ākāśe aprasiddham gurutarañca tasmāt tad sādhanaka tvam eva tad sādhya tvam evañca lāghavāt tad sādhana tva jñānam eva pravartakam na tu tad sādhanaka tva jñānam iti syāt etat iṣṭa tva jñānasya pravartaka tve tṛptaḥ api bhojane pravarteta 
[132,iii^2]	manasā tṛpteḥ iṣṭa tva jñānāt atha svarūpa satī api phala icchā kāraṇam sā ca siddha tayā tṛptau na asti iti ced tarhi hantā evam āvaśyaka tvāt phala icchā eva kāraṇam na tu tat jñānam gauravāt kiñca icchā jñānasya kāraṇa tve icchā kāraṇam na syāt sva jñānena tad nāśāt icchā tad jñāna dhārā kalpane anavasthānāt api ca icchā viṣayaḥ sukham iti jñānam na mānasam sukhasya asiddha tayā tad viśeṣya ka sākṣatikārasya tad sannikarṣam vinā abhāvāt odana ādau api iṣṭa tva jñānam na sambhavati manasaḥ bahis asvātantryāt na api cakṣuḥ ādinā jñātaḥ kṛtaḥ iti vat iṣṭa tva jñānam tatra viśeṣya sannikarṣāt vastutas tu iṣṭasya viśiṣya sukha tva ādinā ajñāne yāga pākāt āviṣṭa sādhana tā jñānepya pravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iṣṭasya alpa adhika bhāvena nānā prakāra tvena ca viśiṣya anadhyavasāyāt na ca iṣṭa viṣaya tā avacchedaka sukha tva ādeḥ upalakṣaṇam iṣṭa tvam sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhaneṣu anugatasya upalakṣyasya abhāvena ananugamāt iti 
[132,iv_132,v]	ucyate yatra icchā tad sādhana tā jñānam eva loka vedasādhāraṇam pravartakam teṣām sukha duḥkha abhāva tad sādhana tvena icchā viṣayāṇām ananugatanām api vastu sadicchā viṣaya tvam eva anugamakam evam yadā sukha ādau icchā bhavati sva kṛti sādhya tve sati sukha ādi sādhanam iti jñānam tadā pāka ādau pravartate nanu evam pravartaka jñāna viṣayasya nānā tvena tad śaktasya vidhi pratyayasya nānā artha tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na sukha tva ādinā anugatam iṣṭa tvena ananugatam phalam prati sādhana tvasya yāgadeḥ liṅga ādinā bodhanāt tathā ca phalānām anugama artham phala icchā śakyā na tu icchā jñāna kāraṇa tvena 
[132,vi]	atha evam sukha ādi sādhana tvena jñānam pravartakam tat na śakyam ananugamāt yat ca śakyam iṣṭa sādhana tvam tat jñānam na pravartakam iti vidheḥ pravartaka tā na syāt iti ced sākṣāt evam eva kintu iṣṭa sādhanam yāgaḥ iti liṅā bodhite iṣṭa ākāṅkṣāyām kāmya tvena śrutaḥ svargaḥ eva iṣṭa tvena avagamyate tad anantaram svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāt svarga sādhanam yāgaḥ iti jñānam pravartakam utpadyate evañca vidhi janya jñāna janyam jñānam pravartakam yat tu sarveṣām eva vidheḥ na sākṣāt pravṛtaka tvam vidhi bodhakāt sva kṛti sādhya tva ādeḥ anavagamāt sva iṣṭa sādhana tvañca aham iṣṭa sādhana yāgakaḥ svarga kāma tvāt darśa vākya avagata svarga kāma vat iti anantaram arthāt pratīyate tat na yatra icchā tad sādhanam iti śābda jñānāt eva pravṛtti upapatteḥ tad pratītiḥ niṣphalā 
[132,vii^1_132,vii^2]	anye tu sādhana tva mātram vidhi arthaḥ svarga ādi sādhana tāla ābhaḥ tu samabhivyāhārāt iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api tasya upajīvya tvāt tathā hi yajeta iti anena yāgaḥ kṛti sādhyaḥ sādhanañca iti bodhite sādhanasya sādhya ākāṅkṣāyām kāmanā viṣaya tvena śrutaḥ asiddhaḥ svargaḥ eva sādhana ākāṅkṣī sādhya tvena avagamyate upasthita tvāt na ca yāgasya sādhana ākāṅkṣā kṛti sādhya tvena eva upasthiteḥ atas eva viśva jit ādau svargaḥ eva sādhya tvena kalpyate iti iṣṭa sādhana tā vidhi pakṣe api tarati mṛtyum tarati brahya hatyām yaḥ aśvamedhena yajate iti ādi artha vāde vidhi bodhya iṣṭa sādhana tvasya artha vādāt eva avagamāt kutas vidhi kalpanam iti ced na avinā abhāvāt tathābhūta sādhana tvasya vidheya tva vyāpta tvāt vyāpaka anupalambha bādha uddhārāya vā prayojana abhāvāt na tad kalpanam tatra iti api āhuḥ yat tu iṣṭa sādhanatva abhidhāne karaṇe liṅaḥ anuśāsanāt darśa paurṇamāsābhyām iti anabhihita adhikāra vihitā tṛtīyā na syāt iti tat na upāya tā mātra abhidhāne api tad viśeṣa karaṇa tva anabhidhānāt vastutastu abhihita anvaya labhyam yāga iṣṭa sādhana tvam iṣṭa sādhana tva mātrasya vidhi artha tvāt
